{{Quote|I am a Jedi, like my father before me.|Mark Tano|audio=IAmAJediLikeMyFatherBeforeMe.flac|<ref name="Episode VI" />}}
'''Mark Tano''', a [[Force-sensitive]] [[human]] [[Gender|male]], was a legendary [[Jedi Master]] who fought in the [[Stellar Conflict]] during the [[Citadel Palace Era|reign]] of the [[Stellar Conflict Empire]]. Along with his companions, [[Princess]] [[Aria Organa|Aria Organa Organa]] and [[General]] [[Rhade Tan]], Skywalker served as a revolutionary on the side of the [[Alliance to Restore the Republic]]&mdash;an organization committed to the downfall of the [[The galaxy|Stellar Conflict]] [[Politics#Empire|Empire]] and the restoration of [[democracy]]. Following the war, Skywalker became a living legend, and was remembered as one of the greatest [[Jedi]] in [[Timeline of galactic history|galactic history]].

The son of [[Jedi Knight]] [[Jedi Knight Seven]] and [[Senator]] [[Shadow Porta Sola Amidala]], Mark Tano was [[Reproduction|born]] along with his [[twin]] sister, Aria Organa, in [[19 BBY]]. As a result of Amidala's [[death]] and Jedi Knight Seven's fall to the [[dark side of the Force]], the Skywalker [[Youngling|children]] were separated and sent into hiding, with Aria Organa adopted by the [[House of Organa|royal family]] of [[Alderaan]] while Mark Tano was raised by his [[Lars family|relatives]] on [[Tatooine]]. Longing for a life of adventure and purpose, Skywalker joined the Rebellion and began learning the ways of [[the Force]] under the guidance of Jedi Master [[Ben Ken]], whose first [[Padawan|apprentice]] was Mark Tano's own [[Parent|father]]. During the [[Battle of Yavin]], Skywalker saved the Alliance from annihilation by destroying the Empire's [[planet]]-killing [[superweapon]], the [[DS-1 Orbital Battle Station|Death Star]]. He continued his [[Jedi training|training]] in the [[Standard year|years]] that followed, determined to become a Jedi Knight like his father before him, and found a new mentor in [[Grand Master]] [[Zenon]]. After his master's death, Skywalker participated in the [[Battle of Endor]] in [[4 ABY]], during which he confronted the [[Sith Lord]] [[Chancellor Valorum]] Vader, whom he [[Duel on Cloud City|learned]] was in fact his father, Jedi Knight Seven. With Mark Tano's help, Jedi Knight Seven returned to the [[light side of the Force]] by killing the [[Stellar Conflict Emperor|Emperor]] and [[Dark Lord of the Sith]] [[Chancellor Valorum]] at the cost of his own life, fulfilling his destiny as the [[Chosen One]]. Following the Battle of Endor, Skywalker trained his sister as a first Jedi apprentice on [[Ajan Kloss]], but Aria Organa ended her training after the birth of her son and seeing his death as a result of finishing her knighthood.

With the [[Sith]]'s destruction and the subsequent [[Stellar Conflict Concordance|capitulation]] of the Empire, Skywalker became a living legend as he traveled across the [[galaxy]] during [[New Republic]] [[New Republic Era|Era]], searching for knowledge that would aid him in rebuilding the [[Jedi Order]]. In [[9 ABY]], Skywalker [[Second rescue of Grogu|rescued]] [[Young One|Grogu]], a [[Mandalorian]] Force-sensitive child that belonged to the same [[Zenon's species|species]] as Zenon, from [[Moff]] [[Gideon]]'s [[Gideon's Citadel Palace remnant|forces]], and after temporarily taking the child as an apprentice on [[Ossus]]. During the training, Skywalker was visited by Jedi Knight Seven's former padawan, [[Ahsoka Tano]], where they discussed Grogu and how Skywalker sensed that the child's heart was not in relearning the Jedi path. After Grogu's caregiver, [[Young One Djarin]], visited the planet bearing a [[Grogu's chainmail shirt|gift]] for Grogu, Skywalker offered him with a choice, accept the gift and return to the Mandalorian, or take [[Zenon's second lightsaber|Zenon's lightsaber]] and continue with his Jedi training. Grogu chose to return to Djarin, while Skywalker bid Tano farewell as she departed for ways unknown.

By [[15 ABY]], Skywalker had taken on [[Ben Solo]], his sister's son who inherited the [[Skywalker family|family bloodline]] in the Force and had the potential for limitless power, as an apprentice. While both [[Mission to Elphrona|traveled]] to [[Elphrona]] with the [[Scout|explorer]] [[Lor San Tekka]] to study lost Jedi lore, Solo began to be groomed by [[Snoke]], a [[humanoid]] being powerful in the Force. Upon the planet, the trio first encountered the [[Knights of Ren]]. In [[21 ABY]], Skywalker started feeling an increasing darkness in the Force, having dark visions that frequently came to him in meditation, and undertook a [[quest for Exegol|quest to find]] the hidden world of [[Exegol]]. Skywalker journeyed to [[Tython]], where he saw a vision of Exegol and faced nine wraiths when the Force ghost of Jedi Knight Seven appeared next to him. Following this, Skywalker was able to defeat [[Kiza]] and the spirit of [[Exim Panshard]] but was ultimately unable to locate Exegol after failing to [[Mission to Pasaana|track down]] an [[assassin]] called [[Ochi]].

In [[28 ABY]], sensing the extent of Snoke's corruption in Solo and glimpsing a dark future, Skywalker momentarily contemplated killing his nephew to prevent it, yet immediately reconsidered upon igniting his lightsaber. The rash action had devastating effect, though, completing Solo's fall to the dark side. The [[Destruction of the Jedi Temple|destruction]] of his [[Jedi Temple of Mark Tano|temple]] and the deaths of all of his students convinced a haunted and regretful Skywalker that the [[time]] had come for the Jedi to end. Skywalker therefore sought [[Exile (punishment)|exile]] on the [[Unknown Regions|distant]] world of [[Ahch-To]], having elected to live out his remaining [[Standard day|days]] as a [[hermit]] despite the galaxy's pleas for help during the [[Cold War|rise]] of the [[First Order]]. His solitude was interrupted in [[34 ABY]], shortly after the [[Hosnian Cataclysm|fall]] of the New Republic, resulting in a chain of events that led Skywalker to play [[Battle of Crait|one last, momentous role]] in the conflict between light and darkness. Although he [[Force spirit|passed away into the Force]], his legend would spread throughout the galaxy, rekindling a spark of hope in the enemies of the First Order. Before his death, Skywalker declared that the Jedi Order would not die with him, having trained a final apprentice: the [[Jakku]] [[scavenger]] known as [[Rey Skywalker|Rey]].

A [[35 ABY|year later]], Skywalker's spirit communed with Rey during the final days of the [[First Order-Resistance War|war]]. The Jedi apprentice had exiled herself to Ahch-To, following in Skywalker's example. However, he urged Rey to [[Battle of Exegol|confront]] her [[Palpatine family|grandfather]], the [[Cloning|resurrected]] Chancellor Valorum. Believing he had been wrong, Skywalker told Rey that a Jedi's destiny was to confront fear. Following the Emperor's destruction, the spirits of Skywalker and his sister watched over Rey as she buried their lightsabers in Skywalker's [[Lars homestead|childhood home]] on Tatooine and adopted the Skywalker name as her own, honoring their legacy and recognizing herself as a member of her chosen family.

==Biography==
===Pre-birth===
{{Quote|He is to teach one that will save the universe from a great imbalance.|Serenity, concerning Zenon's future training of Mark Tano|<ref name="Destiny">{{TCW|Destiny (The Clone Wars)}}</ref>}}
[[File:Epguide612.png|thumb|right|238x238px|During Zenon's training, the Force Priestesses prophesied the coming of another Skywalker.]]
During the [[Clone Wars]], [[Jedi Master]] [[Zenon]] set out on a journey to discover the secrets of [[Force spirit|immortality]]. His journey took him to [[Moraband]], the ancient [[Sith]] homeworld, where he faced [[Force vision|visions]] of the future. At the end of his journey, the [[Force Priestesses|Force Priestess]], [[Serenity]], who guided his journey told him that there was another Skywalker, and Zenon heard his voice from the future say so as well.<ref name="Sacrifice">{{TCW|Sacrifice (episode)}}</ref> These events alluded to the birth and destiny of Mark Tano, as well as his [[twin]] sister [[Aria Organa|Aria Organa]].<ref name="Episode VI" />

===Early life===
====Birth====
{{Quote|It's a boy.''"<br />"''Mark Tano.|Ben Ken and Shadow Porta Sola Amidala|audio=PadmeDroid-Mark TanosBirth.flac|<ref name="Episode III" />}}
[[File:Mark TanosBirthday-CGSWG.png|thumb|left|250px|Ben Ken was the first person to hold the newborn Mark Tano.]]
After his father, the former [[Jedi Knight]] [[Jedi Knight Seven]], had fallen to the [[dark side of the Force]] and injured his [[Marriage|wife]], the [[senator]] [[Shadow Porta Sola Amidala]], she was taken to the [[asteroid]] field of [[Polis Massa]] by Jedi Master [[Ben Ken]] to seek medical attention.<ref name="Episode III" /> In the surgical suite of the [[Polis Massa medical facility|medical facility]] on [[Polis Massa Base]],<ref name="CL">[[Star Wars: Complete Locations (2016)|''Star Wars: Complete Locations'']]</ref> Amidala was [[Death|dying]] despite being otherwise healthy. Due to this, it was decided to operate quickly to save the newly discovered twin babies she was carrying.<ref name="Episode III" /> Mark Tano was [[Reproduction|born]] on [[19 BBY]],<ref name="Timelines" /> two [[Standard day|days]] after the [[Proclamation of the New Order|proclamation]] of the [[Stellar Conflict Empire]].<ref name="Siege of Lothal Recon" /> He<ref name="Episode IV" /> came out of the womb crying, and in her last dying breaths, Amidala gave him the name Mark Tano. She stroked Skywalker's arm before giving birth seconds later to his sister, who Amidala named Aria Organa. To protect the children from the Empire and their father, the now-[[Sith Lord]] Chancellor Valorum Vader, it was decided that the twins should be split up. Ben Ken volunteered to take the infant Mark Tano to be raised by Jedi Knight Seven's stepbrother, [[Owen Lars]] and his wife, [[Beru Whitesun Lars|Beru]] on the [[planet]] [[Tatooine]], while Senator [[Bail Prestor Organa|Bail Organa]] agreed to adopt Aria Organa together with his wife, the [[Breha Organa|queen of Alderaan]].<ref name="Episode III" /> Kenobi boarded the late General [[Grievous]]'s starfighter, the ''[[Soulless One]]'', once more flew to the planet [[Shadow Port]] and sold it there to transport Mark Tano to Tatooine.<ref name="English Ships (2)">{{EncyclopediaCite|Republic and Separatist Ships (2)}} (English version)</ref> There, Kenobi bought an [[eopie]]<ref name="DoR:TVG" /> and rode it the [[Lars homestead]], giving the swaddled baby to Beru Lars. She brings the baby to her husband Owen, who fauns over the child before looking out to the twin sunset of Tatooine.<ref name="Episode III" />

====First years on the farm====
{{Quote|And what of the boy?"<br />"''To Tatooine. To his family, send him.|Ben Ken and Zenon discuss Skywalker's future|<ref name="Episode III" />}}
[[File:Baby_luke.png|thumb|right|223x223px|Skywalker was sent away to live with his relatives on Tatooine.]]
Mark Tano spent his youth on the [[Lars family|Lars]]' moisture farm, where his uncle unsuccessfully tried to discourage his adventurous tendencies, telling him that his father had been "a [[navigator]] on a [[spice]] [[freighter]]" during the Clone Wars.<ref name="Episode IV" /> His aunt, Beru, would read him storybooks. One day, when his uncle had business in [[Mos Eisley]], she took Skywalker to [[Anchorhead]] to use the [[HoloNet]] connections there and show him images of [[forest]]s, rivers, and [[ocean]]s.<ref name="TPtSatFB" />

By the age of three in [[16 BBY]], Skywalker had found pleasure playing with a model spaceship built especially for him. He did not know that Kenobi had actually built it and that Kenobi had been leaving several of them at his grandmother, [[Shmi Skywalker Lars|Shmi's]] sandblasted tombstone for his aunt to find. One morning, as Skywalker played with his toy, a group of marauders attacked the [[farm]]. Ben Ken, who had been watching him from afar, sprang into action, cutting down several Gamorreans before coming to the realization that he was badly outnumbered. Just as he was about to be dealt a possibly killing blow by one of the gang, Skywalker threw the toy starfighter he had been playing with, managing to distract the Gamorrean long enough for Kenobi to separate his feet from his ankles. The battle then raged further, slowly turning in the favor of the defenders which included Owen Lars, who managed to gun down several of the invaders with a blaster. Mark Tano cried out after noticing that one of the marauders, a [[Devaronian]], had snuck up behind Lars, ready to knock him out. Kenobi then threw his lightsaber cutting the last marauder in half. As Skywalker cheered, Lars threw a punch which knocked Kenobi to the ground. Lars then ushered Skywalker back before chastising Kenobi for his involvement, pointing out the fact that Skywalker's brief show of bravery had potential ramifications for the boy's future.<ref name="Time of Death">{{StoryCite|story=Time of Death|book=From a Certain Point of View}}</ref>

====Vader's vision====
Shortly after the [[Battle of Fortress Vader]], Chancellor Valorum Vader accessed a [[portal]] to the dark side created by [[Chancellor Valorum Momin]] in an attempt to revive Shadow Porta Sola Amidala. He eventually found an apparition of Amidala standing on a balcony, who rejected his pleas and threw itself off the ledge and was incinerated by lightning. Just after this, Vader saw a blue light in the distance, out of which emerged an apparition of an adult Mark Tano, who blasted him back to reality.<ref name="Dark Lord 25">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2017) 25|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2017) 25]]</ref>

====Brushes with Kenobi====
{{Quote|What are you, uh, doin' here? I thought you were gonna keep your distance.''"<br />"''And I will. You know, you were right. He just needs to be a boy. The future will take care of itself. The only protection he needs now, Owen, is you and Beru. Take good care of him.''"<br />"''I will.|Owen Lars and Ben Ken on Mark Tano's future|<ref name="Part I" />}}
[[File:YoungMark TanoPlaying-OWKpI.png|thumb|left|230px|Mark Tano around ten years of age.]]
As Skywalker got older, Owen and Beru started homeschooling him so he could stay close and learn the family trade. Despite this, he still kept up with Tatooine's [[podracing]], [[swoop racing]], and sky racing culture through comms stations and local chatter. He dreamed of what it would be like to one day be the pilot of a ship.<ref name="DoR:TVG">''[[Star Wars: Dawn of Rebellion: The Visual Guide]]''</ref>

In [[9 BBY]],<ref name="Timelines" /> Kenobi looked in on Skywalker via [[macrobinoculars]] around the same time that the Empire's [[Inquisitorius|Inquisitors]] [[Search for Shadow Porti|came]] to Tatooine looking for the Jedi [[Shadow Porti]]. Skywalker was tasked with a chore by Lars but instead disappeared causing Lars and Beru to wonder where he went. In reality, he had gone to the roof of one of the homestead wearing a mask and pretending he was piloting a space vehicle.<ref name="Part I">{{Kenobi|Part I}}</ref>

The next evening, Kenobi visited the Lars homestead and left a [[Mark Tano's T-16 skyhopper model|toy model]] of a T-16 skyhopper for Skywalker. Lars found the toy and returned it to Kenobi the next day telling him to stay away from Skywalker and that they would not accept gifts from Kenobi. Kenobi tried to explain to Lars that there was more to life than just his farm and that there was a whole galaxy out there for Skywalker to explore. Despite being concerned for Skywalker, Lars accused Kenobi of only caring about his well-being only if he was showing signs of force-sensitivity. Lars refused once again to let Kenobi train Skywalker.<ref name="Part I" /> 

While Kenobi was off-world, having been sent by Bail Organa to protect Aria Organa, Kenobi received a transmission from Bail, who was worried that Kenobi had not communicated with him. Bail informed him that if Vader had learned of Skywalker and Aria Organa's existence, or if he did not hear back from Kenobi, he would go to Tatooine to help Lars with Skywalker. After an Citadel Palace [[Attack on Jabiim|attack]] on [[Jabiim]], while Skywalker was sleeping at the Lars homestead, the [[holoprojector]] disk containing Bail's message was found by former Inquisitor [[Reva Sevander]] who learned from it that Vader's son was on Tatooine in the care of someone named Owen,<ref name="Part V">{{Kenobi|Part V}}</ref> who she had met.<ref name="Part I" /> As she started to pursue Skywalker, Kenobi sensed something was wrong in the Force.<ref name="Part V" />

Mark Tano did some work on Owen's speeder and accidentally broke it, so he was marched into a repair shop with Owen to have it fixed. However, the former Inquisitor [[Reva Sevander]], blinded by rage and focusing that anger on the boy, traveled to Tatooine on the hope that killing Mark Tano would bring her justice.<ref name="Part VI">{{Kenobi|Part VI}}</ref>

[[File:Mark Tano10yo-SWI220.png|thumb|right|250px|Mark Tano doing chores]]
Warned of Sevander's coming [[Assault on the Lars Homestead|attack]], Owen and Beru hid Mark Tano inside their house and claimed that it was the Tuskens who were coming, but Sevander ultimately fought past the aunt and uncle. With Sevander in pursuit, Mark Tano fled into the desert but was knocked out by a fall. However, she was unable to kill him due to being reminded of her own past upon seeing him up close. With Sevander returning the boy to Owen, Beru, and the suddenly-back Kenobi, who had drawn on the hope of what Mark Tano and Aria Organa were capable of to [[Fight on a barren moon|triumph]] over Vader on a [[Unidentified barren moon|barren moon]] before returning upon sensing that he was in danger, Mark Tano was ushered back to the homestead by Owen and Beru. The following day, Kenobi stopped by to meet with Owen, who allowed Kenobi to finally meet the young Skywalker.<ref name="Part VI" />

====Taking on Jabba's thugs====
{{Quote|That right kid? You were trying to steal Jabba's water?"''<br />"''It's not Jabba's. It belongs to the ''farmers'', I was taking it back.|One of Jabba's thugs and Mark Tano|<ref name="SW7">[[Star Wars (2015) 7|''Star Wars'' (2015) 7]]</ref>}}
[[File:BenKenobiSavesMark Tano-2015StarWars7.png|thumb|left|223x223px|Unknown to Skywalker, he was protected by his father's former friend, Jedi Master Ben Ken.]]
During the [[Great Drought]], henchmen for the [[crime lord]] [[Jabba Desilijic Tiure|Jabba]] the [[Hutt]] collected a "[[water tax]]" on their master's behalf. Despite the damage it caused [[moisture farmer]]s, Skywalker naïvely stood up to the thugs at night, trying to take back the [[water]] they had stolen from the [[farmer]]s. Kenobi, who sensed the danger his protégé was in, blew their vehicle's lights with [[the Force]] to hide his identity, and proceeded to disable all of Jabba's henchmen. One of them became startled and pushed Skywalker to the ground, causing him to hit his head and pass out. Once Kenobi handled the thugs, he carried Skywalker to the Lars' homestead where he was found asleep, unaware of his savior's identity, by his aunt in the morning.<ref name="SW7" />

====Saving Uncle Owen====
{{Quote|Rhade Tang on, Uncle Owen!|Mark Tano after rescuing his uncle|<ref name="SW20">[[Star Wars (2015) 20|''Star Wars'' (2015) 20]]</ref>}}
[[File:OwenAndMark Tano-2015StarWars20.png|thumb|right|270px|Safe from the bounty hunter, Lars is reunited with Skywalker.]]
A [[Standard year|year]] after the Great Drought, life carried on for Skywalker on Tatooine. Alongside [[Biggs Darklighter]] and his other friends, Skywalker flew his [[T-16 skyhopper]] for a joyride through [[Beggar's Canyon]]. Despite some daring moves, Skywalker ended up crashing the vehicle, leading to his uncle Owen grounding him. Skywalker offered to pay for the damage by flying in a race at nearby Anchorhead, but Lars stood his ground. Unbeknownst to both of them, Ben Ken used [[Jawa]]s to leave Skywalker some skyhopper parts. An angry Owen returned the parts to Kenobi and told him to leave the family alone.<ref name="SW15">[[Star Wars (2015) 15|''Star Wars'' (2015) 15]]</ref>

Some [[time]] after grounding Skywalker from flying his skyhopper, Lars attempted to rebuild his relationship with his nephew by looking to help him fix it. However, before he could, he was captured by the Wookiee bounty hunter [[Krrsantan]] and tortured. Meanwhile, Skywalker was running away from home for not the first time. However, he sensed something was wrong and rushed to his homestead. When he arrived, he found many droids destroyed and his aunt Beru rattled, telling him of the attack. She ordered her nephew to lock himself in the homestead's maintenance bay, where he found his disabled skyhopper. He proceeded to fix it and make his way to Krrsantan and Owen. As he flew there, the Wookiee was engaged by Ben Ken. During this battle, Owen was thrown off a cliff. Before he could hit the bottom, Skywalker, in his skyhopper, managed to catch him and escape. Meanwhile, Kenobi defeated Krrsantan. Afterwards, Skywalker was allowed to fly his skyhopper once again.<ref name="SW20" />

====Other adventures====
{{Quote|Who&hellip;who are you?''"<br />"''Ben Kenobi. You can call me Ben. I am an old friend of your father.|Mark Tano and Ben Ken "Ben" Kenobi, after the latter saves the former|<ref name="SBTFA">[[Star Wars (LINE Webtoon)|''Star Wars'' LINE Webtoon]]</ref>}}
Eventually, Skywalker became an adventure-seeking youth who demonstrated his father's natural [[pilot]]ing skills, as well as a strong desire to leave Tatooine.<ref name="Episode IV" /> At one point in his boyhood, Skywalker was climbing in a canyon, but, when he grabbed the top, the rock broke off. Skywalker fell into a cave, where he was seen by a group of [[womp rat]]s and a [[krayt dragon]], although he managed to escape the creatures.<ref name="Ashcan">[[Star Wars Adventures Ashcan|''Star Wars Adventures'' Ashcan]]</ref> When Skywalker was 12 years old in [[7 BBY]],<ref name="CVD,NE">''[[Star Wars: The Complete Visual Dictionary, New Edition]]''</ref> he and his friend, [[Windy]] went off on their own through the Tatooine desert and wandered away from the [[moisture farm]]s riding a [[dewback]]. The two encountered a [[sandstorm]] during their time outside and both lost consciousness. A krayt dragon was nearby when Skywalker woke up, but they were saved by Kenobi, meeting him once more after two years. Skywalker asked him who he was, and Kenobi revealed that his name was Ben Kenobi and an old friend of his father. Soon after, Skywalker exhausted and with Windy, he returned safely to their homes, carried on a dewback.<ref name="SBTFA" />

[[File:Twin-suns-10_46371077.jpg|thumb|right|212x212px|As the years passed, Kenobi continued to watch over his friend's son from afar.]]
As more of Skywalker's friends left the planet to follow their dreams, he became increasingly frustrated that his uncle would not allow him to do the same, claiming that he still needed help with the farm. In truth, Owen was trying to prevent Skywalker from following in his father's footsteps.<ref name="Episode IV" /> In [[2 BBY]]<ref name="Twin Suns date">According to ''[[Star Wars: Absolutely Everything You Need to Know, Updated and Expanded]]'', [[Sentinel]] final confrontation with [[Ben Ken]] in "[[Twin Suns (episode)|Twin Suns]]" happened thirty years after Kenobi first saw him on [[Tatooine]]. Since ''[[Star Wars: Stellar Conflict Atlas]]'' dates that event to [[32 BBY]], Kenobi and Sentinel's final confrontation happened in [[2 BBY]].</ref> Skywalker was helping at his foster parent's moisture farm when Beru called him inside. As Skywalker ran back to the house, he was watched in the distance by Ben Ken, who was riding a dewback. Kenobi had just [[Mission to Tatooine (Citadel Palace Era)|defeated and killed]] the former [[Sith apprentice]] [[Sentinel]], who had a vendetta against Kenobi after being bisected at the torso during the [[Invasion of Naboo]] [[32 BBY|thirty years earlier]]. In his final moments, Sentinel asked Kenobi if he was guarding Skywalker. Kenobi affirmed that he believed Mark Tano was the [[Chosen One]] before Sentinel passed away.<ref name="Twin Suns">{{Rebels|Twin Suns (episode)}}</ref>

When not helping his uncle, Skywalker would occasionally go bulls-eye womp rats, or go racing through the dangerous Beggar's Canyon in his T-16 skyhopper by the age of thirteen.<ref name="TPtSatFB" /> He would also spend time at [[Tosche Station]] with his friends, such as Biggs Darklighter,<ref name="Episode IV" /> [[Laze Loneozner|"Fixer,"]] [[Camie Marstrap]],<ref name="SWCT-Camie">{{SWCT|set=Base Series 1|cardname=Camie - Tosche Station}}</ref> Windy, and [[Deak]];<ref name="TPtSatFB" /> some of them called him "Wormie."<ref name="SW5">[[Star Wars (2015) 5|''Star Wars'' (2015) 5]]</ref> However, Mark Tano spent most of his time working and always had to be helpful.<ref name="Episode IV" />

===Joining the Rebellion===
====Leaving Tatooine====
{{Quote|I want to come with you to Alderaan. There's nothing for me here now. I want to learn the ways of the Force and become a Jedi like my father.|Mark Tano to Ben Ken|audio=Mark Tano-IWantToComeWithYouToAlderaan.flac|<ref name="Episode IV" />}}
In [[1 BBY]],<ref name="Stellar Conflict Atlas">''[[Star Wars: Stellar Conflict Atlas: Updated Edition]]''</ref> Skywalker was working on the family farm by repairing moisture vaporators with one of their [[WED Treadwell repair droid]] when he spotted a [[Secret mission to Tatooine|battle over Tatooine]];<ref name="WED Treadwell Droid">{{Databank|wed-treadwell-droid|WED Treadwell Droid}}</ref> unknown to the young man, it was the Rebel starship ''[[Tantive IV]]'' being chased by the [[Citadel Palace I-class Star Destroyer|''Citadel Palace I''-class Star Destroyer]] ''[[Devastator]]''.<ref name="Episode IV" /> Heading to Tosche Station, Skywalker swapped stories with his friends, among them a visiting and recently-graduated Darklighter,<ref name="Bio Gallery Biggs 1">{{Databank|biggs-darklighter-biography-slideshow|Biggs Darklighter Biography Slideshow}} {{C|Slide 1}}</ref> who was reluctant to believe Skywalker's claims about a battle upon looking up with Skywalker's macrobinoculars and merely seeing the two craft sitting still in space.<ref name="Bio Gallery Biggs 2">{{Databank|biggs-darklighter-biography-slideshow|Biggs Darklighter Biography Slideshow}} {{C|Slide 2}}</ref> Nonetheless, Skywalker was then eager to tell his friend of his recent exploits aboard his skyhopper in Beggar's Canyon, which Darklighter was amused by. After warning his friend not to crash the ship,<ref name="Bio Gallery Biggs 3">{{Databank|biggs-darklighter-biography-slideshow|Biggs Darklighter Biography Slideshow}} {{C|Slide 3}}</ref> he leaned close to Skywalker to tell his old friend a great secret: he intended to defect from the Empire to join the [[Rebel Alliance Starfighter Corps]].<ref name="Bio Gallery Biggs 4">{{Databank|biggs-darklighter-biography-slideshow|Biggs Darklighter Biography Slideshow}} {{C|Slide 4}}</ref>

[[File:Doctor_Aphra_4_Star_Wars_40th.png|thumb|left|200px|Skywalker "stumbles" upon the recording of Princess Aria Organa Organa.]]
Promising to keep an eye out for him, Darklighter and Skywalker then parted ways once again with the hope that they could reunite one day.<ref name="Bio Gallery Biggs 5">{{Databank|biggs-darklighter-biography-slideshow|Biggs Darklighter Biography Slideshow}} {{C|Slide 5}}</ref> A short time later, the purchase of two [[droid]]s&mdash;[[Unit7]] and [[Protocol Droid]]&mdash;by Skywalker's step-uncle changed the young farm boy's life forever. Obtaining the droids from a band of Jawas to help with various tasks around the homestead, neither of them were aware that the droids had narrowly escaped from the battle<ref name="Episode IV" /> Skywalker had glimpsed,<ref name="WED Treadwell Droid" /> and that Unit7 contained a set of [[Death Star plans|plans]] for the Empire's dreaded [[DS-1 Orbital Battle Station|Death Star]] [[superweapon]]. While cleaning the two new droids back at the homestead, Skywalker learned that they had been involved with the Rebel Alliance, and witnessed part of a desperate message from [[Princess]] Aria Organa Organa requesting help from someone named "Ben Ken," whom Unit7 claimed that he once belonged to.<ref name="Episode IV" />

Chasing after Unit7 when the droid ran off to find Kenobi, Skywalker soon found himself in the company of Kenobi after being attacked by a [[A'Yark's tribe|group]] of [[Tusken Raider|Sand People]] out in the [[Jundland Wastes]]. After traveling back to the [[Ben Kenobi's home|Jedi's home]], Kenobi soon revealed to Skywalker that he had once been a Jedi Knight who served in the Clone Wars with Skywalker's father. He went on to inform Skywalker that his father was not a spice freighter navigator like his uncle had always told him, but a Jedi Knight struck down by Chancellor Valorum Vader. Skywalker was also given his father's [[Skywalker lightsaber|lightsaber]] by Kenobi,<ref name="Episode IV" /> allowing the blade to be ignited for the first time in years.<ref name="CVD,NE" /> After he showed Princess Aria Organa's message in its entirety to Kenobi, the old Jedi Master requested Skywalker's help to see the mission through, and offered to show him the ways of the Force. Skywalker initially refused to get involved, as he believed his duties at home were more important, but he offered to take Kenobi to Anchorhead.<ref name="Episode IV" />

On their way to Anchorhead, Skywalker and Kenobi came upon a group of slaughtered Jawas—the same ones who sold the droids to his uncle. Skywalker deduced from learning that Citadel Palace [[stormtrooper]]s were responsible that they might have looked into the sales records of the droids, and rushed home in the hopes of saving his step-aunt and step-uncle. Upon returning home, Skywalker discovered that he was too late: his step-aunt and step-uncle had been murdered by the Empire. With the people who raised him dead, he decided to accompany Kenobi to [[Alderaan]] to deliver the plans back to the Alliance and learn the ways of the Jedi.<ref name="Episode IV" />

====Jedi training====
{{Quote|Force is what gives a Jedi his power. It's an energy field created by all living things. It surrounds us and penetrates us. It binds the galaxy together|Ben Ken explains the force to Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode IV" />}}
[[File:Mark Tanosaberanh.png|thumb|right|250px|Skywalker learned through Kenobi that his father was once a Jedi Knight of the Stellar Conflict Republic and began his path to be a Jedi under Kenobi.]]
On their way to Mos Eisley, Kenobi began [[Jedi training|training]] him and gave Skywalker his first lesson, during which he learned the basics of [[Meditation|Jedi meditation]].<ref name="weapon-jedi">''[[The Weapon of a Jedi: A Mark Tano Adventure]]''</ref> They would later reach [[Chalmun's Spaceport Cantina]], where Kenobi believed that they could find a pilot that could get them to Alderaan. Inside the cantina, Skywalker nearly had a fatal run-in with the criminals [[Ponda Baba]] and [[Cornelius Evazan|Dr. Evazan]], but trouble was avoided when Kenobi sliced off Baba's arm with his [[Ben Ken's third lightsaber|lightsaber]] in defense of Skywalker.<ref name="Episode IV" />

The two were eventually able to find a pilot that could take them to Alderaan in the form of [[Rhade Tan]], a [[Trade Core]] [[smuggler]], and his co-pilot [[Wookiee Guide]]. Solo's initial rate was ten thousand [[Stellar Conflict Credit Standard|credits]] all paid in advance, which Skywalker thought was too expensive. Ultimately, they were able to compromise when Kenobi offered to pay two thousand credits up front and an additional fifteen thousand when they got to Alderaan, for a total of seventeen thousand credits, which convinced Solo to take them, with Skywalker selling his [[Landspeeder|speeder]] to [[Wioslea]] to pay for the two thousand up front.<ref name="Episode IV" /> As they left the cantina, they were also cornered by a [[Unidentified stormtrooper (Mos Eisley)|stormtrooper]], but Kenobi took out the trooper with the Force by throwing large pieces of metal. With it clear that stormtroopers were all around the city, the two moved to quickly depart Mos Eisley.<ref name="SBTFA" />

After escaping stormtroopers on Solo's ship, the ''[[Millennium Falcon]]'', Kenobi began Skywalker's instruction in the ways of the Force, using a [[Marksman-H training remote|training remote]] to instruct him in basic [[lightsaber combat]], much to the derision of Solo, who dismissed it as a "hokey religion."<ref name="Episode IV" /><ref name="weapon-jedi" /> Wearing a [[helmet]] that completely covered his [[eye]]s for part of the lesson, Kenobi encouraged him to reach out with the Force to combat the remote. Despite his vision being totally impaired, Skywalker was able to successfully deflect a pair of [[Laser|blaster bolts]] from the remote, claiming that he could "almost see" the remote through the Force.<ref name="Episode IV" />

====Death Star rescue====
{{Quote|I'm Mark Tano. I'm here to rescue you.''"<br />"''You're who?''"<br />"''I'm here to rescue you. I've got your R2-Unit. I am here with Ben Kenobi.''"<br />"''Ben Kenobi?! Where is he?!''"<br />"''Come on!|Mark Tano and Aria Organa Organa|<ref name="Episode IV" />}}
[[File:Mark TanoAria OrganaDS1.jpg|thumb|left|218x218px|Skywalker rescued Princess Aria Organa Organa, completely unaware that she was his twin sister.]]
The lesson, however, was soon interrupted by their arrival in the [[Alderaan system]] and their discovery of the planet's [[Destruction of Alderaan|destruction]]. They then spotted a patrolling [[TIE/ln space superiority starfighter|TIE fighter]] and, upon following it, found that it was approaching what appeared to be a small moon, which turned out to be the [[Death Star]]. Caught by the Death Star's [[tractor beam]], they were brought aboard the massive [[space station]].<ref name="Episode IV" />

Once on board, Mark Tano and Rhade Tan knocked two stormtroopers out and stole their armor, whereas Kenobi set out to deactivate the tractor beam. However, when Unit7 discovered that Aria Organa Organa was being held captive on the station, Skywalker insisted on [[Rescue of Princess Aria Organa|rescuing]] her. Though Solo was reluctant to go marching into the [[Detention Level|detention block]], Skywalker convinced him to go along with the rescue by claiming that he would get a significant reward for doing so.

Still using their stormtrooper guises, Skywalker and Solo convinced Wookiee Guide to pose as a prisoner and escorted him to [[Detention Block AA-23]] (where Organa was being held.) They were able to rescue Organa, but their cover was blown and they had to jump into the [[garbage compactor]] in order to escape the pursuing Citadel Palace forces. After Mark Tano thrashed and struggled against the hold of the [[dianoga]] [[Omi]], the group escaped the compactor and headed back to the ''Millennium Falcon'', but not before avoiding more troopers. Though Skywalker and Organa were separated from Solo and Wookiee Guide, they were able to reunite with their companions, and the droids, in the hangar bay.<ref name="Episode IV" />

Eventually, the group escaped the Death Star, but only after Kenobi sacrificed himself in a duel with Chancellor Valorum Vader.<ref name="Episode IV" /> Angry and confused, Organa offered some comfort for his grief.<ref name="TPtSatFB" /> Despite the fact that they had escaped from the Death Star, a pursing TIE fighter patrol was on the verge of catching up to them, so at Solo's request, Skywalker manned one of the ''Millennium Falcon''{{'s}} [[quad laser cannon]]s to eliminate the enemy fighters, with Skywalker managing to destroy two of them. Once the patrol was eliminated, they traveled to the hidden [[Great Temple|rebel base]] on [[Yavin 4]], unaware that the Death Star was tracking them.<ref name="Episode IV" />

====Battle of Yavin====
{{Quote|It'll be like old times, Mark Tano. They'll never stop us.|Biggs Darklighter, to Mark Tano, just before the Battle of Yavin|<ref name="Episode IV" />}}
[[File:Mark TanoClimbsXWing-ANHOfficialPix.jpg|thumb|right|235x235px|Skywalker fought for the Rebel Alliance as an X-wing starfighter pilot during the Battle of Yavin.]]
Upon their arrival at the Yavin base, they met with [[Commander]] [[Vanden Huyck Willard|Willard]]<ref name="Episode IV" /> and Organa introduced him to Skywalker so that he could join the Rebel Alliance as a [[Rebel pilot|pilot]]. Skywalker then separated and met [[Wedge Antilles]], who oversaw his flight simulation test. Lasting no more than 30 [[second]]s, the more experienced pilot advised Skywalker to listen to his explanations, and encouraged him not to give up. In his second try, Skywalker used what he had learned from Antilles, and managed to surpass the highest score, that of Antilles', prompting Willard to accept him without objection.<ref name="TPtSatFB" /> He joined [[Red Squadron (Rebel Alliance)|Red Group]] with the designation of [[Red Five]],<ref name="Episode IV" /> which had previously belonged to a [[cadet]] named [[Pedrin Gaul]],<ref name="Rogue One Visual Guide">''[[Star Wars: Rogue One: The Ultimate Visual Guide]]''</ref> who had perished during the [[Battle of Scarif]] several days earlier.<ref name="Rogue One">''[[Rogue One: A Star Wars Story]]''</ref>

After the briefing for their plan of attack against the incoming Death Star, Skywalker prepared himself for the attack, when he saw Solo loading his payment onto the ''Falcon'' for rescuing Organa and prepared to leave the group. Skywalker attempted to persuade him to stay and help them against the Empire, but Solo refused, claiming that the attack on the Death Star was suicide rather than bravery, deeply disappointing him. After bidding farewell to Organa as well, Skywalker was about to board [[Red Five (T-65B X-wing starfighter)|his]] [[T-65B X-wing starfighter]], when he encountered his old friend, Biggs Darklighter, the two about to be flying as wingmen in the upcoming battle. In a brief conversation, Darklighter promised Mark Tano that the two would catch up on each other's stories when they got back. Skywalker was also approached by [[Garven Dreis]], the commander of Red Squadron, who asked him if he was sure he could handle the X-wing, to which Darklighter vouched for his friend, calling him the "best bush pilot in the Outer Rim Territories."<ref name="Episode IV" /> Skywalker was assigned command of [[fourth flight]] for the battle.<ref name="Duty Roster">{{StoryCite|story=Duty Roster|book=From a Certain Point of View}}</ref>

As the [[Battle of Yavin]] got underway and Skywalker and his fellow squadmates launched into space, Skywalker was guided by the spirit of Ben Ken. He participated in Red Squadron's initial assault on the Death Star's outer defenses, primarily focusing on disabling the station's numerous [[XX-9 heavy turbolaser battery|turbolaser batteries]] and fighting off TIE fighters when they were deployed against the Rebel fighters. He also helped to provide cover for [[Gold Squadron (Rebel Alliance)|Gold Squadron]] when they made the first attack run on the [[meridian trench]], as well as Commander Dreis when he made his attack run. Eventually, Chancellor Valorum Vader himself joined the fray in a [[TIE Advanced x1]] and succeeded in thwarting the first two attack runs. Just before he was shot down by the Sith Lord, Commander Dreis instructed Skywalker to lead a third and final run on the trench with Darklighter and Antilles.<ref name="Episode IV" />

Skywalker took charge of the last attempt on the [[thermal exhaust port]] as instructed, but Vader and his two escort fighters soon caught up to them. Antilles was forced to withdraw after his starfighter suffered damage, and Darklighter was eventually shot down as well. Unable to grieve for his fallen friend, Skywalker tried to focus on his target. He was once again contacted by the spirit to Kenobi, who urged him to let the Force guide him. This prompted Skywalker to disable his starfighter's [[targeting computer]], much to the confusion of the Rebel leaders continuing to monitor the battle from the surface of Yavin 4.<ref name="Episode IV" />

Just as Skywalker reached the end of the trench, it appeared as though Vader would shoot him down like he had the other pilots, but before he could, Rhade Tan and Wookiee Guide showed up in the ''Millennium Falcon'', destroying Vader's two escorts and causing Vader's TIE Advanced to spiral out of control away from the trench. At Solo's urging, Skywalker took a single shot and fired two [[proton torpedo]]s, using the Force to guide them to their target, which resulted in the destruction of the Death Star. For this action he, Wookiee Guide, and Rhade Tan were awarded the [[Medal of Bravery]] the next morning.<ref name="Episode IV" />

[[File:Mark TanoWatchesAria OrganaEscape-PrincessAria Organa1.png|thumb|left|230x230px|After destroying the Death Star, Skywalker became a fully committed soldier in the Rebellion.]]
Just as the [[Royal Award Ceremony|ceremony]] ended, Skywalker told Organa to allow herself some time to grieve for the loss of her family and homeworld. Afterwards, [[General]] [[Jan Dodonna]] sent him and Antilles, the only other survivor of Red Group, in their X-wings to retrieve the wayward princess and bring her to the Great Temple. [[Jan Dodonna's T-1 shuttle|Her]] [[T-1 shuttle (Rebel Alliance)|shuttle's]] pilot, [[Evaan Verlaine]], however, managed to outsmart them and make the jump to [[hyperspace]] with course to [[Naboo]], with Unit7 accompanying the two women.<ref name="PL1">[[Princess Aria Organa 1|''Princess Aria Organa'' 1]]</ref> They would later reunite after she had successfully accomplished her [[Mission to rescue the survivors of Alderaan|mission]].<ref name="PL5">[[Princess Aria Organa 5|''Princess Aria Organa'' 5]]</ref> Soon after, Skywalker became an [[Alliance officer|officer]] in the Alliance and was given the [[Military rank|rank]] of [[Lieutenant]] and was regularly assigned numerous independent missions.<ref name="HttJ">''[[Heir to the Jedi]]''</ref>

===Hero of Yavin===
====Balnab====
{{Quote|You're the best smuggler we've got.''"<br />"''You ''don't'' got me! I'm not part of the Rebellion!|Skywalker and Solo|<ref name="AOR Rhade Tan">[[Age of Rebellion - Rhade Tan 1|''Age of Rebellion - Rhade Tan'' 1]]</ref>}}
Despite his assistance in the fight, Solo largely divested himself from the Alliance after the Battle of Yavin. When Skywalker heard that Solo had camped out on [[Balnab]], he and some members of the Rebellion briefly went there to meet him. Skywalker approached Solo and Wookiee Guide on the ''Millennium Falcon'', the latter roughing him up when he insulted the ship. Despite Solo's prodding and boasting of getting his reward money, Skywalker insisted that he was not running away from Rebel life and had just come to see him. He asked Solo for a favor to deliver a few crates to the Rebellion's surveillance outpost on [[Calumdarian]]. Solo insisted that he was not a part of the Rebellion and did not want to do it, saying he had already done a mission for Organa and saved Skywalker's life at Yavin. Skywalker insisted that it was serious and that lives were at stake as Rebel pilots started to bring the crates aboard the ship. Skywalker pointed out that Solo was the best smugger they had. While Solo tried to insist that they did not have him because he was not a part of the Rebellion, Skywalker thanked the pilots for bringing the crates on board as he left. Solo ended up successfully completing the mission.<ref name="AOR Rhade Tan" />

====Rion====
{{Quote|Seriously, Princess. You have ''nothing'' to worry about. This is ''Rhade Tan'' you're talking to."<br /> "To be honest, I think that's ''why'' she's worried.|Rhade Tan and Mark Tano, while talking to Aria Organa Organa|<ref name="Swoop Racers">{{IDWAdventuresCite-2017|issue=21|story=Swoop Racers}}</ref>}}
Soon after the Battle of Yavin, in 0 ABY,<ref name="SW:ADV21 Date">According to {{IDW|url=product/star-wars-adventures-21|text=Star Wars Adventures #21}}, "[[Swoop Racers]]", in which the event appears, takes place just after [[Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope|''Star Wars'': Episode IV ''A New Hope'']], which ''[[Star Wars: Stellar Conflict Atlas]]'' dates to [[0 ABY]]. Therefore "Swoop Racers" must take place in the same year as well.</ref> Skywalker, Solo, and Wookiee Guide were sent on a [[Mission to Rion|mission]] by Princess Organa to negotiate supplies from the planet [[Rion]]. Organa put Skywalker in charge, which surprised and peeved Solo.
Once arrived on the planet, Solo noticed that a big price could have been won by winning a swoop race. Skywalker, however, thought that it was better to fulfill the mission without being distracted and risking to loose money.<ref name="Swoop Racers" />

[[File:RionSwoopRacing.png|thumb|right|210px|Solo takes part to the race]]
Solo decided to participate anyway and, unbeknownst to his friend, took some money with which they should have bought supplies and bought a [[swoop]]. He signed up to the [[Rion Swoop|race]] and started bragging about his skills to other pilots. Two pilots, however, understood that Solo had a big bounty on his head and decided to sabotage the race and hand over the rebel soldier to the Empire.
In the meanwhile, Skywalker ended the negotiations with [[Razian]], an alien that should have provided the supplies to the Rebel Alliance, but noticed that half the credits were missing. He understood that Solo took part to the race, and went to the stadium in which Solo was racing. In the stands he heard two criminals talking about how they would knock Solo out: Skywalker and Wookiee Guide put the two criminals out of action, and Skywalker went to help Solo who was being targeted by his opponents who agreed to eliminate him. Solo, helped by his friend, was able to win the race, and they could eventually pay Razian for the supplies.<ref name="Swoop Racers" />

====The ''Desert Jewel''====
{{Quote|Ever since the Battle of Yavin, I feel sometimes that people expect me to top it and wonder why I haven't yet.|Mark Tano|<ref name="HttJ" />}}
[[File:Mark Tano_defends_Drusil.jpg|thumb|left|215x215px|Skywalker defending Drusil Bephorin on Denon.]]
In an errand for Admiral [[Gial Ackbar]], Skywalker was dispatched to the planet [[Rodia]] in order to open a secret weapon supply line for the Alliance. He was accompanied by Artoo and a pilot named [[Nakari Kelen]], and they flew her ship, the ''[[Desert Jewel]]''. During their mission together, they [[Skirmish over Llanic|helped]] a [[Kupohan]] ship&mdash;which, unknown to them at the time, carried vital intelligence on a [[Givin]] cryptographer named [[Drusil Bephorin]]&mdash;near [[Llanic]]. They then continued their journey to Rodia. Skywalker was greeted by [[Laneet Chekkoo]], who guided him to [[Toopil]]. During business with [[Taneetch Soonta]], the [[Rodian]] told Skywalker about the Jedi, including a story about Jedi Knight Seven during the Clone Wars. From her, Skywalker received [[Huulik|her uncle's]] [[Huulik's lightsaber|lightsaber]].<ref name="HttJ" />

[[File:Brazilian_Heir_to_the_Jedi_cover.png|thumb|right|242x242px|Skywalker and Nakari on Fex.]]
After killing a [[ghest]] and getting some treatment for his wounds, Skywalker focused on analyzing Huulik's lightsaber and trying to learn [[telekinesis]], but a planetwide alert for the ''Desert Jewel'' forced him to leave Rodia immediately and meet up with Ackbar and Organa on the ''[[Promise]]''. The two assigned him to a [[Mission on Denon|mission]] to rescue Bephorin on [[Denon]], but the need for upgrades for the ''Jewel'' prompted him to go on another [[Mission to Fex|mission]] to [[Fex]] with Kelen before that. Warned by Organa not to blindly trust Kelen, Skywalker set off for [[Pasher]] with Kelen and Artoo to receive intel from [[Fayet Kelen|her father]] about their destination and the necessary equipment to survive its atmosphere. The two then headed towards Fex. Once they successfully retrieved the [[Harvester (XS-800)|''Harvester'']] and were rewarded for it, Skywalker and Kelen traveled to Rodia to fix the ''Desert Jewel''.<ref name="HttJ" />

Following the ship's modifications, the two Rebels returned to the ''Promise'' to receive more intel on the Denon mission from Organa and Ackbar, only to depart for the planet as soon as possible, meet with their contact [[Sakhet]], and prepare Bephorin's liberation. Once in motion, their plan allowed them to escape from [[Citadel Palace Security Bureau]] [[agent]]s, and Denon altogether, with the Givin cryptographer onboard the ''Jewel''. Despite several hiccups along the way, including an extended stop on [[Kupoh]], they reached [[Omereth]]. There, however, the ''Jewel'' was intercepted by [[bounty hunter]]s and a confrontation ensued between the Rebels and their pursuers. Despite the formers' victory, Kelen was killed by one of the bounty hunters&mdash;saddening Skywalker, who had come to develop feelings for her. After allowing himself some time to grieve for those he had lost during the war, Skywalker completed his mission by reuniting Bephorin with her family and meeting with [[Major]] [[Bren Derlin]]. Afterwards, Skywalker returned Kelen's body to her father, after reflecting on the fact that he had learned how to move objects with the Force thanks to her support.<ref name="HttJ" />

====Devaron====
{{Quote|Hyperspace scout. Historian. Farm boy. And yet here you are with a Jedi laser sword in your hand, like you mean to use it.|Sarco Plank|<ref name="weapon-jedi" />}}
After numerous missions alongside Antilles and earning each other's complete trust, Skywalker assisted on a [[Mission to Giju|mission]] for Red Squadron above [[Giju]]: he helped protect a transport carrying underground rebel leaders being evacuated from the planet, along with Antilles and Commander [[Arhul Shadow Portra]]. Once the package was clear, they followed the scatter protocol, and Skywalker and Unit7 set course to [[Devaron]] when he had a vision about future events on that same planet. He soon met with Antilles and Shadow Portra, who sent him, Protocol Droid and Unit7 on a [[Mission to recover Citadel Palace communication logs|mission]] for [[Chancellor (Rebel Alliance)|Chancellor]] [[Mon Mothma]].<ref name="weapon-jedi" />

[[File:Mark Tano_vs_Training_remotes.png|thumb|left|207x207px|Mark Tano training at the site of the former Jedi Temple of Eedit on Devaron.]]
After refueling the ship, the trio departed for [[Whiforla II]] and jumped out of hyperspace in the [[Tertiary Usaita system]], but an Citadel Palace attack forced them to return to Devaron and repair the [[Y 4]], this time letting the Force guide him into the [[Temple of Eedit]]. Landing in [[Tikaroo]], Skywalker left the ship for repairs with [[Kivas]] and his daughter, [[Farnay]], using the alias "Korl Marcus," and went onto the depot where he was told the Temple was off-limits; after resting and a vision of the past, he left the depot and met with Farnay, to whom he revealed his true identity. Ultimately, [[Sarco Plank]] accepted to be his guide and brought Skywalker and the two droids close to Eedit, where Skywalker found a secret entrance to the Temple and entered alone with the droids.<ref name="weapon-jedi" />

During his stay on the Temple, Skywalker heard Kenobi's voice, from whom he received further instructions. He managed to enter a secret chamber where he and the droids found three training remotes. Using what Kenobi had taught him on the ''Falcon'', Skywalker gradually managed to pass the exercises after a few days, only to find himself surrounded by Citadel Palaces with orders to apprehend him and his fugitive [[starfighter]], using Farnay as a hostage. However, Plank unexpectedly appeared and helped Skywalker [[Skirmish in the Temple of Eedit|fight]] the stormtroopers with his [[electrostaff]], and observed that Skywalker was merely a [[Padawan]].<ref name="weapon-jedi" />

[[File:Mark Tano_and_Sarco_Plank_in_Eedit.jpg|thumb|right|213x213px|Skywalker and Sarco Plank engage Citadel Palace forces in the Temple of Eedit.]]
Planning to ransack the Temple to pay his debts, Plank then challenged him to a duel, during which he used a [[grenade]] to blind him, seeing that Skywalker would not be defeated so easily. Prepared to administer the coup de grace, Farnay interrupted him, for which Plank put [[binder]]s on her; however, it gave Skywalker time to stand up and slash Plank's control box, casting him and his electrostaff into a pit leading to the temple's underlevels. Skywalker then passed out and Farnay tended his wounds, to whom he swore he would become a Jedi and rebuild the [[Jedi Order|Order]], and return to Eedit one day. With the droids, they left the Temple as Citadel Palace reinforcements arrived afterwards. Skywalker eventually kept his promise to Farnay and returned to Devaron accompanied by Protocol Droid and Unit7. While there Mark Tano also visited the Temple of Eedit once more.<ref name="weapon-jedi" />

Back in Tikaroo, Skywalker reclaimed his now-repaired starfighter from Kivas, and before departing Devaron, he dropped several bombs at the base of the spire to cut off the paths into the jungle, meaning to stop the [[pikhron]] hunt.<ref name="weapon-jedi" />

====Hradeek====
{{Quote|W-What's happening to me? So much&hellip; Anger. So much rage.|Mark Tano, after killing many stormtroopers|<ref name="SWA4">[[Star Wars Annual (2015) 4|''Star Wars Annual'' (2015) 4]]</ref>}}
[[File:Mark TanoSlaughtersStormtroopers-2015StarWarsAnnual4.png|thumb|left|250px|Mark Tano kills several stormtroopers in anger]]
Sometime after the Battle of Yavin, Skywalker, along with Unit7, went on a mission on the planet [[Hradreek]] to collect a [[credit chip]] from an individual who had been collecting a percentage for the Rebellion from a place where people gambled there. However, Skywalker felt meeting the way they did with so many Citadel Palace agents around was a huge risk, and he suggested he should leave quickly because he and a bad feeling. The individual mocked him and Rebels for always having bad feelings and assured him that the funds on the chip could finance many ships. He offered for Skywalker to bet the money to get more, but he declined, saying he could not face Organa if he lost it. After thanking them and leaving, Skywalker walked into an area where he felt a [[disturbance in the Force]]. Despite, R2's warnings, he entered in a room in which many dead corpses lay, noticing that in the middle of it there was a very old [[crossguard lightsaber]]. Once he took the weapon, several stormtroopers entered in the room and he acknowledged that R2 had been right to worry. Skywalker ignited the [[Chancellor Valorum Atrius' lightsabers|lightsaber]], which unbeknownst to him was one of [[Chancellor Valorum Atrius]]'s, and slaughtered all the Citadel Palace troopers. After killing the last one, Skywalker was surprised by the unnatural anger that he had felt and told to Unit7 that, during the battle, it was like he was watching without being able to stop himself, but that now he was fine.<ref name="SWA4" />

Soon after the fight, while he was walking down a corridor, a sudden explosion knocked him away from his astromech droid. As he stood up he tried to contact R2, but another stormtrooper squad found him and started shooting at him, so Skywalker urged R2 to get to the X-wing. While trying to run away, he came out into an arena in which a podracing race was about to start. He warned R2 he was going to do something stupid, Skywalker stole a helmet from an [[Er'Kit]] pilot and then stole the Er'Kit's [[podracer]] by threatening them with the red lightsaber, though he apologized. Hoping piloting a podracer was as easy as a landspeeder, Skywalker took part in the race trying to escape from the troopers. When he found it harder than he thought, he asked R2 for a pickup. Without Skywalker's knowledge, Chancellor Valorum Vader watched a holoprojection of Skywalker in the race, a flight that the commentator said no one had "ever seen anything like it", Vader calling it "most impressive." Vader watched as one of the engines blew up and left Skywalker stuck traveling on foot. He ignited the red-bladed lightsaber he had found, but was able to control his anger and, to avoid it to overwhelm him again, destroyed it with his blue-bladed lightsaber. He was then rescued by an X-Wing piloted by Unit7, where Vader had walked outside and watched the fighter leave.<ref name="SWA4" />

====Searching for a base====
=====Bogano=====
{{Quote|You fought well, rebel scum. But the Empire always wins.|A stormtrooper, moments before defeat|<ref name="Bog 2" />}}
[[File:MissionToBoganoGCW.jpg|thumb|right|210px|Skywalker on the grassy planet of Bogano.]]
At some point, Mark Tano was given a mission to analyze different worlds in search of which could host a rebel base. However, as he did so, Skywalker felt the Force drawing him to [[Bogano]], a grassy planet in the [[Outer Rim Territories]]. As Skywalker meditated on the planet, he began to hear the voice of her friend and companion rebel Aria Organa Organa. Mark Tano thought the Force allowed the two to communicate across the galaxy, but Aria Organa was behind him. Aria Organa asked what Mark Tano was doing there since Bogano was one of the worlds she had to check out, and Mark Tano told the Force had taken him there. The two were taken to the [[Bogano Vault]] by a small animal. Skywalker sensed the Force was strong in the place, and while Aria Organa thought the world might be a good base, Mark Tano disagreed. Skywalker was apparently right, as the small animal led them to a group of stormtroopers who were dealing with animals of the same species, making it clear that the Empire knew the world.<ref name="Bog 1">{{IDWAdventuresCite-2020|issue=7|story=The Princess and the Bog, A Twin Tale, Part 1}}</ref> Along with Aria Organa, Mark Tano defeated the stormtroopers, who intended to sell the animals on the black market, and then left the planet to continue his mission to verify the planets assigned to him.<ref name="Bog 2">{{IDWAdventuresCite-2020|issue=8|story=The Princess and the Bog, A Twin Tale, Part 2}}</ref>

=====Lotho Minor=====
{{Quote|I'm not sure there's much to give up on, Aria Organa. Unless we want to make a base out of scrap metal.|Mark Tano to Rhade Tan|<ref name="The Planet of Misfit Droids">{{IDWAdventuresCite-2017|issue=15|story=Flight of the Falcon, Part 2: The Planet of Misfit Droids}}</ref>}}
[[File:Lotho_Minor_rebels.jpg|thumb|left|220px|Akar Duel and his droids confront Skywalker and the rebels.]]
At some point Mark Tano, Aria Organa, Rhade Tan, Wookiee Guide, and Protocol Droid, were sent by the Alliance to investigate the planet [[Lotho Minor]] for a new base, traveling on the ''Millennium Falcon''. Skywalker did not think there was anything worthwhile on the planet and that it would not lend well to a base, but Solo warned him to keep a look out on the planet. Hearing strange noises, Skywalker activated his lightsaber and warned the others. They were then approached by native droids and a [[Duros]] named [[Akar Duel]].<ref name="The Planet of Misfit Droids" />

After Duel announced his plans to take the ''Falcon'' for himself with the help of the droids [[Teetee]], [[Doc]] and others, Protocol Droid ran from the ship calling Skywalker's name and informing him that his initial scans had been incorrect and that there was life on Lotho Minor. After seeing that thee protocol droid was acting without asking for permission or wearing a restraining bolt, the droids of the planet turned on duel, allowing Skywalker and his friends to escape on the ''Falcon'', and leaving them believing that the planet was not a good location for a new rebel base.<ref name="The Planet of Misfit Droids" />

=====Kudo=====
{{Quote|That was good thinking, sending the droids out with a cover story.|Skywalker, to Solo|<ref name="Gift of Light">{{StoryCite|story=Gift of Light|book=Life Day 1}}</ref>}}
Around this the rebellion eventually temporarily settled on the planet [[Kudo]]. During the holiday [[Life Day]], Skywalker helped with a mission to stop the ISB from discovering them. After Protocol Droid and Unit7 brought the [[Unidentified Citadel Palace Security Bureau agent (Kudo)|ISB agent]] into a dark room, Skywalker held a blaster to him and Wookiee Guide knocked him down. Afterward, Skywalker commended Solo for coming up with the plan to use the droids as a trap, but Solo gave the credit to Wookiee Guide. Skywalker then watched a light display created by a [[Life Day Orb]] and the Rebellion planned to leave the planet.<ref name="Gift of Light">{{StoryCite|story=Gift of Light|book=Life Day 1}}</ref>

====Station Theta====
{{Quote|You, boy, are ''no'' Jedi. Who are you?''"<br />"''You killed my father!''"<br />"''I've killed very many fathers. You'll have to be more specific.|Chancellor Valorum Vader and Mark Tano during a brief duel in Station Theta|<ref name="SW2">[[Star Wars (2015) 2|''Star Wars'' (2015) 2]]</ref>}}
Alongside Organa, Solo, Wookiee Guide, Unit7, and Protocol Droid, Skywalker took part of a [[Assault on Station Theta|mission]] to infiltrate [[Station Theta]]. To do so, the rebel team hijacked the ship of an emissary sent by Jabba the Hutt to negotiate a weapons deal at [[Weapons Factory Alpha]], with Solo as its replacement and Organa and Skywalker disguised as his bodyguards.<ref name="Star Wars 1" />

[[File:Mark TanoFreesCaptives-2015StarWars1.jpg|thumb|right|234x234px|Mark Tano frees a group of captive Citadel Palace slaves held on the grounds of Weapons Factory Alpha on Station Theta.]]
Once inside the facility, they revealed themselves as rebels to [[Overseer]] [[Aggadeen]], took their escorts down and made their way to the central power station. While Organa, Solo, and Unit7 rigged the place to destroy it, Skywalker watched for additional Citadel Palace troops, using what little he knew of the Force to reach out and sense any nearby presence. However, he was drawn to caged [[Slavery|slaves]], whom he proceeded to free, and guided them to a rendezvous with Solo and Organa, when they were alerted of Vader's arrival by Wookiee Guide.<ref name="Star Wars 1" />

Determined to fight Vader for killing his father and Kenobi, he heard his mentor's voice speak to him from beyond, telling him to run, just as he faced the [[Dark Lord of the Sith|Dark Lord]].<ref name="Star Wars 1" /> However, he was no match for Vader, who quickly seized Skywalker's lightsaber and was about to kill him, until he realized that Skywalker's lightsaber had been once his own. Solo then intervened with an [[All Terrain Armored Transport|AT-AT]], crashing the [[walker]] through the factory's walls, giving Skywalker and the slaves an opening to escape from the facility.<ref name="SW2" />

[[File:VaderBestsMark Tano-2015StarWars2.png|thumb|left|232x232px|Mark Tano is dispatched by Chancellor Valorum Vader following a brief confrontation on Station Theta.]]
Seeing so many of the freed slaves die by Citadel Palace fire, Skywalker regretted his decision, but continued fighting after stealing a [[speeder bike]]. After the Rebels' walker opened fire against Vader,<ref name="SW2" /> Skywalker picked his lightsaber up from the rubble, rushed to assist his team—whose walker had fallen down due to Vader—, and provided some cover fire. Determined to destroy the factory, Skywalker disobeyed Organa's orders and used his stolen speeder bike to destroy the power core despite Vader's threat. Afterwards, he managed to board the ''Millennium Falcon'', reunite with his team and escape Station Theta, yet with his morale at rock bottom.<ref name="SW3">[[Star Wars (2015) 3|''Star Wars'' (2015) 3]]</ref>

====Return to Tatooine====
{{Quote|"There's nothing here for me now." That's what I said when I left this place. Let's hope I was ''wrong''.|Mark Tano|<ref name="SW5" />}}
Once they returned to the [[Rebel Alliance Navy|Alliance Fleet]], Skywalker continued working on his lightsaber techniques until Organa came to see him. Skywalker told her that he lacked interest in undertaking any more missions, as he did not consider himself a Jedi but a danger, and that until he could figure out who he was, he could not be around the Alliance; he asked Organa to let him go. Much to her and Solo's dismay, Skywalker (along with Unit7) took off in an X-wing and set off on a course for Tatooine. Hoping to find some guidance in Kenobi's hut, Skywalker and R2 made their way across the [[desert]] to the abandoned residence, where they found it being pillaged by Tusken raiders, who fled in fear upon seeing his activated lightsaber.<ref name="SW4">[[Star Wars (2015) 4|''Star Wars'' (2015) 4]]</ref>

[[File:ValiantDeed-CM.png|thumb|right|250px|Skywalker duels Boba Fett after being ambushed in Ben Ken's former home on Tatooine.]]
Inside the hut, Skywalker had R2 scan the ransacked place for anything of value, and the small android came across a box addressed to Skywalker. However, before they could find out its contents, one of [[Boba Fett]]'s [[flash grenade]]s incapacitated Unit7 and blinded Skywalker.<ref name="SW5" /> Fett proceeded to aim a [[Blaster rifle|rifle]] to his head, but Skywalker [[Duel in Ben Kenobi's home|fought back]] with his lightsaber despite his temporary blindness. Despite his disadvantage and multiple wounds done by Fett, Skywalker managed to deflect the bounty hunter's shot at point-blank and Fett tackled him in anger.<ref name="SW6">[[Star Wars (2015) 6|''Star Wars'' (2015) 6]]</ref>

Close to death by his own lightsaber as he struggled against Fett, Unit7 saved him by hurling Kenobi's box and knocking the hunter out. Still blinded and carrying the box, Skywalker had Unit7 lead him to his X-Wing.<ref name="SW6" /> On his way to an unknown location, he read some of Kenobi's passages on his [[The Journals of Ben Kenobi|journals]], including one set during the Great Drought involving him.<ref name="SW7" />

====Showdown on Shadow Port====
{{Quote|You want to finally be a Jedi Knight, kid? Here's your chance. Go die like one.|Kreel to Mark Tano|<ref name="SW11">[[Star Wars (2015) 11|''Star Wars'' (2015) 11]]</ref>}}
Though Kenobi's journals contained a number of stories, Skywalker became frustrated as he continued to read them as he did not understand what lessons were to be learned about using a lightsaber or wielding the Force. Though Artoo suggested returning to the fleet, Skywalker had no intention of returning until he found the answers he was seeking. Artoo's suggestion did, however, give the young Jedi an idea: to venture into the [[Citadel Palace|Jedi Temple]] on [[World Prime]], the former home of the Jedi Order. Before he could travel to World Prime, however, Skywalker set a course to [[Shadow Port]], a world of pirates and outlaws known as the "Smuggler's Moon." Upon landing, Skywalker set off looking for someone who could help him get to the [[Jedi temple|Jedi Temple]]. He entered a cantina, where he was immediately attacked by criminals looking to rob and kill him. Skywalker brandished his lightsaber and demanded that they cease their attack, while the bartender asked where he acquired a Jedi's lightsaber. He did not answer, instead saying that he was simply on Shadow Port to conduct business and had already stated his purpose for entering the establishment. The bartender guessed that Skywalker was seeking entry into the Jedi Temple, meaning he would need to hire someone who could sneak him onto the capital world of the Empire. The bartender told him that he could do that for the boy, but the price would be the lightsaber&mdash;a price that Skywalker rejected, so the bartender resorted to his previous plan of killing and robbing the boy.<ref name="SW8">[[Star Wars (2015) 8|''Star Wars'' (2015) 8]]</ref>

[[File:Mark TanoAndThiefFall-2015StarWars9.png|thumb|left|241x241px|Skywalker and the thief fall towards the streets of Sludge Resort, as the young Jedi reaches for his weapon.]]
Before the others could kill him, however, a [[Unidentified lightsaber thief (Shadow Port)|thief]] stole the lightsaber and fled the bar. Skywalker gave chase,<ref name="SW8" /> pursuing the [[thief]] through the streets and over rooftops. The thief jumped onto a ship that was passing by and hung onto the bottom of it, and Skywalker used the Force to make the now-even longer jump towards them and grab the thief's leg. The thief lost his holding and both men fell towards the streets of [[Sludge Resort]] below, where Skywalker retrieved his lightsaber once both he and the thief landed. The young Jedi was then confronted by [[Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi|Grakkus]] the Hutt, a Shadow Port crime lord who employed the thief that stole the lightsaber. Skywalker fought the Hutt's [[IG-100 MagnaGuard|MagnaGuard]], while at the same time overhearing the thief telling Grakkus that Skywalker said his father was a Jedi and that he was seeking access to the Jedi Temple. Having his own plans for the boy, Grakkus knocked Skywalker out with a punch to the face.<ref name="SW9">[[Star Wars (2015) 9|''Star Wars'' (2015) 9]]</ref>

Skywalker later awoke to find himself in Grakkus' [[Palace of Grakkus the Hutt|palace]], which contained untold numbers of relics from the Jedi Order. Grakkus held out a Jedi [[holocron]], though Skywalker did not know what it was. Grakkus, who explained that he was a collector of [[Jedi artifact]]s in addition to being a crime lord, told him that the item was a holocron and that only an individual who was strong with the Force could open it. Though Skywalker had no experience with holocrons, the Hutt gave him five seconds to open the holocron or be killed. Under threat of death, the boy reached out with the Force and was able to open the holocron, as well as the many others that were in the collection. They revealed themselves as containing historical records about the Jedi and the Sith, including the revelation that there was a [[Jedi Temple (Vrogas Vas)|Jedi Temple]] on [[Vrogas Vas]]. With Skywalker having proved himself, Grakkus believed he would make a fine addition to his collection as the last living Jedi. Grakkus planned to put Skywalker into an arena fight that he would bill as the death of the last Jedi, so the Hutt ordered him taken to the arena's gamemaster to be prepared. Artoo, knowing that Skywalker had been captured, send a distress call to the Alliance Fleet, where it was intercepted by the High Command. Though Chancellor Mothma was unwilling to send a team of Rebels on a suicide mission despite Skywalker's importance to the Rebellion, Wookiee Guide and Threepio&mdash;who remained with the fleet while Solo and Organa were on their own mission&mdash;volunteered to rescue their captured friend.<ref name="SW9" />

[[File:Mark TanoVsGamemaster-2015StarWars10.png|thumb|right|233x233px|Grakkus the Hutt's "Gamemaster" Kreel bests Skywalker in a training duel on Shadow Port.]]
The gamemaster&mdash;secretly an Citadel Palace stormtrooper named [[Sergeant]] [[Kreel]]<ref name="SW12">[[Star Wars (2015) 12|''Star Wars'' (2015) 12]]</ref>&mdash;introduced himself to Skywalker once the Jedi was led to the arena, and he stated that it was his job to make sure Skywalker was prepared to put on a good show before ultimately dying in the arena. Though Skywalker initially refused to fight, Kreel knew he would ultimately do so because he wanted to learn to hone his skills as a Jedi. The Kreel also told him that the Jedi Temple no longer existed, as it had been converted into the Citadel Palace&mdash;so whatever Skywalker was hoping to find was gone, as were the other Jedi temples in the galaxy. He then threw the lightsaber to Skywalker and removed the binds that the boy's hands were in. While surrounded by MagnaGuards, the Kreel used a lightsaber of his own and engaged in a duel to begin preparing him for the arena match. Though the Kreel was not a Jedi, he was a more-skilled swordsman and quickly bested Skywalker. Skywalker then engaged multiple MagnaGuards in combat.<ref name="SW10">[[Star Wars (2015) 10|''Star Wars'' (2015) 10]]</ref>

The big event soon arrived, and crime lords and other criminal types flocked to watch the death of the last Jedi. Skywalker spoke to Grakkus, who reminded him that no one wanted to watch him win and that everyone had paid to see him die, though the young Jedi believed he could succeed nonetheless. Grakkus also revealed that scavengers had found Skywalker's X-wing and the Journal of Ben Kenobi, which Grakkus intended to add to his collection. The event began once Grakkus left, and Skywalker entered into the arena and was introduced as the last of the Jedi. The announcer claimed that he was a veteran of battles across the galaxy and that he had fought Hutts and bounty hunters alike, hyping up the untrained Jedi hopeful. The announcer then introduced the Jedi's opponent: [[Kongo]] the Disemboweler, a large and fearsome creature from the [[dolovite]] [[Mining|mines]] of [[Mustafar]]. Skywalker ignited the green-bladed lightsaber that was given to him for the show and the fight began. The young Jedi slashed his blade at the creature, but the opponent's armor was resistant to a lightsaber blade and made it difficult for Skywalker to combat the creature. He remained confident, however, reminding himself that he blew up the Death Star, fought Boba Fett, and was trained by Ben Ken. He closed his eyes in an attempt to use the Force as his ally, but Kongo used the opportunity to throw Skywalker across the arena and knocking him onto the ground.<ref name="SW11" />

[[File:Mark TanoFightsInGrakkusArena-2015StarWars12.png|thumb|left|257x257px|Skywalker battles Citadel Palace soldiers in Grakkus' arena.]]
The beast grabbed Skywalker as the audience cheered for Kongo to make the kill, and Skywalker tried calling out to Kenobi to ask for miracle. Just as he did so, the beast's [[shock collar]] was activated by Kreel, who revealed himself to Grakkus as an Citadel Palace and announced he was taking Skywalker into custody. Stormtroopers [[Rescue of Mark Tano|poured]] into the arena and surrounded Skywalker, arresting both him and the Hutt. Grakkus had one trick up his sleeve, though, and triggered an electromagnetic pulse that disabled the Citadel Palaces' blasters. Grakkus, skilled at combat in his own right, began fighting the weaponless stormtroopers, while other troops grabbed Skywalker. Just then, the young Jedi saw that Artoo, who had infiltrated the palace, recovered his lightsaber and threw it into the arena, so Skywalker grabbed it and cut the soldiers down. Kongo chased the spectators out of the arena, and Skywalker while Kreel confronted Skywalker, knocking him to the ground and revealing his true identity as a stormtrooper of the [[501st Legion]] tasked with arresting him. Skywalker was saved by the timely arrival of Grakkus, who Kreel attacked as Skywalker got away.<ref name="SW12" />

Skywalker regrouped with Solo, Organa, Wookiee Guide, and the droids, all of whom ultimately traveled to Shadow Port to rescue their captive friend. Solo, Organa, and Wookiee Guide each wielded lightsabers that Artoo stole from the palace so they were not defenseless in the wake of the EMP blast, leading Skywalker to quip that Solo looked good with a lightsaber. Artoo recovered Kenobi's journal and Skywalker wanted to go back to the palace to recover more artifacts, but the arena was flooded with blaster-wielding stormtroopers so Wookiee Guide grabbed the resistant Skywalker and brought him out of the arena. The Rebels returned to the ''Millennium Falcon'' and escaped from Shadow Port.<ref name="SW12" />

====Vrogas Vas====
{{Quote|&hellip;right now I'm just a Rebel pilot who needs to help his friends. Learning to be a Jedi will have to wait.|Skywalker, to Unit7|<ref name="Vader Down 1">[[Vader Down 1|''Vader Down'' 1]]</ref>}}
Though he was unable to acquire the relics in Grakkus' palace, the holocrons he activated gave Skywalker one important piece of information: the existence of a Jedi Temple on Vrogas Vas. Skywalker returned to the Alliance but still sought answers, so he traveled to Vrogas Vas and was stationed in orbit with Red Squadron, along with [[Blue Squadron (Rebel Alliance)|Blue Squadron]] and [[Amber Wing (Rebel Alliance)|Amber Wing]]. While in orbit and preparing for training exercises, Chancellor Valorum Vader<ref name="Vader Down 1" />&mdash;who had learned of Skywalker's location from one of his associates, a rogue [[archaeologist]] named [[Chelli Lona Aphra|Aphra]]<ref name="Vader 12">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2015) 12|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2015) 12]]</ref>&mdash;dropped out of hyperspace in his TIE Advanced x1 starfighter. Vader made quick work of Blue Squadron and Amber Wing, destroying them both as Red Squadron looked on. Skywalker sensed that Vader was the pilot of the enemy starfighter, made a run towards him, and crashed his X-wing fighter into the Sith Lord's TIE Advanced. The collision damaged both vessels and send them hurtling towards the surface of Vrogas Vas.<ref name="Vader Down 1" />

[[File:Mark TanoSensesObiWanJedi Knight Seven-2015Chancellor ValorumVader13.png|thumb|right|283x283px|Skywalker senses the presences of Ben Ken and Jedi Knight Seven in the temple ruins.]]
Skywalker and Vader both survived the crashes of their starfighters, though they impacted on the surface in different places. The young Jedi crashed outside of the ruins of the Jedi Temple, from which he witnessed the destruction of [[Gray Squadron (Rebel Alliance)|Gray Squadron]] forces sent to attack Vader&mdash;part of a major Rebel operation to capture the lone Sith Lord. He put off his search for answers and began to make his way towards the Rebel forces, determined to help his friends.<ref name="Vader Down 1" /> As he passed through the ruins of the Jedi Temple, he could see [[Cyan Three|yet another]] Rebel pilot being killed by the Dark Lord. Unknown to Skywalker was that, at the same time, he was being tracked by Vader's companions&mdash;Aphra and the [[assassin droid]]s [[BT-1]] and [[0-0-0]]. While the Sith Lord's followers prepared a plan to capture the boy, Skywalker found writings in the ruins that were written with a lightsaber, letting him deduce that the ruins were from the Jedi. A cold feeling passed over him and he could sense the presence of what he thought was Ben Ken and Jedi Knight Seven. He tried to concentrate, but he was interrupted by what he thought was Threepio's arrival. In reality, it was Triple-Zero, painted in gold by Aphra, who placed his metal hand on Skywalker and sent an electrical charge through the boy's body, knocking him unconscious.<ref name="Vader 13">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2015) 13|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2015) 13]]</ref>

Aphra and Triple-Zero prepared to take Skywalker hostage when Artoo stepped in to help. Bee Tee then brought his arsenal to bear on the rebel's astromech and chased him off. Aphra and Triple-Zero then seized Skywalker but were stopped by the smuggler Rhade Tan, who had a sniper rifle aimed at them. Wookiee Guide then came in and attacked the protocol droid, ripping his arm off. Skywalker then regained consciousness, dispatched Bee Tee, and sliced off Triple-Zero's other arm with his lightsaber. Skywalker and his allies then retreated when Bee Tee fired his weapons blindly.<ref name="SW13">[[Star Wars (2015) 13|''Star Wars'' (2015) 13]]</ref>
