Skywalker, Solo, Wookiee Guide, and Artoo made their way back to the Millennium Falcon. They then lifted off in order to aid princess Aria Organa. They were forced to the ground when their ship was crashed into by the Wookiee bounty hunter Black Krrsantan. While Solo and Wookiee Guide dealt with the mercenary, Skywalker left to head back to the Jedi ruins.<ref name="DV14">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2015) 14|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2015) 14]]</ref>

Mark Tano arrived back at the the Jedi temple looking for Aria Organa. It was then that he heard the voice of Ben Ken, who told him that he should not have come to this place and that he was not ready for what is coming. Mark Tano was then intercepted by a company of stormtroopers who opened fire on him. He retreated behind cover but was hit in the head and knocked unconscious.<ref name="SW14">[[Star Wars (2015) 14|''Star Wars'' (2015) 14]]</ref>

Mark Tano was taken prisoner by the forces of Commander [[Karbin]]. However Chancellor Valorum Vader, who had a rivalry with Karbin, used the force to crash the shuttle Skywalker was kept in. Now free, he then caught up with Solo, Wookiee Guide, Protocol Droid, and Unit7. They made their way back to the Millennium Falcon, however Dr. Aphra had laid out a minefield to stop them. When she was distracted she was knocked out from behind by Princess Aria Organa. Believing her to be of use, Organa decided to take the archaeologist with them. As they departed Vrogas Vas, Skywalker felt remorse that he would not be able to go back to the temple and see what was hidden there.<ref name="DV15">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2015) 15|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2015) 15]]</ref>

====Learning the ways of the smuggler====
{{Quote|How else are we gonna replace the money we just lost?''"<br />"''Heh, don't worry, kid. I know just the thing. It's a big galaxy. And believe me, there's always something somewhere in need of smuggling.|Skywalker and Solo|<ref name="SW16">[[Star Wars (2015) 16|''Star Wars'' (2015) 16]]</ref>}}
[[File:SkywalkerSoloAndNerfs-2015StarWars18.png|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker and Solo deliver nerfs on Ibaar.]]
Upon returning to the Rebel fleet with their new prisoner, Doctor Aphra, Skywalker and his friends went their separate ways; Organa, Artoo, and Threepio went to detain Aphra at an Alliance-controlled space station, [[Sunspot Prison]], with the assistance of [[Sana Starros]], whom Organa hired to transport them to the prison. Meanwhile, Solo and Skywalker were dispatched to buy supplies for the rebellion. Solo attempted to double the money he was given for supplies by betting on [[sabacc]]. However, he was caught cheating, and had to escape with Skywalker on the ''Millennium Falcon''.<ref name="SW16" />

Skywalker and Solo traveled to Shadow Port where Mark Tano was tasked with finding a customer in need of a ship. He made a deal to haul [[nerf]]s to [[Ibaar]] for 5,000 credits, which was just enough to replace the credits lost by Solo. Skywalker and Solo were soon intercepted by TIE fighters who suspected the Falcon of smuggling illegal livestock.<ref name="SW17">[[Star Wars (2015) 17|''Star Wars'' (2015) 17]]</ref> Mark Tano was able to shoot the fighters and he and Solo made it to Ibaar with the nerfs. While on Ibaar, Skywalker blackmailed Solo into allowing him to fly the Falcon for a few parsecs by threatening to tell Aria Organa about losing the credits in a Sabacc game.<ref name="SW18">[[Star Wars (2015) 18|''Star Wars'' (2015) 18]]</ref>

After buying the supplies, Skywalker and Solo received a distress call from Sana and arrived at Sunspot Prison. They were immediately knocked out and taken captive by the [[Eneb Ray|masked assailant]] who was attacking the prison. Neither came to until after the battle had already ended and the attacker had been captured.<ref name="SW19">[[Star Wars (2015) 19|''Star Wars'' (2015) 19]]</ref>

====Temporary outpost====
{{Quote|I just go word that the cargo vessel just arrived. Looks like the mission was canceled. Hope you didn't go through too much trouble.|Mark Tano to Unit7|<ref name="Droid Dilemma">{{StoryCite|story=Droid Dilemma|book=Star Wars (2015) 25}}</ref>}}
Sometime after the assault on Sunspot Prison, the Alliance established a temporary [[LX-Robynsun V|outpost]] on the Outer Rim planet [[Reamma]]. Organa gave Mark Tano a mission to find a missing Alliance cargo vessel. Skywalker and Unit7 prepared to make the flight to look for them. Before they could do that, however, Organa informed Skywalker that the vessel reported in, cancelling the mission.<ref name="Droid Dilemma" />

====Hijacking the ''Harbinger''====
{{Quote|Chances are...This is the last voyage of the ''Harbinger''. So let's make it a memorable one.|Skywalker to Organa and Solo|<ref name="Star Wars (2015) 22">[[Star Wars (2015) 22|''Star Wars'' (2015) 22]]</ref>}}
Sometime later, Skywalker and Organa rendezvoused with rebel leadership. Admiral Ackbar, General Dodonna, and Mon Mothma presented them with the task of providing aid to the people of [[Tureen VII]], a planet that had provided aid to the rebellion in the past. A heavily blockaded planet with Citadel Palace bases on both of its moons and swarms of TIE fighters in orbit, the Alliance could not risk sending the fleet. Mark Tano and Aria Organa proposed stealing an Citadel Palace Star Destroyer and using it to infiltrate the blockade. Despite some reluctance from Dodonna, Ackbar and Mothma realized that it was the only choice left.<ref name="Star Wars 23">[[Star Wars (2015) 23|''Star Wars'' (2015) 23]]</ref>

====Skorii-Lei Rescue====
Afer the hijacking of the [[Harbinger (Citadel Palace I-class)|''Harbinger'']], Aria Organa ended up grievously injured on the planet [[Skorii-Lei]]. Cared for by former engineer [[Pash Davane]] and carrying vital Alliance information, Organa was pursued by stormtroopers and barely managed to escape aboard the ''Millennium Falcon'' with Skywalker, Solo, and Wookiee Guide. Aboard the ''Falcon'', Davane provided Skywalker with Aria Organa's data tape, which he noted was a sign of great trust between the two of them. With her place as a friend of the Alliance confirmed, Skywalker and his allies returned Davane to her home on Skorii-Lei.<ref name="Star Wars Annual 2">[[Star Wars Annual (2015) 2|''Star Wars Annual'' (2015) 2]]</ref>

====Journey to Vagadarr system====
{{Quote|You remind me of him. But more than that... you remind me of me. You... you're nothing but a frightened child, just like I was. Do you know the only thing I was good at... when I was a child? Walking away.|Garro to Skywalker|<ref name="SW30">[[Star Wars (2015) 30|''Star Wars'' (2015) 30]]</ref>}}
[[File:OldManGarro-2015StarWars30.jpg|thumb|right|250px|Skywalker worked with Garro to revive a giant of living stone.]]
Despite the escape from the ''Harbinger'', the heroes quickly realized that Protocol Droid was captured during the commotion, and Skywalker was unable to stop Unit7 from commandeering an [[X-wing starfighter|X-Wing]] to rescue the [[protocol droid]] on his own. With his own X-wing's [[hyperdrive]] temporarily disabled, he resumed reading Ben Kenobi's journal. Identifying a symbol in the journal as a [[star map]], Skywalker decided to visit the [[Vagadarr system]] after reading of a Jedi Master who had ventured there in the past and encountered enormous [[Giants of living stone|giants]] made of living stone that gave those in close proximity a power known as [[Stonepower]]. Skywalker hoped that going there would give him the knowledge he needed to save Unit7 and Protocol Droid.<ref name="SW28">[[Star Wars (2015) 28|''Star Wars'' (2015) 28]]</ref>

Like the Jedi Master before him, Skywalker was able to navigate through the [[Vagadarr Prime|planet]]'s heavy debris field and land on the surface, where he encountered [[Garro]], the last remaining native human, who initially wanted to use Skywalker's life force to kill the few remaining giant children. Determined to protect them, Skywalker inspired Garro to change his mind and sacrifice his own life force to revive a dead giant. Skywalker and the giant children then ventured into the giant's cave to find the heart of the mountain and finish what Garro started in reviving the giant, thus completing the mission of the Master from years past and taking another step in his journey to becoming a [[Jedi]].<ref name="SW30" />

====Horox III====
{{Quote|So, come, shake hands, have dinner with the nice lady, and we walk away with an actual sentient Ancient Jedi. You get your teacher, I get an eyewitness to the Ancient past." <br />"I'm not sure.." <br /> "C'mon, are you out, farm boy? Or are you in, Jedi Knight?|Aphra and Mark Tano on the visit to Ktath'atn|<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1">[[The Screaming Citadel 1|''The Screaming Citadel'' 1]]</ref>}}
[[File:HoroxIIIBar-TheScreamingCitadel1.png|thumb|left|200px|The bar on Horox III]]
Sometime later, as the Alliance was setting up a [[Horox III rebel outpost|temporary outpost]] on [[Horox III]], Skywalker went to a local [[Unidentified bar (Horox III)|bar]]. Threatened by its denizens for being a human, he was forced to defend himself against them despite his warnings that he would be able to defeat them in a fight. The fight was compounded when Doctor Aphra, who had lied to Sana Starros in order to find Skywalker, arrived and sparked the anger of the entire bar after saying Skywalker was with her, forcing Skywalker, Aphra, and Black Krrsantan to fight the entire bar. After the fight, Skywalker told Aphra he did not want her following him because he did not want to have anything to do with someone who worked for Vader, but she caught his attention by saying she knew where to find a Jedi Master.<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" />

Skywalker first refused to admit he was trying to be a Jedi, Aphra explaining that she had figured it out from Vader's vendetta and Skywalker's one-in-a-million shot to destroy the Death Star plus his general talent. She introduced him to the [[Rur Crystal|Rur crystal]] of the ancient Jedi splinter group known as the [[Ordu Aspectu]] with an ancient Jedi personality inside of it. By playing off Skywalker's hopes to be better with the Force and a true Jedi Knight, Aphra convinced an initially hesitant Mark Tano to [[Mission to Ktath'atn|visit]] the [[Citadel of Ktath'atn|Screaming Citadel]] with her, explaining that that introducing him to the [[Unidentified Queen of Ktath'atn|Queen of Ktath'atn]] as a Jedi would convince the Queen to reactive the crystal for them. On the way there, Skywalker reaquainted himself with 0-0-0 and BT-1, remembering the former for electrocuting him and the latter from R2 kicking him. Skywalker lamented not telling Solo, Organa, or Starros about where he was going, but he and Aphra both agreed they would have tried to stop them and they had no time to waste.<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" />

[[File:TemporaryRebelOutpost-TheScreamingCitadel1.png|thumb|right|250px|The temporary Rebel Outpost on Horox III.]]
Meanwhile, at the Rebel Outpost on Horox III, Solo then enlisted Starros' help in communicating with Skywalker's temporary [[R5 series astromech droid|R5]] astromech droid [[Essfour|S4]], who could only speak [[Binary]] and thus was not easily able to communicate with Organa. Organa asked the droid for Skywalker's whereabouts but the droid responded that he could not tell. Questioning the droid, Starros learned that Skywalker did not go by himself but that he went with Doctor Aphra. An unhappy Aria Organa and Solo wondered why Skywalker would go with Aphra, Organa suggesting she kidnapped Skywalker while Solo and Starros suspect she could have reprogrammed the droid to keep a secret.<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" />

====The Screaming Citadel====
=====The Queeen of Ktath'atn=====
{{Quote|I know every sort of creature you can image, Doctor. And many I'm sure you cannot. They have all been paraded through the halls of this citadel. All by people desperate to gain my favor. But never once has anyone brought me a Jedi|The Queen of Ktath'atn to Skywalker and Aphra|<ref name="SW 31">[[Star Wars (2015) 31|''Star Wars'' (2015) 31]]</ref>}}
[[File:CitadelOfKthathatn-TheScreamingCitadel1.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker journeyed to the Screaming Citadel with the hope of learning more about the Jedi.]]
After arriving on Ktath'atn, Skywalker and the others encountered a mob of villagers. Skywalker wants to help feed them and Aphra just calls him adorable and has Krrsantan scare them off. After making the trek to the the entire party, except for Krrsantan were allowed into the citadel. Skywalker was curious how Aphra met Krrsantan but she just said it was a long story and that she owed him a lot of money. Skywalker then asked how Aphra had found him. Noticing he was struggling, Aphra helped Skywalker put his [[Spavat]] on to meet the Queen, and after finished he insisted that he was more than just a farm boy. While walking toward the main hall, 0-0-0 teased Skywalker for stuttering when Aphra commented on her attractiveness but she told the droid only she was allowed to tease him.<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" />

In the ballroom, Skywalker was mesmerized by the crowd. Aphra told Skywalker to follow her lead and advised him to hide his lightsaber, but implies he is used to keeping his Jedi identity, which he hopes to solidify, a secret. When Skywalker asked about the Jedi in the crystal, Aphra said she only met him briefly but that he had strong opinions. After encountering an [[Ezaraa]]n guest, Skywalker was initially excited by them wanting to take down the Empire, but after they explained they wanted to replace it with a [[Dominion of the Ezaraa]] where they would consume the flesh of all "lesser species," Skywalker expressed that he thought the guests were crazy. The two soon saw the [[Unidentified Queen of Ktath'atn|Queen of Ktath'atn]], and after being welcomed by one of her servants, [[Varroa]], Aphra presented Skywalker, describing him as a very interesting Tatooine farm boy, but was rejected. When the Ezaraan mocked Skywalker, Aphra defended him, but the Ezaraan grabbed her arm. Skywalker warned the Ezaraan to leave Aphra alone and used the Force to throw the Ezaraan to the ground, intriguing the Queen and earning a compliment from Aphra. Varroa ordered all the guests to leave but allowed Skywalker and his companion to stay so that the Queen could hear his request in the morning, Aphra telling him he did great. Later, the Queen told her servant [[Vespinax]] that Skywalker's power and little experience made him perfect for her intentions to eat him. She then grew her power in anticipation of eating the Jedi.<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" />

The next morning, Skywalker and Aphra made their way to a dining hall to have breakfast with the Monarch. On the way, after Skywalker expressed how creepy he thought the place was, Aphra assured him that the Queen's obsession with Jedi would get her to do what they wanted, but Skwalker was worried by this because of his encounter with Grakkus the Hutt and Aphra's mention that the Queen "keeps" her oddities. Aphra told Skywalker to let her do the talking and then the two walked inside and sat at a table with the Queen, Aphra introducing the both of them. Excited to see a Jedi, but wanting more verification, the Queen commanded Skywalker to move a nearby dining tray with the Force, though he was unable to until the Queen's servant, [[Vespinax]], threatened him with a knife to his throat. However, moving the tray revealed that under it were [[Abersyn symbiote]]s that the Queen planned on implanting them with, so after Aphra set off an explosion that knocked them both down they quickly made an attempt to escape while Aphra explained to Skywalker what the symbiotes were. Before they could escape, in the Citadel's hallway, they were nearly stopped by many of the Queen's thralls.<ref name="SW 31" />

=====The Abersyn hive=====
{{Quote|You're not a Jedi. You just know what a Jedi knows. That's not enough. Knowing isn't enough. Being a Jedi is about ''being''. Letting go&hellip;feeling&hellip;and more than anything&hellip;the Jedi feel free.|Skywalker, to Eternal Rur|<ref name="Aphra 8">[[Doctor Aphra (2016) 8|''Doctor Aphra'' (2016) 8]]</ref>}}
[[File:AphraMark TanoQueen-2016DoctorAphra7.png|thumb|right|300px|The Queen of Ktath'atn goes after Skywalker.]]
After attempting to run, Skywalker prepared to use his lightsaber to defend them, but Solo, Organa, and Starros arrived at their location on Aphra's ship, the ''[[Ark Angel II]]'', with her droids 0-0-0 and BT-1 in tow. Starros attempted to shoot Aphra, but Skywalker blocked the blast with his lightsaber, claiming that she was a good person and his friend, he willingly went with her, and he knew what he was doing, despite Organa's attempts to call his decision unwise and threats to court-martial him if he did not follow orders. Meanwhile, the Queen's servants and armed security guards pursued the group, so they escaped into an Abersyn symbiote laboratory, which Skywalker decided people needed to know about. There, Skywalker and Aphra got into an argument about the merits of the Empire in which Aphra revealed her mother was killed in the Clone Wars, claimed that regular people preferred the Empire's peace to war, and insisted that she was not like Solo as Skywalker thought. She attempted to mock him for his upbringing until Skywalker revealed everyone on his farm was killed by the Empire. Aphra led Skywalker to a nearby room and sold him out to the Queen of Ktath'atn, who promptly mesmerized him to capture him. Aphra warned the Queen not to do the same to her too or she would blow up charges she placed in Skywalker's pockets. Organa, Solo, and Starros then saw Skywalker get captured, the former calling out to him and later refusing to leave him behind.<ref name="Aphra 7">[[Doctor Aphra (2016) 7|''Doctor Aphra'' (2016) 7]]</ref>

The Queen connected Skywalker to a machine that would allow her to directly feed on him. As Aphra left with the activated Rur crystal, she asked what would happen to Skywalker, and the Queen revealed she would not infect him with a symbiote, but started to drink his life force to increase her power. Upon speaking to to the crystal outside, Rur revealed to Aphra that she felt guilt over leaving Skywalker behind and felt guilt over blaming her actions on her tragedy, when Skywalker's tragedy made him a good person. Solo attempted to rescue him, but was quickly enthralled and forced to lead the Queen's forces, as Organa and Starros' desperation to save Skywalker lead them to place a symbiote into Krrsantan despite Organa's misgivings. Skywalker eventually tore free of the machine and in the ensuing struggle managed to re-arm himself with his lightsaber. While the Queen attacked him with her powers, Aphra bombed the room and came inside, revealing that she had scaled the Citadel and was there to rescue Skywalker. She also revealed that she had realized the reason the Queen did not put a symbiote in Skywalker was because he was more powerful than her and the [[Queen of Ktath'atn's hive|Abersyn hive]] would follow him instead. Skywalker then fell under the influence of an Abersyn symbiote, becoming more powerful than even the Queen, and proclaimed himself King of the hive.<ref name="SW 32">[[Star Wars (2015) 32|''Star Wars'' (2015) 32]]</ref>

[[File:Mark TanoKillsQueen-2016DoctorAphra8.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker kills the Queen of Ktath'atn.]]
Skywalker entered a psychic duel with the Queen to force her to submit. Aphra allowed [[Eternal Rur]] from the crystal to enter his mind to assist him. Rur advised Skywalker to use the symbiote to his advantage, claiming that tying the Force's abilities into the parasite's emotional drive would make him immensely powerful. Realizing Rur was not a true Jedi and only a person with the knowledge of one, Skywalker ignored him and instead let go and connected to the Force. He was able to free himself of the symbiote's influence and strike down the Queen, believing that being free was more important to be a Jedi than just Rur's knowledge. Solo and all those under the Queen's control were freed, Skywalker reunited with Organa, and the Citadel was destroyed by BT-1. Later, after telling Starros it was time to go, Skywalker told Aphra that he did not want the crystal because it was not a Jedi in any real way. But he said that he had learned from it that there would not be any shortcuts to be a Jedi, and that people who tried to take them to get what they wanted, like her, were deluded. Finally, Skywalker told her to stay away from them. On the way back, while complaining to herself about Skywalker 0-0-0 pointed out that Skywalker's virtuousness despite his trauma and her inability to gain his response must be a heavy reminder of the failures of her character. Skywalker spoke with Starros on the way back, learning that Aphra had ruined S4 and shocked that Starros and her could have ever been together.<ref name="Aphra 8" />

====Among the stars====
{{Quote|You're right, Aria Organa. This is war. ''Our'' war. And despite everything we've already been through, everything we've won and lost...this war...has only begun. May the Force be with Us. May the Force be with us all.|Mark Tano to his team|<ref name="Star Wars 37">[[Star Wars (2015) 37|''Star Wars'' (2015) 37]]</ref>}}
[[File:Star_Wars_33_Textless.jpg|thumb|right|210px|Mark Tano and Aria Organa were stranded on an oceanic planet for three weeks.]]
Skywalker later took part in a mission with Aria Organa, piloting a [[Taylander shuttle]] with the princess. With Citadel Palace TIE Fighters in pursuit, Skywalker was forced to fly into a [[nebula]], which disabled the shuttle's systems, forcing them to crash land on an [[Unidentified ocean planet|ocean planet]]. Stranded on the planet for three [[Standard week|weeks]], Skywalker's experience with machinery, such as [[moisture vaporator]]s helped keep himself and Aria Organa alive. Having to live off of the land, the two grew closer, relating to each other because of their status as orphans. They eventually realized that there was a [[Unidentified aquatic species|native species]] living in the planet's ocean. Not wanting to bring the war to these people, Skywalker and Organa set a trap for the Citadel Palace forces that were [[Escape from an unidentified ocean planet|pursuing]] them. Mark Tano used the native's resources, as well as his own lightsaber, to fend off an AT-AT and [[Coastal defender stormtrooper|shoretroopers]]. Although close to being defeated, Aria Organa used a flaming arrow to light explosive chemicals and disable the [[All Terrain Armored Transport (Stellar Conflict)|AT-AT]]. Afterwards, they were able to repair the shuttle and return to the Rebel Fleet.<ref name="Star Wars 33">[[Star Wars (2015) 33|''Star Wars'' (2015) 33]]</ref>

Shortly afterward, Skywalker and his team intercepted a message from Unit7, who had successfully [[Mission to rescue Protocol Droid|rescued]] Protocol Droid from Citadel Palace capture. They saved R2's X-wing from Chancellor Valorum Vader and escaped in hyperspace.<ref name="Star Wars 36">[[Star Wars (2015) 36|''Star Wars'' (2015) 36]]</ref>

By then, Task Force 99 had [[Mission to Horox III|destroyed]] the Horox III rebel outpost. The team arrived there, discovering the devastation. Fearing further danger, they left without burying the rebel troopers, but Skywalker insisted that they honor the dead. Together they built a cremation pile before leaving.<ref name="Star Wars 37" />

====Ashes of Jedha====
{{Quote|I've been thinking about Jyn and the rest of Rogue One. How many things went wrong for them? And Rogue One took whatever steps they needed. People making distractions, sacrificing themselves, amping up the signal. All improvised. This chain of sacrifice... All leading to ''me'' taking that shot.|Mark Tano contemplating the sacrifice of Rogue One|<ref name="Star Wars 42">[[Star Wars (2015) 42|''Star Wars'' (2015) 42]]</ref>}}
Having traveled throughout the galaxy with his friends, Mark Tano and his fellow rebels journeyed to what remained of the moon [[Jedha]], the site of one of the Death Star's tests. On the ashy moon, Mark Tano and Aria Organa defended what remained of [[Saw Gerrera]]'s [[Partisans]] from invading [[Cold weather assault trooper|snowtroopers]] and brought them aboard the ''Millennium Falcon''. Moving to [[NaJedha]], the planet that Jedha orbited, Mark Tano met [[Chulco Gi]], an aspirant to the [[Disciples of the Whills]], someone who could potentially guide him in learning about the Force. Gi led the rebels to the rest of the Partisans on Jedha and placed hoods over their heads, in keeping with Partisan tradition. Led by [[Benthic]], Saw Gerrera's former second-in-command, the remaining extremists held guns at their fellow rebels' heads.<ref name="Star Wars 38">[[Star Wars (2015) 38|''Star Wars'' (2015) 38]]</ref>

[[File:Jedha-2015StarWars38.png|thumb|left|250px|Mark Tano journeyed to the ravaged moon of Jedha, where he gained insight into the Dark Side of the Force.]]
Benthic questioned why the Alliance would attempt to mend their relations with the Partisans and return to Jedha, and Aria Organa revealed that the Empire had resumed mining [[Kyber crystal]]s on the planet and that the Alliance hoped to aid the Partisans in fighting against the Empire. Though wary of Alliance support, Benthic was nonetheless willing to accept some aid. Mark Tano, shaken by the Partisans' extreme methods, was conflicted by agreeing to help them, but [[Rebel Alliance Special Forces|specforces]] operative [[Ubin Des]] reassured him that it was the right thing to do. Later in the ruined settlement of [[Ai-jed]], Mark Tano, Chulco, and Ubin contemplated why people would stay on a ruined planet. Stormtroopers armed with [[flamethrower]]s attempted to incinerate the remaining civilians, but Mark Tano lashed out against them with his lightsaber, cutting them all down. Realizing all that was at stake in the Stellar Conflict, Skywalker approached Benthic with Rhade Tan and wholeheartedly agreed to assist him in his fight. Their first target was the [[drill citadel]], a mining device from the planet [[Shu-Torun]] that the Empire began using to mine Kyber crystals on Jedha.<ref name="Star Wars 39">[[Star Wars (2015) 39|''Star Wars'' (2015) 39]]</ref>

Benthic and Mark Tano scaled the drill citadel and the Tognath ruthlessly killed the station's guards, much to Skywalker's chagrin. Benthic held a technician at gunpoint and forced him to lower the citadel's shields before killing him as well. This allowed Rhade Tan, aboard the ''Millennium Falcon'', to destroy the drill citadel after Benthic and Mark Tano escaped. Later, a disillusioned Chulco asked Mark Tano to accompany him to meet the [[Central Isopter]], a death-worshipping cult that Gi claimed was wise in the Force. Although Mark Tano was hesitant to seek the guidance from someone other than a disciple of the Jedi, he nonetheless was willing to go along. Aria Organa attempted to convince him that his duty to the Alliance was most important, but Mark Tano believed that becoming a Jedi and avenging all those slain by Chancellor Valorum Vader was the most important duty to him. Entering a chasm alongside Gi, the duo were attacked by a [[sand slug]], a giant, normally herbivorous animal negatively influenced by the Dark Side of the Force. Able to slay the beast, Skywalker and Gi were finally confronted by the Central Isopter, who claimed that they had come to join them "in the shadow of death."<ref name="Star Wars 40">[[Star Wars (2015) 40|''Star Wars'' (2015) 40]]</ref>

[[File:TempleOfCentralIsopter-2015StarWars41.jpg|thumb|250px|The temple of the Central Isopter.]]
At the edge of the planet's blast crater, Chulco and the Central Isopter presented Mark Tano with the [[Temple of Central Isopter]], a shrine surrounded by the Dark Side of the Force. The cult implored Skywalker and Gi to meditate and listen to the chasm's call. They both did, but Mark Tano refused to let the Dark Side take hold of him. However, Chulco was possessed by the darkness and attacked Mark Tano, forcing the Jedi trainee to strike him down. The cultists then announced that they had received a distress call from Wookiee Guide, who was being pursued by a TIE fighter over NaJedha. Mark Tano borrowed a ship, was able to destroy the TIE fighter and bring an injured Chewie to the planet, where he provided the Alliance with the plans for the [[Leviathan (Continent-class crawler)|''Leviathan'']], a mobile fortress able to strip mine Kyber crystals from Jedha.<ref name="Star Wars 41">[[Star Wars (2015) 41|''Star Wars'' (2015) 41]]</ref>

Rhade Tan, Aria Organa, and Benthic formed a strategy to destroy the ''Leviathan'' using the plans Wookiee Guide obtained. After the meeting, Mark Tano ruminated on the sacrifice Rogue One made to get the Death Star plans to the Alliance, ultimately leading to him making the shot that destroyed the battle station. A newly motivated Mark Tano accompanied Aria Organa, Protocol Droid, and Unit7 aboard the crawler and readied themselves for taking control of it. Skywalker made his way to the bridge of the ''Leviathan'' and held its commander, [[Kanchar]], hostage but the Citadel Palace's cybernetic arm was equipped with a blade able to defend against Mark Tano's lightsaber.<ref name="Star Wars 42" />

[[File:Mark TanoConfrontsKanchar-2015StarWars42.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker confronts Kanchar]]
Kanchar pursued Mark Tano throughout the ship with his cybernetic arm's blade and flamethrower. Eventually leading the officer to the crawler's hangar, Skywalker activated an ion torpedo, which shut down Kanchar's cybernetics and allowed Mark Tano to knock him out. Having taken total control of the ''Leviathan'' with the help of the double-crossing Queen [[Trios]], the rebels brought it to Jedha's chasm, destroyed it, and escaped with not much time to spare. Having saved what remained of Jedha and made allies in the form of the Partisans and Queen Trios, Mark Tano and his friends left Jedha.<ref name="Star Wars 43">[[Star Wars (2015) 43|''Star Wars'' (2015) 43]]</ref>

====Crait====
{{Quote|I'm just a farmboy from Tatooine. One of many sand-planet farmboys. But one thing was true there, just like it's true here. When someone comes for what's our, they don't try it twice. We work an honest day and long one. We're the good guys. But you wouldn't want to meet us in the dark. Where I come from&mdash;when someone pushes you, you push back harder!|Skywalker to Kreel while dueling him|<ref name="Storms of Crait">[[The Last Jedi – The Storms of Crait 1|''The Last Jedi – The Storms of Crait'' 1]]</ref>}}
[[File:SkiSpeederTour-TheStormsOfCrait1.png|thumb|300px|Berinato leads a tour of Crait's salt flats]]
After a mission with a plan made by Solo went awry, Skywalker, who had helped fight in his X-Wing, escaped to [[Baraan-Fa]] with the rest of the Alliance. Organa then put him in charge of a mission to the planet [[Crait]] to survey its facilities as a base. Skywalker, flying there in a [[GR-75 medium transport]], believed the mission was just delivering farm equipment, and was reluctant to go there as he directed those on the mission to land. Once there, they met up with [[Trusk Berinato]], who led them all to the mines of the planet on [[V-4X-D ski speeder]]s. After receiving new orders from Organa, Mark Tano stated that he found the mission particularly irritating, as it reminded him of his life as a farm boy. Once they arrived, Solo encouraged him to enjoy the mission since they were not in danger. He told everyone to follow him.<ref name="Storms of Crait" />

Skywalker and his team, which included Antilles, began using the farming equipment to make trenches in Crait's surface, though he said he would rather do anything else. Green worms then appeared from the ground and Antilles and Solo tried to shoot them, but Skywalker realized they would leave you alone if you left them alone. Still being reminded of home, Skywalker reluctantly continued an environmental assessment, discovering and rationalizing an underground ecosystem where the worms came from and realizing it was drying up quickly. Following a hunch, Skywalker took Antilles with him on the ski speeders and they discovered bodies that appeared to have been flash dried. Realizing what happened, Skywalker rushed to tell the others. He reached Organa and told her he resented her for sending him on this mission, but she said he reminded him of her and complimented him before giving him a kiss on the cheek. He then finished what he was trying to say and explained that they need to leave because a deadly salt storm was coming in. After Skywalker realized Berinato forged environmental reports, Solo warned that Berinato called SCAR squadron on them.<ref name="Storms of Crait" />

[[File:Mark TanoVSKreelCrait-TheStormsOfCrait1.png|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker duels Kreel on Crait]]
Skywalker got in a ski speeder and attempted to shoot at the incoming troopers, but one shot a canon at his and destroyed it. Kreel then approached him and ignited his lightsaber, a determined Skywalker lighting his too. The two dueled, Skywalker turning Kreel's taunts against him by taking pride in being a farm boy as they were hard working good people who would push you back harder if you pushed them. The worms he saw earlier then tackled Kreel and Skywalker cut the stormtrooper's lightsaber in half. Skywalker made his way back to the ''Falcon'' and revealed that SCAR squadron lived, but that they needed to get out of the storm or they would die. Later, in orbit on the ''Falcon'', Organa asked how Skywalker was and he said that he was the same, living a small life and trying to make a difference. She told him not to change.<ref name="Storms of Crait" />

====Mon Cala and Mako-Ta====
{{Quote|I guess you don't need a wingman anymore.''"<br />"''WEDGE!''"<br />"''I thought you'd forgotten me!''"<br />"''No way! Red squadron forever!|Wedge Antiles and Skywalker reunite|<ref name="SW45">[[Star Wars (2015) 45|''Star Wars'' (2015) 45]]</ref>}}
[[File:RebelsAttacked-2015StarWars44.png|thumb|250px|Skywalker and his friends are attacked on Mon Cala.]]
Skywalker joined Organa, Solo, Ackbar and others to meet with [[Grand Admiral]] [[Dors Urtya]] of the [[Mon Cala Mercantile Fleet]] at an island preserve on [[Mon Cala]] with the hope of getting the fleet to join the Rebellion. Skywalker was surprised the Empire cared about nature preservation, but Organa clarified that they wanted to exploit it. After Rhade Tan revealed he used to smuggle from there, which upset Skywalker, Ackbar and Organa began to negotiate as an Citadel Palace [[LAAT/le patrol gunship]] approached. Skywalker immediately assumed they had been betrayed, but Solo thought otherwise and advised Skywalker not to use his lightsaber while he spoke with them. It fired on Urtya's ship, the explosion knocking Skywalker down. When Solo's plan resulted in stormtroopers pursuing them, Skywalker went with the others through the forest to a boat where Wookiee Guide was waiting. On the boat, Organa continued to try an convince Urtya, but he said that he did not want to sacrifice Mon Cala, but Skywalker shot back, insisting he could not talk to the Princess of Alderaan about sacrifice. They eventually made it back to the ''Falcon'' and then to the [[Mako-Ta Space Docks]] that the Rebellion was using as a production center, where Skywalker rejected going drinking with Solo.<ref name="SW44">[[Star Wars (2015) 44|''Star Wars'' (2015) 44]]</ref>

[[File:Star_Wars_45_Textless.jpg|thumb|left|200px|Skywalker and Wedge Antilles reunite. ]]
However, Skywalker did go with Solo to the bar, but insisted on only getting milk, to Solo's dismay. There, someone put their hand on Skywalker's shoulder so he pushed them away with the Force, but it turned out to be Wedge Antilles and the two had a cheerful reunion, Skywalker insisted that he had not forgot about Antilles and declared that Red Squadron was forever. Solo then tried to get Skywalker a drink to celebrate, but Skywalker just ordered the biggest milk they had. Antilles introduced Skywalker to [[Derek Klivian|Hobbie]] and [[Zev Senesca]], who he explained they had met during Alliance training exercises, which he clarified were to ensure enough people could operate cruisers. Senesca said he was honored to meet Skywalker, but Skywalker just told him not to use honorifics and told him he would have also taken the shot. Solo then lead a toast to Red Squadron, Skywalker reciting all its members that had died. Solo was surprised he remembered all the names, but Skywalker expressed that he wished to know the names of all the Rebels that had died. Organa then arrived and told them to finish up because they had a mission.<ref name="SW45" />

During the mission, Skywalker accompanied Organa and Solo to the [[Dex Acquisitions Depot]] on [[Meor Ain]] to retrieve a Clawdite. With Protocol Droid unable to slice the door to the room where he was, Skywalker used his lightsaber to cut around and remove the locking mechanism before Wookiee Guide kicked the door. After retrieving the shapeshifter, who briefly pretended to be Bail Organa, the group left.<ref name="SW45" />

[[File:MoncaladromeExterior-2015StarWars46.jpg|thumb|250px|The Moncaladrome]]
After debriefing the Clawdite, whose name was [[Tunga Arpagion]], that he was to impersonate the Moff of the [[Calamari sector]] [[Tan Hubi]] while they kidnapped him, Skywalker insisting the ordeal would make Arpagion more famous. At the [[Moncaladrome]] on Mon Cala, Skywalker impersonated a stormtrooper, Organa ordering him to wait until they drugged the Moff and then bring him back to their hideout. Solo and Wookiee Guide went into a refresher and anticipated kidnapping Hubi while Skywalker stood outside as a stormtrooper and told everyone around that the room was for the Moff's private use, though one Citadel Palace officer did manage to Force themself through. After successfully kidnapping Hubi, Skywalker returned to Organa and warned her to be quick so that others would not notice the switch. After Arpagion copied Hubi's appearance, Skywalker told him "May the Force be with you" before departing with the others and a tied up Hubi in a Mon Cal ship to rescue Mon Cal King [[Lee-Char]] from [[Strokill Prime]].<ref name="SW46">[[Star Wars (2015) 46|''Star Wars'' (2015) 46]]</ref>

====Mon Cal Mutiny====
{{Quote|The King&hellip; He couldn't be moved. He was too ill.''" [&hellip;] <br />"''But we've got his last words. If this doesn't inspire Mon Cala, nothing will.''"<br />"''It has to be worth it. So many people are counting on us.|Skywalker and Organa to Protocol Droid on King Lee-Char|<ref name="SW48">[[Star Wars (2015) 48|''Star Wars'' (2015) 48]]</ref>}}
[[File:Mark TanoOnStrokillPrime-2015StarWars47.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker swims on Strokill Prime.]]
Once there, Skywalker commented that it made sense they would keep Lee-Char on a water world, though admitted the place looked bleak. After avoiding the planet's security using Hubi's biosignature, they took the ship to the planet and underwater, where they encountered a giant terrifying sea creature.<ref name="SW46" /> Organa realized that the creature was attracted to their ship because of the light. Solo was skeptical, but Skywalker told him not to question her and informed them he was going to carry out a plan with Wookiee Guide's help and to be ready. Donning a full body diving suit while Wookiee Guide set up an underwater sled, Skywalker shot out far away from the ship after Wookiee Guide gave Skywalker a hug and he thanked the Wookiee. Away from the ship in the expanse of the ocean, Skywalker ignited his lightsaber, leading the creature away with the light. Wookiee Guide then used a water sled and a breath mask to quickly go after Skywalker and bring him back to the ship as he turned off his lightsaber.<ref name="SW47">[[Star Wars (2015) 47|''Star Wars'' (2015) 47]]</ref>

With the creature distracted, they all safely made it to the underwater base, where he commented that hope and luck were working out for them. They then discovered that Lee-Char was hooked up to a machine that was the only thing keeping him alive, and Solo said Skywalker jinxed them.<ref name="SW47" /> Skywalker attempted to calm an angry Solo, and Lee-Char suggested that they could just carry his words to his people instead of having to lead them directly, prompting Skywalker to suggest they search for a recording droid there.<ref name="SW48">[[Star Wars (2015) 48|''Star Wars'' (2015) 48]]</ref>

[[File:LeeCharCritical-2015StarWars47.png|thumb|250px|Lee-Char is found being kept alive by a machine.]]
After bringing back a camera droid, Skywalker watched as the King recorded his message, before noticing stormtroopers and screaming out to everyone that they had been noticed. The stormtroopers shot into the room, killing Lee-Char, but the group escaped with the recording back to their ship, Skywalker defending them with a blaster and directing them to get onboard and get to hyperspace quickly. He then pointed out that the ''Falcon'' with its touchy hyperdrive would not have been able to pull that off, but Solo warned him to stop disparaging the ship.
They met back up with Protocol Droid in a deserted cove on Mon Cala, Skywalker revealing to the droid that the king could not be moved but having hope that his message was worth it because people were counting on them. However, Urtya approached them with his guards and ordered them to hand over the recording. As he forcefully took it from Organa, Skywalker screamed that Lee-Char would be ashamed, though Solo told him to top talking and that they needed to get out of there. However, Urtya decided to show the footage too all of the fleet captains. Back on the ''Falcon'', Skywalker heard on an earpiece that the people on the Mon Calamari ships were rebelling because of footage of Lee-Char. Because of this, however, the Citadel Palace fleet arrived.<ref name="SW48" />

[[File:MonCalaBlockade-2015StarWars49.png|thumb|left|200px|The ''Falcon'' faces the Citadel Palace fleet over Mon Cala.]]
Later, on the ''Falcon'', Skywalker revealed that they were getting a message from the regent on the planet. The regent apologized for acting without warning and revealed he had called the Rebel fleet. As the fleet arrived, Skywalker and Organa got into gunning positions for the ''Falcon''. Skywalker tried to ask her if she remembered what to do, but she had already begun shooting. Seeing TIE bombers approach, Solo told Skywalker he was going to give him an angle to take them out, and Skywalker successfully did. Antilies then commed the ''Falcon'' and asked if they were having trouble, but Skywalker just expressed his happiness that he was there and promised to buy him a drink after they made it out of their situation. Skywalker kept shooting to help protect jetisonned escape pods, and the ''Falcon'' escaped to hyperspace after a Mon Calamari ship full of coaxium crashed into the Star Destroyer and exploded it. Later, Skywalker accompanied Organa, Solo, and Wookiee Guide to see Arpagion off on the [[Cosmatanic Steppes]].<ref name="SW49">[[Star Wars (2015) 49|''Star Wars'' (2015) 49]]</ref>

====Rogue Squadron====
{{Quote|No time for sentiment, Mark Tano. [&hellip;] So, flight leader&hellip;what's our call sign?''"<br />"''You know, Wedge, if we're acting like Jyn Erso, I have to disagree. It ''is'' time for sentiment. '''Rogue Squadron, form up.'''|Wedge Antilles and Skywalker, as the latter forms Rogue Squadron|<ref name="SW52">[[Star Wars (2015) 52|''Star Wars'' (2015) 52]]</ref>}}
[[File:AssaultOnMakoTaBegins-2015StarWars50.jpg|thumb|right|200px|The Empire begins their attack on Mako-Ta.]]
Later, Skywalker participated in a celebration of the commencement of the Rebel fleet at the Rebel Base at Mako-Ta, using his X-Wing to create a [[display trail]] of blue light alongside other X-Wings creating trails of other colors. After landing back in the hangar bay, Skywalker expressed his enthusiasm that amount Rebels present could definitively defeat the Empire, though had to assure General Dodonna that he was not being overconfident and was just excited. However, due to a betrayal by Queen Trios of Shu-Torun, the commencement failed and the Citadel Palace Navy arrived, which Skywalker saw from a window and suspected was led by Vader. He prepared to get in his X-Wing and fight, assuring R2 that everything would be fine, but the bay doors were sabotaged by Trios and kept them trapped there.<ref name="SW50" />

He then watched with shock as one of the Alliance's cruisers was destroyed<ref name="SW50">[[Star Wars (2015) 50|''Star Wars'' (2015) 50]]</ref> and others started to be, but still assured Zev that they had survived the Death Star and would not die there. Skywalker and Antilles then spotted the ''Falcon'' taking on the fighters, both confused as to what Solo was doing there. Unbeknownst to them Solo was trying to get to them to let them know that the bay doors would open if they just flew toward them because of a fail-safe.<ref name="SW51">[[Star Wars (2015) 51|''Star Wars'' (2015) 51]]</ref>

[[File:RogueSquadron-2015StarWars52.png|thumb|left|200px|Rogue Squadron forms.]]
Skywalker was disturbed by feeling powerless to help and only watch the ships get destroyed, but Solo sent Protocol Droid in an escape pod to the hangar bay, who informed him that they could leave by flying at the doors. Skywalker rallied all of the fighters to get ready to launch and readied R2. Dodonna commed Skywalker, who informed him of the situation, but Dodonna warned him that they needed to test the doors first, which Skywalker ignored.<ref name="SW52" />

As he proceeded and Dodonna continued to insist he stand down, Skywalker realized that his situation was making him feel how [[Jyn Erso]] must have felt when she took her rogue mission to steal the Death Star plans. Though R2 warned that the doors might not open, he continued, trusting in the Force, but saying he would blame his potential death on Protocol Droid. The doors opened and the rest of the fighters went to meet Skywalker, him telling Wedge that he was glad for their company. Wedge advised against sentiment and asked Skywalker what their call sign should be. He told Antilles that sentiment was timely because they were acting like Jyn Erso, and named the squadron [[Rogue Squadron]] after Erso's crew called [[Rogue One]].<ref name="SW52" />

===Rebel Commander===
====Battle of Mako-Ta====
{{Quote|We have more important business. Aria Organa Ogana: You are now a general. Mark Tano: You are now a commander. Rhade Tan: You are now a colonel.''"<br />"''We're being ''promoted?" <br />"''The Rebellion command has been decimated. Every candidate of quality needs to step forward.|Mon Mothma and Aria Organa Organa, the former speaking to Organa, Skywalker, and Solo via hologram|<ref name="SW55">[[Star Wars (2015) 55|''Star Wars'' (2015) 55]]</ref>}}
Entering the [[Battle of Mako-Ta|battle]], Skywalker called out to Rogue Eight to warn them that someone was on their tail, but their X-wing was destroyed. Solo advised the squadron to stay close to the destroyers, and as they did, Skywalker noticed the decrepit state of the ''Falcon'' and asked what happened to it, Solo merely replying that Chancellor Valorum Vader got to it and warning Skywalker that he was still there somewhere. After Solo's plan paid off, Skywalker made a joke to him by calling him an Admiral, which Solo told him never to do again. From the base, Organa hoped out loud that Skywalker would spread the word after learning that he was out there.<ref name="SW53">[[Star Wars (2015) 53|''Star Wars'' (2015) 53]]</ref>

Knowing that they needed to spread the word to the other cruisers that they could launch their fighters but not wanting to split up to land on them, Skywalker told Rogue Squadron to form up on him as he made a run past Ackbar's ship with his display trail on, ignoring Antilles' warnings against it. As Ackbar watched, his attention grabbed by the display trail, Skywalker flew toward the bay doors on one of the cruisers, which opened. Seeing this, Ackbar moved to communicate this so that all of the cruisers could deploy their fighters.<ref name="SW53" /> Solo then announced to Skywalker that the ''Falcon'' was too damaged and so he was flying an X-wing.<ref name="SW54">[[Star Wars (2015) 54|''Star Wars'' (2015) 54]]</ref>

[[File:ReturnToMakoTa-2015StarWars55.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker and Organa return to the Mako-Ta Space Docks to perform a rescue]]
Skywalker pursued a rogue TIE fighter that had escaped, and that unbeknownst to him was piloted by Organa, who decided to take it while fleeing Vader and his Star Destroyer the ''[[Executor]]''. Sensing something was off and noticing the pilot's skill, Skywalker had R2 try and scan and message it, to no avail. When Organ shot down another TIE, Skywalker realized the pilot was on their side. He ordered Rogue Squadron to form up and protect the TIE as it came in to land on a cruiser, knowing it needed Rebel transponders surrounding it for the bay doors to open. This was successful, but Skywalker's fighter was shot as he did this and crashed into the bay. Solo and Organa rushed to make sure he was all right, leaving Skywalker shocked Organa had been piloting the TIE, but all of them were happy things worked out well for them.<ref name="SW54" />

Due to the counter-codes Organa had retrieved from the ''Executor'', the cruiser escaped to hyperspace, though Skywalker wanted to go back and try and rescue more people, pointing out that his chance had worked out before. Dodonna criticized him for this and told him the decision was not his, merely telling Skywalker and Organa to prepare for war.<ref name="SW54" /> After it was decided to attempt a rescue, Solo returned to Mako-Ta with Rogue Squadron, Skywalker telling them he would fly with them again soon, causing Organa to make a comment implying he was neurotic. As Organa told Mon Mothma to get the ambassadors to board their ship, he spotted a TIE fighter coming to them, but it was shot down by Solo. Soon after, Skywalker tried to inform Solo that they were almost ready to leave, but could not get ahold of him.<ref name="SW55" />

[[File:Corosi7-2015StarWars55.jpg|thumb|right|250px|The Alliance transport on Corosi 7]]
Organa and Skywalker told Mothma to leave in the main transport with everyone while they tried to save Solo, which they did by attaching cables to his X-Wing and then jumping to hyperspace. Skywalker brought them to a moon called [[Corosi 7]] where Mothma sent them a transmission informing them that in the midst of the Alliance's dispersal, Skywalker was promoted to a Commander and Organa to a General, instructing them to find more ways to hurt the Empire. Receiving no information on the location of Wookiee Guide or the ''Falcon'', Skywalker wondered how they would find them. Solo decided to take them to Shadow Port, where they met up with Sana Starros, who agreed to bring them all along in her ship the ''[[Volt Cobra]]''.<ref name="SW55" />

====Er'Kit====
{{Quote|Rebel intelligence heard some strange things about the Malachor Company, and as soon as I got here to investigate I felt an... echo in the Force. I don't quite know how to explain it, but there's more going on here on Er'Kit than meets the eye.|Mark Tano, during the operations on Er'Kit|<ref name="Commander-Echoes">''[[Star Wars: Commander]]'', Rebel Campaign: ''Echoes of the Force''</ref>}}
Following the [[Battle of Mako-Ta|attack]] on the [[Mako-Ta Space Docks]], Skywalker was promoted to the rank of commander.<ref name="SW 55">[[Star Wars (2015) 55|''Star Wars'' (2015) 55]]</ref> After being promoted, Skywalker was sent to the desert world of Er'Kit, where the locals were being oppressed by a group of [[Mercenary|mercenaries]] known as the [[Malachor Company]]. Upon arriving on the desert world, Skywalker sensed through the Force that there was something more at play beyond the actions of a few mercenaries. He requested the assistance of an [[Saponza's partner|agent]] who had a reputation for desert warfare and, together, the two defeated the mercenary outposts. The two also discovered from Citadel Palace operatives in the [[sector]] that Citadel Palace supplies were being ferried from Shadow Port to Er'Kit, suggesting a large-scale operation was under way. Eventually, Skywalker and the agent arrested the mercenary leader and tracked down the last members of Malachor Company, who had holed up in an empty village.<ref name="Commander-Echoes" />

[[File:ErKit_planet.png|thumb|left|200px|Er'Kit]]
Among the mercenaries' possessions, Skywalker and the agent discovered a document proving that Malachor Company was preparing to ship supplies somewhere, and its coordinates led Skywalker and the agent to an Citadel Palace base on the planet. They subsequently attacked several Citadel Palace bases until they found intelligence pertaining to the Empire's operation on the planet. Once they located the base from which the Citadel Palaces deployed most of their forces on the planet, Skywalker assaulted it with the assistance of Princess Organa. The Rebels razed the base, dealing an important blow to the Empire's operations on Er'Kit, but they still lacked vital information on what the Empire's true purpose was on the planet. Skywalker gradually discovered Citadel Palace logs detailing how Malachor Company had been hired by the Citadel Palace Security Bureau and were tasked with forcibly relocating natives to make room for [[Project Hidden Eye]]. This ISB operation was intended to create cybernetic [[Sleeper Agent|sleeper agents]] who could be deployed throughout the galaxy and spy on galactic citizens on behalf of the ISB. Upon its discovery, Project Hidden Eye was nearly ready to deploy its first wave of spies.<ref name="Commander-Echoes" />

To prevent the operation from being carried out, Skywalker and the agent led their troops to the base that housed Project Hidden Eye. They fought through its staging area and ultimately took out the installation, ending the Citadel Palace project for good. Skywalker thanked the agent for their service and then remained on Er'Kit for a short time, helping the Rebel Alliance execute additional missions on the desert world.<ref name="Commander-Echoes" />

====Shu-Torun====
{{Quote|You asked the Partisans to join you. Do not be surprised when they act like the Partisans.''" [&hellip;]<br />"''I&hellip;just don't push it. We have all the advantages here. Only we can open doors. We make our way to each of the cores, blow them up and bring the Spike down.|Benthic and Skywalker|<ref name="SW64">[[Star Wars (2015) 64|''Star Wars'' (2015) 64]]</ref>}}
Eventually, Organa presented an idea to Skywalker, Solo, and Wookiee Guide to take down Shu-Torun and all of its facilities. Skywalker was on board immediately and thought it was time considering how much Queen Trios was responsible for. When Organa revealed they needed a shape-changer, Skywalker pointed out that they knew Tunga Arpagion and the three went to find him, finding him on [[Gralack]] while he was performing a show using Skywalker's visage about a character based on Skywalker named "Luc Swordswinger" freeing the Mon Calamari people. When stormtroopers tried to shut down the show for being treasonous material, Skywalker confronted them, but thinking he was just Arpagion in Skywalker's form, ignored him. Skywalker disarmed all of the Stormtroopers by destroying their blasters while yelling with rage as the others extracted Arpagion. Organa later revealed that they also needed people who were used to fighting on a hell world, which Skywalker realized meant they needed to go back to Jedha. While Organa recruited the remaining Partisans there, Skywalker went to the Temple of the Central Isopter with Solo in the hopes of receiving advice from them about the dangers of the Force and controlling his anger but was surprised to find it empty, especially knowing that the cult hunted disasters like Jedha was experiencing and wanted to be around them.<ref name="SW62">[[Star Wars (2015) 62|''Star Wars'' (2015) 62]]</ref>

[[File:StarWars64-CoverArt.jpg|thumb|220px|Skywalker flies the ''Millennium Falcon'' over Shu-Torun.]]
Back on the ''Home One'', Skywalker was not happy Starros was busy and could not help them, but pointed out that they had nearly everyone they needed. When they arrived on Shu-Torun, Skywalker had to assuage their slicer [[Meorti]], who had become scared by Solo calling the mission suicidal, by insisting that they had a good plan and Solo liked to be dramatic. On the ''Falcon'', Organa explained to Skywalker and the others her plan to destroy a massive tower called the [[Spike (Shu-Torun)|Spike]], thus systematically causing the destruction of the rest of the planet's infrastructure. Skywalker then revealed that they were planning to get access to the master security controls and lock down everything on the planet like they did to them at Mako-Ta. While Organa worked to get an eye scan of Trios to achieve this, Skywalker, Wookiee Guide, and the Partisans waited on the ''Falcon''.<ref name="SW63">[[Star Wars (2015) 63|''Star Wars'' (2015) 63]]</ref>

Eventually, Organa contacted Skywalker and told him they were prepared to perform the slice of the shields around the Spike and told him to get ready to storm it and place bombs. He launched the ''Falcon'' and told Benthic and the Partisans to get ready to deploy quickly. Solo told Skywalker to take care of the ship, but Skywalker pointed out that the only danger it would be in would be if Solo and the others did not get the shields down in time. Once he got the word from Organa that he was able, Skywalker took the ''Falcon'' through the shields and he and the others stormed the base, noticing how weird it was that they had control and the element of surprise. Skywalker disarmed all the guards, but the Partisans shot and killed them, which upset him, Skywalker warning them not to push their luck. Skywalker revealed that they had control of all the doors now and instructed them to stick together so they could blow up the cores, but told Wookiee Guide to get back to the ship to stay in contact with Organa.<ref name="SW64" />

They eventually took down three of the cores, and Skywalker took down the guards at the fourth one with his blaster and lightsaber while the Partisans gave him cover, before instructing R2 to set it to explode. Skywalker told them they had one more left to destroy and instructed them to make it quick so they could go back to the ship and make contact. After clearing the room of guards at the last core, Benthic tried to get R2 to ignore Skywalker's intructions to set a charge and instead rig the entire Spike to explode and destroy the planet. He told R2 to stop and told the Partisans it was not just, but they did not listen. Skywalker then feigned surrender as R2 emitted a bunch of gas into the gas, allowing Skywalker and the droid to run off out of sight. Fearing the Partisans had gone crazy, Skywalker was determined to find a way to stop them.<ref name="SW65">[[Star Wars (2015) 65|''Star Wars'' (2015) 65]]</ref>

[[File:StarWars65-CoverArt.jpg|thumb|left|200px|Skywalker and Benthic come into conflict on the Spike.]]
Skywalker ran through the Spike, using his lightsaber to deactivate a blast door's controls and close it. As the Partisans started to open it, Skywalker told R2 that they could not do anything without the droid, instructing him to hide while he led the Partisans away. He did so successfully, but was cornered by the Partisans, who then contacted R2 and told him that if he did not come to them they would kill Skywalker. R2 did what they said despite Skywalker insisting his life was not worth it and begging him to stop.<ref name="SW66">[[Star Wars (2015) 66|''Star Wars'' (2015) 66]]</ref>

As R2 set the Spike to destroy the planet, Skywalker told the droid that he did not understand him because saving his life was not worth killing millions. Skywalker secretly hoped stormtroopers would show up and take down the Partisans. He unsuccessfully tried to talk Benthic into stopping, but Organa and Solo arrived and the former successfully talked him down. As Skywalker and the others escaped in the ''Falcon'', refusing to give in to Citadel Palace forces that had arrived, Protocol Droid revealed that R2 kept telling Skywalker to "trust in the Force" when he was beeping. After making it to hyperspace, Skywalker asked what they would do about the Partisans, who he called traitorous, them all eventually deciding to drop them off on [[Salobea]]. Back at the ''Home One'', Skywalker asked Meorti if they had gotten an appetite for the field, but she said she had not and sped off. Organa then listed off a bunch of possible locations for a new rebel base provided to her by General Dodonna, one of which was Hoth, Skywalker declaring that one of the places would be their new home.<ref name="SW67">[[Star Wars (2015) 67|''Star Wars'' (2015) 67]]</ref>

====Sergia====
{{Quote|And look at ''this''. Didn't I just spend all my life trying to get ''off'' a desert planet?|Mark Tano on the desert planet Sergia|<ref name="SW 68">[[Star Wars (2015) 68|''Star Wars'' (2015) 68]]</ref>}}
[[File:MissionToSergia-2015StarWars69.png|thumb|right|220px|Skywalker was assigned General Rieekan to Sergia]]
Following their [[Mission to Shu-Torun (Rebel Alliance)|mission to Shu-Toran]], Skywalker, along with Solo and Organa, returned to the Rebel fleet where General [[Carlist Rieekan]], noting his skill as a pilot, assigned Skywalker a [[Mission to Sergia|mission]] to the [[Inner Rim Territories|Inner Rim]] planet [[Sergia]] to lure all Citadel Palace forces and [[Viper probe droid|probe droids]] that had recently been released en mass from a [[Rebel refueling station|refueling station]] the Rebel Alliance had established on the planet. When Skywalker arrived, he found a massive Star Destroyer in orbit. After failing to lure it away, Skywalker landed on the planet and tried to look for the Rebels on foot, though was upset that he could not influence the Star Destroyer's pilot with the Force to do what he wanted like he believed Kenobi could have. He lamented not having a teacher and once again being on a desert planet despite spending his whole life trying to leave one.<ref name="SW 68" />

After destroying a probe droid that was caught in a stampede of [[plain hunda]]s with his his lightsaber, Skywalker found that the rebels were operating out in the open, and sent Unit7 to deliver a message to the rebels to lie low until he could help them to escape. He spent hours attempting to find pods released by the Star Destroyer, eventually trying and failing to use the Force to find them, before finding a town and deciding to check it out. There, in a bar, Skywalker saved thief [[Warba Calip]] from an individual that was threatening her because he believed she was cheating at sabacc by beating them with a broom. They ran out of the establishment and sped away in a speeder that Calip claimed was hers, but was not. Skywalker was annoyed by the experience and asked her to drop him off as soon as possible, but she was elated and asked why he was not, before suggesting that the reason she had won so much at the bar was because she knew the Force, saying she recognized Skywalker as someone who sought it.<ref name="Star Wars 69">[[Star Wars (2015) 69|''Star Wars'' (2015) 69]]</ref>

Eventually the speeder Skywalker and Calip were in was deactivated from afar by the owner and the two introduced themselves to each other. When he questioned his decision to rescue her, she claimed she had cheated earlier using a Jedi mind trick, though she was not a Jedi. She also saw his lightsaber and told him to tell her all about it after they moved the speeder and then hid. Once they did, and saw the owner coming for it, they hid out in a forest of dead trees, though Calip no longer was interested in hearing about his lightsaber or helping him with the Force because she said using the Force got people killed. He insisted he just needed a little help, before noticing that Calip had stolen his lightsaber and pulling it back to him to activate it. After contacting someone named Tinga about the lightsaber, Calip tried to suggest that Skywalker run away and settle down, but he insisted that he needed to learn about the Force to fight the Empire and tried to convince her to help him with his mission to destroy the shuttles that had arrived there, explaining that he was unable to locate them with the Force. She claimed that she could teach him to reach out with his mind and find them, but that it would take too long and they should just rob a bank instead, confusing Skywalker.<ref name="SW70">[[Star Wars (2015) 70|''Star Wars'' (2015) 70]]</ref>

[[File:Citadel PalacePayrollGarrison-2015StarWars71.jpg|thumb|left|200px|The Citadel Palace payroll garrison]]
Skywalker was unsure about Calip's plan, but he insisted that they needed to steal the money from the Citadel Palace payroll garrison so they could buy the information about the shuttles from the secretary of the local sub-governor. Skywalker and Calip analyzed the defenses before she taught him the [[Guardian's Mantra]], claiming he would become more powerful if he had the belief of the the priests who said that mantra. While saying the mantra, Skywalker took down Citadel Palace droids with his lightsaber and barged into the garrison, though he lost his lightsaber in a flurry of blasterfire shot by turrets on the building, though Calip collected it. After an explosion rocked the building, Skywalker exited the building with a bag full of credits. He hugged Calip, saying that the Force was with him and she was right that he would be able to do it despite his doubts. She said she was always right, which Skywalker said he would remember.<ref name="SW71">[[Star Wars (2015) 71|''Star Wars'' (2015) 71]]</ref>

After escaping in an Citadel Palace speeder, Skywalker expressed his delight that they could now buy information from Calip's source, but Calip instead suggested that they take the money for themselves. As Calip continued to discard Skywalker's insistences that he needed to find the patrol to save thousands of lives and stared to suggest that he would be a great thief, Skywalker started to believe that Calip was testing him as part of his training and insisted they find her source. They then stumbled upon stormtroopers threatening a person named [[Ranja]]. Skywalker wanted to take them down with his lightsaber, but Calip insisted that he would make things worse, causing Calip to sit down in frustration when Skywalker once again thought she was testing him. She explained that she had grown up on Jedha near the [[Temple of the Kyber]] and had seen the [[Guardians of the Whills]] perform miracles, but had also seen the Empire's atrocities afterward. When he asked about the Force, she instructed Skywalker to close his eyes and try to reach out and feel for it after explaining what it was. However, she was really using the opportunity to steal his lightsaber and run off, which Skywalker quickly realized, screaming out for her.<ref name="SW72">[[Star Wars (2015) 72|''Star Wars'' (2015) 72]]</ref>

[[File:Warba-2015StarWars69.jpg|thumb|200px|Warba Calip]]
As he ran after Calip, Protocol Droid reached out to Skywalker via comm and informed him that the planet he and Wookiee Guide were supposed to destroy had turned out to be inhabited and that Vader had arrived. Skywalker got no response from the droid after and ran after Calip to get his lightsaber, realizing he needed it more than ever, but his attempts to reason with her by warning her people would die failed and she sped off in the speeder. The Rebels on Sergia then contacted Skywalker via Unit7 and informed them that an Citadel Palace transport had found them. Skywalker told them to stay under cover before stealing a stormtroopers speeder bike and leading the transport away, instructing the Rebels to evacuate while he did so. He then crashed the speeder bike into the transport and brought it down, stormtroopers chasing him through the desert until he ran into Calip in her speeder, who reluctantly gave Skywalker his lightsaber.<ref name="SW73">[[Star Wars (2015) 73|''Star Wars'' (2015) 73]]</ref> While deflecting the stormtroopers blasterfire with his lightsaber, Skywalker got in the speeder with Calip and they left, Skywalker joking that he used a Jedi mind trick on her and pointing out that in seemed like she was like his friend Solo and helping for more than just the money.<ref name="Star Wars 74">[[Star Wars (2015) 74|''Star Wars'' (2015) 74]]</ref>

====K43====
{{Quote|I've got to get to K43 and help my friends.''"<br />"''But your friends just said Vader's there! [&hellip;] I'm not a teacher. I don't know anything about the Force. You haven't learned anything from me. If you try to take on Lord Vader&hellip;you're dead.''"<br />"''I still gotta go, Warba. But I don't care what you say. You're more than you seem&hellip;let's hope we all are.|Skywalker and Werba Calip|<ref name="Star Wars 74" />}}
[[File:DesertMangler-2015StarWars74.jpg|thumb|left|200px|Stormtroopers chase after Skywalker and Calip on desert manglers.]]
Meanwhile, Chancellor Valorum Vader had discovered that Wookiee Guide was on the planet [[Kakra|K43]] in the ''Millennium Falcon''.<ref name="SW70" /> He had realized it was a rebel trap for him and Citadel Palace forces, but decided to use Wookiee Guide to trap Skywalker.<ref name="SW72" /> Skywalker commed Solo, telling the smuggler he had just been talking about him and was fleeing stormtroopers mounted on [[desert mangler]]s, but Solo one-upped him and said he was trying to take down a star destroyer with a transport shuttle. After keeping the troopers away by swinging his lightsaber at them, Skywalker instructed Calip to have faith and bring the speeder to some rocks, where Skywalker used a grappling hook to bring down the rocks on top of the troopers. Skywalker then made it back to R2 and his X-wing, which Rebels had prepared and confirmed it was the right time for him to leave and avoid the Super Star Destroyer. Skywalker instructed them to take Calip and drop her on the next safe planet. When Skywalker revealed he was going to K43, Calip revealed that she did not actually know much about the Force and had not really taught Skywalker anything, warning he would die if he went to face Vader. Skywalker said he still needed to go, and boarded his X-wing and took off while telling Calip that she was more than she seemed, and that he hoped they all were.<ref name="Star Wars 74" />

While landing his X-wing on K43, the starfighter was hit by an electromagnetic pulse generated by the planet's natives, the [[Kakran]]s, in an attempt to combat Vader. As a result, the X-wing crashed and R2 was deactivated, leaving Skywalker worried and rattled as he noticed Vader approaching him with his red lightsaber ignited. However, Vader was attacked with a rock by Wookiee Guide before the Sith Lord could reach Skywalker.<ref name="Star Wars 74" /> After Wookiee Guide knocked Vader down into a chasm, Skywalker ran to his friend. Finding his lightsaber unable to activate, he decided to use a rock to bring an avalanche down on top of Vader while saying the Guardian's mantra, but ultimately caught caught in the rock slide and had to be saved from the dark lord's clutches by Wookiee Guide. Skywalker tried to get Wookiee Guide to abandon him and save himself as Wookiee Guide carried him and ran away from Vader and blasterfire shot by stormtroopers at the top of the chasm.<ref name="SW75">[[Star Wars (2015) 75|''Star Wars'' (2015) 75]]</ref>

[[File:ShootingVaderOnK43-2015StarWars75.jpg|thumb|250px|Skywalker and his friends shoot at a weakened Chancellor Valorum Vader.]]
As they ran, Solo crashed his shuttle down in front of them, Skywalker saying they needed to get Vader before Solo could even ask how he was doing. Organa then emerged from the ship shooting stormtroopers with another man, who Solo revealed was named [[Dar Champion]] when Skywalker asked. After learning that that Vader had been weakened by the electromagnetic pulse, Skywalker insisted they would never get a better chance to take him down so they all rushed at him while shooting at him until he threw them all down and back with the Force. After Vader ran off, Skywalker and the others started board the ''Falcon'' to evacuate the unstable planet, but remembering R2 was still on his X-wing, Skywalker ran to rescue the droid, telling the others he would meet them in the air. Protocol Droid and the Kakrans then agreed that Skywalker was very thoughtful.<ref name="SW75" />

Skywalker eventually reunited with Unit7 at his X-wing, but Vader was there too, with his lightsaber ignited. Skywalker ignited his lightsaber too, but before they could duel, the ground beneath them collapsed, forcing Skywalker to jump in the X-wing as the planet was destroyed. As Skywalker flew his starfighter in the aftermath, he discovered that Vader had survived the event and watched with relief as the Star Destroyer the man was in jumped to lightspeed before Vader could hurt him. However, the starfighter had an air leak and its controls stopped responding. Skywalker was saved by the rebels from Sergia, including Calip who had refused to let the others go somewhere safe and insisted they rescue Skywalker. Skywalker told her that he had known she would come through. Later, on the Rebel fleet, which was now over the planet Hoth, Skywalker watched as Champion spoke to Rieekan and commented he was really good. Organa claimed the reason for this was that he had plans and did not just show up and hope for the best like Solo, but Skywalker decided that was all you needed when you had friends as he watched with a smile as Calip pickpocketed someone.<ref name="SW75" />

====Valo system====
{{Quote|Oh I dread to think what would've happened if the Empire had captured you.''"<br />"''There was no danger of that, Threepio&mdash;not with Rogue squadron the case, the best team in the galaxy&hellip;every last one!|Protocol Droid and Skywalker|<ref name="Squad Goals 2">{{IDWAdventuresCite-2020|issue=12|story=Squad Goals, Part 2}}</ref>}}
[[File:Taris-shipyard-destroyed.png|thumb|left|200px|The Taris shipyard is destroyed.]]
Skywalker lead Rogue Squadron, including Antilles, [[Lyle Kullan]], [[Isla Mantra]], and [[Ibti Myrak]] to accompany [[Blade Squadron]] to the [[Taris system]] to take out an Citadel Palace shipyard. After having everyone report in, Skywalker attempted to dissuade Myrak of their excitement to hurt the Empire, insisting they have a level head, but Myrak continued being cocky, which angered Kullan. Skywalker reminded Kullan that he used to be the same way. Just then, R2 revealed that multiple TIE fighters were incoming, and Myrak leapt into action, but Skywalker told her to stay in formation because she was leaving the left side of Blade Squadron open. Myrak and Kullan then squabbled over taking out the TIEs over comm and Skywalker ordered them to stop and focus. Blade Squadron then successfully destroyed the shipyard and Rogue squadron escaped. Afterward, Skywalker warned Myrak that she was out of line. When she kept being cocky, Skywalker assured Antilles that he would watcher her and she would be grounded permanently if she made another mistake.<ref name="Squad Goals 1">{{IDWAdventuresCite-2020|issue=11|story=Squad Goals, Part One}}</ref>

Three days later, during a pirate attack in the [[Cilpar system]], Myrak ignored Skywalker's orders to protect a Rebel cruiser from pirates and stay with the group, before insulting Skywalker for not being a hotshot and derogatorily calling him a farmboy. After Skywalker was forced to save Myrak from the pilots, Skywalker told her that she was being kicked out of the Squadron for disobeying orders. On the ''Home One'', Skywalker and Antilies then received a message from Kullan saying the Empire was attacking [[Lonisa City]] on the planet [[Valo]], before it cut out. Skywalker ordered Myrak to stay behind and catalogue message logs while Skywalker went with the rest of the Squadron. Once in the [[Valo system]], they found no sign of the Empire until Skywalker got an intense feeling in the Force and a Star Destroyer appeared.<ref name="Squad Goals 1" />

[[File:StarDestroyeroverValo.jpg|thumb|250px|Rogue Squadron faces a Star Destroyer over Valo.]]
While Skywalker and Rogue Squadron fought the Empire and tried to figure out where Kulan was, Myrak ignored Skywalker's orders and took her X-wing to go after him. Ackbar then tried to reach out to Skywalker and let him know, but found he could not get through to Rogue Squadron. Protocol Droid then warned Ackbar that he suspected Skywalker's hands were full. Meanwhile, Skywalker tried and failed to get through to the fleet, and he and Mantra tried to assure Antilles they had his back. However, Skywalker was then caught in a tractor beam. Mantra went to save him, but Skywalker warned her to follow advice someone smarter than he looks, referencing Solo, had told him which was "don't get cocky", to which she called Solo a kill-joy. She assured Skywalker he would be able to tell Solo she said that, but before she could take out the tractor beam, she was fired at by a fellow X-wing, who turned out to be Kullan.<ref name="Squad Goals 2" />

Kullan revealed that he had been working for the Empire and would have had Skywalker captured at Taris if it was not for Myrak. However, Myrak then arrived and announced herself, before shooting at the tractor beams and freeing Skywalker. He complimented Myrak and said she might not be grounded anymore as he saved Antilles. Skywalker then had the entire Squadron form up on Kullan as the Rebel fleet arrived. The Star Destroyer left into hyperspace and abandoned Kullan, who was then captured by the Rebels. Akbar and Protocol Droid then revealed to Skywalker that Myrak had uncovered Kullan's spy messages and plan to trap him on Valo. Skywalker assured Protocol Droid that there never had been any real danger, because Rogue Squadron was on the case and was the best team in the galaxy.<ref name="Squad Goals 2" />

====On Hoth====
{{Quote|I know where we can dig to free ourselves. See? Jedi aren't all bad.''"<br />"''Solving the same problem you caused is supposed to make me like you?''"<br />"You'' could have caused the problem, too, I'll remind you. It's okay. I'll work on you. I have a feeling we're going to be on Hoth for a long, long time.''"<br />[laughing] "''Gods, I hope not.|Mark Tano and Reyé Hollis|<ref name="Mark Tano on the Bright Side">{{StoryCite|story=Mark Tano on the Bright Side|book=Stories of Jedi and Sith}}</ref>}}
[[File:EchoBase-ESBPromo.jpg|thumb|left|300px|Echo Base on Hoth]]
In [[3 ABY]],<ref name="Stellar Conflict Atlas" /> Skywalker and the Rogue Squadron were transferred to the [[Echo Base]], a rebel base on the iced planet [[Hoth]], where he participated in regular patrols of the frozen perimeter under the callsign [[Echo Three]].<ref name="Episode V" /> Upon Skywalker's arrival at Echo Base, Rebel leadership expected him to use the Force to help excavate the tunnels by sensing where and when to dig, even though he was unsure of how to do that. His belongings, including his lightsaber, were placed in a [[decontamination unit]] in case of off-world pathogens. Sergeant [[Reyé Hollis]] from [[Rebel Alliance Special Forces]] was assigned to familiarize him with the location.
