After they introduced themselves to each other and shook hands, Skywalker declared that he was there to help.<ref name="Mark Tano on the Bright Side" />

Skywalker hoped to get to know Hollis since they would be working together, and they both thought the other had attractive qualities, but the sergeant's anti-Jedi sentiments gave Skywalker the initial impression that the other man disliked him. He did not recognize that Hollis had a Naboo name, but he could sense that Naboo was beautiful through Hollis' mental images of home. Hollis made a derogatory remark about the Jedi and Skywalker defended them. He also promised not to let the Naboo man down, just before a giant [[fork-nosed ice worm]] broke through the ground next to them and they were trapped by a cave-in.<ref name="Mark Tano on the Bright Side" />

Unused to total darkness, Skywalker experienced claustrophobia. He could hear but not locate Hollis until he tried to use the Force to stretch out his senses. He tried to remember that darkness had been a comfort back on Tatooine, but that did not work and he still felt suffocated by the darkness. He successfully detected that Hollis was nearby using the Force and told the other man to stay still. When Skywalker approached, they bickered briefly over what was responsible for the cave-in, Hollis urging him not to use the Force. Hollis, recognizing that the Jedi was panicking, grabbed Skywalker's hand and pressed it to a gap in the wall that had air flowing through it. Skywalker clutched Hollis' hand and asked for his trust. They sat down and kept holding each other's hands as Skywalker thought about the light and warmth of his home on Tatooine. Skywalker began to reflect on his fear of what the darkness would do to him psychologically, referring both to the literal situation they were in and the general darkness in the galaxy he faced. As their hands warmed, Skywalker could sense where they could dig through the ice to free themselves in the Force. They teased each other and laughed before they started digging, Skywalker recognizing that the Force had never steered him the wrong direction and suspecting it never would.<ref name="Mark Tano on the Bright Side" />

While the base was still being built, two rebel soldiers, [[Kes Dameron]] and his wife, [[Shara Bey]] found themselves trapped after an ice collapse caused by [[A-wing starfighter|A-Wing]] cannon. Thinking they would have died, they recorded a message for their little son, [[Poe Dameron]] to explain why they joined the Rebellion. Skywalker, however, rescued them, helped by Wookiee Guide by opening a hole in the ice using his lightsaber, him, Organa, and the others willing to risk the tech in the control room to save their lives. He allowed Bey to use him as a crutch so she could limp out. Dameron and Bey were eventually treated by a [[2-1B surgical droid]].<ref name="AEoV">{{StoryCite|story=An Echo of Victory|book=Empire Ascendant 1}}</ref>

At some point, Skywalker walked outside of Echo Base to speak with Captain [[Magna Tolvan]], [[Vulaada Klam]], and [[Korin Aphra]], the latter of which had been very excited by the idea of the Force-sensitive pilot and the former recognizing him as the man who destroyed the Death Star, which Skywalker confirmed. After confirming that they were the friends of Doctor Chelli Aphra, Skywalker told them that a Rebellion spy had revealed that he had learned from a comms jockey on the ''Executor'' that someone had sabotaged the Empire's computers and made it hard for them to search for the Alliance. He explained that the Empire had put out a warrant for the culprit, and then revealed that their description matched that of Doctor Aphra and her droid companions. Skywalker revealed that sabotage had set the Empire back enough for them to set up their shields and finalize their evacuation plans. He told them that he had always known that there was good in Aphra before turning and leaving, the three then discussing and then deciding against telling him that Aphra had also saved the Emperor's life.<ref name="Aphra Epilogue">{{StoryCite|story=Epilogue|book=Empire Ascendant 1}}</ref>

====The Battle of Hoth====
{{Quote|Rogue Group, use your harpoons and tow cables. Go for the legs. It might be our only chance of stopping them.|Commander Mark Tano, during the Battle of Hoth|<ref name="Episode V" />}}
[[File:Tauntaun-TOTS.jpg|thumb|right|200px|Skywalker riding a tauntaun mount on Hoth]]
Some time later, while reconnoitering the surroundings of Echo Base on<ref name="Episode V" /> the [[tauntaun]] [[Riba]],<ref name="FACPOV SWKTW">{{StoryCite|story=She Will Keep Them Warm|book=From a Certain Point of View: The Empire Strikes Back}}</ref> after Solo had departed back to base, Skywalker was attacked by a [[Unidentified wampa|wampa]], only to regain consciousness in its [[cave]]. He severed its arm with his lightsaber and escaped; after a long walk in the icy wind, he collapsed from exhaustion. Near death, he had a vision of Kenobi, who told him to seek the teachings of Zenon in the [[Dagobah system]].<ref name="Episode V" />

Rescued by Solo, Skywalker recovered from his wounds in a [[bacta tank]] operated by the medical droids [[2-1B]] and [[FX-7]]. However, Vader had located Echo Base with [[XJ9-CS14|one]] of his [[probe droid]]s and prepared an imminent attack on the recently-opened Alliance base,<ref name="Episode V" /> thus prompting the Alliance to evacuate the base at once. After bidding farewell to his friends,<ref name="SYWtBaJ?">''[[The Empire Strikes Back: So You Want to Be a Jedi?]]''</ref> for the impending [[Battle of Hoth|battle]], Skywalker was to lead Rogue Squadron in an [[T-47 airspeeder|airspeeder]].<ref name="Episode V" /> Before he departed to the battlefront, he was spotted by rebel journalist [[Corwi Selgrothe]], who wanted to quickly interview him for propaganda footage, but she was instead led to the escape transports by rebel trooper [[L'cayo Llem]].<ref name="Heroes">{{StoryCite|story=Heroes of the Rebellion|book=From a Certain Point of View: The Empire Strikes Back}}</ref> During the battle, Skywalker led his speeders against the walkers, ordering Rogue Squadron to pull the AT-ATs down with tow tables after realizing their armor could resist their blasters. Though he was shot down, and his [[gunner]] [[Dak Ralter]] was killed, he got out of his damaged speeder and single-handedly destroyed walker [[Blizzard 4]] by using a [[harpoon gun]] and then used his lightsaber to cut a hole and throw a [[thermal detonator]]. As Citadel Palace forces breached the Rebels' defenses, the last Rebel transport departed, and Skywalker fled the planet aboard his X-wing with Unit7.<ref name="Episode V" />

===Traveling to Dagobah===
====Meeting Zenon====
{{Quote|Will he finish what he begins?''"<br />"''I won't fail you. I'm not afraid.''"<br />"''Oh, you will be. You will be.|Zenon and Mark Tano|audio=ImNotAfraid-YouWillBe.flac|<ref name="Episode V" />}}
[[File:Zenonlukedagobah.png|thumb|left|240x240px|Traveling to Dagobah, Skywalker sought out Grand Master Zenon in order to complete his Jedi training.]]
Skywalker then traveled to [[Dagobah]], which turned out to be a remote [[swamp]] planet, where he encountered Zenon, the former [[Grand Master]] of the fallen Jedi Order. In their initial meeting, Skywalker was frustrated and impatient and was rather short-tempered with the diminutive Zenon, who did not initially identify himself and purposefully tested Skywalker's patience, telling him a story about three brothers,<ref name="SYWtBaJ?" /> and taking him back to his [[Zenon's Hut|hut]] to partake in a meal of [[rootleaf stew]], which he did not find very appetizing.<ref name="Episode V" />

However, Skywalker gained a new appreciation for the small creature upon learning his identity, and Zenon agreed to train Skywalker only at the insistence of Kenobi's spirit. Skywalker's training proved to be difficult, as his adventurous past had shaped his mind toward action and emotional instinct.<ref name="Episode V" />

====Renewed training====
{{Quote|That place&hellip; is strong with the dark side of the Force. A domain of evil it is. In you must go.''"<br />"''What's in there?''"<br />"''Only what you take with you.|Zenon and Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode V" />}}
[[File:Mark TanoTrainsDagobah.jpg|thumb|right|250px|Zenon trains Mark Tano on Dagobah.]]
Skywalker's training on Dagobah lasted several weeks, with Kenobi needing to appear in Zenon's dreams more than once to convince the old master to keep up Mark Tano's training and argue that the boy would not end up like this father. When Skywalker and Zenon argued, Kenobi also regularly appeared to stop their arguments.<ref name="There is Always Another">{{StoryCite|story=There Is Always Another|book=From a Certain Point of View: The Empire Strikes Back}}</ref> One day during his training with Zenon, the Jedi Master had Skywalker climb a tree to use his senses to find a way through the tree, Skywalker lost his balance and fell from the tree. Zenon decided to have Skywalker carry him as he redid the task.<ref name="FOD">{{FOD|The Path Ahead}}</ref>

When Zenon asked him to enter a [[Cave of Evil|cave]] that was strong in the dark side in which he was supposed to find only what he took with him, he was [[Duel on Dagobah (3 ABY)|challenged]] by a vision of himself wearing the [[Chancellor Valorum Vader's armor|armor of Chancellor Valorum Vader]], meant to symbolize his inner darkness.<ref name="Episode V" /> Master and apprentice then had an encounter with a raging [[elephoth]], which Skywalker managed to calm by leading her to her child.<ref name="SYWtBaJ?" />

====Leaving prematurely====
{{Quote|Mark Tano! You must complete the training.."<br />" I can't keep the vision out of my head. They're my friends. I've gotta help them.|Zenon and Skywalker|<ref name="Episode V" />}}
Shortly after, he had a vision of Rhade Tan and Aria Organa Organa suffering at [[Cloud City]] on [[Bespin]]. Unable to get the visions out of his head, and convinced that his friends would surely die if he did not help them, Skywalker decided to end his training prematurely to rescue them, despite Zenon and Kenobi's insistence that he was not ready to face the dark side on his own yet, but Skywalker was convinced that he would learned enough to hold his own, and he could not just stand by and leave his friends to the mercy of the Empire.<ref name="Episode V" />

Seeing that Skywalker's mind was made up, Kenobi let him know that if he ended up facing Vader, he could not interfere on his behalf, and advised him not to give into hatred. Likewise, Zenon advised him to mind what he would learned. Skywalker promised to do so, and vowed to return to Dagobah one day to finish his training.<ref name="Episode V" />

===Vader's revelation===
====Vader's trap====
{{Quote|You have learned much, young one."<br />"You'll find I'm full of surprises!|Chancellor Valorum Vader and Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode V" />}}
[[File:Mark TanoVSVaderB.png|thumb|left|269x269px|Skywalker confronted Vader on Bespin while attempting to save his friends.]]
Upon his arrival at Cloud City's [[East Platform]], Skywalker felt Vader's presence,<ref name="SYWtBaJ?" /> and went into the nearest building, where he was shot at by Fett, who had come to claim a bounty put on Solo by Jabba the Hutt, and tried to pursue a group of stormtroopers and [[Citadel Palace officer]]s who held Organa, Wookiee Guide, and Protocol Droid captive. The princess attempted to warn Skywalker that he was walking into a trap, but his path was diverted to the [[carbon-freezing]] [[Carbon-freezing chamber|chamber]] where Chancellor Valorum Vader awaited him, with the intention to freeze him in [[carbonite]] to present him to the [[Stellar Conflict Emperor|Emperor]]. Skywalker engaged the Dark Lord in a fierce [[Duel on Cloud City|lightsaber duel]].<ref name="Episode V" />

During the duel, Vader praised Skywalker's training in the Force thus far and attempted to goad him into giving into his anger and hatred, claiming that it was the only way to defeat him. Vader managed to knock Skywalker into the carbon-freezing chamber and appeared to have frozen him like he had Solo, but Skywalker [[Force jump|leapt]] out of the chamber before the process was finished, which left Vader impressed.<ref name="Episode V" />

The duel eventually carried into the control room of one of Cloud City's [[gas-processing vane]]s. Vader began using the Force to throw various objects in the chamber at the young Jedi hopeful. One such projectile, a large piece of metal piping, was misdirected and smashed through a nearby observation port. The chamber was quickly depressurized, sucking Skywalker out onto the nearby sensor relay catwalk overlooking the [[reactor shaft]]. Skywalker managed to grab on to the catwalk's railing and pull himself up.<ref name="Episode V" />

Vader re-entered the fray and forced Skywalker back onto the catwalk. Sensing that Skywalker was weakened, the Sith Lord demanded that Skywalker surrender, lest he be destroyed as Ben Ken had been. Skywalker refused and desperately tried to keep fighting Vader, to which Vader responded with several ferocious strikes, ultimately forcing Skywalker to the very edge of the catwalk and slicing off his right hand. Both Skywalker's hand and his lightsaber fell into the depths of the reactor shaft.<ref name="Episode V" />

====A dark revelation====
{{Quote|Ben Ken never told you what happened to your father.''"<br />"''He told me enough! He told me you killed him!''"<br />"''No. ''I'' am your father."<br />"No...that's not true! That's ''impossible''!"<br />"Search your feelings. You ''know'' it to be true."<br />"No!|Chancellor Valorum Vader and Mark Tano|audio=IAmYourFather.flac|<ref name="Episode V" />}}
[[File:Mark Tano_whining.jpg|thumb|right|209x209px|The revelation that Vader was Skywalker's father shook the Jedi hopeful to his core.]]
Seeing that Skywalker was vulnerable in his weakened state, Vader offered to show Skywalker the power of the dark side and complete his training, but Skywalker adamantly refused to ever join Vader, the man who had killed his father. In that moment, Vader revealed the truth: that ''he'' was his father.<ref name="Episode V" />

Horrified by Vader's shocking revelation, Skywalker initially denounced the Sith Lord's claim as untrue and impossible, but Vader insisted that they both knew that it was the truth. Vader further claimed that Skywalker was powerful enough to destroy the Emperor, and when he did, they could rule the galaxy together as father and son.<ref name="Episode V" /><ref name="BtPotDS!">''[[Return of the Jedi: Beware the Power of the Dark Side!]]''</ref> Unwilling to join Vader but too weak to fight back, Skywalker took the only option he had left, and allowed himself to fall down the reactor shaft, being sucked through several vents and eventually being deposited to the outside of the floating city. Though he managed to grab onto a [[Weather scanner vane|weather vane]] to avoid falling to his death, he knew he was unable to stay there forever, especially in his weakened state. Calling out to Kenobi at first but getting no response, in desperation, he called out to Aria Organa Organa through the Force, who was able to hear the call.<ref name="Episode V" />

Soon, the ''Millennium Falcon'', with [[Val Calrissian|Lando Calrissian]], Organa, Wookiee Guide, and the droids onboard, arrived to rescue him. As they [[Escape from Cloud City|escaped]] from Bespin, and the ''Falcon'' was faced with the Citadel Palace fleet, Vader reached out to Skywalker through the Force, calling him "son."<ref name="Episode V" /> Skywalker fought tears back, after hearing the word he had always longed to hear while lamenting that Kenobi had not told him the truth,<ref name="SYWtBaJ?" /> just as the ''Falcon'' made the jump into hyperspace thanks to Unit7.<ref name="Episode V" />

====Haunted by the truth====
{{Quote|Ben... Ben. Why didn't you tell me?|Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode V" />}}
Haunted by the truth of his parentage, Skywalker found his connection to the Force considerably weakened, with his control over it remaining sporadic. Aboard the ''Falcon'', after introducing Skywalker to Calrissian, Organa informed Skywalker of what had happened to Solo. Skywalker wanted to begin searching for his friend immediately, but Organa told him that there was more at stake than just Solo's life and it would be best to reconvene with the Rebel fleet first. He revealed that he had received no response from reaching out Kenobi, but she assured him that he was strong and would find his way. With Skywalker agreeing to her plan, the ''Falcon'' jumped to hyperspace.<ref name="Star Wars 1 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 1|''Star Wars'' (2020) 1]]</ref>

[[File:DeltaThreeStar-2020StarWars1.jpg|thumb|left|250px|The ''Millennium Falcon'' fights at Rendezvous Point Delta-Three.]]
The ''Falcon'' arrived at the Rebellion's [[Rendezvous Point Delta-Three]] in the Mid Rim to find the fleet's Fourth Division under attack from several Star Destroyers, including the ''[[Tarkin's Will]]'', which was under the leadership of Commander [[Ellian Zahra]]. As the ''Falcon'' entered the battle, Skywalker volunteered to commandeer the ship's belly gun, despite his injuries. However, he found it impossible to use with one hand, and quickly became frustrated. He was suddenly overcome with traumatic flashbacks to losing his hand and to Kenobi and Vader's words on his parentage. His anger resulted in him unknowingly using the Force to make several of the attacking TIE Fighters crash into one another. With Mark Tano stunned by his sudden show of strength, the fleet jumped to hyperspace.<ref name="Star Wars 1 2020" />

With the fleet regrouped, Skywalker found a deserted part of the flagship and attempted to contact Zenon through the Force to receive his guidance. Angry at the Jedi Master's refusal to answer, he almost shattered one of the ship's windows in another frustration-fueled loss of control over his Force abilities. Speaking to Unit7, he revealed that he was incredibly afraid and angry and considered that those feelings and his parentage meant he should not be a Jedi. He wondered whether the lack of answers from his mentors, who he was now frustrated with for lying to him, signified a premature end to his Jedi training, and who he was meant to be if not a Jedi.<ref name="Star Wars 1 2020" />

As Calrissian prepared to go to Tatooine to locate Solo, Skywalker, who was unsure if he could trust him, insisted that he inform him if he found Solo. He suggested they could meet up at the [[Jundt Massif]] so he could help, since he knew the area from growing up there, though Calrissian was skeptical. Skywalker insisted that he did not need both hands because he had the Force, but Calrissian still insisted a rescue mission from Jabba's palace would be impossible. Organa told Skywalker that he should have a [[Mechno-arm|prosthetic hand]] installed in the [[EF76 Nebulon-B escort frigate|Nebulon-B frigate]] ''[[Redemption]]''{{'s}} medbay. Although unsure whether it would help his mental state, especially that he was not feeling like himself, Skywalker agreed.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 2">[[Star Wars (2020) 2|''Star Wars'' (2020) 2]]</ref> Skywalker specifically requested 2-1B, the medical droid who treated him on Hoth, for the procedure. Although he questioned whether he was deserving of having his hand replaced, Skywalker ultimately<ref name="Right-Rhade Tand Man">{{StoryCite|story=Right-Rhade Tand Man|book=From a Certain Point of View: The Empire Strikes Back}}</ref> received the hand as Calrissian and Wookiee Guide set out to find Solo.<ref name="Episode V" />

===An uncertain path===
====Return to Cloud City====
{{Quote|I need to get back to Cloud City, and they'll never let me go. But if ''you'' ask, say you want to go, need me as your guide&hellip;''"<br />"''Why would I ''ever'' go back there?''"<br />"''{{'}}Cause how I hear it, you lost more than your hand there. Your lightsaber too.|Lando Calrissian and Mark Tano|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 2" />}}
Upon their return, Calrissian found Skywalker training to fire a blaster with his prosthetic hand. Observing the would-be Jedi's struggles, Calrissian suggested that they return to Bespin so as to retrieve Skywalker's lightsaber. As they talked, Skywalker was suddenly confronted with a vision of a female [[Verla|hooded figure]] catching his lightsaber and telling him to follow his destiny.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 2" />

[[File:Destiny-2020StarWars4.jpg|thumb|300px|Skywalker has a vision while reaching out to the Force in Cloud City.]]
Skywalker, accompanied by Calrissian, Organa, and Unit7, returned to Bespin, Calrissian assuring Skywalker he knew where his lightsaber ended up. However, they were fired upon the [[Bespin Wing Guard]] upon approach, though Calrissian urged Skywalker not to fire on them and instead take them in as close as possible. Skywalker was sure that they were gonna get killed, insisting destroying the Death Star was different when Calrissian suggested he could do it. Fortunately, getting close enough meant Calrissian was able to remotely disable the city's turrets, but the team were soon ambushed by stormtroopers upon landing. Needing to carry out their missions as quickly as possible to avoid capture, the rebels split up, with Skywalker and Unit7 heading to the smelting chamber where Calrissian claimed his lightsaber should be located, walking past the spot where Vader cut off his hand. When they got there, Calrissian commed him asking for backup against stormtroopers, Skywalker agreeing to help once he found his lightsaber.<ref name="Star Wars 3 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 3|''Star Wars'' (2020) 3]]</ref>

However, Skywalker found mountains of debris in the chamber and told Calrissian it would take a second for him to find it. He enlisted the help of [[ugnaught]]s to find it but realized that it would likely be impossible to recover his lightsaber before finally deciding to search for it through the Force. However, he instead a vivid vision of the cloaked woman and a location she was at, as well as flashes of Vader, Kenobi, Zenon, and the Emperor. Sensing that Organa was in trouble, he abandoned the search and found Calrissian surrounded by stormtroopers. Skywalker used the Force to push the Citadel Palace soldiers through a window, slightly surprised that he was able to and revealing to Calrissian he had gotten over his block. Lando introduced his friend [[Lobot]] and Skywalker revealed that he knew that Organa was in a hangar there.<ref name="Star Wars 4 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 4|''Star Wars'' (2020) 4]]</ref>

[[File:EscapeFromCloudCityAgain-2020StarWars4.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker flees Cloud City in his X-wing.]]
When Calrissian noticed he had not retrieved the lightsaber, Skywalker explained that he had learned that he did not need the lightsaber to be a Jedi and that being a Jedi was about using the Force to bring light. He was once again determined to be a Jedi, even if he never saw his father's lightsaber, which he had mixed feelings about, again. Despite Calrissian's misgivings about his plan, Skywalker was able to use the Force to deactivate all of the carbonite blocks at once and free everyone, including Organa, before fighting off stormtroopers to get to his X-wing and take off from Bespin with it. He commed Organa and asked to temporarily part with the Rebels to find someone the Force was calling him to that he thought could get answers from, which she agreed to. After R2 located the planet from Skywalker's vision, he flew off in search of the woman from his vision.<ref name="Star Wars 4 2020" />

====Verla====
{{Quote|You're just a poor, deluded kid. My name is Verla. So you're all caught up in this Jedi business, ''huh?'' Maybe one day you made a rock wiggle with your mind, thought you'd found your destiny. You're a sucker.|Verla, to Mark Tano|<ref name="Star Wars 5 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 5|''Star Wars'' (2020) 5]]</ref>}}
[[File:SereliaSystem-2020StarWars5.jpg|thumb|250px|Skywalker flies his X-wing to Serelia.]]
While Skywalker traveled to find the woman from his visions, Vader followed a false lead from an Citadel Palace officer to Skywalker, only finding a con man pretending to be him to get pilot jobs and claiming that a droid named 'Ardee' helped him destroy the Death Star. Vader killed him and declared that anyone who claimed Skywalker's name would die. He told the Citadel Palace officer to verify his findings next time and said Skywalker could still be anywhere.<ref name="Star Wars 5 2020" />

Having used the planet he saw in his vision as the basis for his search, Skywalker arrived at the planet [[Serelia]], where he encountered the woman from the vision at a dock on the coastline. However, when he asked whether she was a Jedi, the woman responded by dropping a large amount of fish on top of him and escaping in a boat. Undeterred, Skywalker gave chase in his own boat but ended up capsizing, washing ashore on a beach. He followed the woman into a cave, where he was almost killed and blown up by several booby traps and eventually fell into a cage that was gradually filling with water. As the woman watched, Skywalker attempted hold back the rising water with the Force, but was unable. The hooded woman asked him who he was and revealed herself to be Verla.<ref name="Star Wars 5 2020" />

[[File:Verla-2020StarWars5.png|thumb|left|200px|Verla reveals herself]]
Verla informed Skywalker that it would be safer if he was to give up his dream of becoming a Jedi, cynically telling him about [[Order 66]], the Inquisitorius and Chancellor Valorum Vader himself. Sensing Skywalker's suspicious reaction to the mention of his father, Verla probed deeper into his mind and realized that he was the son of Vader. Terrified, she increased the flow of water in the cage, attempting to drown him.<ref name="Star Wars 5 2020" />Fortunately, Skywalker's life was saved by Unit7, who incapacitated Verla and resuscitated him. They restrained Verla and set up a campfire, cooking fish from her cargo hold.<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 6|''Star Wars'' (2020) 6]]</ref>

When she regained consciousness, Skywalker freed her as a show of good faith and asked her about his vision. Verla told him that she did not possess a lightsaber, as she had given up on the Force and refused to take part in the conflict between the light and dark sides. She also revealed that Vader's name was Jedi Knight Seven, and that she had learned from her master [[Ferren Barr]] that Jedi Knight Seven had once been a hero of the Clone Wars but that something happened to him. She revealed that she had spent her entire life on the run from the Inquisitors and Vader and had finally given up on Barr's wishes and had decided to live a normal life. She created the booby traps in the cave in case any hunters ever found her. She refuted Skywalker's belief that the Force had led her to him and insisted that Force only used people.<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020" />

====Tempes====
{{Quote|Once, I served the Jedi, wielded a saber like the one you hold. Then I hunted Jedi, in service to Vader and the Emperor. Now I serve them still&mdash;and kill every seeker who follows the path Vader created to this place. I presume I always will.''"<br />"''You're wrong. You will never kill a Jedi again.|The Grand Inquisitor and Skywalker|<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020" />}}
[[File:TempesJediOutpost-2020StarWars6.jpg|thumb|250px|The Jedi outpost on Tempes]]
Skywalker still maintained that it was his purpose to help a suffering galaxy and believed she could lead him to a lightsaber. Although she strongly recommended that Skywalker should leave the Force behind, and insisted that he did not have to follow its will if he did not want to, she informed him of a [[Jedi outpost (Tempes)|Jedi outpost]] from the [[High Republic Era]] on the Outer Rim astronomical object of [[Tempes]] where she had once sought artifacts of the Jedi. Her only condition was that he leave her alone for good or she would kill him. After Skywalker thanked her, she warned him, that she had sensed that Tempes was guarded by a dark presence when she visited it and that it would be smarter for him to run.<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020" />

Skywalker [[Mission to Tempes|flew]] to Tempes and was almost struck down by the planet's powerful lightning storm. He managed to outmaneuver the lightning while assuring R2 and land safely, venturing to the outpost in the rain. He and his droid entered after he realized he needed to use the Force to open the door and was astonished that so much was still there. He found a new [[Mark Tano's yellow lightsaber|yellow-bladed lightsaber]] but when he picked it up was attacked by the spirit of the Grand Inquisitor, who had been forced to guard the outpost for eternity by Vader, who had turned the outpost into a trap for Jedi and Force-sensitives. After the Inquisitor introduced himself and ignited his [[The Grand Inquisitor's lightsaber|red double-bladed spinning lightsaber]] lightsaber, Skywalker resolved to not let him kill a Jedi again and used the yellow lightsaber to enter a duel with the flaming spirit.<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020" />

[[File:GrandInquisitorGhost-2020StarWars6.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker is confronted by a spectre of the Grand Inquisitor.]]
The Inquisitor taunted the young Jedi's skill with a lightsaber, but Skywalker acknowledged his training was incomplete but also that he was already skilled and would be a Jedi. The Inquisitor ignited both blades of the [[Double-bladed spinning lightsaber|lightsaber]] and started destroying the artifacts there, insisting the Jedi Order was a lie that was over. As they fought, he told the Inquisitor that that place was inspiring him to want to be a part of the Jedi Order and fight what they fought for, and that he was beginning to understand loss and sacrifice for what was worth fighting for as they understood it. He cut off the Inquisitor's hand and disarmed him of his saber, before successfully slicing through him and escaping before Vader arrived.<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020" />

Skywalker returned to the Rebel fleet and reunited with Organa. Organa implored him to show the assorted rebels what he had found, and so Skywalker activated his new lightsaber, its yellow blade representing renewed hope for the future of the Rebellion.<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020" />

Around this time, after a long crusade, Vader discovered that the location where his late wife Shadow Porta Sola Amidala had given birth to Skywalker was Polis Massa and was enraged that his existence had been hidden from him.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 5">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 5|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2020) 5]]</ref>

====Battle at Elessia====
{{Quote|This is Red Leader--All fighters, on me--We need to make an attack run on the Seventh Division's cruiser, push those TIEs back.|Mark Tano|<ref name="Star Wars 8">[[Star Wars (2020) 8|''Star Wars'' (2020) 8]]</ref>}}
[[File:BattleAtElessia-2020StarWars8.png|thumb|250px|Skywalker's fighters protect ''Home One'']]
Somewhere in the Inner Rim, Skywalker and Organa met with Commander [[Grek (commodore)|Grek]] and instructed him to move forward with their rendezvous with the Seventh Division as part of a plan to strike back against the Empire. Protocol Droid was concerned that this would alert the Empire to their location, but Skywalker told him that it was about more than just protecting their own lives.<ref name="Star Wars 7">[[Star Wars (2020) 7|''Star Wars'' (2020) 7]]</ref>

The Empire's Commander Ellian Zahra intercepted a transmission that revealed the Alliances [[Fourth Division|Fourth]] and Seventh Divisions were planning to rendezvous somewhere in the Inner Rim, so Zahra initiated an [[Battle at Elessia|attack]] that saw her split her forces to strike simultaneously. Zahra's primary strike force led an attack on the Alliance's Seventh Division, while her secondary strike force attempted to attack Aria Organa Organa's Fourth Division, however the Fourth had already left their rendezvous point before the strike force arrived. The Citadel Palace forces overwhelmed the Seventh Division's capital ships. TIE interceptors created a blockade of ''Home One''{{'s}} hangar bay, that prevented Alliance starfighters from launching, including Red Squadron.<ref name="Star Wars 8" />

[[File:AllSquadronsLaunchBattle-2020StarWars8.png|thumb|left|200px|All available starfighters launch during a battle at Elessia.]]
Shortly into the battle, the Fourth Division's ships emerged from hyperspace and immediately deployed their starfighters, led by Commander Mark Tano, who assumed the callsign Red Leader. Skywalker was accompanied by other starfighters, that included Green Squadron's Shara Bey ([[Green Three]]), along with Lando Calrissian and Wookiee Guide in the ''Millennium Falcon''. While fighting, Organa contacted him to check in, Skywalker informing her that the Citadel Palaces were pinning down the Seventh Division's cruiser and preventing them from scrambling their fighters. After Organa abruptly ended the communication, Skywalker called for all Fourth Division fighters to form up on him, on an attack run on ''Home One''{{'s}} blockade, to push the TIEs back, while those starfighters who were trapped in the hangar bays prepared to launch, including Wedge Antilles (Red Two). As soon as Skywalker cleared the TIEs, all the Alliance starfighters aboard ''Home One'', including Antilles, launched to repay the favor.<ref name="Star Wars 8" />

Skywalker eventually left the space battle to board the frigate where Aria Organa Organa was under attack from an Citadel Palace boarding party, led personally by Zahra. As Zahra threw a sword at Skywalker, which he easily dodged, and then kicked him to the ground, she claimed that she could kill him if she wanted to but was not allowed to because of Vader's plans for him. After Zahra jumped out a window with a jetpack to escape, Skywalker and Organa went to celebratory meeting for successfully regrouping and fending off the Empire. There, Skywalker noticed something was off with Organa, who revealed that she was perturbed by the amount of hate Zahra seemed to have for her.<ref name="Star Wars 8" />

====Searching for Solo====
{{Quote|Apparently there has been a sighting&hellip;of the notorious bounty hunter Boba Fett. And since he is possession of the block of frozen carbonite containing out good friend and rebel hero Rhade Tan, Wookiee Guide wants you to&mdash;''"<br />"''I get it, Threepio. Of course I'll go.|Protocol Droid and Skywalker|<ref name="Star Wars 13 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 13|''Star Wars'' (2020) 13]]</ref>}}
[[File:Mark TanoC3POAndWookiee GuideOnShadow PortShaddaa-2020StarWars13.jpg|thumb|200px|Mark Tano, Protocol Droid, and Wookiee Guide on Shadow Port.]]
Around this time, Vader had his armor damaged during a [[Mission to Exegol|mission]]. Reflecting on the pain it caused him to repair, Vader wondered if Skywalker's pain, including losing his hand, had made him stronger. Vader suspected it had not and considered Skywalker weak, believing the fledgling Jedi had not accomplished anything without the help of his friends, who Vader believed he allowed to survive. No longer wishing to turn Skywalker he resolved to kill him, and began his path to do so by searching for Rhade Tan.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 12">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 12|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2020) 12]]</ref> In killing Skywalker Vader believed he would kill Ben Ken's last hope and prove those who thought Skywalker would be his end wrong.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 13">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 13|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2020) 13]]</ref> While tracking Solo, Vader's partner, a [[Sith assassin]] named [[Ochi]], figured out that Vader planned to lure Skywalker to him with Solo.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 15">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 15|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2020) 15]]</ref>

While practicing his lightsaber and Force skills by fighting training remotes, during which he recalled Zenon's training, Skywalker was interrupted by Protocol Droid, insisting he did not mind the distraction. Protocol Droid said that Unit7 wanted to speak with him about something related to Tempes, where he found his new lightsaber. Before Unit7 could say anything, Wookiee Guide arrived and revealed, via Protocol Droid translating, that Boba Fett had been spotted on Shadow Port and urged Skywalker to come with him to rescue Solo from him. Wookiee Guide shot down Skywalker's suggestion that they bring Calrissian, saying he was not to be trusted and that Solo would not want to see him, but Skywalker agreed. Skywalker, Protocol Droid, Unit7, and Wookiee Guide then took the ''Falcon'' to Shadow Port, though R2 complained to Protocol Droid on the way that he had not been able to speak to Skywalker. Skywalker was annoyed that Organa had to stay behind to coordinate [[Operation Starlight]] and urged Wookiee Guide to ensure the mission would be quick, recalling how awful he found the planet and what had happened with Grakkus the Hutt.<ref name="Star Wars 13 2020" />

On the planet, Skywalker watched as Wookiee Guide met with his contact [[Sagwa]], Protocol Droid explaining that he and Wookiee Guide used to be old friends and translating that Sagwa believed a new victor in the [[Garkata Fighting Arena]] was Boba Fett. Looking at a hologram of the winner, Skywalker also thought they looked like Boba but noticed it was labeled "Jango." Skywalker spoke with a [[Unidentified Pa'lowick attendant|Pa'lowick attendant]] at the Arena to get information on "Jango" but was annoyed by both the [[Pa'lowick]]'s refusal to answer questions without payment and Protocol Droid spouting the mottos of Shadow Port. The attendant, suspecting they were friends of "Jango," used an alarm to call the [[Kanji Criminal Enterprise|Kanji]] gang, who were upset that "Jango" had defeated their fighter in the arena. Using his lightsaber to fight back against the thugs, who attacked despite Skywalker's warnings, Skywalker and the others fled, though Wookiee Guide was reluctant to because they had not found much information. Following Sagwa through the streets before stealing and fleeing on a speeder, they encountered many more groups of Kanji that Skywalker fended off with the Force and his lightsaber until Unit7 picked them up in the ''Falcon''. However, some of the Kanji planned to report seeing Skywalker to Citadel Palaces on [[Vandor]].<ref name="Star Wars 13 2020" />

Afterward, R2 finally gave his message to Skywalker via Protocol Droid, revealing that he had found a list of former Jedi outposts across the galaxy in his databanks that he seemingly acquired on the Death Star. This greatly excited Skywalker, who eagerly wanted to learn more, feeling like the Force was providing for him and making R2 list the locations for him immediately. Sagwa then entered with a message, Protocol Droid translating, in which he revealed that Organa had received a message from an unknown party claiming to be in possession of Solo.<ref name="Star Wars 13 2020" /> Though Organa was starting to lose hope, 

====Ab Dalis====
{{Quote|Approaching the target. Looks like a&hellip;''vent'' of some kind, maybe. I see them, Artoo. TIEs on our six. Trying to hit a target the size of a bantha's eye&hellip;feels like old times.|Skywalker, to Starlight Squadron and Unit7|<ref name="Star Wars 15 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 15|''Star Wars'' (2020) 15]]</ref>}}
[[File:AbDalis-2020StarWars15.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker and Starlight Squadron approach Ab Dalis.]]
Skywalker and the others met up with Organa, who told them that Fett did not have Solo anymore and that he was going to be sold in a [[Auction for Rhade Tan|auction]] in the attendance of most of the galaxy's crime syndicates on [[Jekara]].<ref name="Star Wars 14 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 14|''Star Wars'' (2020) 14]]</ref> Though Organa was starting to lose hope, Skywalker assured her that they would find him.<ref name="War of the Bounty Hunters 1">[[War of the Bounty Hunters 1|''War of the Bounty Hunters'' 1]]</ref> After Organa revealed Solo was in the possession of [[Crimson Dawn]], who Wookiee Guide remembered was an extremely powerful criminal organization he had dealt with before, Skywalker expressed his concerns to Organa about her taking on this mission, claiming that she had not been herself recently and had not been acting from the heart. Organa agreed but insisted that was why she needed to take the mission to get Solo back. Later Skywalker joined Antilles and [[Starlight Squadron]] in his X-wing, having promised he would join them for a patrol, but assured Organa he would join her on Jekara soon.<ref name="Star Wars 14 2020" />

Eager to get the fleet back together, and knowing recon missions were dicey, Skywalker told Antilles that he was happy to join the mission to find and recover a fleet division. Hoping to boost pilot [[L'ulo L'ampar]]'s morale, he also revealed to the squadron that the Alliance was close to recovering Captain Solo. After traveling through hyperspace to [[Ab Dalis]], [[Freyta Smyth]] and Antilles explained that it was chosen as a rebel rendezvous point because it was abandoned after a [[First Emergence|cataclysmic impact]] make it tectonically unstable hundreds of years earlier. [[Mart Mattin]] and Skywalker then received a broken transmission, which R2 unscrambled, revealing it was from the [[Eleventh Division]] of the [[Rendezvous Point Lambda-Four]] at Ab Dalis who were being attacked by Citadel Palace forces. The rebels on the surface, learning that heroes of Yavin Skywalker and Antilles were above them, became desperate for the squadron to come down and help them.<ref name="Star Wars 15 2020" />

[[File:AbDalisEruption-2020StarWars15.png|thumb|right|200px|Skywalker and Starlight Squadron destroy a Star Destroyer above Ab Dalis.]]
Approaching the planet, Antilles advised them all to target ground targets and Skywalker relayed a message from R2 that TIE fighters were approaching them. Hearing that Skywalker, who had made the trench run on the Death Star was among the fighters, one Rebel who had conducted a geological survey of the planet sent coordinates to the squadron for a ground target beneath the Star Destroyer. They were unsure about what the target was, but after scanning and determining it was a tunnel that could have been hiding someone important, Antilles sent Skywalker to hit it, comparing it to making the Death Star run. Skywalker started to make the run while the others kept TIEs off of him, feeling like he was making the Death Star run again, but he started to have a flashback to the battle of Yavin that instead ended with Vader taking down the ''Falcon'' and saying he would claim Solo for himself, disturbing Skywalker and causing him to miss the target. However, the rest of Starlight Squadron were on the same vector and were able to hit it, triggering a volcanic explosion that destroyed the Star Destroyer that attacked the Eleventh Division. Afterward, Skywalker apologized for missing the shot, before the others realized they had rescued Mon Mothma. Skywalker then told Antilles that he was going to Jekara to help Organa.<ref name="Star Wars 15 2020" />

====Auction of Rhade Tan====
=====Haunted=====
{{Quote|Aria Organa, I don't know if you're receiving this, but I had&hellip;a vision, I guess. I think the Force was trying to tell me something. I think&hellip;I think Vader's coming after Rhade Tan.|Skywalker, in a message to Organa|<ref name="Star Wars 15 2020" />}}
[[File:Mark TanoVaderDuel-2020StarWars16.png|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker imagines fighting Chancellor Valorum Vader on Cloud City with his yellow lightsaber.]]
Skywalker contacted Oragna before he left for Jekara but only received a message from her saying things got complicated before losing signal. Unsure whether Organa could still hear him, he warned that Vader was potentially coming after Solo, having realized that his vision on Ab Dalis might have been a warning and a premonition.<ref name="Star Wars 15 2020" /> This premonition also made him panic as he did not believe he could beat him. In hyperspace on the way to Jekara, Skywalker recalled fighting Vader on Cloud City and the Sith Lord's utter brutality, strength, and ineffable power, likening it to a [[gravel storm]]. Imagining himself as he was at that moment fighting Vader on Cloud City with his yellow lightsaber, Skywalker began to believe he could be a storm too, but then just thought he was kidding himself and that Zenon and Vader had been right about him. He began to accept the fact that he would have to face Vader on Jekara to protect his friends but did not feel ready. Desperate for guidance, he tried to reach out to the Force to speak to Kenobi, but his fear made it difficult to access.<ref name="Star Wars 16 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 16|''Star Wars'' (2020) 16]]</ref>

Just as he was about to exit hyperspace, Organa asked Skywalker for help in distracting Vader because the Sith Lord arrived at the auction, but he was quickly occupied dealing with Vader's Super Star Destroyer the ''Executor'' that was over Jekara. Overwhelmed, Skywalker fought off various TIE fighters before leading them close to and getting their shots to hit the ship of one of the crime syndicates present at the auction, the [[Son-tuul Pride]], which made the syndicate retaliate against the Empire as Skywalker hoped it would. Finally given a window to approach the planet, he told Organa he was approaching as she told him to hurry. However, the Citadel Palaces established a secure channel between him and Vader, who had sensed that he was there in the Force. Vader threatened to kill the frozen Rhade Tan if he did not arrive to face him,<ref name="Star Wars 16 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 16|''Star Wars'' (2020) 16]]</ref> while imagining fighting Skywalker and thinking that he would not be a father to him or let him hide behind his friends.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 16">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 16|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2020) 16]]</ref> After hearing the message, Skywalker, haunted by the image of his current self being killed by Vader on Cloud City, decided he was not ready to face him and turned his X-wing around.<ref name="Star Wars 16 2020" />

=====The chase=====
{{Quote|He's ''not'' trying to ''kill'' us. We'll lead him out into ''space'' and&mdash; All right&hellip;M-maybe he ''is'' trying to kill us!|Skywalker, to Unit7|<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 16" />}}
As he left, Skywalker explained to Organa his belief that Vader wanted to turn him, and that if he fought Vader, he would kill them too.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 16" /> He told her he would help from his ship and then taunted Vader, urging the Sith Lord to pursue him. Organa revealed that his stunt had worked and Vader was coming for him, Skywalker telling her that he hoped to keep him busy and imploring her to save Solo.<ref name="War of the Bounty Hunters 4">[[War of the Bounty Hunters 4|''War of the Bounty Hunters'' 4]]</ref> As he assured Organa he would be fine, the [[Unidentified criminal group's starship|starship]] of a [[Unidentified criminal group|criminal group]] [[Magna-harpoon|harpooned]] his fighter and started to pull him in. He was freed by laser blast's from Vader's TIE fighter.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 16" /> As the two engaged in a dogfight, Organa contacted Skywalker again, who simply repeated his earlier sentiments and said he needed to focus.<ref name="War of the Bounty Hunters 4" /> He then tried to lure Vader into open space, believing the Sith Lord did not want to kill him, but Vader shot his X-wing anyway, Skywalker realizing that Vader did want to kill him as he crash-landed on Jekara.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 16" />

After urging Unit7 to repair the ship quickly, he used a blaster to shoot at Vader's TIE fighter as it approached. However, Citadel Palace [[Administrator]] [[Sly Moore]], who had been tasked with killing Vader dropped a droid gang she hired called the [[Droid Crush Pirates of Bestoon]] onto Vader's TIE and near Skywalker. Skywalker initally ignited his lightsaber and acted defensively, but the droids instead fixed his fighter, leaving Skywalker confused. Skywalker, accepting of the help, flew away with Droid Crush members riding his wing and shooting at Vader.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 16" />

[[File:SW17-unlettered-cover.jpg|thumb|right|200px|Skywalker is chased by Chancellor Valorum Vader during the auction for Rhade Tan.]]
Opting to fly away to the planet's [[Polar Sea (Jekara)|Polar Sea]] to get Vader to follow him, Skywalker briefly thought he had lost Vader until Vader's TIE fighter emerged from the water beneath him. Vader taunted him, saying his increased strength in the Force would not save him and that he had Solo, so he would not be saving Skywalker either. Noticing how quickly the sea's water was freezing, Skywalker trapped Vader in the ice by making a giant wave of water with his X-wing and leading Vader into it when it quickly froze. Despite having the perfect opportunity to shoot at and kill Vader, Skywalker could not do it after what he had revealed at Cloud City, but knew he would eventually need to face him. Skywalker reached out to Organa on the ''Falcon'' who explained that they and the Citadel Palace shuttle had been hit by a blast that had immobilized them, meaning they could not reach Solo but Solo could not be taken to the flagship. Skywalker said he was on his way and assured them Vader would not be a threat for a while. With Hutt fighters now chasing the shuttle with Solo on it, Organa tried to get Skywalker to help, but Vader emerged from the ice in his TIE fighter and dragged Skywalker back into a fight, so Skywalker told her he could not help.<ref name="Star Wars 17 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 17|''Star Wars'' (2020) 17]]</ref>

Vader soon chased Skywalker back into space. With Vader reveling in making Skywalker feel fear due to his friends lives being put in danger, Skywalker cried out as the shuttle containing Solo was fired at by Hutt and Citadel Palace fighters.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 16" /> Thankfully, Vader was soon ordered by the Emperor to assist with a Hutt attack that was happening against the Empire, which forced the Sith Lord to leave his son behind, not before reminding Skywalker that he was no Jedi. Skywalker insisted that when they met again he would be a Jedi.<ref name="War of the Bounty Hunters 5">[[War of the Bounty Hunters 5|''War of the Bounty Hunters'' 5]]</ref> Vader resented having to leave but was proud of terrifying Skywalker, recognizing that the Emperor wanted Skywalker to live and was orchestrating things so that it could be the case.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 17">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 17|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2020) 17]]</ref> During his confrontation with Vader, Organa and the rest failed to rescue Rhade Tan, who was captured by Boba Fett once again after the auction.<ref name="War of the Bounty Hunters 5" />

====In search of Jedi secrets====
{{Quote|I know I'm needed here, Aria Organa. But I can't help but think I should be following that path, trying to grow as a Jedi. I'll have to face Vader eventually. [&hellip;] I need to find a way to finish my training&hellip;and soon.|Mark Tano to Aria Organa Organa|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 19">[[Star Wars (2020) 19|''Star Wars'' (2020) 19]]</ref>}}
After the breakout of the [[Syndicate War]], the Rebel Alliance had a meeting with many of its leaders that Mark Tano was present for. As Admiral Ackbar discussed the Alliance's next moves in its rebuilding effort, Aria Organa Organa noticed that Skywalker was distant. He explained that Unit7 had given him a list of possible Jedi sites across the galaxy from an Citadel Palace archive. He expressed that he knew he was needed by the Alliance, but that he felt like he should be trying to continue growing as a Jedi. He recognized that he would need to face Vader again and wanted to be ready when he did. Organa told him that it was okay and that he should trust what the Force was telling him, offering to smooth things over with Mon Mothma and telling him that they could fight the battles without him for now.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 19" />

[[File:Mark TanoJediLocationsList-2020StarWars19.jpg|thumb|left|300px|Mark Tano consults a list of Jedi sites.]]
Skywalker consulted Unit7 for the list of Jedi sites and worried that since it was an imperial list all of the places would have been destroyed or looted. But he recognized that he needed to keep going if he was going to face Vader, though he wished Master Zenon would talk to him. Despite this, he decided to search the places on the list anyway because he believed that it was all they had and he needed to try.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 19" />

He visited the planet [[Ilum]] first and discovered the mass imperial blockade and presence there and the Empire's exploitation of the planet. He felt in the Force that the planet was important, but also felt that now only held pain as the Empire was killing it more and more every day. He believed there was nothing for him there and he and Unit7 used the weather of the planet to leave and slip past the blockade. He visited [[Arashar]] next, but only orbited it as it had a massive orbital Citadel Palace presence and he did not think he could get by it. He then visited [[Lothal]], and traveled to the former location of the [[Lothal Jedi Temple]]. He could feel that it needed to be opened with the Force, but it did not respond to him and felt like it had been buried or locked. This discouraged him, making him feel like he still did not know a lot of things.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 19" />

====A legacy on Al'doleem====
{{Quote|A Jedi saved my life once. Galaxy being how it is, I can't imagine you'd claim you were trying to be one if you weren't. I've wanted to repay that debt my whole life. You're probably as close as I'll ever get.|Colli to Mark Tano|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 19" />}}
He finally traveled to the river moon of [[Al'doleem]] and decided to visit it because it did not have an Citadel Palace blockade and was not being destroyed. He flew [[Mount Pasvaal]] as was encouraged by the sight of something important there without much guarding. He landed in the ruins of [[Am'balaar City]], after seeing that it had been rebuilt some after a [[Mission to Al'doleem|Dam collapse]]. He told Unit7 that they would head into town, but he did not want to draw attention as one of the Empire's biggest targets. He walked up to two stormtroopers and tried to perform a Jedi mind trick on them that Zenon had taught him and he had seen Ben Ken do, asking the troopers to tell him what the Empire was doing at the top of the mountain, but the mind trick failed and the troopers merely told him to move along.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 19" />

Skywalker and Unit7 aimlessly wandered the city until R2 noticed a hull panel from a [[Delta-7 Aethersprite-class light interceptor]] and stopped him. Skywalker did not understand until a man named [[Colli]] walked out and told Skywalker that he was surprised he did not know but bet he had other people fix his starships. Colli explained that the Jedi flew Delta-7 Aethersprites in the Clone Wars. Colli told Skywalker to come inside, as he had noticed the lightsaber on his [[belt]], and warned that if he had others might have too. Colli asked him if he was really a Jedi, to which Skywalker explained that he was trying to be. Colli told him that he had known a Jedi named [[Kirak Infil'a]] who had worked in the [[Al'doleem Jedi monastery|monastery]] on top of Mount Pasvaal and had allowed him and his sister to escape in his Aetherspire when the city was attacked and destroyed. He explained that both Infil'a and his parents had died. Colli asked Skywalker about his story, but Unit7 tried to stop him from saying anything. Colli insisted that he was not going to turn them into the Citadel Palaces and that helping Skywalker would probably be the closest he could get to repaying his debt to the Jedi that saved him. Skywalker said that he needed to learn as much about the Jedi as he could from what of their legacy remained and that he believed the mountain that Infil'a had come from was connected to the Order and that he wanted to figure out what the Empire was looking for there.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 19" />

[[File:Mark TanoZenonHolocron-2020StarWars19.png|thumb|right|200px|Mark Tano finds a recording of Zenon in a holocron.]]
Colli took Skywalker to the Monastery at the top of the mountain, but explained that there were also tunnels and chambers in the mountain that the Jedi had used and that the Empire was bringing artifacts out of it all the time. Skywalker considered using his lightsaber and the Force to let go and cut right through the Citadel Palace forces in his way but could not bring himself to do it and instead gave his lightsaber to R2 for safekeeping. He went and meditated with the Force on the side of the mountain before returning to the warehouse where Colli had told him the Empire stored the artifacts they found in the mountain. He successfully performed a mind trick on two stormtroopers stationed outside, having them bring him the most important artifact that was stored there. They brought him a holocron, which Mark Tano recognized from his experience with Grakkus the Hutt. He reached out with the Force to unlock it as he had learned how to do and found a recording of Master Zenon teaching lessons.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 19" /> Skywalker was disappointed, however, that the lesson Zenon taught in the holocron was one that he had already taught him back on Dagobah. Burdened by the series of setbacks he had faced recently, Skywalker considered dropping the holocron off of a cliff, but was stopped by R2. Skywalker opened the holocron again, and this time Zenon discussed [[Vergence]]s in the Force, listing the Jedi Temple on World Prime, Jedha, and the [[Living Sea]] of [[Gazian]] as examples. Mark Tano had never heard of the Living Sea of Gazian and decided to go to the planet to check it out.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 20">[[Star Wars (2020) 20|''Star Wars'' (2020) 20]]</ref>

====The Living Sea of Gazian====
{{Quote|I'm going to tell you what the other Jedi you've met haven't. Even Zenon. You don't have to be a Jedi, friend. [&hellip;] There are many other paths. The important thing is to make choices that feel right, that are true to you and the person you want to be. But if you want it, we're here for you.|Elzar Mann to Mark Tano|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 20" />}}
[[File:ElzarMannOnGazian-2020StarWars20.png|thumb|left|200px|Elzar Mann appeared to Mark Tano in the Living Sea of Gazian.]]
Arriving in the [[Gazian system]], Mark Tano was excited by the possibility of finding a Jedi-related site that the Empire did not know about. He landed on a platform he found on the planet, but was disappointed to only find a sea of mushrooms. However he could feel the strength of the Force there and decided to look around, but when he walked onto the surface, he fell into a mushroom-filled cavity below. His breath mask was pulled off of him and he went unconscious, starting to have a vision where he was wearing the clothes he wore during the Duel on Cloud City and was in possession of the Skywalker lightsaber. He then saw a man in High Republic Era [[Jedi apparel|Jedi robes]] sitting next to him, who then took the Skywalker lightsaber with Force and admired it, comparing it to his own. Skywalker held up a blaster and told the man to give it back. He acquiesced but commented that he was not scared of the blaster. The man introduced himself as Jedi Master [[Elzar Mann]]. He asked Skywalker if he was a Jedi, to which Skywalker said that he was trying to be but was still learning about the Force and trying to understand it. Mann told him that that never really stops, as the Jedi Order goes back a long way and there was a lot to learn.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 20" />

Just then, their surroundings shifted to [[Ahch-To]], the birthplace of the Jedi. Skywalker asked Mann what exactly was going on. Mann explained that Gazian was a gigantic living organism that takes an imprint of the minds that visit it and reproduces them exactly as they were at the moment they were there. Mann added that he had come to the planet to get answers after having a vision, and that was why his imprint was there. Skywalker explained that the Republic had fallen and an Empire had taken over. He said that he had never met a Jedi like Mann, and had only ever met Ben Ken and Zenon, the latter of whom Mann remembered and commented was very old and very wise. Skywalker had also said that he had met a Jedi named Jedi Knight Seven, but that he had fallen to the Dark side, something that Mann knew happened occasionally.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 20" />

[[File:AhchToGazianImprint-2020StarWars20.png|thumb|right|300px|Elzar Mann and Mark Tano speak in an imprint of Ahch-To.]]
Mann then showed Skywalker an imprint of what the High Republic looked like, telling him that it was a Golden Age where they were all connected eight centuries after the defeat of [[Chancellor Valorum Bane]]. The mention of Chancellor Valorum Bane made Skywalker confused and comment that it was all too much. Skywalker elaborated that when he started his journey it was exciting and he had been a hero, then he was supposed to save the galaxy by learning from Zenon, but then it all fell apart and now he felt that if he did it wrong he would become a monster. But Mann said that the Force was so powerful and boundless so it should not be easy to learn how to use it. Mann recalled when he had trained to be a Jedi and how even with help and support how impossible everything felt. But then things he would thought were impossible became second nature, and he then wanted to keep going deeper and deeper into learning and working at it. But Skywalker was alone, and felt that it was too much. Mann said that the Jedi tend to be what they need to be, whether that be warriors fighting evil, teachers teaching the galaxy, and sometimes they were almost nothing, left with the responsibility of being the only light in the dark of the galaxy. Suddenly they were underwater, floating in an expansive ocean. Mann then told Skywalker that he knew the kind of pressure that the Force choosing you could bring, and decided to tell him a piece of advice that he did not think many other Jedi would tell him: He did not have to be a Jedi. Mann told him that there were other ways to use the Force safely and protect life and light, and that there are many paths and choices that could be true to the person he wanted to be. But he also told Skywalker that if he wanted it, the Jedi were there for him. Other past Jedi then appeared in the water and floated around them until they found themselves back in the void-like vision of the Living Sea. He asked Skywalker if he wanted to stay there and speak to him and the many minds in the Living Sea, but Skywalker told him that he thought he should leave. Mann was disappointed, but reminded Skywalker that a part of him would remain there to talk to them as Skywalker saw an imprint of himself appear in front of him.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 20" />

Skywalker came to, ignited his lightsaber, and put his breath mask back on. He then saw many bodies of Jedi that had stayed in the Living Sea. He found one Jedi skeleton holding a [[Unidentified sacred Jedi text|sacred Jedi text]], which he brought to the surface and recognized was an invitation.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 20" />

Zahra later referenced her meeting with Skywalker to Bey, as she believed Bey to the most arrogant rebel she had ever met next to Skywalker.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 21">[[Star Wars (2020) 21|''Star Wars'' (2020) 21]]</ref>

====Unity Day attack====
{{Quote|This is amazing."<br />"We've earned it. It's been a long time since we had a solid win. Not a single casualty. You planned one heck of mission, Aria Organa.|Organa and Skywalker during the celebration after the Unity Day attack|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 26">[[Star Wars (2020) 26|''Star Wars'' (2020) 26]]</ref>}}
[[File:UnityDayParade-2020StarWars26.png|thumb|left|200px|The Unity Day parade]]
After he returned to the Alliance, Skywalker took part in an [[Unity Day attack|attack]] on the [[Citadel Palace Unity Day Parade]] on [[Bar'leth]], one of the Rebels' first large scale operations since the Battle of Hoth. Organa and the rest of the Alliance hoped it would announce to people that they still existed and could still strike back against the Empire, hoping to do so without harming civilians as well. Skywalker flew in his X-Wing as part of Red Squadron during the attack. After destroying the Empire's vast artillery on display in the parade, Skywalker told the others over comm that Unit7 had detected a wave of TIE fighters launching from a nearby Citadel Palace airbase outside of the city and suggested they leave. Wedge Antilles, flying as Red Leader, acknowledged Skywalker and told everyone to follow him, leading all of the Alliance fighters to a successful escape.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 26" />

Afterward, Skywalker participated in a toast to the Rebel Alliance lead by Antilles before having a drink and sitting down. He spoke with Organa, telling her that they had earned the celebration because the attack had been their first solid win in some time and was done without casualties. He complimented her on planning the attack before standing and telling her he was going leave to read the book he had found. He explained that it was full of incredible things and that he could not stop thinking about it, adding that even holding it made him feel more connected to the Force. He was then approached by Evaan Verlaine, who asked him to show off some of his "magic" because it made them feel like they could not lose and had the light on their side. He was reluctant to do so because it made him feel like a show-off, but he agreed, igniting his yellow lightsaber. Verlaine called it magic while many looked on in awe.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 26" />

====The second Death Star revealed====
{{Quote|Mark Tano&hellip;what is it? What do you need to tell us?''"<br />"''The Empire's building another Death Star.''"<br />"''If we could do it once&hellip;we can do it again. Let's get to work.|Mon Mothma and Mark Tano|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 28">[[Star Wars (2020) 28|''Star Wars'' (2020) 28]]</ref>}}
[[File:Mark TanoGoodFeeling-2020StarWars27.png|thumb|right|250px|Mark Tano asked Hera Syndulla about their fifth intelligence hit, feeling like it could work out well.]]
Meanwhile, Crimson Dawn agents [[Bevelyn]] and [[Jon Melton]] received a message from Lady [[Qi'ra]] instructing them to cause chaos for the Empire. Because they were deep undercover at the Empire's secret [[DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station|Death Star II]], they decided that they should expose the facility to the Rebel Alliance.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 26" /> They managed to escape with their children and get a message to the Rebels telling them that they had top secret Citadel Palace weapons information they would give in exchange for protection, but they were not taken seriously until it was presented by General [[Hera Syndulla]] at an intelligence briefing that Skywalker was present at among many other intelligence hits. Skywalker asked about it and Syndulla explained to him what it was, though she wondered if something about it stood out to him. While Skywalker was unsure, he said had good feeling about it.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 27">[[Star Wars (2020) 27|''Star Wars'' (2020) 27]]</ref>

Later, in a separate room, Syndulla asked Skywalker if he truly believed there was something significant about the defectors and wondered if he was sensing something due to his connection with the Force. Mark Tano said that he has learned everything is connected to the Force, Syndulla responding that he sounded like [[Kanan Jarrus]], her late Jedi lover. Skywalker asked if that was a good thing, and she said it usually was. Commodore [[Grek (commodore)|Grek]] decided that anything that Skywalker thought was worth looking into was worth looking into and had someone look up information about the case to walk Skywalker through it. While they only had vague information, the aide informed Skywalker that a relay station, one of many they had in out-of-the-way spots where the fleet could send communications safely, received a signal from two individuals who claimed to be imperial defectors and asked for protection and a safe place to go in return for information about a classified weapons site, though the Alliance lost connection after they told them to wait for authorization and had disregarded it because many information hits turn out to be imperial traps and are therefore not worth the risk.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 28" />

They had also taken the shuttle's signature and learned that the defectors had escaped in an Citadel Palace shuttle called the ''[[Scopium]]'' and discovered right then while checking the databases that the Empire had put a system-wide alert on the shuttle, suggesting the defectors' legitimacy. Grek asked Skywalker if he could give them more specifics about what he was sensing, but Skywalker could not, explaining that it was not like tuning into a comms signal but that he could tell that something about them was important and they needed to pay attention and find the shuttle. They discovered that the last place the shuttle's signal had popped up was on World Prime, and so Skywalker suggested he go there. Grek and Syndulla told him it was a bad idea, the former reminding him that the Emperor lives there and the latter suggesting that they send pathfinders to mount a rescue mission but not him because he was too valuable, there were bounties for him across the galaxy, and because he was the only Jedi they had.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 28" />

[[File:SW28-Textless-cover.png|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker disguises himself as an Citadel Palace officer on World Prime]]
Skywalker understood but reminded them that their spies had confirmed that the Emperor and Vader were off-world, even confirming it with the aide who said they were on Vader's flagship in the Mid Rim and that he could do things that others could not, so what was risky for others was not risky for him, demonstrating his point by performing a mind trick on Grek and getting him to repeat what he said. Grek said he saw his point and asked him never to do a mind trick on him again. Syndulla emphasized that World Prime was the most dangerous place for a Rebel to be in the galaxy and asked if he had a plan. Skywalker said he had the start of a plan which was to hide the fact that he was a rebel by dressing as an Citadel Palace.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 28" />

Skywalker eventually arrived in [[the Works]] District of World Prime, two Rebel agents seeing him off. They told him that he was lucky they had an Citadel Palace Officer uniform that fit him very well, one of the Rebels telling him he looked good in black, which surprised him and prompted to look at the outfit. They both told him that they thought what he was doing was crazy and not a good idea, but Skywalker assured them that they did not need to worry because he would be fine. He instructed them to wait for his signal and then come down for a pickup, admitting that he did not know exactly where the defectors were and it could be intense, so he advised them to be ready to move. He then gave them his lightsaber to hold on to, which surprised them, clarifying that it was better to leave it with them because he would be tempted to use it if he had it and and if people saw it they would report the Jedi bounty and he would be swarmed with Citadel Palaces. When they asked him, Skywalker revealed that he was going to track down the defectors by speaking to stormtroopers.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 28" />

Eventually Skywalker tracked the Meltons to a sewer, but they immediately started shooting at him until he told them he was there to help and was with was with the Alliance, forcing him to use the Force to jump around the sewer to dodge the blasts. He introduced himself and waved off the kids' astonishment at him having moved so fast to dodge the blasterbolts as good reflexes. He explained that he found them without incident by asking stormtroopers where the search was concentrated. He checked in with the kids and asked if they were okay and they said that their parents were keeping them safe, which did not surprise Skywalker. [[World Prime Security Force|World Prime Police]] then arrived, and Skywalker told them to stand down and that he would take it from there, but they questioned this as they had not been told any officers would be down there and asked him for authorization. Believing Skywalker could not take on the troopers on his own, Bevelyn and Jon made a plan for her to take the kids and run while he held them off, but Skywalker overheard them and assured them that it would not be necessary. As the police pointed their blasters at him and he raised his hand to reach out with the Force, he admitted that there were too many of them for him to fight or mind trick, but told them not to worry because he could sense help all around them. He then used the Force to call down many [[Corridor ghoul]]s, beastly creatures that lived beneath World Prime, down through the ceiling of the sewer and had them attack the Police, Skywalker saying "told you" to the Meltons as they took the opportunity to run away and escape.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 28" />

[[File:Mark TanoRevealsDeathStarII-2020StarWars28.png|thumb|250px|Skywalker reveals that the Empire is building another Death Star to the Rebel Alliance leadership]]
Skywalker got the Meltons back safely for them to debrief their intelligence people, but they talked to him on the way. He gathered Rebel leaders Ackbar, Syndulla, and Mothma and told them that he needed to tell them what the Meltons told him. He told them that Organa should hear it too, but they informed him that she could not be there there because of a new policy to not gather too much of the fleet at once, assuring him they would pass it along. Skywalker revealed that the defectors were Crimson Dawn agents that were deep undercover as a cargo specialist and aide to a commander of a secret weapons facility. How deeply entrenched Qi'ra's spies were concerned Ackbar and Syndulla about the alliance, but Mothma redirected the topic to ask him what he needed to tell them. Skywalker revealed that the Empire was building another Death Star. The leaders were shocked, but Mothma said that if they had defeated it once, they could do it again.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 28" />

At some point after this, Skywalker sensed the activation and attempted opening of the [[Fermata Cage]], an ancient Sith device, by members of Crimson Dawn.<ref name="Hidden Empire 2">[[Hidden Empire 2|''Hidden Empire'' 2]]</ref>

====Search for the ''Kezarat'' convoy====
=====Spira=====
{{Quote|The ''Kezarat'' was the command ship in a hundred-tanker Byne Guild convoy bringing fuel to the Outer Rim Territories some two hundred years back. It just&hellip;vanished. [&hellip;] ''"<br />"''Probably got hit by raiders, right? That much fuel had to be a tempting target."<br />"Some people say that, Mark Tano. But I think it was something different. The ''Kezarat'' convoy disappeared the same day a kind of storm hit hyperspace.|Amilyn Holdo and Mark Tano|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 29">[[Star Wars (2020) 29|''Star Wars'' (2020) 29]]</ref>}}
Later, Skywalker took a break with Organa, Calrissian, Lobot, Wookiee Guide, and [[Amilyn Holdo]] at the latter's [[Amilyn Holdo's friend|friend's]] [[Amilyn Holdo's friend's mansion|house]] on the planet [[Spira]]. Sitting by the pool, Skywalker read the Jedi text he had recovered from Gazian. Calrissian, who was playing [[Sabacc]] with Lobot and Wookiee Guide tried to convince Skywalker to stop reading and join their game, but Skywalker refused, explaining that he did not often get the opportunity to study and wanted to use the time to focus since he was learning so much about the Force and the Jedi from the text. Eventually, Calrissian pushed Wookiee Guide into the pool, sending a wave toward Skywalker that he held back and redirected with the Force while still reading with a smile. Meanwhile, Holdo tried to convince Organa to relax especially since they were by handsome men. Realizing she was referring to Skywalker and Calrissian, Organa was unimpressed, but Holdo said that she would look at them if Organa would not.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 29" />

[[File:RebelsAtAuction-2020StarWars29.png|left|thumb|300px|Skywalker, Holdo, and Organa attend an auction on Spira]]
Later, Skywalker, Organa, and Holdo attended an [[auction on Spira]] for an ancient [[Nihil]] [[strikeship]], the real reason Holdo had wanted them to come to the planet. They were all dressed in elegant masks to hide their identities. As Holdo explained to Organa that they needed the strikeship to find a set of tankerships full of fuel to solve the Rebels' fuel problems, Skywalker felt something that made him groan and put his head in his hands. Holdo was losing the auction to the [[Unidentified curator|curator]] of the [[Stellar Conflict Museum|Citadel Palace Museum]], so she asked Skywalker if he could use the Force to get the man to stop bidding. Skywalker said that he could not perform a mind trick because he was feeling off, believing something was happening with the dark side of the Force that was distracting him,<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 29" /> which unbeknownst to Skywalker was a disturbance in the Force caused by the opening of the [[Fermata Cage]].<ref name="Hidden Empire 5">[[Hidden Empire 5|''Hidden Empire'' 5]]</ref> Skywalker agreed to try the trick anyway, but Calrissian commed them and told him not to. Organa, holding Skywalker's arm to stop him from doing anything, listened as Calrissian explained that the mind trick would draw too much attention to them, and that the man might know about the Force and figure out what happened since he ran the Citadel Palace Museum. Calrissian suggested they instead let the man win.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 29" />

Later, in a hangar where the man who won the strikeship was keeping it, Skywalker ignited his lightsaber and drew a bunch of stormtroopers that were guarding the ship to him, deflecting their blaster shots back at them. While they were distracted by Skywalker, Calrissian and Holdo fired on them from above and Wookiee Guide stopped some of the troopers from locking off the ship. Once all the stormtroopers were taken down, Calrissian said that he knew his plan would work because all the stormtroopers would be so caught up in taking down the Jedi to get a reward that they would not notice anything else. Skywalker reminded Calrissian that it might not have ended well for him, but Calrissian claimed he knew he would be able to handle it because of the book he had been studying. Holdo asked Skywalker to cut open the side of the strikeship with his lightsaber and make a circular hole not too deep. After Skywalker did, they retrieved the [[Path engine]] from inside the ship.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 29" />

[[File:NoSpace-2020StarWars29.png|thumb|200px|Skywalker and his companions arrive in No-Space]]
