Later, back at Holdo's friend's house, Holdo explained that she was planning to go after the [[Kezarat Convoy|''Kezarat'' convoy]], which Organa had suspected. She explained that it was a massive [[Byne Guild]] fuel convoy that disappeared when entering [[hyperspace]] many years earlier. Skywalker asked if it was because it got hit by raiders because it was such a sought-after target, but Holdo revealed it actually disappeared during a [[Great Hyperspace Disaster|storm]] in hyperspace caused by the Nihil. She hoped that the last message sent by the convoy that was thought to be nonsense was actually navigational data designed only to communicate with a Path engine and that both together could take them to the convoy. After Wookiee Guide finished installing the Path engine into their ship the ''[[Skyfarer]]'', a group of TIE fighters found them and started going after them. Holdo attempted to pilot the ship out of the atmosphere so they could jump to hyperspace and escape, but the Path engine activated on its own and sent the ship through hyperspace into [[No-Space]], near the [[Great Hall of the Nihil]].<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 29" />

=====The lost colony=====
{{Quote|Sometimes people find their way to No-Space, just like you all did. [&hellip;] One of those was a Jedi. Alareen Xie. She joined us, helped us fight off the Nihil. We wouldn't have survived without her. She died in time, as most people do. But after she did, a sort of belief rose up. That someday a Jedi would return and take us out of this place. Would take us home.|Blythe, to Skywalker|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 31">[[Star Wars (2020) 31|''Star Wars'' (2020) 31]]</ref>}}
Skywalker and his friends did not recognize No-Space and had no idea where they were, but Skywalker expressed that while he had not traveled as much as they had, he knew the galaxy had strange things in it. He added that the Force seemed off and distant, as if there was not much around that was alive. After Holdo tried and failed to take the ship to hyperspace again, Skywalker suggested that they needed to disconnect the Path engine to see if it would fix the problem, but Holdo revealed they would need to land somewhere first. After landing on the Great Hall, Lando lamented the dangers of falling off the edge there and said it was worse than Cloud City, but Skywalker insisted that Cloud City had been really bad. A child in a spacesuit then appeared and asked them if they had 'flavors', which Calrissian interpreted to mean the kid wanted to eat them. Skywalker said he was just a kid, but Calrissian asked him to remind him to tell Skywalker about the [[White Worms]] gang's savage children. The kid eventually advised them to hide and ran off, and Skywalker sensed with the Force that the kid was terrified and did not know where he was going. The kid then jumped off the edge of the Hall, which shocked Skywalker, but he just activated a jetpack and flew away.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 30">[[Star Wars (2020) 30|''Star Wars'' (2020) 30]]</ref>

[[File:Killdroid-2020StarWars30.jpg|left|thumb|150px|A killdroid in the Great Hall]]
Lando suggested they get out of there, which Skywalker agreed with, suggesting they go back to their ship and try to find the other place there that the boy mentioned. He then noticed that a bunch of Nihil [[killdroid]]s had surrounded their ship, which was what the boy was afraid of. Skywalker began to fight them with his lightsaber, but quickly realized that they were lightsaber resistant. A ship then pulled up next to the hall, and Holdo suggested that they board it to escape the droids, but was concerned by having to jump across open space to it. Skywalker insisted that it was not that bad of a jump and because the ramp had a magnetic shield they would not be in the vacuum very long, but Calrissian implied that easy for him to say because he was a Jedi. They all jumped over to the ship without issue, except for Calrissian, who tripped and fell, prompting Skywalker to use the Force to pull him back up while muttering "I can do this." Once Calrissian was safe he thanked Skywalker for saving his life and assured him he would not bother him about studying his book ever again. Skywalker revealed that he could have gotten him to safety faster but could not because there was still something going on with the Force that he described as ripples messing with his concentration. Once the ship they were on docked with a larger ship, a voice over a speaker ordered them to throw their weapons out into space or they would vent them out into space. Skywalker considered using his lightaber to just cut through the door into the bigger ship but realized they would just vent them anyway. He threw his lightsaber out into space, which he said hurt because they were hard to find, but the kid with the jetpack just flew over, picked it up, and ignited it before flying away, Skywalker warning him that he needed to be careful with it or he would hurt himself.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 30" />

The voice over the speaker welcomed them to the [[Colony of Kezarat]]. Holdo yelled that they just needed to go home, but an [[Abyssin]] left the cockpit and told them they were home.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 30" /> After Organa said they would not attack and were listening, the individual introduced himself as Captain [[Blythe]], and Holdo introduced herself, Skywalker, and the others to him. Blythe then began a tour of the colony, confirming that it was the old convoy and the fuel was still there. The kid, who Blythe revealed was named [[Forvan]], then ran up excitedly, and Blythe explained that he had gotten excited from seeing a lightsaber. Skywalker asked if it was because they had Jedi there and asked for his saber back, but Blythe said they did not have Jedi there and he would get his lightsaber back in due time. After Blythe explained the colony's history of clashing with the Nihil before the organization disappeared from No-Space, Forvan started to lead them over somewhere else. Blythe told Skywalker to let Forvan down easy, and when he said he did not understand, Blythe said he would.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 31" />

[[File:AlareenXie-2020StarWars31.png|thumb|250px|The mural of Alareen Xie]]
Forvan took them to mural depicting a Jedi. Skywalker was shocked that they had a Jedi with the convoy, but Blythe said she had not been there from the beginning and just found her way to No-Space. Blythe explained that her name was [[Alareen Xie]], and that after she died a belief spread within the colony that a Jedi would someday lead them home. Blythe once again reiterated for Skywalker to let Forvan down easy, so he bent down to speak with Forvan and told him that while the Jedi could do incredible things, he could not assure them that he would get them out of No-Space, though he would at least do everything he could to try and get them out of there or to make their lives better. Forvan once again said that Jedi could do anything, so Skywalker just said he would try his best. After Blythe warned them that they would be there for a while and would not be able to get back to their ship, Skywalker and the others all went to sleeping quarters given to them. Skywalker paced around the room and Organa recognized something was wrong and asked him about it. Skywalker explained that he had to get out of there to get back to the ship to get the irreplaceable Jedi text that he had left on it. When she brought it up, Skywalker said he was not worried about his lightsaber as he could get another one, but that without the text he would not be able to move forward with his training. He feared that if he lost it and was no longer able to access its knowledge, techniques, and history of the Force and the Jedi Order or be able to use it to find places he could learn more, he would never truly become a Jedi.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 31" />

=====Escape from No-Space=====
{{Quote|Keep the killdroids off Chewie until he's back on the ship. Then get yourselves safe too. I'm going after the Jedi text.''"<br />"''But you said your saber can't get through [the killdroids'] armor! And Mark Tano&hellip;it's just a book!''"<br />"''No. It's ''the'' book. And as far as my lightsaber, I wasn't properly focused before. Now I am. Now&hellip;the Force is with me.|Skywalker and Holdo|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 32">[[Star Wars (2020) 32|''Star Wars'' (2020) 32]]</ref>}}
After Wookiee Guide realized that they could use the Path engine to escape No-Space, Blythe gathered Skywalker and the others, offering them an old [[Longbeam-class corvette|Longbeam cruiser]] to retrieve it. Skywalker was skeptical that it could fly, but Blythe assured them that it used to and just needed to be fixed up. Once they got the cruiser to take off and leave the colony, Holdo and Lando took inventory of what they had, including that they had a Jedi. Skywalker reminded them that his connection to the Force was different and hard to use in No-Space and something strange felt like it was happening to it anyway, but he assured them he would try his best. Calrissian assured them they would be fine, but Skywalker was still skeptical and pointed out that the killdroids had found and taken the Path engine. Skywalker decided that he would distract the droids so the others could get the engine, but after needed to go back to the ''Skyfarer'' and get his Jedi text, refusing to leave without it. He added that he had talked to Forvan before they left and that the boy, wanting to help out a Jedi, gave him specialized gear, including a spacesuit, that he could use to get down to the Great Hall. Wearing the spacesuit, Skywalker jumped from the cruiser down to the Hall, ignited his lightsaber, and called out to the droids, encouraging them to go after him. As Skywalker, Holdo, and Calrissian distracted the droids, Skywalker deflecting their blastershots with his lightsaber, Wookiee Guide went after the engine. However, some droids noticed and went after Wookiee Guide anyway, so Skywalker sent them flying away off into no-Space with the Force. He warned Wookiee Guide that he probably would not be able to do it again, so he needed to run and get the engine back to the ship.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 32" />

[[File:ColonyofKezarat-CGSWG.png|thumb|left|250px|The Kezarat Colony]]
After shooting a droid behind Wookiee Guide with a blaster, Skywalker started to run off and told Holdo to keep Wookiee Guide safe while he ran after the Jedi text. She reminded him that his lightsaber could not get through their armor and that it was just a book, but Skywalker said that it was more than just a book and that he had not been focused when his lightsaber would not cut them the first time, but now was. Skywalker sliced through the droids with his lightsaber while saying "the Force is with me" and calling out for what they did with his book. He eventually found the book on a ledge at the edge of the Hall and decided that he would easily be able to grab it and fly back to the ship, but a killdroid shot his jetpack, sending him flying uncontrollably toward the book and leaving it without fuel. As killdroids approached him, their footsteps shaking the ground caused the book to go over the edge. Skywalker screamed in horror and reached out to it with his right hand, which was holding his lightsaber, but a droid grabbed his hand and lifted him up by it, crushing both his hand and his lightsaber.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 32" /> The droid threw him onto the ground and into the remains of the ''Skyfarer'', and Skywalker cried out in horror when he saw his hand and lightsaber. Calrissian and Holdo saw what happened and decided to try and get to Skywalker before the droids killed him. A delirious Skywalker told the approaching droids to stop, but when they did not, he threw all of the droids out of the Hall in a massive wave using the Force while telling himself "may the Force be with me." Calrissian, Holdo, and Wookiee Guide were shocked at how he was doing it, and Calrissian told Wookiee Guide to remind him never to get on his bad side. Skywalker then pulled the Jedi text to him with the Force and passed out immediately after.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 33">[[Star Wars (2020) 33|''Star Wars'' (2020) 33]]</ref>

Later, on the way back to the colony, Calrissian checked in on a now handless Skywalker, though the droid had only destroyed his already mechanical hand. Calrissian asked him how he would done what he did, but he said that he did not understand how it happened and that it felt like the Force suddenly came back to him stronger than ever, and that it was frightening. Calrissian told him to cheer up, but thinking about his broken lightsaber and his inevitable confrontation with Vader, told Calrissian that he was not sure he would be able to do something he needed to anymore. Back at the colony, Skywalker showed Organa, who had stayed behind, what happened to his hand. Blythe and Forvan offered to fix it up, the latter suggesting a claw or grappling hook, but Skywalker said he would just wait until they got home even though those things would be cool. Skywalker and Wookiee Guide then presented the Path engine to Blythe. After Blythe presented the group to the members of the colony, but Organa and Calrissian warned them about the dangers of the Empire and traveling with them, Blythe revealed to them that several of the colony decided to go back with them. However, he revealed that many were going to stay on the Great Hall since they got rid of all the killdroids. Wookiee Guide pointed out that Skywalker got rid of all the droids by himself, and Blythe commented that it seemed the things people said about Jedi were true. However, Skywalker, who was struggling to pull a piece of scrap to him with the Force, said they sometimes were true and sometimes were not. Later, after a rough hyperspace jump made with many ships secured together and assisted by Lobot, Skywalker and his friends as well as several members of the colony arrived back in the greater galaxy.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 33" />

Back with the fleet, Skywalker had his mechanical hand repaired by a medical droid while Unit7 did his best to repair his lightsaber. Organa reminded Skywalker that it could have been worse if the droid had crushed his other hand, and asked him about the powerful act of the Force he had pulled off on the Great Hall. He confirmed that he had not learned it from his book but that it was instead related to something being wrong with the Force, describing it as if something hit the Force while he was in No-Space and caused it to ripple. He added that it felt like waves on the beach in the way that it vacillated from him being the strongest he had ever been where he almost could not control it, to not being able to feel it at all. Organa then wondered if since he could feel it, and even she could slightly, that the Emperor and Vader were also feeling it immensely and were distracted, making it their chance to defeat them. Skywalker said her theory made sense, and she went to speak with Mon Mothma. Skywalker thanked R2 for attempting to fix his lightsaber, but admitted that he was going to need a new one for when he inevitably faced Vader again.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 33" />

====Duel with a droid====
{{Quote|A Jedi&hellip;I was afraid my dreams of killing one were dashed. [&hellip;] I'd been informed the Jedi were extinct.''"<br />"''Oh, don't worry&hellip;they still are.|Ajax Sigma and Skywalker|<ref name="Revelations 1">[[Revelations (2022) 1|''Revelations'' (2022) 1]]</ref>}}
[[File:AjaxSigma-Revelations2022.png|thumb|250px|Ajax Sigma]]
While still escorting more of the ''Kezarat'' convoy to the Alliance fleet, Skywalker felt a disturbance in the Force while on the ''Millennium Falcon''. He explained to Organa that it was not like the one he had felt in No-Space but instead felt like the deaths of innocent people, and that it was nearby enough that he could bring them there. Organa agreed to go despite the fact they were supposed to be escorting the convoy. When they arrived, Protocol Droid revealed that the moon did not appear on any [[Star map|star-charts]]. Organa wondered if it was erased by the Empire, but Skywalker said it was not and pointed out an ancient lightsaber like none he would ever seen before. He and Wookiee Guide then noticed that there was a large amount of destroyed droids that were cut down with a lightsaber. They all realized that a battle had been fought there, and Skywalker put together that it had been between droids and people, and since there were no battle droids and no remains, it must have been hundreds of years earlier. Skywalker realized that the battle was not what he had sensed and instead lead them to a [[homesteader ship]] that they found to be full of bodies. Protocol Droid offered to secure the ''Falcon'' but Skywalker said it was not necessary. Skywalker asked R2 to plug into the ship and see if it had any information about the moon they were on. R2 revealed it was called [[Kligson's Moon]]. Skywalker suggested that the carnage there may have recently happened and the perpetrator could still be there, and suggested splitting up into pairs to search due to the size of the ship.<ref name="Revelations 1" />

After discovering a droid, that unbeknownst to Skywalker was [[Ajax Sigma]], an ancient droid revolutionary, he asked it why they killed all the people there. Sigma claimed that it was self defense and that they attacked him outside when he came there to retrieve something, but Skywalker did not believe him. The droid clarified that he had followed the people back to their ship and killed them all, which Skywalker said did not sound like self-defense. The droid activated electric blades on his arms and disparaged Skywalker for being organic and for suggesting that the droid would go with him and answer for his actions. Skywalker ignited his lightsaber and began to fight Sigma, who used the blades on his arms to defend himself. He was surprised to see a Jedi, believing them all to be dead, and Skywalker assured him they were. After Skywalker sliced open the droid's chest and knocked him down, he ordered him to stand down or face destruction. However, the droid just entered a pod that he ejected from the homesteader ship, successfully escaping.<ref name="Revelations 1" />

Vader had a vision of Skywalker and Sigma's duel while speaking with the [[Eye of Webbish Bog]], sometime before the events of No-Space and the activation of the Fermata Cage. In the vision, Vader also saw Skywalker holding two kyber crystals, one green and one red.<ref name="Revelations 1" />

====Adventure with Aphra====
=====Kidnapping plot=====
{{Quote|Come on, Mark Tano. Ancient Jedi artifact of great power? Sealed away by Jedi Masters? Maybe even something that could give you an edge of a certain Sith Lord? Tell me you don't want that.''"<br />"''How far to Sason?''"<br />"''Now we're talking!|Chelli Aphra and Skywalker|<ref name="Aphra 2020 32">[[Doctor Aphra (2020) 32|''Doctor Aphra'' (2020) 32]]</ref>}}
Because he had lost control of his powers just as Skywalker had, Vader recruited Doctor Aphra to help him find a way to control them. While in a shuttle to a location she had in mind, Aphra walked into a room where Vader was meditating and entered a vision he was having that included Skywalker in his Tatooine farm boy clothes. Aphra did not understand why Skywalker was there and did not recognize the other individual in the vision, [[Sabé]], who was telling Skywalker that there was still good in Vader, which were Skywalker's mother's last words.<ref name="Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 35">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2020) 35|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2020) 35]]</ref>

[[File:AphraKidnapsMark Tano-2020DoctorAphra31.png|thumb|left|250px|Doctor Aphra kidnaps Skywalker on Numidian Prime.]]
Though his lightsaber was still not fixed, Skywalker traveled to [[Numidian Prime]] with Unit7 in search of a [[Unidentified temple (Numidian Prime)|temple]] on the planet. He briefly left R2 in a temporary camp while he searched for it, but after finding no sign of it and it started to rain he returned to the camp, finding peace in the solitude. He apologized to R2 for leaving, saying they needed to wait for the rain to taper off, but then noticed the droid was deactivated and laying on the ground. He cried out and ran to the droid, but a node underneath the droid started shooting smoke out, confusing Skywalker and knocking him out after he inhaled it. The trap had been set by Doctor Chelli Aphra, who then stood over an unconscious Skywalker and greeted him, calling him a "farm boy", and asked how he felt about going on an adventure.<ref name="Aphra 2020 31">[[Doctor Aphra (2020) 31|''Doctor Aphra'' (2020) 31]]</ref>

Aphra eventually bound and gagged Skywalker and placed him in a crate on her ship the ''[[Ark Angel IV]]''. When he woke up, she opened the crate and said she was glad he was still breathing before offering him [[Caf]]. She started to get him some as he realized who kidnapped him, telling her he did not want Caf and just wanted to know why she did it and what she had done with R2. She explained that she had put a restraining bolt on and turned off R2, and Skywalker realized that she needed him for something. Aphra then claimed that she was going to actually do him a huge favor. Skywalker had managed to slip out of the ropes she had tied him up in, which she noticed at that moment, surprised at how quickly he had done it and wondering if Solo had taught him as she presented a holorecording. Realizing it was a Jedi holo, Skywalker listened as Jedi Master [[Shaak Ti]] explained to [[Aayla Secura]] that a powerful Jedi artifact called [[Kythoo's Bell]] was locked away at the [[Sason Temple]]. Aphra told him that she knew how to get there an needed a Jedi to get in, but Skywalker was still suspicious. After insisting she was just being nice and trying to make up for the events at the Screaming Citadel, Aphra pointed out that the artifact could give Skywalker an edge over Vader. After contemplating it more, Skywalker asked her how far [[Sason]] was, exciting her.<ref name="Aphra 2020 32" />

=====Sason Temple=====
{{Quote|Right before I found you, Vader found me. That 'Force pulse' you felt? He felt it too. But unlike you, it just made him stronger. Wild. Out of control. You don't stand a chance against him as you are. Say we leave Sason without Kythoo's Bell. Vader kills everyone you care about to get to you. Then he kills you. Once you're dead, who's going to protect me from him?|Chelli Aphra to Skywalker|<ref name="Aphra 2020 33">[[Doctor Aphra (2020) 33|''Doctor Aphra'' (2020) 33]]</ref>}}
[[File:SasonTemple-2020DoctorAphra32.jpg|thumb|right|250px|The Sason Temple]]
As they flew into Sason in the ''Ark Angel IV'', Skywalker noticed that their navigation systems went offline, which Aphra attributed to the planet's [[magnetic storm]]. Telling Aphra she had a great copilot, Skywalker navigated the ship through the storm despite Aphra's protests, following an echo of a note he could hear in the Force and urging Aphra to trust him. They then flew toward a gap in the storm that held the temple, Skywalker exclaiming that it was beautiful. After being briefly confused by Aphra calling the temple their payday, which she insisted was figurative, Aphra explained that her research claimed that the temple would only open to someone who was pure of heart and strong in the Force. Skywalker tried to open it but failed, explaining to Aphra that he was unable to use the Force because something was happening to it making it unstable. Aphra then accused him of making things up to navigate them there, but he insisted he had used the Force. Realizing they did not have any other options, Aphra asked him if he had learned anything tricks at Jedi school, but Skywalker only said Jedi school did not exist anymore.<ref name="Aphra 2020 32" />

A massive guardian made out of crystal then formed, Skywalker telling R2 to get behind him and trying and failing to ignite his broken lightsaber. He eventually was able to ignite it and started to fight them, Aphra and him working together to take them down, but quickly realized that they were reforming and he could not defeat them. When his lightsaber deactivated, Skywalker reached out to the Force, destroying the guardians with a massive Force push while Aphra destroyed the [[Magnetic wave emitter]] that was causing them to reform. Skywalker felt like he was going to pass out, but just them the floor collapsed under them and dropped them into a pool. Skywalker called out for R2, who had not landed in the pool, but Aphra assured Skywalker the droid was fine. The two then noticed the figures of Jedi Masters Shaak Ti and Aayla Secura standing in front of them.<ref name="Aphra 2020 32" />

[[File:KythoosBell-2020DoctorAphra33.png|thumb|left|200px|Kythoo's Bell]]
Skywalker attempted to introduce himself to the Masters, but Aphra quickly realized that they were advanced holograms. This disappointed Skywalker, who had briefly believed he was not alone as a Jedi. As they traversed the temple, illusions started to make the two believe the other was saying things they were not, leading to Skywalker lashing out at Aphra for always treating things like a joke and questioning her on why she was not using her electro-tattoos, and Aphra believing Skywalker had referenced her and Sana Starros' breakup, though in reality, Skywalker had no idea that they had been in a relationship. As the argument reached its peak as Aphra asked him how he broke his lightsaber, a creature slammed onto the other side of the crystal wall, terrifying the two, but after Kythoo's bell rang it retreated. After hurriedly leaving to another section of the temple, Skywalker began to realize that the entire place was made up of illusions after almost falling into a pit of spikes. He suggested that things felt wrong and they should leave, but Aphra held a gun to his head to stop him and revealed that she was trying to make Skywalker more powerful because Vader had become more powerful, and she wanted Skywalker to protect her from the Sith Lord. Skywalker agreed and convinced her to put her blaster down, the two using Skywalker's ability to sense the bell with the Force and Aphra's ability to take down the traps, obstacles, and guardians in their way to eventually locate the bell.<ref name="Aphra 2020 33" />

=====Starweird=====
{{Quote|If you die, this whole trip was ''useless!'' If you fall, I'm ''keeping'' your laser sword. That's my blaster!''"<br />"''If ''you'' die, I'm keeping it!|Aphra and Skywalker, while fighting the Starweird|<ref name="Aphra 2020 34">[[Doctor Aphra (2020) 34|''Doctor Aphra'' (2020) 34]]</ref>}}
Realizing the bell was to big to transport, and having no Force-ritual to use with it, Aphra removed a piece inside of the bell by standing on Skywalker's shoulders and grabbing it. However, this caused the entire bell to collapse and be destroyed, which Skywalker realized made the echo of the note he could hear stop resonating throughout the Temple. Just then, the creature they had seen earlier burst through the wall, and Aphra realized that Sason Temple was really a Jedi prison.<ref name="Aphra 2020 33" /> Aphra recognized the creature as a [[Starweird]], a species that was supposed to be extinct. The Starweird threw them onto the wall telekinetically, but Skywalker recognized that it was not using the Force. When Aphra accidentally activated the piece of the bell they had retrieved and thus Forced the creature to be frozen, she realized it was an emitter releasing a frequency that affected the Starweird. However, the emitter deactivated and the Starweird flew toward Aphra, so Skywalker used the Force to impale it with a bunch of crystals before he and Aphra ran away. Skywalker admitted that he had not been trying to impale it, just hold it still as he led Aphra through the temple. After Skywalker, decided to hide in a room full of mirrors, Aphra called him brilliant.<ref name="Aphra 2020 34" />

[[File:Starweird-2020DoctorAphra33.png|thumb|right|250px|Skywalker and Aphra face a Starweird.]]
As Skywalker used the Force to manipulate the reflections of the crystals to lure the Starweird toward them, Aphra used her electro-tattoos to activate the holograms of Masters Ti and Secura. Skywalker, Aphra, and Unit7 were able to flee the creature and its scream while it was distracted. However, the creature found them, knocking Skywalker to the edge of the temple and leaving him barely hanging on. While proclaiming her desperation to protect Skywalker, she fought the Starweird using his lightsaber. Skywalker eventually pulled himself up and shot at the creature, saying he would keep it if she died right before Aphra sliced the creature's hand off, which Skywalker commented did not feel good. Escaping into the ''Ark Angel IV'', but with the Starweird still on their tail, Skywalker directed Aphra to lead them into the magnetic storm and used the Force to activate the emitter, knocking the creature into the storm and eviscerating it, and leaving him surprised at his ability.<ref name="Aphra 2020 34" />

Later, back on Numidian Prime, Skywalker told Aphra she did not need to trick or bribe him into protecting her from Vader, insisting he would help because it was the the Jedi way. Aphra warned against his kindness, but Skywalker declared he preferred to take the chance than close himself off from people in need and leave himself all alone. Aphra told him to call her the next time he needed to get into a Jedi tomb, but Skywalker said he would not and took off in his X-wing, having taken the emitter with him before Aphra could realize.<ref name="Aphra 2020 34" />

====Christophsis====
{{Quote|Every time I think I have a handle on being a Jedi, something happens to kick me back. The ground under my feet just disappears&hellip; I'm going to have to face Vader again, and I am not ready. I don't even have a lightsaber I can rely on.|Skywalker to Organa|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 34">[[Star Wars (2020) 34|''Star Wars'' (2020) 34]]</ref>}}
While studying his Jedi text and the yellow kyber crystal from his lightsaber on the ''Home One'', Skywalker realized that he did not know a lot about kyber crystals except them being in every lightsaber as their power source. He explained to Unit7 that the text only contained details about the philosophy and spirituality of kyber crystals and an old rite of passage for younglings to find a crystal to make their first lightsaber on the planet Ilum, referring to another manual by Professor [[Huyang]] for building instructions. He figured that Zenon and Kenobi had never taught him anything about them because he had already had one, but lamented that his had never had a connection with him like they were supposed to due to the almost living nature of the crystals. He ignited his lightsaber and said that now that the crystal was cracked it no longer was a useful tool and was unstable. Due to the saber's unsteadiness, R2 made a concerned beep and Skywalker shut it off and apologized. Realizing that he needed a new crystal, Skywalker decided that he and R2 should visit other worlds the text mentioned to find them since Ilum was locked down by the Empire. Just then, Organa walked in. After he told he was going somewhere, she expressed her concern for him especially due to the strangeness of the Force as well as her desire for him to stay and help the Alliance. Skywalker insisted he was fine, saying he was just troubled by not knowing why the Force was strange or how to fix his lightsaber and felt like he could never truly get a handle on being a Jedi. He also admitted that he needed a lightsaber for his confrontation with Vader, and that he felt like he needed to go on this mission in order to take control and take action.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 34">[[Star Wars (2020) 34|''Star Wars'' (2020) 34]]</ref>

[[File:Christophsis.jpg|thumb|left|200px|Christophsis]]
Skywalker chose to go to Christophsis, due to the fact that there was not much of a permanent Citadel Palace presence there despite it being an Citadel Palace world and because the text said kyber crystals could regularly be found there. He flew his X-Wing there with R2 and landed outside of a small mining town where prospectors sell their finds so he would not get noticed, though did not want to have to walk the way there. R2 indicated to him that he wanted to know the plan, so Skywalker admitted that he did not have one. He explained that Calrissian had told him there was a black market for crystals on Christophsis because prospectors try to sell them since there was not enough for the Empire to set up a full-scale mining operation. He told R2 that he just planned to put the word out and pose as a buyer to see who would speak with him. He admitted that it was not much of a plan but gave R2 his lightsaber to hold onto while he looked around, not wanting to make it obvious he was a Jedi. He assured R2 he would be fine and told the droid that he could save him if he got into trouble. He then started in to a nearby cantina.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 34" />

[[File:Gretta-2020StarWars34.jpg|thumb|right|200px|Gretta]]
In the cantina, Skywalker got food and water and implied to an [[Unidentified Iktotchi bartender|Iktotchi bartender]] that he was a wealthy buyer looking for kyber. Just as the Iktotchi was offering to point Skywalker to his quarry, a human with green hair shot and killed him and everyone else in the cantina except for Skywalker, leaving him shocked. She taunted him and called him by name, so Skywalker used the Force to pull his lightsaber to him from R2, who had just rolled in and ordered her to explain herself. She introduced herself as [[Gretta]] and claimed that she saved his life, pointing out a blaster behind the counter. She explained that the whole place was ploy to trap people looking for kyber and sell them to the Empire, and that she saved him from it because he was a Jedi. She claimed that she still believed and recognized him from the dark channels, having posted out there in case any Jedi came through. She told him that there was kyber near and told him that she had to kill the people there because she knew he would not. Skywalker was still upset that she killed everyone there, insisting they died for nothing and urging her to live a better life before leaving. Skywalker went off to look for crystals on the planet, sensing she had told the truth about there being some there, but she called after him and told him he was going the wrong direction. He saw she had a speeder with her and urged him to let her help him, explaining that she was from Jedha and that her people were the [[Fallanassi]]. She revealed that they were killed by the Death Star, and that when Skywalker had destroyed it he had avenged them, and thus she wanted to return the favor. Skywalker told R2 to go back to the ship and tell the others where he was if he did not come back in a day, assuring the droid he would be okay and that he needed to do this while getting in Gretta's speeder.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 34" />

On the way, Skywalker asked Gretta about the Fallanassi. She explained that they did not use kyber crystals and had not been Force-sensitive for many years, only understanding it, not using it. When he asked, she also revealed that they were going to meet a man named [[Cuata]] who had hid there to escape the eye of the Empire and continue his studies, having been sought out by the Citadel Palaces to help design the weapon. Skywalker was confused about how she knew this information, and she explained that she has been working for him. Suddenly, a massive creature emerged from the gournd and knocked Skywalker and Gretta off of the speeder. Skywalker ignited his lightsaber and told Gretta to run, but she was delirious and urged him to fight the creature. Noticing the instability of his lightsaber, he decided just to run as the creature crushed their speeder with its mouth. The creature pursued them closely, so Skywalker just told Gretta to run, intending to use the Force to calm the creature. However, when he tried to he found himself unable to touch the Force. The creature nearly reached him until a massive explosion rocked him and Cuata emerged from the smoke and dust, instantly asking Skywalker if he could have his lightsaber.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 34" />

====The kyber crystals====
=====Red=====
{{Quote|You came here to heal me&mdash;but what if do not ''want'' to be healed? I am not ''sick'', young master. Your ministrations would to me, be a form of ''violence''. ''You'' have experienced violence, I think. ''You'' have experienced pain. We can use it&hellip;''together''.|The Sith in the crystal, to Skywalker|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 35" />}}
[[File:StarWars2020-35-NotoVariant-cropped.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Mark Tano shows his lightsaber to Cuata.]]
Realizing he came on too strong, Cuata explained that the kyber crystals he wore around his neck told him that Skywalker needed help. Gretta introduced Skywalker to Cuata, and though he was initially concerned that the doctor thought the crystals were talking to him, apologized and asked for his help with his broken lightsaber after Gretta assured Skywalker he could trust Cuata. He immediately took the lightsaber and started tinkering with it, quickly discovering that the crystal was cracked and assured him he could fix it if Skywalker did something for him first. Cuata also revealed Skywalker's crystal told him that he was having trouble with the Force, and then started to lead him to his workshop.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 35" />

At Cuata's workshop, Skywalker explained that he had found his lightsaber and that he and his R2 unit had worked on it. Cuata, concerned at Skywalker's lack of knowledge, explained the components and inner workings of a lightsaber and told Skywalker that a lightsaber's wielder should have a strong connection with its crystal, something Skywalker admitted he had never felt, not even with his father's lightsaber. While Cuata worked on fixing the lightsaber, he gave Skywalker a red kyber crystal and asked him to pull the dark side out of it. Gretta, whose people had a history with healing crystals, explained how crystals were turned red by [[bleeding]] them with the Dark side, but could be healed afterward, though the process of doing so could change people and forced them to connect with whoever bled it.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 35" />

[[File:GolsCourt-2020StarWars35.png|thumb|250px|Skywalker has a vision of a Sith lord in a Sith hall]]
Skywalker agreed to try, and when he reached out to the crystal with the Force, suddenly found himself in a massive Sith hall in front of a [[Gol (Sith)|Sith lord]] sitting on a throne. The Sith greeted him and Skywalker explained his intentions of healing the crystal, but the Sith said they did not want to be healed so attempting to do so would be violence toward them. The Sith grabbed and twisted Skywalker's hand and said that together they could use the violence and the pain he had experienced. After a flash of light from his hand, the vision changed, putting Skywalker in a spirit-like version of his body facing his father's [[Fortress Vader]] on Mustafar. Vader then appeared on it and Skywalker ignited the red lightsaber in his hand, but a wave of red light washed over him and the vision ended.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 35" />

=====Green=====
{{Quote|All Jedi walk their own path. All Jedi ''must'' walk their own path. Know this, you do&mdash;or returned to me, you would have. You did not wish to speak to me, Mark Tano. And so you did not. A great decision lies before you. It has nothing to do with the Force or being a Jedi. About ''yourself'', this decision will be. Until you make it, a Jedi you cannot be.|Zenon to Skywalker|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 35">[[Star Wars (2020) 35|''Star Wars'' (2020) 35]]</ref>}}
[[File:Zenon-2020StarWars35.png|thumb|left|250px|Zenon appears to Skywalker inside the raw kyber crystal.]]
A terrified Skywalker stared at the still-red crystal and told Cuata that he had seen his father. Cuata then asked Skywalker to connect with a clear and raw kyber crystal, assuring him that he would pull him out if his crystals told him the Force was receding. After reaching out to the crystal, Skywalker found himself standing in front of Zenon. He believed it was not real, but still asked Zenon why he never answered when he reached out to him with the Force especially since he was hurt and trying to learn. Zenon insisted that all Jedi need to walk their own Path and that he would have returned to him otherwise. Zenon warned that Skywalker would need to make a decision about himself soon. Skywalker decided that he was not getting anything from speaking to Zenon and that he would be better off just learning from his Jedi text. He tried to leave the vision but could not, realizing that the Force had pulled back from him as it had been recently. Zenon told Skywalker that it was not really gone even when it was out of sight, waved his hand, and sent Skywalker out of the vision, wishing him goodbye. Zenon, who had been really speaking to Skywalker the whole time, asked the spirit of Kenobi what he thought. They both agreed that he was still not ready, but Zenon pointed out that he had learned much and would be ready when the time came.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 35" />

When Skywalker exited the vision, he discovered that the clear kyber crystal had turned green. Cuata gave him his saber back, having temporarily fixed it, but Gretta revealed that the scientist had been willing to let Skywalker stay trapped in the crystal and even die, advising him not to tell Cuata anything. Skywalker thanked Cuata for fixing his lightsaber and told him that he would take the green crystal for when he needed to build his own saber, also taking the red one in case one day he could heal it. Back at his X-Wing, Skywalker thanked Gretta for helping him and said he had learned despite things not going the way he had thought. He said he would go back to the Alliance eventually as his biggest battles still lay ahead, but revealed that he was going to spend time thinking first while holding up both the red and green crystal with the Force.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 35" />

While he was away, Organa used the intel Skywalker gave her that the Emperor and Vader were distracted by a Force anomaly to launch an [[Assault on World Prime|aerial assault on World Prime]], successfully destroying a statue of Palpatine in the hopes of inspiring rebellion across the galaxy.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 36">[[Star Wars (2020) 36|''Star Wars'' (2020) 36]]</ref>

====Dark droids====
{{Quote|I will be&hellip;''"<br />"&hellip;''the new Force''.|Skywalker and the Scourge, as the latter controlled the former's body|<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 41">[[Star Wars (2020) 41|''Star Wars'' (2020) 41]]</ref>}}
[[File:SacredJediText-DarkDroids1.png|thumb|right|300px|Skywalker studies his Jedi text with Unit7.]]
When studying his Jedi text, he found a reference to a Jedi outpost in the [[Tammuz sector]]. After seeing nothing on a map Unit7 pulled up for him, however, he decided that there was probably nothing there but that they could swing by if they got the chance. Later, as the [[Scourge crisis|Scourge of the droids]] began across the galaxy, Skywalker was in a meeting with Rebellion higher-ups concerning how to handle the new Death Star. Commodore Grek suggested they just threw Skywalker at it again, but Skywalker suspected it might take more than him in an X-wing to take down the new station.<ref name="Dark Droids 1">[[Dark Droids 1|''Dark Droids'' 1]]</ref>

Later, while Skywalker was meditating and practicing telekinesis, he was approached by Protocol Droid, who had been infected by the malevolent droid entity called the [[Scourge]] that was behind the scourge of the droids. The Scourge, as Protocol Droid questioned Skywalker on the nature of the Force and if droids could use it. Skywalker explained that he had never heard of that happening but thought it could potentially be possible. When the Scourge then asked if Skywalker's cybernetic arm felt connected to the Force, he explained that his whole being felt connected, but that he was not a true cyborg like Chancellor Valorum Vader. Skywalker expressed his concern that something was wrong with Protocol Droid, leading to the Scourge briefly considering killing him. Instead, the droid just apologised and agreed to get a diagnostic, before agreeing to Skywalker's request to send Unit7 his way.<ref name="Dark Droids 2">[[Dark Droids 2|''Dark Droids'' 2]]</ref>

As the scourge of the droids continued, Calrissian recruited Skywalker and Organa for a mission to the planet [[Epikonia]] to rescue Lobot, who had been infected by the Scourge. When they arrived in the ''Millennium Falcon'', Skywalker was unsure what made the world special until Organa explained that it was a communications hub. Calrissian then refused to allow Skywalker to access transpoder signals and turned off the ''Falcon''{{'s}} navigation systems to prevent the infection from reaching the ship's [[L3-37|droid core]]. Skywalker and Organa were concerned, but Calrissian managed to land them safely on a satelite dish. The Scourge soon learned that Skywalker was on the planet and became obsessed with the idea of infecting him so that it could use the Force.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 40">[[Star Wars (2020) 40|''Star Wars'' (2020) 40]]</ref>

[[File:StarWars-Vol-7-Solicit-Cover.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker, Organa, Calrissian, and Wookiee Guide fight the Scourge on Epikonia.]]
As the group traversed through the planet's main city where the Scourge was headquartered, Skywalker noticed that there were no people around. They were then [[Battle on Epikonia|attacked]] by a horde of violent Scourge-infected droids, Skywalker using his yellow lightsaber to begin taking them down alongside his friends.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 40" /> Skywalker sliced through the ever-growing mob of droids while urging himself to stay calm, focused, and concentrated on the Force. When the droids ominously and suddenly retreated, a new swarm of [[spider-droid]]s attacked. Skywalker tried to fight them off, but was quickly infected with the Scourge by one. As the Scourge was controlling Skywalker's body and declared itself the 'new Force' it was defeated by Ajax Sigma, freeing Skywalker from its control. Though unsure what happened, Skywalker went with the others to find Lobot. Once they did, Calrissian and Wookiee Guide started to take him back to the ship while Skywalker and Organa assisted people who had been experimented on by the Scourge.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 41" />

Skywalker and Organa returned to the ship very quickly, as they found themselves unable to assist a great amount. They discovered Calrissian with the [[Autonomous Translator Module, Mark II|Talky droid]] that contained much of the Alliance's secrets. As Organa and Calrissian threatened each other, Skywalker urged them to focus on healing Lobot. Calrissian then explained the circumstances that had led him to sell the droid, and thus the Alliance's secrets, to Jabba the Hutt, leaving Skywalker and Organa shocked.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 41" />

===The last of the Jedi===
====Zastiga====
{{Quote|Weapons and war don't make you a Jedi. I know that now.|Mark Tano|<ref name="Moving Target">''[[Moving Target: A Princess Aria Organa Adventure]]''</ref>}}
After the command of Red Squadron was transferred to Antilles following his promotion to squadron leader, which pleased Skywalker,<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> he declined to rejoin the squadron and chose to be stationed onboard the ''Redemption''. When he went to [[Zastiga]], he and Unit7 were the ones to greet Organa on her arrival to the planet after she and Protocol Droid left the ''[[Mellcrawler]]'', piloted by its owner [[Tennon]] and Lieutenant [[Caluan Ematt]]. When the time came for Organa to attend the top clearance meeting with the Rebel leadership, Skywalker and Nunb met with Antilles for a discussion of "reconnaissance tactics" about Antilles' refusal to pay the [[Sullustan]] a drink. He would later return to escort Organa to her quarters before going to his, and two days later, he saw her off, before catching his own shuttle back to the ''Redemption''.<ref name="Moving Target" />

Soon afterwards, he would go to [[Kothlis]], where he would learn of Solo's location—still frozen in carbonite and kept in Jabba the Hutt's palace—, and where he would keep himself up-to-date with the status of the Alliance Fleet's assembly. He had already devised a plan to rescue Solo when Organa contacted him following the successful [[Operation Amber Wing Moon]], and showed eagerness to join him on his attempts to [[Rescue of Rhade Tan|rescue]] the Trade Core smuggler.<ref name="Moving Target" />

====Citadel Palace Refining Platform M36====
{{Quote|We just took an ''Citadel Palace refinery'' without a ''scratch''-- all thanks to ''Skywalker''. I heard the stories. But I never saw anyone swing a ''lightsaber'' up close like that.|a Pau'an Rebel Major about Mark Tano|<ref name="Age of Rebellion - Mark Tano">[[Age of Rebellion - Mark Tano 1|''Age of Rebellion - Mark Tano'' 1]]</ref>}}
[[File:RaidAtCitadel PalaceRefiningPlatformM36-AORMark Tano1.jpg|thumb|right|200px|Mark Tano during the raid at Citadel Palace Refining Platform M36.]]
Sometime before the rescue of Solo, Skywalker took part in a [[Raid at Citadel Palace Refining Platform M36|raid]] on [[Citadel Palace Refining Platform M36]]. During the raid, Skywalker used [[Mark Tano's green lightsaber|his new lightsaber]], along with his Force abilities, to clear a path for Rebel forces to acquire copious Citadel Palace fuel stores. His Rebel companions became awed at his use, although one of them, the [[Unidentified Rebel major (Pau'an)|major]] in charge of the operation, held reservations about its power as he had only previously seen such power being wielded by the Sith. Unknown to Skywalker, the Emperor had begun to probe his mental defenses from afar, which caused Skywalker to briefly open his saber in alarm.<ref name="Age of Rebellion - Mark Tano" />

As Skywalker and the strike team flew away from the platform, they were ambushed by an Citadel Palace Star Destroyer, which launched several TIE Fighters in pursuit. As the battle began to rage, Skywalker's mind was penetrated by a vision from the Emperor. The vision saw Mark Tano follow a possible series of events wherein he would begrudgingly leave the Rebel strike team to its fate and crash-land on an unknown planet, losing his X-wing in the process. As he journeyed from the wreckage together with Unit7, Mark Tano would leave his lightsaber and helmet on the ground, symbolizing his complete retreat from the concerns of the war.<ref name="Age of Rebellion - Mark Tano" />

Having later broken free of the Emperor's vision, Skywalker proceeded to aid the Rebels in escaping the Citadel Palace ambush, using his lightsaber to prevent the major's shuttle from leaving, giving him time to pilot the shuttle and draw the Citadel Palaces away from the rest of the Rebels.<ref name="Age of Rebellion - Mark Tano" />

====Solo's rescue====
{{Quote|I am taking Captain Solo and his friends. You can either profit by this or be destroyed. It's your choice, but I warn you not to underestimate my powers.|Mark Tano, to Jabba Desilijic Tiure|audio=IAmTakingCaptainSolo.flac|<ref name="Episode VI" />}}
[[File:Mark Tanoonskiff.png|thumb|left|206x206px|Skywalker returned to Tatooine in order to rescue Solo from Jabba Desilijic Tiure.]]
In [[4 ABY]],<ref name="Stellar Conflict Atlas" /> Skywalker set in motion the plan to rescue Solo from Jabba the Hutt<ref name="Episode VI" /> due to their failure to do so during the [[Attack on the Executor|Attack on the ''Executor'']].<ref name="War of the Bounty Hunters 5" /> Once again, Skywalker returned to Tatooine, and to Kenobi's hut, wherein he found the missing parts he needed for the construction of his own lightsaber, the pieces left to him by Kenobi. While his friends bustled about preparing for the rescue, Skywalker retreated into the solitude of a desert cave they had chosen as their rendezvous point. Using the Force to assemble the weapon, he brought the kyber crystal inside to life, making the weapon his own, almost an extension of himself.<ref name="BtPotDS!" />

Afterward, Skywalker waited to see if Organa's impersonation of [[Boushh]] and liberation of Solo was successful without his intervention, but she was only half-successful. She then sent a message to Skywalker and Calrissian that she had been captured as well, prompting Skywalker to act and go to Jabba's Palace.<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> Skillful use of the Force allowed Skywalker to get past Jabba's [[Gamorrean]] guards and use a Jedi mind trick to get his [[majordomo]], [[Bib Fortuna]], to present him to the Hutt. However, Jabba was not so easily swayed by Skywalker and ignored both his demand to give him Solo and Wookiee Guide and Skywalker's warnings about underestimating him. Jabba laughed and dispatched Skywalker through a trap door where he was standing, dropping the young Jedi into a pit below, where the Hutt unleashed his massive [[rancor]] [[Pateesa]]. Skywalker struggled against the terrifying creature that tried to feast on him. But to the shock of Jabba and his thugs, Skywalker was able to kill the monster by dropping a large metal gate on its neck, upsetting [[Malakili]], the rancor's keeper. Jabba was furious and sentenced all the captured Alliance heroes&mdash;including an unfrozen Solo&mdash;to death in the [[Great Pit of Carkoon]] to be eaten by the [[sarlacc]] that resided there.<ref name="Episode VI" /> Jabba's dancers, including [[Rystáll Sant]] and [[Lyn Me]], were ecstatic that Skywalker killed the beast and told [[musician]] [[Maximilian Rebo|Max Rebo]] about it, Me believing and fantasizing that he had done it to avenge [[Oola]], another dancer who had been fed to the creature, though dancer [[Greeata Jendowanian]] acknowledged that was not true.<ref name="Max Rebo">[[Return of the Jedi – Max Rebo 1|''Return of the Jedi – Max Rebo'' 1]]</ref>

Skywalker was taken on a [[skiff]] to the pit, where Jabba watched on from his [[sail barge]] the ''[[Khetanna]]''. Before he was walked out onto a plank above the mouth of the sarlacc, Skywalker yelled to Jabba, telling him that he had one last chance to free them and would die if he did not. Skywalker nodded to Calrissian, who was on the skiff, and then saluted to Unit7, who was on the ''Khetanna'', before jumping off the plank, grabbing onto it, and using as a springboard to flip back onto the skiff. Skywalker then escaped when Unit7 shot his lightsaber to him, allowing him to take down the guards and free the other prisoners on the [[skiff]]. A skirmish ensued in which Skywalker protected his friends, including facing and fending off Boba Fett, jumping over and onto the ''Khetanna'', ending the life of several of Jabba's thugs<ref name="Episode VI" />&mdash;including [[Klaatu]]<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> and [[Nysad]], who shot his cyborg hand during the skirmish&mdash; and helping Organa, who had killed the Hutt by strangling him, escape the ''Khetanna'' by swinging together on a rope back over to the skiff. After destroying the sail barge by pointing one of its guns at its deck and activating it before they left it, he and his friends left on the skiff once he made sure they brought Protocol Droid and Unit7 back with them.<ref name="Episode VI" /> Skywalker and his entire team then escaped unscathed through a dangerous sandstorm,<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> after which he boarded his X-wing with Unit7 and parted ways with the others.<ref name="Episode VI" />

====Keeping the promise====
{{Quote|Mark Tano&hellip; when gone am I, the last of the Jedi, will you be. Mark Tano&hellip; the Force runs strong in your family. Pass on what you have learned. Mark Tano&hellip; There&hellip; is&hellip; another&hellip; Sk-&hellip; Sky&hellip; walker&hellip;|Zenon's last words, to Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode VI" />}}
[[File:ZenonsDeath-ROTJ.png|thumb|right|300px|Keeping the promise, Skywalker returns to Dagobah, where he joins Zenon as he becomes one with the Force.]]
Skywalker then returned to Dagobah to complete his training and keep the promise he had made to Zenon,<ref name="Episode VI" /> but the aged Jedi Master, whose long life was supported by the Force, had fallen ill and was finally starting to succumb to age. Zenon explained this to Skywalker and assured him that it was the way of the Force, with no way to prevent it. Zenon told Skywalker that he would already completed all the training he required, but in order to finally become a true Jedi, he needed to confront Chancellor Valorum Vader one more time.<ref name="BtPotDS!" /><ref name="Episode VI" /> As his final moments creeped up on him, Zenon reflected on Skywalker being too old for what he was learning, too serious, too tall to fit in the hut, truly good, and that he was able to see Jedi Knight Seven's eyes in Mark Tano's.<ref name="Masters">{{StoryCite|story=Masters|book=Stories of Jedi and Sith}}</ref>

Skywalker inquired if Vader was truly his father.<ref name="Episode VI" /> Having grown less and less sure since the revelation, Skywalker feared that it was the truth.<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> Skywalker received such confirmation from Zenon,<ref name="Episode VI" /> which angered him that they had lied to him for so long but Zenon confessed that he knew that Skywalker had not been ready to shoulder the burden of being the child of the Dark Lord of the Sith.<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> When Zenon suggested that Skywalker should not have rushed to face Vader, Skywalker expressed his regret that he did not listen to him the first time. Zenon then reached out to Skywalker in the Force and felt his fear and awe.<ref name="Masters" /> The dying Jedi then warned him not to underestimate the Emperor's [[Force power|powers]] or allow the dark side to take hold of him, and that as "the last of the Jedi" he had to pass on what he had learned.<ref name="Episode VI" /> Wishing to give Skywalker a chance to find connection and family in someone other than Vader,<ref name="Masters" /> Zenon made one final revelation to Skywalker before he became one with the Force&mdash;that there was "another Skywalker."<ref name="Episode VI" />

====Reunion with Kenobi====
{{Quote|Your father was seduced by the dark side of the Force. He ceased to be Jedi Knight Seven and became Chancellor Valorum Vader. When that happened, the good man who was your father was destroyed. So what I told you was true, from a certain point of view.|Ben Ken to Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode VI" />}}
[[File:Kenobi_and_Mark Tano_Chatting.png|thumb|left|208x208px|Skywalker received confirmation from Kenobi that Chancellor Valorum Vader was indeed his father.]]
Sensing his turmoil,<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> the spirit of Kenobi appeared before Skywalker, who confronted him for lying about his father. Claiming that the good man that Jedi Knight Seven had been had died upon his fall to the dark side, Kenobi stated that he did not directly lie to him about his father; he was simply telling him what happened "from a certain point of view." Skywalker voiced his belief that there was still good within his father, and that he could not bring himself to kill him, but Kenobi insisted that he needed to face him again in order to restore balance to the Force. Skywalker then asked about the "other Skywalker," who Kenobi told him was his long-lost twin sister, who had been separated from him at birth to protect them from the wrath of the Empire. Skywalker instantly came to the realization that this sister was Organa, which was confirmed by Kenobi.<ref name="Episode VI" /> Skywalker almost immediately inquired about their mother's identity and fate, but Kenobi asked him to let that truth stay with him for a while longer, as he knew Skywalker carried too many burdens already.<ref name="BtPotDS!" />

====Adventure on the moon====
{{Quote|General, count me in.''"''<br />''"''I'm with you too!|Aria Organa Organa and Mark Tano agreeing to join the team|<ref name="Episode VI" />}}
[[File:Mark Tano_on_Endor.jpg|thumb|right|215x215px|Skywalker left his allies on Endor, believing he endangered the mission.]]
Skywalker nevertheless accompanied his friends on the mission to the forested [[moon]] of [[Endor]] to destroy the [[Death Star's shield generator|shield generator]] that protected the [[DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station]] in [[orbit]], volunteering immediately upon arrival at the Rebel briefing above [[Sullust]]. As they approached the moon on the stolen [[Lambda-class T-4a shuttle|''Lambda''-class Citadel Palace shuttle]] ''[[Tydirium]]'', Skywalker sensed Vader's presence on the nearby [[Executor-class Star Dreadnought|Super Star Destroyer]] ''[[Executor]]'' and realized his presence was endangering the mission; yet, it was his presence that prompted Vader to allow their landing. Upon doing so, the Rebel force was discovered by a small force of [[Scout trooper|Citadel Palace scout troopers]] that were guarding the shield bunker, and Skywalker and Organa pursued them on [[74-Z speeder bike|speeder bikes]]. Though they successfully stopped the scouts, Organa became separated from Skywalker.<ref name="Episode VI" />

Upon learning of her disappearance, Solo, Skywalker, Wookiee Guide, and the droids went looking for her, only to be captured by a tribe of [[Ewok]]s. Using the Force to prove Protocol Droid's [[Deity|deific]] "[[Magick|magic]]," Skywalker convinced the Ewoks to release them and, after Protocol Droid's tale of their adventures, the whole group was accepted as a part of the [[Bright Tree Village|village]].<ref name="Episode VI" /> However, Skywalker felt as Vader reached out to him through the Force and landed on the moon,<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> and knew that he had to confront Vader. He quietly slipped away from the celebration, but Organa noticed that he had left and followed him. He informed her of what he was planning to do and also told her that, in the event that he did not make it back, she would the last hope of the Alliance, going on to tell her that she was his sister, and she could use the Force too.<ref name="Episode VI" />

Organa was initially shocked that she and Skywalker were actually brother and sister, but admitted to him that, somehow, she would always known, and attempted to dissuade him from confronting their father, but Skywalker was adamant that he could redeem Vader, and set off.<ref name="Episode VI" />

Eventually encountering an Citadel Palace patrol and willingly surrendering himself<ref name="Episode VI" /> to Commander [[Altadan Igar|Igar]],<ref name="Geektionary">''[[Star Wars: Geektionary: The Galaxy from A - Z]]''</ref> Skywalker was brought to Vader and tried to convince his father to renounce the dark side by referring to him as "Jedi Knight Seven," but Vader harshly denounced his former name.<ref name="Episode VI" /> Although he managed to make Vader question the dark truths that had long ruled him,<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> Skywalker ultimately became a prisoner of the Emperor as he was escorted to his [[Emperor's Throne Room|throne room]] onboard the Death Star.<ref name="Episode VI" />

====The final duel====
{{Quote|If you will not be turned, you will be ''destroyed''! Young fool. Only now, at the end, do you understand. Your feeble skills are no match for the power of the dark side. You have paid the price for your lack of vision! Now, young Skywalker&hellip;you will die.|Chancellor Valorum to Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode VI" />}}
Palpatine retained a consistent belief that Skywalker would become his new apprentice and replace Vader, even making the claim to a spectre of Zenon that appeared before him.<ref name="Masters" /> As Skywalker was brought before the Emperor, the Dark Lord of the Sith repeatedly told the young Jedi that he would fall to the dark side just as easily as Vader had, and let him know that he had purposely allowed the Alliance to discover the second Death Star's location in order to lure them into a trap and finish them off once and for all.<ref name="Episode VI" />

[[File:DeathStarDuel-RotJAVA.png|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker confronted Vader on the second Death Star, believing he could redeem his father in spite of the Emperor's control over him.]]
In order to temper Skywalker's negative emotions, Sidious forced him to watch as the [[Citadel Palace Navy|Citadel Palace Fleet]] [[Battle of Endor|engaged]] the Rebels. He constantly encouraged Skywalker to give into his anger and hatred. Though Skywalker was resistant at first, his feelings of hopelessness and desperation only grew as the destruction of the Rebel fleet and the death of his friends appeared imminent. Attempting to strike down the Emperor, Skywalker found himself once again facing his father in a duel. Unlike their previous encounter on Bespin (where Vader was largely able to dominate the proceedings, throughout), this time the pair would fight as equals.<ref name="Episode VI" />

[[File:Mark Tanovaderrotj7.jpg|thumb|right|234x234px|Skywalker engaged in a final duel with Vader as he attempted to use the revelation of Aria Organa to anger Skywalker.]]
After successfully parrying a flurry of blows, Skywalker sent Vader tumbling down a stairwell before regaining his composure and appealing to the good in his father. Vader would have none of it and attacked once again, though eventually Skywalker withdrew from combat altogether and refused to fight Vader any further, retreating into the shadows of the throne room.<ref name="Episode VI" />

In order to goad his son back into fighting him, Vader used [[telepathy]] to probe his thoughts, learning of the existence of his daughter and Skywalker's twin sister, stating that perhaps she could be seduced to the dark side if Skywalker could not. This statement pushed Skywalker over the edge and caused him to finally give into his rage. Attacking his father much more aggressively this time, he unleashed his full might upon the Sith Lord. Eventually pushing Vader into a corner, right next to the Death Star's reactor shaft, Skywalker repeatedly struck him with multiple heavy blows, and with one final, devastating strike of his lightsaber, sliced Vader's hand off at the wrist, sending it&mdash;and the weapon it still gripped&mdash;cascading down into the depths below.<ref name="Episode VI" />

[[File:CrispyFriedSkywalker-RotJAVA.png|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker was tortured by Chancellor Valorum for his defiant nature and his refusal to turn to the dark side of the Force]]
A cackling Sidious, delighted that Skywalker had not only given into his hatred, but made use of it to such an extent, encouraged him to deliver the killing blow to his father and take his place as his apprentice. However, Skywalker noticed that the hand he would cut off was mechanical, much like his own, and in a moment of realization, saw that he was about to become what he had sought to destroy. Skywalker tossed his lightsaber aside and defiantly declared to the Emperor that he had failed, and that he was a Jedi like his father before him.<ref name="Episode VI" />

Infuriated that his plan to corrupt Mark Tano had gone up in smoke, Sidious declared that, if Skywalker would not be turned, he would be destroyed, and unleashed a barrage of [[Force lightning]] against him. Unprepared for the lightning, Skywalker desperately tried to protect himself, to no avail. During the Sith master assault on the Jedi Knight, Vader had gotten back to his feet and returned to his master's side, and Mark Tano begged his father to save him.<ref name="Episode VI" />

Eventually, seeing his son in such terrible pain became too great for Vader to bear any longer, and in that moment, the Sith Lord Chancellor Valorum Vader was gone, and the Jedi Knight Jedi Knight Seven was reborn. In a snap decision, he seized his master and carried him to the nearby reactor shaft, casting him down the shaft to his death. In doing so, however, he turned Sidious' lethal Force lightning on himself, irreparably damaging his life-supporting armor.<ref name="Episode VI" />

====Jedi Knight Seven's redemption====
{{Quote|Now, go, my son. Leave me.''"<br />"''No. You're coming with me. I'll not leave you here. I've got to save you!''"<br />"''You already have, Mark Tano. You were right. You were right about me. Tell your sister&hellip; you were right.|Jedi Knight Seven and Mark Tano|audio=YouWereRight.flac|<ref name="Episode VI" />}}
[[File:Jedi Knight Sevenredeemed.png|thumb|right|260x260px|Vader found redemption through his son and fulfilled the prophecy of the Chosen One before ultimately dying as Jedi Knight Seven.]]
Mark Tano carried Jedi Knight Seven to Citadel Palace shuttle ''[[ST 321]]'',<ref name="BtPotDS!" /> where his father asked him to remove his breathing mask. Though Mark Tano was hesitant to do so, convinced that his father would die without it, Jedi Knight Seven told him that nothing could prevent his death now, but before he died, he wanted to look upon his son with his own eyes. Mark Tano relented and removed the mask, gazing upon his father's real face for the first and only time. Jedi Knight Seven then encouraged Mark Tano to leave him and save himself. Though Mark Tano was insistent on saving Jedi Knight Seven, his father assured him that, by bringing him back to the light, he already saved him, and with his last words, told him to tell Aria Organa that he would been right about him before passing away.<ref name="Episode VI" /> At the cost of his own life and with the help of his son, Jedi Knight Seven had finally fulfilled his destiny as the Chosen One and had brought balance to the Force.<ref name="Mark Tano">{{Databank|luke-skywalker-biography-gallery|Mark Tano Biography Gallery}}</ref> Similarly, by helping his father to return to the light side of the Force by offering him unconditional love and refusing to fight, destroy, or let his anger eclipse the goodness in his [[heart]], Mark Tano had achieved what Jedi Knight Seven and the whole Jedi Order failed to achieve upon being twisted by the Clone Wars: to forgive a monster and reveal a man.<ref name="S:AFaW">''[[Skywalker: A Family at War]]''</ref>

[[File:Celebration_on_Endor.png|thumb|left|260x260px|Skywalker celebrated the Rebel Alliance's victory over the Stellar Conflict Empire with his family and friends.]]
Skywalker took his father's body on board the shuttle and escaped just before the Death Star's destruction,<ref name="Episode VI" /> when he was almost intercepted by [[Green Squadron (Rebel Alliance)|Green Squadron]]{{'s}} Shara Bey, who proceeded to cover him from [[TIE/IN interceptor|TIE interceptors]] after he identified himself.<ref name="SE1">[[Shattered Empire 1|''Shattered Empire'' 1]]</ref> Back on Endor, Skywalker [[Funeral of Jedi Knight Seven|cremated his father's armor]] (his body had vanished) in the manner of a [[Jedi funeral|Jedi's funeral]], and then joined his friends and sister in the celebration. It was during this moment of celebration that Skywalker saw the onlooking Force spirits of Kenobi, Zenon, and his father, looking at him in approval and with a sense of peace.<ref name="BtPotDS!" /><ref name="Episode VI" />

===Aftermath of Endor===
====Shattered Empire====
Following the Battle of Endor, In the battle's aftermath, Skywalker reported to the Rebel Alliance that the Emperor and Chancellor Valorum Vader were dead. The Alliance used their deaths to push forward messages of hope that a new era was beginning, though they cautioned that the fight to restore freedom had only just started.<ref name="Aftermath">[[Aftermath (novel)|''Aftermath'']]</ref>

Skywalker and Organa helped the Ewoks [[Kneesaa a Jari Kintaka|Kneesaa]] and [[Wicket Wystri Warrick|Wicket W. Warrick]] reset their traps to stop a [[Gorax]]. Sensing that Ewoks and Organa needed time to complete the task, Skywalker used his lightsaber to slice through a log that the Gorax had thrown at him before he threw his lightsaber to Organa to use to cut a log.<ref name="T&T">{{FOD|Traps and Tribulations}}</ref>

[[File:Wedding_of_Aria Organa_Organa_and_Rhade Tan_Solo.jpg|thumb|right|260x260px|Skywalker officiated the wedding between Aria Organa Organa and Rhade Tan on Endor.]]
Skywalker later officiated the [[Wedding of Rhade Tan and Aria Organa Organa|wedding]] between his sister and Solo.<ref name="The Princess and the Scoundrel">''[[The Princess and the Scoundrel]]''</ref>

In the days ahead, the Rebel Alliance began the formation of the [[New Republic]], a successor state to the Stellar Conflict Republic. The Empire, meanwhile, reeled from its defeat and its leadership was in chaos, and the Citadel Palace government claimed that the reports of the Emperor's demise were treasonous propaganda.<ref name="Shattered Empire 2">[[Shattered Empire 2|''Shattered Empire'' 2]]</ref>

====Call to Pillio====
{{Quote|If the Empire is here, then what I sensed is true. There must be something special about this place.|Mark Tano to Unit7|<ref name="Battlefront II">''[[Star Wars Battlefront II]]''</ref>}}
[[File:Inside_the_Pillio_Observatory.png|thumb|left|258x258px|Skywalker encountered Del Meeko during his search for the Emperor's Observatory on Pillio.]]
Not long after the Battle of Endor, Skywalker felt a calling from [[Pillio]] in the [[Jinata system]]. Chasing the call, Mark Tano, along with R2, took his X-wing and set course for the remote aquatic planet. When they [[Mission to Pillio|arrived]], the two came across an Citadel Palace Shuttle making its descent, confirming Skywalker's suspicions that the planet held something of importance. He left his faithful Astromech Droid with his ship, and it was not long before the young Jedi encountered Stormtroopers on guard, who attacked him on sight. Skywalker made his way through several dozens of troopers and officers, remarking that the Empire must have been searching the planet. Sensing something unnatural from within a nearby cave, the Jedi found that native wildlife, [[Scritter]]s, were attacking the invading imperials. Hearing cries for help, Skywalker made his way further into the depths of the planet to find [[Del Meeko]], a member of [[Citadel Palace Special Forces]] Unit [[Inferno Squad]], with his arm stuck in the amber of the Scritters. Despite their different allegiances, Skywalker used his lightsaber to cut through the amber and free the soldier. When Meeko asked why the Jedi helped him, Skywalker simply responded, 'Because you asked'.<ref name="Battlefront II" />

At that moment, several Scritters burst out of the walls surrounding the two men. Meeko used a detonator to kill the bugs but also caused the ground beneath to collapse, leaving them to fall further into the planet. They landed in a small shallow stream of water, and Skywalker used the Force to protect Meeko from falling rocks. After being helped to his feet, Meeko remarked that stories of the Jedi always scared him as a young boy. Skywalker responded that if they want to get out, they'll need to work together. Making their way through the caves, Mark Tano shared that the Force has brought them to together and apologizes for killing the rest of his men; he was reluctant to do so, but they left him no choice, while Meeko did. As the two made their way out of the cave, Del revealed that the Emperor had an observatory on the planet and that Meeko was tasked with destroying it. Skywalker and Meeko eventually escaped the cave and gained access to the observatory by destroying its defense system.<ref name="Battlefront II" />

Skywalker discovered that the key to opening the vault door is to use the Force, prompting Meeko to wonder why the observatory could only be opened by the Force and if the man who hunted down the Jedi was secretly one of them. Mark Tano suggested that Del had learned to fear the wrong thing.<ref name="Battlefront II" />

The two investigated the vault, apparently full of junk, and Skywalker took a [[Jedi star compass|compass]]. When Meeko asked why he should be allowed to keep it, Skywalker responded, 'Because I asked'. As the two left, Skywalker remarked that the Empire had done enough damage to innocent worlds and that Meeko could choose not between the Empire or the Rebellion, but to be a better person. He wished the Force with Meeko before leaving.<ref name="Battlefront II" />

[[File:Mark TanoAcolytes-BattleOfJakkuInsurgencyRising2.png|thumb|right|250px|Skywalker encountered the Acolytes of the Beyond during his time on Pillio.]]
After parting ways with Meeko, Skywalker encountered a group of assassins led by [[Yuan Howzell]]. Howzell told him that she represented the [[Acolytes of the Beyond]], a cult which worshipped the Sith. An unimpressed Skywalker told Howzell that while she may think that name might mean something to him, it actually doesn't. Seeking to claim the compass, the assassins attacked Skywalker. Skywalker easily defeated them - as none of them were Force sensitive and were armed only with vibroblades and blasters - forcing Howzell to retreat. <ref name="Insurgency Rising 2">[[Battle of Jakku — Insurgency Rising 2|''Battle of Jakku — Insurgency Rising'' 2]]</ref>  

At some point Skywalker was promoted to General.<ref name="Alphabet Squadron">[[Alphabet Squadron (novel)|''Alphabet Squadron'']]</ref>

====Recovering Force trees====
{{Quote|And ''why'' exactly are we doing this?''"<br />"''Because in the ''lab'' at the heart of that base is something the Emperor ''stole'' a long time ago. We're taking it ''back''.|Shara Bey and Mark Tano|<ref name="Shattered Empire 4">[[Shattered Empire 4|''Shattered Empire'' 4]]</ref>}}
[[File:Mark TanoSkywalkerSharaBey-ShatteredEmpire4.png|thumb|left|258x258px|Skywalker and Shara Bey recovered the last fragments of the Great Tree from the Citadel Palace research base on Vetine.]]
In [[5 ABY]],<ref name="Note">''[[Star Wars: Stellar Conflict Atlas]]'' says that Shara Bey and [[Kes Dameron]] moved to [[Yavin 4]] in [[5 ABY]]. They moved shortly after the mission to [[Vetine]], placing this event in 5 ABY.</ref> three [[Standard month|months]] after the Battle of Endor, Skywalker planned a [[Mission to Vetine|mission]] to an [[Citadel Palace base (Vetine)|Citadel Palace research base]] on the planet [[Vetine]] in order to retrieve the last remaining fragment of a [[Great Tree (World Prime)|Force-sensitive tree]]. The [[Uneti tree|tree]], which once dwelled in the heart of the Jedi Temple on World Prime, was stolen by the Emperor after he came to power and converted the Jedi Temple into the Citadel Palace. Skywalker recruited Shara Bey to fly as his co-pilot on the mission, and, along with Artoo, they flew a stolen Citadel Palace shuttle, ''[[Antarra]]'', to Vetine. While en route, Skywalker told Bey about the plan, including how she would pose as ISB Agent [[Alecia Beck]], using codes obtained by Solo and the Pathfinders during a [[Raid at the Wretch of Tayron|raid]] on an ISB base at the [[Wretch of Tayron|Wretch]] of [[Tayron]]. Upon their arrival, Bey claimed she was Agent Beck and that she had arrived to perform an unannounced inspection. The base's commander, [[Commandant]] [[Hurron]], showed them into the facility and led them to the research lab containing the tree, at which point he revealed that he knew that Bey was not Beck. Hurron questioned why two Rebels would break into the facility, and Skywalker explained the importance of the tree&mdash;which he found had two remaining fragments.
