Skywalker and Bey fought their way out of the base, making their way through numerous stormtroopers who attempted to stop their escape. Once back at ''Antarra'', Hurron ordered his forces to throw thermal detonators at the escaping Rebels, but Skywalker used the Force to deflect them back, killing Hurron and several of his stormtroopers in an explosion.<ref name="Shattered Empire 4" />

The Rebel trio made their way back towards the Alliance Fleet. During the trip back, Skywalker and Bey discussed the latter's future plans for service in the Rebellion, as Skywalker knew that Bey was considering leaving the Alliance to reunite with her husband, Pathfinder Sergeant Kes Dameron, and their son Poe. Bey was unsure as to whether she wanted to leave the Rebels behind, but Skywalker's guidance helped Bey decide to leave the Alliance. The Jedi Knight gifted one of the tree fragments to her, as he had only expected to find one, believing that the important relic would be kept safe with Bey and her family. She and Dameron planted it outside of their [[Wetyin's Colony|new home]] on Yavin 4.<ref name="Shattered Empire 4" />

====War's end====
{{Quote|He's ''beautiful'', Aria Organa--I'm so happy for you both...the three of you.''"<br />"''How does it feel to be an uncle, Mark Tano? Maybe that'll keep you close and stop your wandering.|Mark Tano and Aria Organa Organa discussing the birth of Ben|<ref name="Last Stand 4" />}}
[[File:Stellar ConflictConcordance-BattleOfJakkuLastStand4.png|thumb|right|250px|Skywalker attended the signing of the Stellar Conflict Concordance between the Stellar Conflict Empire and the New Republic on Chandrila]]
An [[Unidentified Citadel Palace gunner|Citadel Palace officer]] stationed on a Star Destroyer during the [[Battle of Jakku]] claimed to have seen the Jedi Knight using the Force and a lightsaber to dispatch Star Destroyers in space, causing them to crash into the surface of the planet. When the Star Destroyer crashed into the surface the officer said he was recovered by a figure who dragged him across the desert searching wreckage for other survivors. He also noted the man wore clothes similar to Mark Tano and talked about being raised in another desert.<ref name="Legends">''[[The Legends of Mark Tano]]''</ref> Skywalker was indeed at [[Jakku]], though he confronted [[Ubrik Adelhard]] aboard the [[Scepter (Citadel Palace-class)|''Scepter'']] and was not on the ground.<ref name="Last Stand 4">[[Battle of Jakku — Last Stand 4|''Battle of Jakku — Last Stand'' 4]]</ref>

[[File:TheSkywalkerSoloFamily-BattleOfJakkuLastStand4.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker visited his family shortly after the birth of his nephew Ben.]]
The Stellar Conflict came to a close with the signing of the [[Stellar Conflict Concordance]], a peace treaty between the Republic and the Empire that forced it to remain within pre-established borders, though some of the remnants of the once-powerful military force disappeared into the [[Unknown Regions]].<ref name="TFA VD">''[[Star Wars: The Force Awakens: The Visual Dictionary]]''</ref> Skywalker, along with many other notable individuals witnessed the signing of the Concordance between Mas Amedda and Mon Mothma.<ref name="Last Stand 4" />

Following the signing of the treaty, Aria Organa gave birth to her and Rhade Tan's son and Mark Tano's nephew, Ben Solo. Skywalker visited the family shortly after Ben's birth where Aria Organa hoped that Skywalker being an uncle would keep him closer to home.<ref name="Last Stand 4" /> There were rumors that Skywalker visited his sister and Rhade Tan before disappearing on an untold mission. Others claimed that his absence was conspicuous.<ref name="Empire's End">''[[Aftermath: Empire's End]]''</ref>

===Rebuilding the Jedi Order===
====Training his sister====
=====Becoming a teacher=====
{{Quote|You're going to make me a better teacher.''"<br />"''What do you mean?''"<br />"''Your footwork is terrible. Don't get me wrong, your lightsaber craft is coming along, but&hellip;you do other things. Naturally. What I mean is, you're exceptional. Just&hellip;different.|Skywalker and Organa during the latter's training|<ref name="TROS: Expanded Edition">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: Expanded Edition]]''</ref>}}
[[File:Mark Tano-Aria Organa-training.jpg|thumb|right|250px|After the Battle of Endor, Skywalker's sister became his first apprentice.]]
Some time after the Battle of Endor, Skywalker took on his first student and trained his twin sister in the ways of the Force. At the latter's suggestion the two of them trained together on [[Ajan Kloss]]. Under his tutelage, Organa constructed [[Aria Organa's lightsaber|her lightsaber]], and began to learn the principles of lightsaber combat. Skywalker also instructed in her in the basics of the Force, teaching her about light side, and in meditation. He was impressed by Organa's strength in the Force and how quickly she progressed in her training. While training her, he found it interesting that she struggled with skills and concepts that he had a natural affinity for (like lightsaber combat), but excelled in other areas (like meditation) that were harder for him to master. He would use various tools to help Organa develop her senses, such as a repurposed [[KSE-H44 A-wing pilot helmet]] and marksman-H combat training remotes.<ref name="TROS VD" />

At some point during their training together, Skywalker and Organa spent an hour sparring with their lightsabers. Later that same day, Skywalker attempted to teach her in a scenario similar to what he did with Zenon on Dagobah, where she held herself up in a handstand with the Force.<ref name="TROS: Expanded Edition" /> At another point, Skywalker explained from personal experience that the Force allowed glimpses of the future, past, and at times, departed, and that these voices would offer her guidance from beyond death in times of hardship.<ref name="TROS VD" />

=====The Archivist's Holocron=====
{{Quote|Here. I'll activate it for you.''"<br />"''This doesn't look like the other ones.''"<br />"''Well it's definitely a holocron of some kind, but I've never seen another like it. It responds to&hellip;well. You'll see it'll answer your questions though. I know it did for me.|Skywalker and Organa on the Archivist's Holocron|<ref name="Hidden Empire 5" />}}
Sometime during Organa's training, the two discovered<ref name="Hidden Empire 5" /> a [[The Archivist's Holocron|holocron]] that contained the story of Lady [[Qi'ra]], the former leader of Crimson Dawn, and her [[war against the Sith]] that she had carried out between 3 ABY and 4 ABY shortly before the fall of the Empire. Skywalker had listened to it beforehand and it had answered his questions, so he activated wit for Organa using the light side of the Force. He agreed with Organa that it was unusual for a holocron despite definitely being one, telling her she would see why and assuring her it would answer her questions.<ref name="Crimson Reign 1">[[Crimson Reign 1|''Crimson Reign'' 1]]</ref> As the Archivist described Qi'ra's plans to kill Vader and Palpatine, Skywalker lamented that Qi'ra had never come to them for help and instead kept everything secret and did it by herself. Organa suggested it was because Qi'ra was not trusting.<ref name="Hidden Empire 1">[[Hidden Empire 1|''Hidden Empire'' 1]]</ref> The Archivist suggested that the Rebel Alliance had perhaps been engineered by Palpatine, which Skywalker said the Archivist at at lest gotten wrong, but Organa pointed out that while he did not create it, he definitely used it.<ref name="Hidden Empire 2" /> When she described the presence of Chancellor Valorum Vader as feeling like you were in the presence of an animal eating its own young, Skywalker held onto that idea and repeated it out loud.<ref name="Hidden Empire 3">[[Hidden Empire 3|''Hidden Empire'' 3]]</ref>

[[File:Mark TanoAndAria OrganaHolocron-HiddenEmpire5.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker and Organa with the Archivist's Holocron]]
At the end of the story, the Archivist said that Qi'ra had failed to take down the Sith and saw her hidden empire of Crimson Dawn destroyed, even theorizing that Qi'ra had been killed by the Empire or its [[Citadel Palace Remnants|remnants]] as she had never seen her again. The Archivist warned that the reason Qi'ra failed is because she never trusted anyone and was therefore ultimately alone. Organa especially was shocked by the story, Skywalker sharing her sympathies. He told Organa that the Archivist had been wrong, however, in saying that Qi'ra had failed to take down the Sith and the Empire, as Crimson Dawn agents had been the ones that revealed the existence of the second Death star to the rebellion, Aria Organa adding that Qi'ra's syndicate war had allowed the Rebellion to regroup by distracting Palpatine. Skywalker postulated that because nothing happens in a vacuum, Qi'ra had touched the galaxy and saved it from the Sith, just not in the way she thought. Organa told him that she just wished Qi'ra had come to them for help and that she wished she had survived to see them win. Unbeknownst to them, however, Qi'ra had survived.<ref name="Hidden Empire 5" />

=====Aria Organa's final training session=====
{{Quote|It was the last night of her training. Aria Organa told me that she had sensed the death of her son at the end of her Jedi path. She surrendered her saber to me and said one day it would be picked up again by someone who would finish her journey.|Mark Tano, to Rey|<ref name="Episode IX" />}}
On the final night of her training, Organa experienced a dark vision that her Jedi path would lead to the death of her [[Ben Solo|son]].<ref name="Episode IX" /> Realizing where the galaxy needed her most,<ref name="TROS VD" /> she set aside her lightsaber<ref name="Episode IX" /> to focus on her new family and [[New Republic Senate|senatorial]] duties.<ref name="TROS VD" /> While Skywalker hoped that his sister would resume her training later on, Organa gave him her lightsaber to convince him otherwise, asking to pass it on to a promising student someday. However, Skywalker did not do that and never told her where he stored her lightsaber.<ref name="TROS: Expanded Edition" />

====Quest for knowledge====
{{Quote|I had great hope for the future of the Jedi. I came to believe that if a single Jedi could help bring balance back to the Force, then perhaps a restored Jedi Order could maintain peace and prevent the dark side from ever regaining its hold on the galaxy. So I scoured worlds for the remaining Jedi texts and gathered a new class of apprentices under my tutelage.|Mark Tano|<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi">''[[Star Wars: The Secrets of the Jedi]]''</ref>}}
[[File:Mark TanoSearchForJediStuff-Timelines.png|thumb|300px|right|Skywalker and Unit7 searched out Jedi lore together.]]
With the Empire fallen and the Sith seamlessly vanquished, Skywalker had great hope for the future of the Jedi. He believed if a single Jedi could bring balance to the Force as his father had done, then a revived Jedi Order could keep the peace and prevent the dark side from ever returning to such strength.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" />

Just as he promised Farnay near the start of his own Jedi studies,<ref name="weapon-jedi" /> in 5 ABY,<ref name="Mark Tano lore date">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' states that Mark Tano began searching for Force lore twenty-nine years before the [[Hosnian Cataclysm|Starkiller Incident]], which ''[[Star Wars: Stellar Conflict Atlas]]'' dates to [[34 ABY]]. Therefore, he began traveling the galaxy for Force lore in [[5 ABY]].</ref> Skywalker set about rebuilding the Jedi Order. Despite his optimism, he had many unanswered questions<ref name="TLJ VD">''[[Star Wars: The Last Jedi: The Visual Dictionary]]''</ref> and was hesitant to take on another apprentice after his sister Aria Organa, unsure of his grounding in Jedi lore.<ref name="TROS VD" /> Instead, Skywalker largely disappeared from galactic view and dedicated himself to traveling the galaxy in hopes of finding what remained of the Jedi after the Empire's long efforts to eradicate their history. Through his quest, he came to understand much about himself and his destiny and gained the confidence he needed to rebuild the Jedi Order.<ref name="TLJ VD" /> Mark Tano, being the last Jedi, became a caretaker of the Jedi Order's legacy. As he traveled the galaxy, he also searched for force-sensitives who could possibly become his students.<ref name="Star Wars Book" />

[[File:Elphrona-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Mark Tano visited many places in search of Jedi lore, including Elphrona.]]
Skywalker's research into the Jedi was a long and difficult task that took him years.<ref name="TLJ VD" /> He was aided by [[Lor San Tekka]], an explorer and member of the [[Church of the Force]]<ref name="San Tekka DB">{{Databank|lor-san-tekka|Lor San Tekka}}</ref> who, though not Force-sensitive himself, believed in the Jedi ideals. San Tekka was old enough to remember the Jedi Knights before the Clone Wars, and he did not believe the Emperor's lies about how the Jedi betrayed the Old Republic.<ref name="TFA VD" /> San Tekka, who believed that the return of the Jedi Order was essential to bring balance to the Force,<ref name="Episode VII" /> became a valuable ally for both Skywalker and Organa.<ref name="TFA VD" />

[[Gatalenta]] was one of the first destinations in Skywalker's search,<ref name="Bloodline">[[Bloodline (novel)|''Bloodline'']]</ref> and he also traveled to Moraband,<ref name="The Dark Side">''[[Star Wars: The Dark Side]]''</ref> the ancient home of the Sith,<ref name="Destiny" /> to investigate anything he could about the Force.<ref name="The Dark Side" /> He visited the [[Deep Core]] planet of [[Tython]] many times and studied its ancient [[Force-henge|ruined temple]], impressed by the majesty of the site every time he visited.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> He scoured many worlds and assembled a collection of eight ancient bound [[book]]s<ref name="TROS VD" /> and scrolls<ref name="Episode VIII" /> that described Jedi tenets, history and guidance for those following the path of the Jedi&mdash;[[sacred Jedi texts]]. One of the books was the ''[[Rammahgon]]'', an influential work that was thought destroyed over 5,000 years ago but retrieved by Skywalker while he explored the subterranean ruins of [[Ossus]]. The ''[[Aionomica]]'' was another, a two-volume collection of Jedi explorations and codifications of the Force, part codex, correspondence and scrapbook.<ref name="TROS VD" /> He also found a book that was a catalog of the [[Eeshaypher Collection]], a forbidden gallery of artifacts related to the dark side of the Force.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> At one point, Skywalker journeyed to [[Black Spire Outpost]] on [[Batuu]], searching for ancient Jedi texts and artifacts.<ref name="Galaxy's Edge">[[Star Wars: Galaxy's Edge|''Star Wars'': Galaxy's Edge]]</ref>

[[File:Aionomica.png|thumb|right|250px|Skywalker uncovered the ''Aionomica'' and other Jedi relics on his travels.]]
Skywalker dedicated much of these years to finding the site of the [[first Jedi Temple]]. He uncovered many tantalizing clues that hinted at the origins of the Jedi, but the precise location was a mystery. One key to unravelling the mystery was his study of the spread of the Force-sensitive uneti saplings.<ref name="TLJ VD" /> He also made use of the [[Jedi star compass]] he had discovered in the Emperor's storehouse on Pillio. With a [[plasma]]-encased [[supraluminite]] [[lodestone]] at its center, the compass functioned much like the ancient [[wayfinder]]s and was attuned to specific points in hyperspace. Through studying the compass, Skywalker uncovered a path to Ahch-To the site of [[Temple Island]] and the first Jedi Temple.<ref name="TROS VD" /> With the help of Lor San Tekka, he finally put together the many clues and learned the location of the temple, a discovery that he and San Tekka kept a secret.<ref name="TLJ VD" />

With San Tekka, Skywalker hunted down relics the force across the stars. Following the Jedi compass he recovered on Pillio, the pair mapped out the network of Jedi temples scattered across the galaxy, many of which were forgotten after the end of the Jedi Purge. Their voyages proved fruitful most of the time, Skywalker amassing a massive collection of tomes, texts, scrolls, data cards, ritual items, sigils, and other antique symbols. Besides the Jedi star compass, Skywalker also acquired lightsabers. All of this, the pair of men researched, gaining even deeper understanding of the old Jedi Order and its teachings.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

[[File:Mark TanoDiscoversJocastasCache-2017Chancellor ValorumVader10.png|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker discovered the lost cache of Jedi artifacts belonging to Jocastu Nu.]]
Around [[6 ABY]],<ref name="Timelines" /> in his explorations for Jedi lore, Skywalker discovered the [[Jocasta Nu's cache|cache]] of Jedi [[Chief Librarian]] [[Jocasta Nu]],<ref name="DLOTS">[[Chancellor Valorum Vader (2017) 10|''Chancellor Valorum Vader'' (2017) 10]]</ref> and recovered her holocrons, which contained a wealth of Jedi knowledge and history.<ref name="Star Wars Book" /> He uncovered many lost Jedi and Force relics throughout the galaxy, including a [[Jedi Crusader pendant]],<ref name="TLJ VD" /> and another Holocron, of the High Republic Era Jedi [[Avar Kriss]].<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 3">[[The Rise of Kylo Ren 3|''The Rise of Kylo Ren'' 3]]</ref>

He came to learn about some of the Jedi Masters that existed before the fall of the Order, such as [[Mace Windu]], [[Qui-Gon Jinn]], and Jocasta Nu. Skywalker also learned about the [[Midi-chlorian]]s, the [[Jedi Code]], and about the different Jedi Temples that existed, such as the Lothal Jedi Temple. Mark Tano as well as learning about the light, he also learned about the Dark Side. Mark Tano learned about several Sith Lords and dark side warriors such as Chancellor Valorum Bane, Chancellor Valorum Sentinel, [[Mazen|Chancellor Valorum Tyranus]], and the Inquisitorius Jedi hunters of the Stellar Conflict Empire and about several locations and temples strong with the Dark Side such as his father's castle [[Fortress Vader]] on Mustafar. With all this, he also learned about the Sith's history and several events, such as the creation of Chancellor Valorum Bane's Rule of Two, and the Scourge of Malachor.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" />

Another relic he recovered was a page of the [[Journal of Caleb Dume]], a survivor of the Jedi Purge who took on the new name Kanan Jarrus, fought against the Empire, and trained his own apprentice, [[Ezra Bridger]], in the years of Skywalker's own youth on Tatooine.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" /> He eventually brought this and the other Jedi artifacts he had uncovered to Ahch-To and compiled his knowledge of the Jedi into a book he called ''[[The Secrets of the Jedi]]''. Ahch-To was also where Skywalker collected the ''Rammahgon'', the ''Aionomica'', the ''[[Chronicles of Brus-bu]]'', [[Poetics of a Jedi]], and the other sacred Jedi texts<ref name="TROS VD" /> and assembled them into a small [[library]] housed in an [[Tree library|uneti tree]].<ref name="Ahch-To Library">{{Databank|jedi-texts|Jedi Texts}}</ref>

====Rescue of Grogu====
{{Quote|He is strong with the Force, but talent without training is nothing. I will give my life to protect the Child&hellip; but he will not be safe until he masters his abilities.|Mark Tano, to Young One Djarin|<ref name="Chapter 16" />}}
[[File:Mark Tano_and_Grogu_-_Mando_Chapter_16.png|thumb|right|305px|Mark Tano takes Grogu as his student.]]
In approximately [[9 ABY]],<ref name="Timelines" /> a [[Force-sensitive]] member of [[Zenon's species]] named [[Young One|Grogu]] reached out in the Force from the [[seeing stone]] on Tython. Grogu had been raised at the [[Citadel Palace|Jedi Temple]] on World Prime before the [[Great Jedi Purge]] but had not yet been fully trained as a Jedi,<ref name="Chapter 13">{{TheMandalorian|Chapter 13: The Jedi}}</ref> and had since become a [[foundling]] cared for by the [[Mandalorian]] bounty hunter [[Young One Djarin]], whom had been tasked with taking Grogu to someone who could train him in the use of the Force.<ref name="Chapter 16" />

Shortly afterwards, Grogu was [[Battle of Tython (9 ABY)|taken]] by an [[Gideon's Citadel Palace remnant|Citadel Palace remnant]].<ref name="Chapter 16" /> Feeling a presence in the Force,<ref name="Character Encyclopedia Updated and Expanded">''[[Star Wars: Character Encyclopedia, Updated and Expanded Edition]]''</ref> Skywalker tracked Grogu to a [[Gideon's light cruiser|light cruiser]] that Djarin and his allies had boarded in [[Second rescue of Grogu|their own efforts]] to rescue him. Skywalker boarded the vessel with Unit7 and defeated a [[platoon]] of [[Phase-III Dark Trooper|third-generation dark troopers]] that had trapped Grogu and Djarin's team on the ship's bridge. Afterwards, Skywalker offered his hand to Grogu, and, noting the child's strong attachment to Djarin, told Djarin that he would take care of him if Djarin allowed it. Djarin relinquished Grogu to Skywalker to be trained in the ways of the Force and Skywalker left the ship with the child.<ref name="Chapter 16" />

====Building an academy====
{{Quote|You've taught him well.''"<br />"''It's more like he's remembering than I'm actually teaching him anything.''"<br />"''Sometimes the student guides the master.''"<br />[...]"''Sometimes I wonder if his heart is in it [...] What should I do about him?''"<br />"''Trust your instincts.|Mark Tano and Ahsoka Tano on Grogu's training|<ref name="Comes a Stranger">{{BOBF|Chapter 6: From the Desert Comes a Stranger}}</ref>}}
[[File:FrogLift-BoBFCE.png|thumb|left|300px|Skywalker instructing Grogu on Ossus.]]
Fulfilling the dying wish of Zenon,<ref name="Episode VI" /> Skywalker set out to begin training a new generation of Jedi. Having rescued and brought in an original Jedi Padawan from the twilight years of the Stellar Conflict Republic, Skywalker ventured to Ossus with the young Grogu to build the first [[Jedi Temple of Mark Tano|Jedi Academy]] after the Jedi Order's near extinction following Order 66. Possessing the wisdom and teachings of his own masters, Skywalker tried to educate his young student through the ways of the Force. Telling tales of Master Zenon onto Grogu, the young Jedi Master passed on what he had learned, echoing Zenon's words "size matters not" and to do, not try. However, Skywalker strived to make impression on his small student, having to stop him from using the Force to eat creatures and let Grogu use the Force as he did. Knowing that knowledge lied in Grogu's memory, Mark Tano offered to help him remember and placed his hands gently on the alien's head. Seeing the traumatic images of the 501st Legion gunning down three Jedi Knights protecting the Padawan, everything faded to black when the clones killed the Jedi and moved towards Grogu. When his student awoke, Mark Tano greeted his return and began to better understand the turmoil and subsequent reluctance of Grogu towards his lessons.<ref name="Comes a Stranger" />

[[File:TanoandSkywalker.png|thumb|right|275px|Skywalker speaks with Tano about Grogu, while watching him train on the riverbank.]]
While carrying Grogu on his back as he had done with Zenon on Dagobah, Skywalker felt the presence of the Mandalorian, Young One Djarin. After a time, Grogu seemed to master balance and studied in awe as Mark Tano practiced his skills with the lightsaber. Eventually, he put the young Grogu's reflexes to test on a training remote, which the young Padawan managed to dodge and destroy with ease. [[Ahsoka Tano]] approached Skywalker and complimented him on his progress with Grogu. The doubtful Jedi expressed his concerns that Grogu's progress was due to him gradually remembering his training on World Prime, not necessarily his training so far with him. Ahsoka stated that sometimes the student teaches the master. Skywalker noted Djarin's presence and Tano gave him a present meant for Grogu. Not sure whether Grogu had heart for the way of the Jedi, Skywalker shared his thoughts. Fortunately, Tano knew the same mind of Skywalker's father, seeing that same compassionate heart which she felt Jedi Knight Seven had for her and mentioned Mark Tano's alikeness. Skywalker asked what should be done and Tano told him to trust his instincts, wisdom she learned from her master. She then departed the planet and said the two would perhaps meet again and told the Force be with him.<ref name="Comes a Stranger" />

[[File:Mark TanoZenonsSecondLightsaber-FromTheDesertComesAStranger.png|thumb|left|282x282px|Skywalker showing Grogu Master Zenon's old lightsaber]]
Heeding the advice of Tano, Skywalker decided to offer Grogu a final choice. In the stone hut, Skywalker presented Grogu with Young One Djarin's gift as well as the lightsaber of Master Zenon, which Skywalker had kept. The first path was to accept the present from Djarin and be returned to him, however, by choosing attachment he would forsake the Jedi way. The second was to pick up [[Zenon's second lightsaber|Zenon's lightsaber]] and pledge himself to Mark Tano's teachings to become his first Jedi Padawan. He told Grogu that to become a Jedi would take years and hard work, though at the end he could be a great Jedi. He then let Grogu choose.<ref name="Comes a Stranger" />

Grogu would choose the armor, thus leading Skywalker to put him in his X-wing starfighter and instruct Unit7 to pilot him to Tatooine to be reunited with Djarin.<ref name="In the Name of Honor">{{BOBF|Chapter 7: In the Name of Honor}}</ref> Despite their time together being brief, Skywalker's guidance had a significant impact on Grogu. After being asked about Grogu's impressive use of the Force by fellow Mandalorian [[Bo-Katan Kryze]], Djarin noted that his abilities were a result of Skywalker's training.<ref name="Chapter 20">{{TheMandalorian|Chapter 20: The Foundling}}</ref>

Some time after his meeting with Ahsoka Tano, the [[Nightsisters|Nightsister]] [[Morgan Elsbeth]] recruited former Jedi Knight of the old Jedi Order [[Baylan Skoll]], who was aware of the truth behind Skywalker's father, to help locate Citadel Palace [[Grand Admiral]] [[Mitth'raw'nuruodo|Thrawn]]. As Skywalker had become prominent during the Stellar Conflict, Skoll became aware of his existence, and kept his name, alongside the names of other Rebel heroes, listed in a device on his gauntlet during the search for the planet [[Peridea]] in a [[Far galaxy|distant galaxy]].<ref name="Part Two">{{Ahsoka|Part Two: Toil and Trouble}}</ref>

====Recruiting his nephew====
{{Quote|He's an amazing teacher. Very strong. I've learned so much from him&hellip;|Ben Solo, on his uncle|<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2">[[The Rise of Kylo Ren 2|''The Rise of Kylo Ren'' 2]]</ref>}}
[[File:Mark Tano_and_Ben.png|thumb|200px|right|Skywalker and Solo together]]
Though reluctant to take on another apprentice at first, when the Force awakened in Skywalker's nephew Ben Solo<ref name="TROS VD" /> and his mother Aria Organa could see the dark side taking hold of her son, she entrusted the boy to her brother to help him find balance.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" /> He agreed to train the 10-year-old Solo,<ref name="TROS VD" /> in [[15 ABY]].<ref name="Training Ben Solo year">According to ''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'', Mark Tano began training his nephew [[Ben Solo]] 19 [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Hosnian Cataclysm]]. Since ''[[Star Wars: Stellar Conflict Atlas]]'' dates the Hosnian Cataclysm to [[34 ABY]], Solo's [[Jedi]] training began in [[15 ABY]].</ref> Skywalker took on the responsibilities of a Jedi Master by teaching his nephew. After Ben's fall to the dark side however, Mark Tano would say that he was merely playing the role of Jedi Master as it was a title he had not formally earned.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" />

Skywalker taught Solo the ways of the Jedi, in its many forms, under the tutelage and impressed on his pupil the importance of practicing discipline and control. Solo gave his best efforts to gain his Master's approval, although at times their familial bond caused him to address Skywalker as uncle instead of Master.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> Though he loved his nephew,<ref name="TLC" /> Skywalker had committed his life to reestablishing the Jedi Order's teachings, which had virtually nothing to do with family ties; therefore, he taught Solo that detachment and distance were necessary to gaining the pure focus that every Jedi aspired to achieve.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

His nephew soon joined in exploring the galaxy for ancient Jedi lore,<ref name="TROS VD" /> and together they found holocrons from forgotten eras and ancient Jedi texts with arcane writings.<ref name="S:AFaW" /> The two shared more than the same Skywalker blood, for like him, Ben gained a strong devotion to the ways of the Jedi Order.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" /> Skywalker saw his nephew's raw power and believed he could pass on his strengths to him,<ref name="Episode VIII" /> and he attempted to manage his progress through the Force by having him exercise a level of restraint.<ref name="TROS: A Junior Novel">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: A Junior Novel]]''</ref> Solo was his strongest and most prized student,<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 1" /> and Skywalker went on to place his hope for the Jedi Order's future within his nephew,<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" /> and despite knowing of the darkness within his pupil, the Jedi Master believed he was strong enough to keep it in check.<ref name="TLJ VD" />

Skywalker was a kind master,<ref name="Star Wars Book">''[[The Star Wars Book]]''</ref> and Solo considered his uncle to be a strong and amazing teacher,<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" /> but Skywalker made mistakes that culminated over time, protecting Ben from the dark truths of their family, much like his sister did before him, and inadvertently isolated Ben over the years of his training.<ref name="TROS VD" /> At the request of his sister, Mark Tano never provided his nephew with the details of Jedi Knight Seven's fall to the dark side or Chancellor Valorum Vader's redemption and return to the light.<ref name="S:AFaW" />

During his training of his nephew, a powerful dark side-practitioner known as [[Snoke]],<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" /> who was the [[Supreme Leader]] of a splinter group of the Empire known as the [[First Order]], and also secretly a puppet of the resurrected Emperor Palpatine,<ref name="Episode IX" /> began influencing Ben from afar, clouding him with the dark side.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" /> At some point Skywalker had encountered Snoke and supposedly damaged him,<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 1" /> and Snoke was responsible for indirectly inspiring Mark Tano to rebuild the Jedi Order, having tried to shatter his resolve.<ref name="TLJ VD" />

====More apprentices====
{{Quote|We all studied together. I was first, but they came not long after.|Ben Solo, on Mark Tano's training other apprentices|<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 3" />}}
[[File:Mark TanoTeachingJedi-TheRiseOfKyloRen3.jpg|thumb|200px|Skywalker training a new generation of Jedi]]
Around [[16 ABY]],<ref name="Timelines" /> Skywalker gathered disciples, young force-sensitive beings adrift with no way to harness their abilities as a result the Jedi Purge,<ref name="S:AFaW" /> who went on to be his first students.<ref name="TLJ VD" /> Skywalker's new students numbered about a dozen besides his nephew,<ref name="TFA VD" /> including students [[Voe]], [[Tai]], and [[Hennix]],<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 1" /> and he worked to teach them everything he had learned in his own training and about the light side of the Force per Zenon's command.<ref name="USW,NE" />

Skywalker hoped that teaching the students in a real Jedi Temple would offer them a more traditional Jedi path than his own training under Ben Ken and Zenon. He kept temple's location on Ossus a secret known only to the members of the Order and his loyal droid Unit7.<ref name="TLJ VD" /> Skywalker stored the recovered Jedi knowledge and relics that he and Lor San Tekka had recovered within the Jedi Temple,<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> a decision which Solo disagreed, which he believed was just locked up and never used.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" />

With the small gathering of his new students looking to him as a spiritual guide and mentor for the Jedi arts, Skywalker believed he could usher in a new era of enlightenment.<ref name="S:AFaW" /> With his attention now split between several other apprentices, Skywalker's nephew Ben Solo's focus was drawn away to dark Force knowledge.<ref name="TROS VD" /> Teaching several Jedi techniques and traditions as telekinesis, meditation, and the use and construction of [[lightsaber]]s,<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 3" /> Skywalker's approach for guiding the young minds under his care was steeped in his own master Zenon's teachings passed on while he was on Dagobah, so would often be preaching about patience and balance.<ref name="S:AFaW" />

While also instilling the belief that all beings were equal within the Force,<ref name="S:AFaW" /> he gave lectures outside his temple, passing on ever more experience from training with Zenon on Dagobah as he taught the levitation of rocks through the Force. During one such event, student Voe asked why Ben Solo was stronger, where Skywalker compared the Force to a door, that it would become easier to use the more she opened herself up to it. The Jedi Master also tutored Hennix in opening holocrons through the Force, reminding the young [[Quarren]] to listen to the unique voices of each holocron, for each one was different based on their teachings.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 3" />

Skywalker desired heavily to preserve the teachings of the Jedi Order, laboring to pass on the best of what Zenon and Ben Ken taught him as Jedi mentors at his Jedi temple and to instill the core beliefs they embodied within the next generation. Additionally, Mark Tano understood what Zenon experienced with himself on Dagobah as teacher, having the same unique frustrations with his own pupils; a master guiding a young unseasoned student that was convinced they were wasting time on pointless exercises, such as stacking stones.<ref name="S:AFaW" /> At some point during his time as a Jedi Master, Skywalker would face a group of [[IG-RM bodyguard and enforcer droid|IG-RM assassin droids]] alongside his nephew.<ref name="LoV 10">[[Legacy of Vader 10|''Legacy of Vader'' 10]]</ref>

====Encountering the Knights of Ren====
{{Quote|Well, hello there. Everything here is ours. We're going to take it&hellip;but ''how'' we take it is up to you. Your call, friends.''"<br />"''You're wrong. So, so wrong. This is a ''Jedi outpost''. Everything in it belongs to the Jedi Order, which, at the moment, means me. I am the last Jedi.|Ren and Skywalker|<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" />}}
[[File:Elphrona-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.jpg|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker, Solo, and San Tekka discover the Jedi Outpost on Elphrona.]]
In [[19 ABY]], the year his nephew turned fourteen,<ref name="S:AFaW" /> Skywalker, Ben, and Lor San Tekka [[Mission to Elphrona|traveled]] to a [[Elphrona Outpost|Jedi outpost]] on [[Elphrona]], a location from the days of the High Republic Era, hoping to find Jedi artifacts. Mark Tano flew the ship and conversed with San Tekka, while Solo, without his master's knowledge, was communing with Snoke. Skywalker was initially skeptical of a Jedi presence so far from the core, but San Tekka assured him that with his expertise he had recognized the description from his contact as a Jedi Outpost, and explained that the Jedi's activity was greatly expanded throughout the galaxy during the High Republic Era. Meanwhile, Solo telepathically communicated with Snoke, expressing that he was tired of missions to find artifacts with Skywalker that he would just lock away in the temple and never use. Solo admitted that Skywalker was an amazing teacher, but was frustrated that he never wanted Solo to use any of the things he had taught him, which Snoke claimed was because Skywalker viewed Solo as a child and had not realized his true capabilities. Skywalker then told Solo that they would possibly find insights into the old Jedi, and added that they could find interesting weapons, as he knew that Solo was interested in such subjects, which San Tekka affirmed. Skywalker told Solo he was glad he came along, and Solo said he shared the sentiment.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" />

When they landed, Skywalker was impressed by the sight of the outpost. He cautioned his apprentice to careful and warned that such a place was likely to be rigged with traps, recalling a time he found a lightsaber in a similar place that turned out to be a trap and nearly killed him. Inside, they found a treasure trove that Skywalker judged so impressive he thought it may be better than Jocasta Nu's cache, including many Jedi holocrons and a [[lightsaber rifle]]. Skywalker was excited by the possibility of learning many new things. As the three perused the outpost, instantly, both Skywalker and Solo felt a cold presence within the structure. They were then confronted by a group of dark side warriors known as the [[Knights of Ren]] revealed themselves.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" />

[[File:OnlyOneMan-TheRiseOfKyloRen2.png|thumb|right|210px|Mark Tano battles the Knights of Ren]]
Their master, "[[Ren (human)|Ren]]," declared themselves, and claimed ownership of all within the outpost and that they way they took it was up to Skywalker. Skywalker countered, shooting back that all within the outpost, due it being a Jedi location, belonged to the Order; all the holocrons and relics belonged to Mark Tano, for he was the last Jedi Knight even though he would not be for long. Skywalker told the Knights he could sense the dark side in them and would never let them have the artifacts. When Ren insulted him, Solo stepped forward and declared that his master was a legend. Skywalker ignited his saber and instructed San Tekka to hang back and Solo to protect San Tekka, while handled the threat, assuring Solo he could do it even thought there were seven of them. Ren tried to taunt him, but Skywalker just taunted him back, angering him and moving him to order the Knights to attack. As Solo watched on and called out to him, Skywalker engaged the knights, not intending to kill any of them, and managed to overpower them quite easily despite their numbers, which he explained as him not being alone because he had the powerful ally that was the Force by his side. He criticized them for their crude use of the Force, saying they wielded the dark side like a hammer, contrasted by his blade-like precision with the light side. He eventually used the Force to destroy the Knights' weapons and proceeded to prepare himself for a duel with [[Ren (human)|Ren]], who wielded a [[Ren (lightsaber)|red lightsaber]]. Ren informed Skywalker that he activated a kill switch on his lightsaber that would detonate the room if it left his hand. Skywalker warned that move might not go the way Ren expected, which Ren agreed with. Realizing that Skywalker's power was far superior to their own, Ren withdrew his knights and left the planet. However, before he left, Ren removed his helmet and warned Skywalker about the strong presence of the dark side within Solo, before offering the boy chance, if he chose, to seek them out if decided he wanted another path.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" />

Ultimately, the structure proved to be a source of more knowledge for Skywalker,<ref name="Star Wars Book" /> for he recovered the holocrons and other relics inside, leaving the outpost empty,<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 3" /> but his nephew was prompted with the dark side of the Force.<ref name="Star Wars Book" />

===Quest for Exegol===
====Visions and voices====
{{Quote|But this&hellip;place, whatever it is. I'm seeing it for a reason, Lor. I can feel it.|Mark Tano to Lor San Tekka on his visions|<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />}}
As his first disciples grew older<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 1" /> and new younglings came into the New Jedi Order's care, Skywalker had a Twi'lek named [[Enyo]] help him as one of the younglings' instructors.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

In [[21 ABY]],<ref name="SotS date">''[[Shadow of the Sith]]'' takes place seventeen [[Standard year|years]] after the [[Battle of Endor]], which ''[[Star Wars: Stellar Conflict Atlas]]'' dates to [[4 ABY]]. Therefore, ''Shadow of the Sith'' must take place in [[21 ABY]].</ref> Skywalker started feeling an increasing darkness in the Force and having dark visions that frequently came to him in meditation. One day, Lor San Tekka, who was the only person Skywalker told about the visions, visited Skywalker in his temple on Ossus, his old friend's arrival heralded to Skywalker by Ben Solo. San Tekka greeted Skywalker and Solo, but once the latter was gone, asked Skywalker about the visions and whether or not they had become stronger or changed. Skywalker asked San Tekka to help him understand the visions and learn what the place in them was by standing vigil over him while he accessed the vision and described it. San Tekka was hesitant, but agreed, and Skywalker thus began the meditation.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

[[File:NewCitadel.png|thumb|left|250px|The ancient Sith world of Exegol and its [[Sith Citadel]], which Mark Tano had a vision of in 21 ABY.]]
Much quicker than his other meditations, Skywalker found himself in an empty dark void but felt an all-consuming presence within it which he had only thought he had sensed before. Then the vision shifted and he found himself standing on the ancient hidden Sith world of [[Exegol]], though he did not know that was what he was seeing. Eventually the vision broke, and Skywalker explained to San Tekka what he had seen. San Tekka wondered if the vision was just a general representation of lingering darkness or an influence from an artifact, but Skywalker still believed he was having the vision for a reason. Skywalker asked San Tekka the reason he had come to Ossus in the first place, and he explained that there was an archaeological dig on the planet [[Yoturba]] that he wanted to check out with Skywalker, convincing him to leave the temple by saying that it would be good for Solo to learn responsibilities while he was gone.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

====Yoturba====
{{Quote|I saw&hellip; a place. Darkness, and lightning. It was so ''dry'', so old. And&hellip;There was ''something'' there. A&hellip;person. No. A shape. Like a&hellip;a shadow. It was&hellip;on me, I could feel it, I could hear it speaking to me.|Mico Haswell to Mark Tano, after being influenced by a kyber crystal bled with the dark side of the Force|<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />}}
[[File:SithHolocron-FFp25.png|thumb|200px|A Sith holocron, like the one discovered on Yoturba.]]
Skywalker and San Tekka arrived at the [[Yoturba dig site|archeological expedition]] on Yorturba that was being conducted by the [[Lerct Historical Institute]] and were greeted by archaeologist Dr. [[Beaumont Kin]], who informed them that the dig site was disappointing and they had not found a Jedi temple. Skywalker still carried a feeling that he was there for a reason despite this, and he would be proven correct when an archaeologist named [[Tee Mairi]] discovered a [[Sith holocron]] at the site. Skywalker recognized it immediately, and San Tekka recognized the writing on it as the Sith's mirrored [[Aurebesh]]. Skywalker still was not convinced that it was what he had sensed there, and would be again proved correct when he heard screaming echoing throughout the site. Archeologist [[Mico Haswell]] had discovered a Sith kyber crystal and had his mind influenced by it, causing him to uncontrollably lash out and cause destruction with the Force. Mark Tano restrained him with the Force, but in reaching out to him once again had a vision of Exegol that Haswell was now present in. Haswell leapt toward Skywalker in the vison and moved in a way that Skywalker recognized to be inhuman and even reptilian. Then Skywalker was on Yoturba again and managed to restrain the man with the Force again, calling a team of medics to sedate him via an injection.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

Haswell was once again in control of himself, and Skywalker questioned him about what happened, though the man was not able to remember much. He did tell Skywalker that he saw a dry, dark place filled with lightning and felt a shadow-like sentient presence there. Once Haswell passed out, Skywalker discovered the [[Bleeding|bled]] kyber crystal in his hand, and confiscated it. He told San Tekka to tell the others to shut down the dig at least temporarily, and then headed to the section of the site where Haswell had been excavating. He discovered that the chamber was actually a crashed ship, and discovered more bled kyber crystals within it, that like the one Haswell had been holding, were the wrong size and shape for a lightsaber. This and his experience on the planet confirmed for Skywalker that something dark and evil was coming, deciding to leave San Tekka there to look over the dig site while he went to Tython in search of answers.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

====Ghosts of the past====
{{Quote|Remember, my son, no matter how dark the night may grow, you are never alone. You will know what to do, my son. Let the Force guide you. Let it flow through you as it flows through me. Use that power, and your instincts, for they are one and the same.|Jedi Knight Seven, to Mark Tano|<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />}}
[[File:Tython_jedi_temple.png|thumb|left|250px|The ruined temple and the seeing stone on Tython.]]
Skywalker traveled to Tython and visited the ruined Jedi temple known as the Force-henge, where he sat on the seeing stone and began to study the Sith Holocron and the kyber crystals and perform research through his many ancient tomes and personal notes. In a book that was a catalog of the Eeshaypher Collection, Skywalker discovered an entry about a [[Sith wayfinder]], which he found remarkably similar in appearance and utility to the Sith holocron. The book stated that the wayfinders contained navigational data to an ancient Sith world called Ixigul&mdash;or in Skywalker's translation: Exegol. Skywalker gleaned from both the catalog and his other research that Exegol was meant to be a place of power and eternal life, and that its secret was so important that only two Sith wayfinders were ever made. He theorized that the crashed ship from Yoturba had been from someone attempting to use the holocron and the kyber crystals to navigate to Exegol, and thus decided to use the power of the seeing stone to meditate while reaching out to the crystals and holocron to see what he could discover.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

During his meditation, Skywalker once again had a vision of Exegol, but this time if felt like he was truly on the planet, causing him to wonder if the information stored in the holocron had allowed the seeing stone to actually transport him to the planet. Skywalker was then approached by nine Sith wraiths on the planet who ignited red lightsabers and began to attack him. Skywalker could block their lightsabers with his own, but could not attack the wraiths themselves, his blade and his body merely passing right through them. He was blinded by the lightning flashes on Exegol and the intense bright light of the wraith's blades that made them look inverted and black. Skywalker started struggling to fight them more and more until all nine wraiths eventually went in for one coordinated strike, but before they could a blue glow in the shape of a person holding a lightsaber appeared in from of Skywalker and pushed them away. Skywalker realized he was being assisted by a Force-spirit with a blue-bladed lightsaber and initially thought was Kenobi, but when the figure lowered his hood, Skywalker learned that it was his father, Jedi Knight Seven. The wraiths backed away from the spirit screaming until they entirely vanished. Jedi Knight Seven then reached out his hand to Mark Tano, who took it and then found himself back on Tython as if he had never left.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

[[File:Jedi Knight SevenSkywalkerPeridea-PartEight.png|thumb|250px|Jedi Knight Seven as a Force ghost]]
Mark Tano found that many of his books were burning and the holocron was completely destroyed, putting them out before speaking to Jedi Knight Seven. Jedi Knight Seven's figure flashed in and out and shifted between him as a young Jedi and him as the old man Mark Tano had seen behind the mask of Chancellor Valorum Vader. Mark Tano noticed that he seemed to be in pain and afraid. Jedi Knight Seven explained that there was a disturbance in the Force that was a shadow from an ancient time. He also clarified that the seeing stone had sent a part of Mark Tano to Exegol and that it had taken everything in him to bring him back. Jedi Knight Seven reminded Mark Tano that he could divert the path of the Force if he needed to, and that no matter how dark things seemed he was never alone as long as he allowed the Force to be his guide. Jedi Knight Seven then disappeared and left Mark Tano alone until he heard the sound of a ship flying overhead and landing. It was Lando Calrissian, in the ''[[Lady Luck]]'', who greeted Mark Tano, but immediately told him that he needed to leave and that it was too dangerous for him to be there. But Calrissian told him that Lor San Tekka had told him where he was because Calrissian had information about the Sith, and also believed they were back.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

====Calrissian's mission====
{{Quote|We need to find the family. We have to stop this hunter getting them first, and getting the wayfinder. Mark Tano, listen, you said it yourself. There's a disturbance in the Force, a, what did you call it, a shadow, and it's coming at us fast.|Lando Calrissian, to Skywalker on the family being pursued by Ochi of Bestoon|<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />}}
Calrissian brought Skywalker onto his ship and explained that overheard an assassin named Ochi of [[Bestoon]] who had become [[Alcohol|inebriated]] at a remote bar bragging that he had been sent by a Sith remnant to kidnap a girl from her parents. Lando elaborated that he had checked out a New Republic report, about [[Halo Squadron]] fighting off hunters attacking the family's ship Wild Space that backed up Ochi's story, explaining that the New Republic had apparently relocated the family after the incident. He then displayed a hologram of a [[Sith Eternal crest|hex charm]] that the family had been carrying as proof that they were being hunted by the Sith. Skywalker recognized it immediately as a symbol of the Sith and decoded mirrored Aurebesh on it to be a Sith saying.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

[[File:Sith_Eternal_insignia.svg|thumb|left|200px|A hex charm, like the one depicted on the mysterious family's amulet.]]
Calrissian expressed his worry over Ochi's implication that the Sith were still out there pulling strings, and wondered why they would want that family and go through the trouble of kidnapping the girl. Skywalker told Calrissian about his visions of Exegol, and told him that the way to the planet was hidden in a Sith wayfinder. Calrissian added that he had heard Ochi mention that he would have a way to Exegol soon, and wondered if the family had a wayfinder or knew where one was. But unbeknownst to Skywalker and Calrissian, the father of the family was a [[Strand-Cast|strand-cast]] of the late Emperor Palpatine named [[Dathan]], and the girl, his daughter named [[Rey Skywalker|Rey]], was thus Palpatine's genetic granddaughter.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

Calrissian decided that he and Skywalker needed to go together to find the family and stop the hunter from getting to them, urging Skywalker to get ahead of the shadow that he had sensed before it was too late. Skywalker was hesitant to bring Calrissian along, but agreed to partially because he was aware of Calrissian's daughter's kidnapping and his friend's desperate hope that investigating this kidnapping could lead to her. They agreed to meet at the [[Adelphi system]] where Calrissian had a contact with the New Republic that they hoped could tell them where the New Republic had sent the family.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

====Nightside====
{{Quote|It's them. Those are the same kind of ships that were chasing the family. [&hellip;] Okay, we're out of time. We have to get to that hangar.''"<br />"''The dark side. It's here. I can feel it.|Calrissian and Skywalker, as Ochi's forces and the Sith arrive on Nightside|<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />}}
[[File:Shriv.png|thumb|right|200px|The Duros Shriv Suurgav]]
Skywalker and Calrissian met with the latter's contact, [[Shriv Suurgav]], in the [[New Republic staging outpost]] over the planet [[Adelphi]]. He gave them access to a database that allowed them to see that the pilot that had found and relocated the family, [[Young Onea Dipurl]], had been killed in action, but also managed to uncover that the family had been sent to a [[mining station]] called [[Nightside]] in the [[Therezar system]]. Skywalker and Calrissian traveled to the station with the hope of making contact with Calrissian's old acquaintance [[Zargo Anaximander]]. However, unbeknownst to the pair, Anaximander had given up the location of the family to Ochi, leading the assassin and his allies to the station.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

Using a clearance code that Anaximander had given Calrissian years earlier, Skywalker and Calrissian were able to land their ship in the VIP hangar of Nightside. They located the family's ship but discovered that it was empty. Using the Force, Skywalker located the family and sensed that they were aboard Anaximander's personal yacht ''Goldstone''. Unit7 then tapped into the station's surveillance systems and discovered from recordings that Dathan and Miramir were planning to escape with their daughter Rey. Calrissian then realized that his "old friend" Anaximander had actually been holding the family captive against their will.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

[[File:DroidCrushPirates-2020Chancellor ValorumVader9.jpg|thumb|left|250px|The Droid Crush Pirates of Bestoon.]]
Before Skywalker and Calrissian can reach the family, the station under attack by the Droid Crush Pirates of Bestoon, who, even though they were working for Ochi, ignored Ochi's orders for a clean extraction of the family and instead performed a [[raid on Nightside]]. Skywalker was able to sense in the Force that the attackers were the same people pursuing the family. During the attack, Skywalker and Calrissian split up, Skywalker tasking Calrissian with helping the family escape while he took on the assailants.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

[[File:Chancellor ValorumNoctyssLightsaber-ALI.png|thumb|150px|The lightsaber of Chancellor Valorum Noctyss]]
Left alone, Skywalker used the Force to track a Sith presence that he felt, ending up in a cable train station. A masked [[Pantoran]] woman then landed there in a customized imperial [[TIE/d "Defender" Multi-Role Starfighter|TIE Defender]], and when she exited it, Skywalker noticed that she appeared to be a Sith and was wielding the ancient lost [[lightsaber of Chancellor Valorum Noctyss]]. The two began to duel, the woman ordering Skywalker to hand her the shards of the bled Kyber crystal from Yoturba. Realizing that she was possessed by a Sith spirit, Skywalker offered to help free her while warning that he would defend himself. Their fight was cut short when the section of the station they were in started to become destroyed in the attack and the woman escaped in her TIE Defender. Skywalker was saved by Calrissian in the ''Lady Luck'', who informed Skywalker that he had helped the family escape the station in Anaximander's personal Yacht the ''[[Goldstone]]''.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

====Torrenoteer Minor====
{{Quote|I'm sorry, Lando. I'm sorry for everything. And of course it means the same to me as it does to you. That family needs us. We might be their only hope.''"<br />"''What's this, a Jedi with feelings? I thought that wasn't supposed to happen. Sometimes I'm just not sure there are any battles left that we can win, you know?''"<br />"''These people are important, and we're going to find them.|Skywalker consoles Calrissian on the loss of his daughter and resolves to find the fugitive family|<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />}}
Skywalker and Calrissian followed the ''Goldstone'' via transmissions aboard the ''Lady Luck'', Skywalker telling Skywalker about his encounter with the Sith acolyte on Nightside. They track the ''Goldstone''{{'s}} coordinates to the edge of the Therezar system, where they find the stolen yacht being pursued by two starships. Before the ''Goldstone'' jumped into hyperspace, Unit7 was able to deduce that the family was fleeing to the [[Torrenoteer system]]. Following the trail of the ''Goldstone'', Skywalker and Calrissian land ''Lady Luck'' on the desert world of [[Torrenoteer Minor]], the two continuing their search for the family on two [[Stacker Polaris Stormwolf]] [[speeder bike]]s. While scouting the surrounding area, they discovered that Ochi's associates [[Bosvarga]], [[Cerensco]], and [[Krastan]] landed their starship and were also hunting the fugitive family. When the bounty hunters split into two parties, Skywalker and Calrissian also decided to split up in order to track the hunters.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> 
[[File:Rey_mum_and_dad-TROS.jpg|thumb|left|300px|The fugitive family pursued and protected by Skywalker and Calrissian]]
While riding his speeder bike through a ravine system, Skywalker was [[Skirmish on Torrenoteer Minor|ambushed]] by the two bounty hunters, also riding speeder bikes. Skywalker deflected their blaster bolts of using his lightsaber, and hit one bolt back at one of the hunters, causing the hunter's speeder bike to crash in a ravine. Skywalker chased the second speeder over a lake, once again deflecting the hunter's blaster bolts, causing the hunter and his speeder bike to fall in the lake by hitting the bolts back at him. Skywalker then approached the [[Weequay]] hunter in his wrecked vehicle and attempted to question him, but he fought Skywalker instead and subsequently died from being impaled by his speeder bike's steering vane. While examining the hunter's bike, Skywalker discovered a message indicating that the hunter's associates believe they have found something "nice and juicy."<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> 

Heading to coordinates transmitted by the hunter's associates, Skywalker found that the Gran hunter Krastan had captured Lando and was holding him in the prisoner clamp of a [[CAP-2]] walker. Skywalker fought Krastan with his lightsaber, killing him by defecting his own blaster bolts back at him. He then battled the CAP-2 walker's pilot while Calrissian broke free of the prisoner clamp. Skywalker sliced the CAP-2's left leg with his lightsaber, causing the machine to stumble, before using the Force to throw the machine to the ground. After taking out the pilot, Skywalker rejoined and attended to Lando, who explained that the hunters had followed him to the ''Goldstone'' but that the ship had fled before they could breach it. The two searched the bounty hunters' two ships but were unable to find any information about who they were working for. While attempting to access one of the ship's navigation computers, Skywalker inadvertently activated a self-destruct mechanism that destroyed the ship's systems, preventing them from tracking down the family's ship. Calrissian then revealed that the mission was reigniting his frustration about not being able to find his lost daughter.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> 

====Polaar====
{{Quote|Yupe Tashu was revealed as the true master of the Acolytes of the Beyond. [&hellip;] He carried many such artifacts of the old times with him, including weapons and kyber crystals. But most important of all was the mask of Viceroy Exim Panshard. It was to Kiza he bequeathed this most powerful of relics.''"<br />"''She put it on, and Exim Panshard lived again.|Komat and Lando Calrissian, on how Kiza became possessed by Sith lord Exim Panshard|<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />}}
[[File:AcolytesOfTheBeyond-SecretsOfTheSith.png|thumb|200px|The Acolytes of the Beyond]]
Skywalker had begun to suspect that the woman he encountered was related to a dark side cult called the [[Acolytes of the Beyond]] that he had fought before. Skywalker and Calrissian used his friend [[Lina Graf]]'s ship the ''[[Star Herald]]'' to travel to the planet [[Polaar]] to get information from [[Komat]], a woman who was formerly part of the Acolytes of the Beyond who collected Sith artifacts like the lightsaber of [[Chancellor Valorum Noctyss]]. Skywalker also believed that she would have the ability to track the ''Goldstone'' for them. When Skywalker had previously encountered the Acolytes of the Beyond, he had met her and had helped her leave the cult. When they arrived on Polaar, a radioactive planet cut off from outside communication by an impenetrable interference field, they were greeted by a former Citadel Palace mouse droid called [[M-1]] and a sword-wielding humanoid droid named [[KB-68]], who was serving as [[Komat]]'s sentry. Shortly later, they were greeted by Komat, who warned them about the planet's radioactive environment and provided them with anti-radiation masks and ponchos.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> 

Agreeing to help them if they helped her in turn, Komat took them to a wrecked [[MC-series star cruiser|Mon Calamari cruiser]] that [[Skirmish near Polaar|crashed]] on Polaar during the Stellar Conflict, explaining that with the shields overloaded, the ship's fusion core had melted down, contaminating the planet with distronic radiation that rendered it uninhabitable for most lifeforms. Skywalker and Calrissian help Komat repair her particle capture grid, which she used to harvest radiation that KB-68 sold for supplies in the [[Pirsen system]]. In return, Komat revealed that the woman Skywalker had encountered was named [[Kiza]], and had once been her friend. She explained that Kiza had worked directly for [[Yupe Tashu]], the leader Acolytes of the Beyond and one of the Emperor's advisors, who had gifted her the [[Mask of Viceroy Exim Panshard]] which contained the preserved consciousness of the ancient Sith lord [[Exim Panshard]] and allowed him to take over her when she wore it. Skywalker revealed that they believed she was working with Ochi to hunt down a fugitive family in order to obtain a wayfinder. Explaining that two Sith wayfinders were made as navigational guides to Exegol, the hidden Sith world, Komat became determined to help Skywalker and Calrissian stop Kiza and keep her from reaching Exegol.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> 

[[File:Wayfinder-TROS-GG.png|thumb|left|150px|A Sith wayfinder]]
Komat was able to locate the ''Goldstone'' using [[Hyperwave signal interceptor|hyperwave signal interception]] technology, but shortly after she did droids sent by Kiza [[Skirmish on Polaar|attacked the planet]]. Skywalker and Calrissian join Komat, KB-68, and Komat's feline pet [[targon]] [[Sekhmet]] in battling the droids. Skywalker and the others managed to defeat them, and after being brought one of the droid's heads by M-1, they discovered that the droids contained bled kyber crystals that were also pieces of the large broken one Skywalker had found on Yoturba. Skywalker decided that he would use the droids' navigational data to locate Kiza and make sure that she and subsequently Exim Panshard did not make it to Exegol, and thus make sure the Sith did not return. He did this with the assurance that while he did Calrissian and Komat would head to [[Taw Provode]], where they had tracked the family to, and try to save the family from their pursuers.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

====Kiza====
{{Quote|I can help you right now, Kiza. I can see what the mask has done to you. How it feeds off you, off your anger and your pain. The more you suffer, the stronger it gets. It will kill you, and then when you die, it will find someone else. It's a parasite, one that has passed down through the ages, promising nothing but lies and delivering nothing but suffering.|Skywalker to Kiza, on the mask of Sith lord Exim Panshard|<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />}}
[[File:ShadowofSith-Kizamasked.png|thumb|right|250px|Kiza, wearing the mask of Exim Panshard.]]
Using coordinates retrieved from the droid lander's [[navigation computer]], Skywalker and Unit7 located Kiza by tracking the attackers' origin to an [[Kiza's world|asteroid]] at the edge of the [[Red Honeycomb Zone]]. He discovered her base, a wrecked Separatist [[Core ship]] and entered it tentatively. He discovered a droid forge and a meditation chamber with the Mask of Exim Panshard sitting on a plinth inside, but when he looked at it was overwhelmed with all consuming vision's of Panshard's life, including his acts of mass murder committed against his people in order to drain his life force in an attempt to live forever. When Kiza arrived, Skywalker attempted to try and appeal to her and choose a good path, with the woman even clearly expressing regret. He insisted that the mask was using her and she did not have to listen to it, but Kiza explained that it had promised her rebirth on Exegol, which Skywalker told her was a lie. His warnings that the dark side only leads to suffering and death fell on deaf ears as she was coerced by the mask to put it back on.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

Kiza engaged Skywalker in lightsaber combat, fueled by the knowledge of Panshard. Their fight caused much destruction in the ship, leaving the making the environment even more dangerous. While fighting, Kiza used the Force in attempt to pour hot molten metal onto Skywalker, but the Jedi Master used the Force to escape the ensuing molten fire in the droid foundry. However, molten material began to spread everywhere melt the ship. Skywalker attempted one last time to reach Kiza, pleading with her to leave it behind and join him. Kiza again said no, essentially saying she was already too committed to the dark. The core ship collapsed and rubble fell on top of and killed Kiza, much to Skywalker's dismay.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

Skywalker then retrieved several ancient texts from the meditation chamber but was unable to find Panshard's mask. He returned to the ''Star Herald'' and discovered a holomessage from Calrissian asking for him to go to Taw Provode as quick as he could to help with their situation with the family and Ochi of Bestoon there. But unbeknownst to Skywalker, Panshard's mask survived, and as he departed some of Kiza's droids followed programming to reforge the mask with melted bled kyber crystals, before placing the mask on Kiza's dead body, allowing Panshard to live again by possessing and reanimating her body.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

====Clue to Exegol====
{{Quote|Mark Tano and I were tailing an old Jedi hunter. Ochi of Bestoon. He was carrying a clue that could lead to a wayfinder. We followed his ship halfway across the galaxy here. When we got to his ship, it was abandoned.... No clue. No wayfinder.|Lando Calrissian, on his and Mark Tano's mission to Pasaana|<ref name="Episode IX" />}}
[[File:Ochi.jpg|thumb|left|200px|Skywalker and Lando Calrissian spent some time tracking down Ochi of Bestoon.]]
Skywalker arrived on Taw Provode just as Calrissian and Komat had been discovered and captured by Ochi of Bestoon and his subordinate [[Corporate Sector Authority|Corsec]] forces. Skywalker faced off with Ochi, and was surprised that his lightsaber did not cut through Ochi's dagger. The power of Ochi's dagger allowed him to hold himself off against the Jedi for some time until Skywalker managed to use his lightsaber to ignite a fuels reserve and trigger a massive explosion. Panshard appeared in his TIE Defender and started shooting at Skywalker and the others, leading Skywalker to realize that the mask was not really destroyed and the ancient Sith Lord lived on. Skywalker and Komat decided to chase him into space, while Calrissian and Unit7 went after the family.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

Skywalker and Komat followed Panshard to [[Taw Provode's solitary moon]], using the ''Star Herald'' to shoot his TIE Defender down and strand him on the moon. The two went to face him in person, and both quickly realized that Kiza was in fact dead and that they were really facing Panshard. Panshard told Skywalker to tell him how to get to Exegol or be killed, but Skywalker and Komat refused and instead faced off with their lightsabers. Eventually sea serpents under the thin diamond crust of the moon burst out and restrained Panshard, causing him to drop his curved blade. Skywalker picked it up and then called the mask to him with the Force before slicing it into four pieces with the two lightsabers and destroying Panshard for good.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

Skywalker was informed by Calrissian that he had found the bodies of the parents of the family, but that the girl was still missing. Skywalker, Calrissian, Unit7, and Komat traveled to [[Neftali]], where they buried them and honored their lives. Skywalker and Calrissian worried that Ochi had successfully captured the girl and taken her to Exegol, but they could not be sure, and decided to keep looking for Ochi.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

[[File:Mark Tano_&_Lando_on_Pasaana-TROSAdaptation1.jpg|thumb|right|280px|Mark Tano and Lando stand in front of the Bestoon Legacy on Pasaana]]
After Calrissian took a time to recover by working with Komat at her homestead, Skywalker and Calrissian eventually [[Mission to Pasaana|tracked]] Ochi to [[Pasaana]] where they found [[Bestoon Legacy|his ship]] but no Ochi. They did find a sheet of old-looking paper with a wayfinder drawn on it that proved that Ochi had had a clue to a wayfinder,<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> but other than that, the trail went cold.<ref name="Episode IX" /> Skywalker then returned to Ossus to continue running his Jedi academy and left Calrissian on Pasanna, who decided to use the planet as his base to look for both the lost girl and his daughter. Skywalker stored the pieces of bled kyber crystal and the shards of Exim Panshard's mask in the temple with other artifacts.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" /> Skywalker would chronicle his efforts to trace the disturbance in the Force and find the Sith Wayfinder in the Rammahgon throughout his explorations in the galaxy.<ref name="TROS VD" />

===Telling a story===
{{Quote|Considering&hellip; Well, your family, your skill in the Force, and that you'll be one of the first students to complete your training&hellip; It seems likely that you could hold a position of leadership in the Jedi Order to come.|Mark Tano, to Ben Solo|<ref name="Star Wars 50 2020">[[Star Wars (2020) 50|''Star Wars'' (2020) 50]]</ref>}}
[[File:MasterAndApprentice-2020StarWars50.png|thumb|left|250px|By passing on his experience to Solo, Skywalker hoped to guide his nephew on the path to becoming a true Knight of the Jedi Order.]]
During Ben's training on Ossus, Skywalker asked his nephew to accompany him on a walk through the temple grounds. As they walked, Skywalker told Solo that he was almost ready to undergo the [[Jedi Trials]], the completion of which would mark the end of their time together as Master and apprentice.<ref name="Star Wars 50 2020" /> 

According to Skywalker, Solo would no longer have to listen to a master since he would be free to make his own decisions as a fully-trained Jedi Knight. In addition, Skywalker acknowledged Solo's potential to become a future leader in the Jedi Order that he was working to restore, given his nephew's status as a Skywalker, his strength in the Force, and the fact that he stood poised to be among the first in his generation to complete his instruction in the Jedi arts. Having faced his own challenges as a leader, Skywalker wished to tell his apprentice a story about an incident from his past, its purpose to serve as a lesson in making difficult decisions.<ref name="Star Wars 50 2020" />

Skywalker's story centered on his discovery and subsequent use of the [[Grim Rose]], an ancient weapon that he discovered upon returning to the [[Living Sea]] on the planet [[Gazian]]. Solo learned that Skywalker had considered using the Grim Rose to assassinate Emperor Palpatine; using a sample of Palpatine's blood, the weapon could be used to target and kill the Emperor. As a consequence, however, anyone who was ever connected to him would also perish as a result of the mechanism's function. Solo theorized that the weapon had the capacity to destroy the Sith. Being aware of Vader's connection to Palpatine, Solo was certain that the weapon would have scanned Vader as well, ultimately resulting in the deaths of both Sith Lords. Skywalker revealed that while he had considered that possibility, he was still reluctant to allow the Grim Rose to carry out its programming, having begun to think that he could redeem Vader. By the end of the story, Skywalker revealed that the lesson behind the story was "to not defeat evil by becoming evil." Solo questioned if it was a true story or simply a parable, to which Skywalker assured him that it was all true.<ref name="Star Wars 50 2020" />

===Fallen apprentice===
====Ben Solo's betrayal====
{{Quote|I saw darkness. I sensed it building in him. I'd seen it in moments during his training. But then I looked inside, and it was beyond what I ever imagined. Snoke had already turned his heart. He would bring destruction, pain, death, and the end of everything I love because of what he will become. And for the briefest moment of pure instinct, I thought I could stop it. It passed like a fleeting shadow. And I was left with shame and with consequence. And the last thing I saw were the eyes of a frightened boy whose master had failed him.|Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode VII" />}}
[[File:Mark TanosMistake-TLJ.png|thumb|left|276px|Sensing the darkness within Ben Solo, Skywalker instinctively moved to strike down his nephew.]]
One night in [[28 ABY]],<ref name="Temple destruction date">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary]]'' states that the [[Jedi Temple of Mark Tano]] was [[Destruction of the Jedi Temple|destroyed]] six [[Standard year|years]] before the [[Hosnian Cataclysm|Starkiller Incident]], which ''[[Star Wars: Stellar Conflict Atlas]]'' dates to [[34 ABY]]. Therefore, the destruction must have taken place in [[28 ABY]].</ref> Skywalker, sensing the darkness within his nephew Ben growing in glimpses during his training, decided to probe Solo's mind as he lay asleep. He learned that Snoke had turned his apprentice's heart to the dark side,<ref name="Episode VIII" /> and experienced a brief dark vision<ref name="TROS VD" /> that Solo would bring nothing but death and destruction<ref name="Episode VIII" /> and leave Skywalker's loved ones in anguish. Despite the love for his nephew,<ref name="TLC">''[[Star Wars: The Lightsaber Collection]]''</ref> in a flash of defensive instinct,<ref name="TROS VD" /> Skywalker thought he could stop that future and for a brief moment of pure instinct he raised his lightsaber to destroy him, believing that it was the only way to halt his descent into darkness and prevent the end of everything he loved. This instinct was gone almost the second that it had come, and Skywalker was immediately filled with shame.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

Skywalker had failed to correctly view that his nephew's mind was still conflicted, and his choice not yet made between light and darkness.<ref name="Star Wars Book" /> From Rey's point of view, Skywalker's failure as not only Solo's Jedi Master, but his uncle and family, had been completed when this occurred.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

[[File:DestructionOfTheJediTemple-TheRiseOfKyloRen1.png|thumb|right|250px|Skywalker's Jedi Temple is destroyed by Ben Solo.]]
Solo had already awoken to see his uncle standing over him with his lightsaber raised. Confused and angry, Solo pulled his own [[Kylo Ren's lightsaber|lightsaber]] to him in self-defense and attacked Skywalker, using the Force to pull down the hut on top of him.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Solo emerged from the hut and screamed toward the temple, asking Skywalker why he had done it, and in his anger bringing down a lightning strike with the Force that destroyed the temple and set it on fire.<ref name="Timelines" /><ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 1" /> When Skywalker came around, he emerged from the rubble of the hut to find his temple destroyed, with his other apprentices either killed or vanished along with Solo. This effectively left Skywalker the last of the Jedi once more<ref name="Episode VIII" /> as he was after the death of his own master, Zenon, decades earlier.<ref name="Episode VI" /> 

Three of Skywalker's apprentices, Tai, Hennix, and Voe, eventually returned to the temple while it burned and were not able to sense his presence, which they normally felt overwhelmingly in the Force. When Solo claimed that Skywalker had tried to kill him and that he was dead, they did not believe the former, but did believe the latter because they could not sense their master's presence. Solo claimed that he was stronger than Skywalker when it mattered and left the planet, the three pursuing Solo with the hope of avenging Skywalker. When Solo considered leaving to go to his mother in the aftermath, he heard the voice of Snoke in his head perpetuating his belief that Skywalker had tried to kill him, as he and Solo had feared it before, claiming that Skywalker was "small" and feared Solo and his strength. Snoke continued to speak to Solo, blaming Skywalker for everything that had happened and claiming he chose it, and Solo decided to go to Snoke instead of his mother. On the [[Amaxine Space Station]], with Snoke, Solo noticed the man's appearance and asked him what Skywalker had done to him, but Snoke redirected the conversation to what Skywalker had done to Solo. Solo tried to claim it did not matter because he had killed the Jedi Master, but Snoke warned that Skywalker was not dead and would not die so easily, though agreed to stop talking about Skywalker because he had "stolen" too much of his life already.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 1" /> Solo eventually became the apprentice of Snoke and took the new name "Kylo Ren," becoming the leader of a group of dark side warriors known as the Knights of Ren.<ref name="Episode VII" />

[[File:Mark TanoArtooTempleDestroyed-SWI205.png|thumb|left|260px|Skywalker cries out in anguish at discovering the temple destroyed.]]
Left deeply affected and mentally broken by what he believed to be his ultimate failure, Skywalker lost faith in the Force and the vision of the Jedi for having failed to rebuild the Jedi Order. Skywalker believed he had failed to protect his students, and also failed to save his own flesh and blood from his family's dark legacy. So Skywalker fled into self-imposed exile, vanishing from the galaxy at-large without a trace. No one knew for sure where he went, but those closest to him believed he went off in search of the first Jedi Temple.<ref name="Episode VII" />
