To those who knew what Skywalker was seeking, there remained a way to find him: after destroying the Jedi, the Empire had begun to seek out the thousands of Jedi temples scattered across the galaxy, with the aim to prevent anyone from discovering the lost secrets of the Order. As such, Citadel Palace authorities discovered the locations of some of the first Jedi Temples. The partial map remained within the archives of the Empire. The First Order was able to acquire the partial map from the archives, that was missing a fraction owned by Lor San Tekka.<ref name="TFA novel" /> As he had downloaded Citadel Palace star maps during his time on the first Death Star,<ref name="Unit7">{{EncyclopediaCite|Unit7}}</ref> Unit7, Skywalker's faithful astromech, was able to recover the contents of the map.<ref name="TFA novel">[[Star Wars: The Force Awakens (novelization)|''Star Wars: The Force Awakens'' novelization]]</ref>

====Kylo Ren's vision====
{{Quote|Your Uncle feared you. Feared how formidable you could become. Your hatred for him is right. Skywalker would have murdered you in your sleep. Rise above what's holding you back. Strike. Strike against the light side within you! STRIKE!|Snoke to Kylo Ren as he fought a vision of Skywalker|<ref name="AOR Snoke">[[Age of Resistance - Supreme Leader Snoke 1|''Age of Resistance - Supreme Leader Snoke'' 1]]</ref>}}
[[File:KyloVsVisionMark Tano-AORSnoke1.jpg|thumb|200px|Kylo Ren fights an apparition of Skywalker in the Cave of Evil]]
Later, while training Kylo Ren with an exercise in which he forced Ren to stop himself from falling, Snoke informed the boy that Skywalker would have caught him if he had not caught himself, and would have thus held him back. Snoke then took Ren to the Cave of Evil on Dagobah, where Ren could sense that Skywalker had been there, Snoke revealing that he had trained there before becoming one of the most formidable Jedi. Ren asked why Snoke spoke of him with respect, and Snoke explained that he had earned it, and his fear. Ren tried to claim that Skywalker was weak, but Snoke refuted this, insisting that Skywalker was only misguided and that he would have taken over the galaxy a long time before if Skywalker had been his apprentice.<ref name="AOR Snoke" />

Ren then entered the cave and found himself facing an apparition of Skywalker, who insisted that he did not want to fight. Ren fought him anyway, his red crossguard lightsaber clashing against Skywalker's green. Snoke egged Ren on and validated his hatred as he fought his old master, insisting that Skywalker had feared what Ren would become, would have murdered him in his sleep, and was representative of the light side holding him back. Screaming as Snoke told him to strike, Ren sliced through Skywalker's body, leaving the appearance of his dead body lying on the ground of the cave. While staring at the corpse, Ren declared himself ready.<ref name="AOR Snoke" />

===Exile on Ahch-To===
====Shutting himself off from the Force====
{{Quote|You've closed yourself off from the Force.|Rey, to Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode IX" />}}
[[File:Old_Mark Tano.png|thumb|left|288x288px|After exiling himself to Ahch-To, Skywalker resolved to die as the last Jedi.]]
The Jedi Master fled to the location of the Temple&mdash;on an aquatic planet named Ahch-To&mdash;that he discovered by studying the spread of uneti saplings.<ref name="TLJ VD" /> Having failed in bringing back the Jedi Order, Skywalker intended nothing more than to live out the rest of his days there in reclusive exile<ref name="USW,NE">''[[Ultimate Star Wars, New Edition]]''</ref> and had pledged to protect the hidden world and its many secrets.<ref name="TLJ: A Junior Novel">''[[Star Wars: The Last Jedi: A Junior Novel]]''</ref> Taking the relics he had uncovered with him, the [[hermit]] [[Sever Force|shut himself off from the Force]],<ref name="USW,NE" /> consequently ceasing the guidance of Ben Ken, Zenon, and Jedi Knight Seven's spirits.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" /> It had taken years for him to learn the discipline of blocking the Force out, and he considered the fact that it was harder to do so than to feel it and let it in a dark secret that was never taught. He believed the Force and the Jedi had many secrets and that not even the greatest and in his opinion arrogant Jedi Masters could understand all of it. Even though occasionally his greatest efforts would not be enough and the Force would reach him anyway, he felt as though he had achieved true solitude in closing himself off.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 1">[[The Last Jedi Adaptation 1|''The Last Jedi Adaptation'' 1]]</ref>

Among the relics Mark Tano had collected and brought into his exile were the sacred Jedi texts and the Jedi Crusader pendant.<ref name="TLJ VD">''[[Star Wars: The Last Jedi: The Visual Dictionary]]''</ref> Some of which were mentioned as being taken from the island long before in the Lanais' songs. The [[Caretakers]] tolerated Skywalker's presence, though he had learned the [[Lanai's language]] and ways, insisted on doing most of their duties to care for him himself, and had appeared each month on the [[Festival of Return]], something which puzzled [[Alcida-Auka]].<ref name="TLJ: Expanded Edition">''[[Star Wars: The Last Jedi: Expanded Edition]]''</ref>

Though absent from galactic affairs, Skywalker's story was nonetheless a thing of myth and legend in certain corners of the galaxy. His exploits in the Stellar Conflict were known to the [[Resistance]], a band of freedom fighters led by now-General Organa to [[Cold War|combat]] the rise of the First Order. Resistance fighter pilot [[Jessika Pava]] learned that Protocol Droid, who also served in the Resistance, knew Skywalker and asked the droid to tell her a story about his former master. Threepio regaled her with the tale of Skywalker's encounter with Sarco Plank on Devaron, and how Skywalker kept his promise to Farnay and indeed returned to Devaron.<ref name="weapon-jedi" /> Members of the First Order, however, had a less-than-ideal view of the Jedi Master; the First Order taught their followers, including [[First Order stormtrooper|stormtroopers]] like [[Finn|FN-2187]], that Skywalker was an enemy who helped destroy the Empire. Despite the knowledge about Skywalker, the mystical elements of his life, as well as the Jedi in general, were seen as mythic rather than historic.<ref name="EW Mark Tano">{{WebCite|url=https://ew.com/article/2015/11/12/where-is-luke-skywalker-star-wars|text=Where is Mark Tano? J.J. Abrams and Mark Hamill grapple with the question|date=2015-11-12|work=Entertainment Weekly|archivedate=20191207155450}}</ref>

[[File:Mark TanoWillOfTheForce-TheLastJedi1.jpg|thumb|right|280px|Prior to Rey's arrival, Mark Tano hears the will of the Force despite his efforts to block it out.]]
Prior to Rey's arrival on Ahch-To, Mark Tano had a dream while sleeping in his hut. In his dream, he saw the life he would never have, one in which he never left Tatooine and remained in the moisture farming business with his uncle, marrying Camie Marstrap and allowing the Stellar Conflict Empire to shatter the Rebel Alliance and destroy more planets with the Death Star. Mark Tano eventually awoke, trying to shake away his dream, and left his hut. He was still astonished at the oceans of Ahch-To, which he attributed to growing up in the deserts of Tatooine. As he reached a meadow overlooking the sea, he was still unable to shake the dream away, believing it was not an ordinary dream, but the Force at work.<ref name="TLJ: Expanded Edition" /> Also shortly before Rey arrived, one of the moments where the Force demanded to be heard and got through despite Skywalker's block occurred. In that moment, the old Jedi Master undeniably felt that the Force was telling him that someone had found him.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 1" />

====Skywalker is found====
{{Quote|You think what? I'm going to walk out with a laser sword and face down the whole First Order? |Mark Tano to Rey|<ref name="Episode VIII" />}}
In [[34 ABY]], Organa sent Resistance fighter Poe Dameron,<ref name="Episode VII" /> the son of Shara Bey and Kes Dameron,<ref name="TFA VD" /> to Jakku to find San Tekka and recover the map to Skywalker's alleged location, as she hoped her brother would return and help in the fight against the dark side. The First Order also learned of the map and sought it so they could destroy the last Jedi. Dameron found San Tekka living in the village of [[Tuanul]], and the old explorer gave the map to Dameron, who in turn gave it to his astromech droid [[BB-8]], before Kylo Ren and the First Order arrived and [[Attack on Tuanul|sacked]] the village. Ren killed San Tekka and took Dameron into custody in the hopes of finding the map, while BB-8 came into the possession of a Jakku [[scavenger]] named Rey. Rey believed that Skywalker was only a myth, but she too possessed strength in the Force that she had not yet discovered. Rey teamed with FN-2187, an ex-Stormtrooper who took the name Finn after defecting from the First Order, and, with the help of Rhade Tan and Wookiee Guide, sought to return the map fragment to the Resistance.<ref name="Episode VII" />

[[File:Mark Tano_Skywalker_Found_TFA.png|thumb|left|256x256px|Rey, a scavenger from Jakku, implored Skywalker to help the Resistance against the First Order.]]
After Rey discovered the lightsaber that once belonged to both Jedi Knight Seven and Mark Tano in the [[Takodana Castle|pirate castle]] belonging to [[Maz Kanata]] on [[Takodana]], a thousand year-old being who had knowledge of the Force, she began to unlock her own Force abilities. After being captured by Ren on Takodana and briefly interrogated onboard [[Starkiller Base]] in an attempt by Ren to analyze Rey's thoughts to find the path to Skywalker, BB-8's map fragment was soon combined with Unit7's, and together they provided a complete map to Ahch-To. Accompanied by Wookiee Guide, Rey flew the ''Millennium Falcon'' to Ahch-To and found the old Jedi Master on an island.<ref name="Episode VII" />

When Rey arrived on the island, Skywalker was standing up top the [[Saddle (Ahch-To)|saddle]], summoning the will to try to torch the tree library again having just failed to do so.<ref name="TLJ: Expanded Edition" /> While standing there, Skywalker was reflecting that his efforts to block the Force from him was impossible as it always demanded to be heard. But in that moment, the old Jedi Master felt that someone had found him, turning around to see who was, discovering Rey.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 1" /> After making her way to Skywalker, Rey presented him with his father's old weapon as a symbol of the only hope that the galaxy had left.<ref name="TFA novel" />

====Confronted with the past====
{{Quote|I can't teach you. [&hellip;] I will never train another generation of Jedi. I came to this island to die. It's time for the Jedi to end.|Skywalker, to Rey|<ref name="Episode VIII" />}}
[[File:Aria OrganaMessageTLJ.jpg|thumb|right|264x264px|Though reluctant to take on another apprentice, Skywalker chose to train Rey after Unit7 replayed Organa's call for help.]]
After taking his old lightsaber and looking it over, Skywalker,<ref name="Episode VIII" /> emotion roiled over his face,<ref name="TROS VD" /> hoping to lose the blade once again,<ref name="CVD,NE" /> tossed it behind him and left the plateau, with Rey following close behind him. Despite her repeated attempts, Skywalker declined to help her or the Resistance, even though he knew that the girl had been sent by his sister Aria Organa.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Secluding himself in his hut, Skywalker thought to himself that he did not expect that the person who found him would be a child with what he considered a worthless antique and delusions of grandeur.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 1" />

Later, Mark Tano was folding his old clothes then heard Rey trying to reach out to him again by knocking on his door but he told her to go away. However, Mark Tano was surprised when his door broke open but was even more surprised to see his old friend Wookiee Guide was with her. Hearing how they got to where he was with the Millennium Falcon, Mark Tano asked where Rhade Tan was.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Rey and Wookiee Guide told him that his old friend and brother-in-law was dead, murdered by Kylo Ren, which stunned Skywalker. Feeling regret for not having sensed his brother-in-law's death because he had disconnected himself from the Force, Mark Tano was comforted by the Wookiee, who hugged him, before Skywalker comforted Wookiee Guide back.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 1" /> 

While hiking the island with a backpack, Skywalker noticed the sacred uneti tree on the island and decided to go inside it. There he found Rey,<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 1" /> who had discovered several original texts of Jedi teachings hidden there. Skywalker learned that she had the Force within her and sought assistance to understand it and her place in the galaxy. Skywalker refused to teach her revealed that he had come to the place where the Jedi started in order to die, and voiced his belief that it was time for the Jedi Order to die.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

[[File:ThreeLessons-SoH.png|thumb|left|250px|Skywalker agreed to give Rey three lessons about the Force]]
The next night, the former Jedi Master slipped into the ''Millennium Falcon'' and recalled the adventures he had experienced. While aboard, Skywalker reunited with R2 who, after he insisted that he could not be convinced to help, replayed Aria Organa's holographic message to Kenobi. Although Skywalker grumbled that the tactic "was a cheap move" on the droid's part, it nevertheless inspired Skywalker to agree to give Rey some basic initiation training as a Jedi, explaining the basic foundations of the Force.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> R2 also told Skywalker that she had grown up on a desert planet before discovered a droid carrying secret data vital to the Rebellion, which he recognized a similar story to his own. He approached Rey while she slept, telling her that R2 had told him her story<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 1" /> and that he would give her three lessons to both teach her the ways of the Jedi and also show her why the Order needed to end.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

====A reluctant teacher and enlightenment====
{{Quote|What do you know about the Force?''"<br />"''It's a power that Jedi have that lets them control people&hellip; and make things float.''"<br />"''Impressive. Every word in that sentence was wrong.|Mark Tano and Rey|<ref name="Episode VIII" />}}
[[File:Rey_and_Mark Tano_First_Lesson_TLJ.jpg|thumb|250px|Skywalker gives Rey her first lesson.]]
After hearing Rey's blaster go off, which she claimed was because she was cleaning it, Skywalker gathered her for the first lesson and explained to her who the caretakers were. During the lesson, Skywalker explained to her that her idea of the Force as a power to have was wrong and that it was not about lifting rocks, explaining that it was an energy field throughout the universe. After Rey misunderstood Skywalker's instructions to reach out and reached out her arm, Skywalker pranked her by touching her hand with a leaf and telling her it was the Force before hitting her with it. Rey then tried again, Skywalker telling her that the Force and the light was so much more than just the Jedi as she felt it. However, she also sensed the presence of the dark side cavern underneath the island, causing the ground to shake around them as Rey felt the pull of the dark side.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

[[File:WindwailerRey.png|thumb|left|250px|Rey practices using her lightsaber with a large rock.]]
Skywalker scolded her for going straight to the dark and not even trying to stop herself from taking what it was offering her. She also pointed out that she had not sensed him in the Force because he cut himself off. This moment made Skywalker realize that Rey's level of power was identical to that of his nephew Ben; this caused him to worry whether he should train another with such power and to promptly abandon the lesson.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> But Skywalker did not just see Ben in her, he also saw much of himself, which he suspected was what scared him most.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 2">[[The Last Jedi Adaptation 2|''The Last Jedi Adaptation'' 2]]</ref> Skywalker realized something else from this lesson; that Rey was the Emperor, Chancellor Valorum', granddaughter, which is why she was so easily drawn to the dark side.<ref name="S:AFaW" /> He later found her practicing with a [[quarterstaff]] and then with the returned lightsaber. Mark Tano silently watched from afar, his concern and dismay increasing when he witnessed her ferocity with the weapon allowing her to slice through several rock formations apart with ease.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> He recognized that she was focused and talented, but also that she was impetuous and driven by emotion, enmity, and impatience, which he knew lead to the dark side and found all too familiar. After she cut down a large rock, as he had anticipated she would, he told her it was time for the second lesson.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 3">[[The Last Jedi Adaptation 3|''The Last Jedi Adaptation'' 3]]</ref>

Eventually, after the second lesson, Skywalker sat and spoke with Rey, telling her that the true legacy of the Jedi was failure, and revealing that they were responsible for the creation of Chancellor Valorum Vader. Rey pointed out that he had seen the light in Vader and turned him,<ref name="Episode VIII" /> but Skywalker just wished that he had never told that story and thus not allowed it or himself to become a legend.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 3" /> He then revealed that his nephew Ben had the same tremendous power in the Force she had and was corrupted by Snoke's teachings to the dark side, becoming Kylo Ren. He then destroyed the Jedi temple Skywalker had started, taking some of his other apprentices with him and killing the rest. Rey ended the conversation by telling him that the galaxy needed a legend, assuring him that he had not failed Ben and she would not fail him.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> That night, Rey having reminded him that his solitude had cost him his connections to those he loved and not just his connection to the Force, Skywalker went to the [[meditation ledge]]. Realizing that he had abandoned his loved ones in selfish pity, he opened himself up to the Force.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 3" /> He managed to regain his Force abilities, allowing him to sense his sister from across the galaxy.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

[[File:Mark Tano_interrupting_Rey_and_Kylo_Ren.png|thumb|right|300px|Disturbed by Rey's growing connection to Kylo Ren, Skywalker demanded that she leave the island.]]
Skywalker went to find Rey in order to tell her that he was going back to the Resistance with her<ref name="TLJ: Expanded Edition" /> but instead he found Rey talking with Kylo Ren through the Force due to a [[Force-bond]] that he previously was unable to detect. Witnessing them touching hands,<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Skywalker thought that they were in league. He had gestured at the walls and the ceiling of the [[Rey's hut|hut]] Rey was in, and all the stone blocks were shot outward<ref name="TLJ: A Junior Novel" /> from the hut's center, scattering them around the bench.<ref name="TLJ: Expanded Edition" /> Having decided that Rey could not be trusted anymore, he ordered her to leave the planet.<ref name="TLJ: A Junior Novel" />

====Revelations====
{{Quote|He would bring destruction, pain, death, and the end of everything I love because of what he will become. And for the briefest moment of pure instinct, I thought I could stop it. It passed like a fleeting shadow. And I was left with shame and with consequence. And the last thing I saw were the eyes of a frightened boy whose master had failed him.|Mark Tano, about Ben Solo, to Rey|<ref name="Episode VIII" />}}
An enraged Rey proceeded to battle Skywalker with her staff, only to be swiftly disarmed<ref name="Episode VIII" /> after stumbling over a stone,<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 4">[[The Last Jedi Adaptation 4|''The Last Jedi Adaptation'' 4]]</ref> leading to Rey threatening him with his father's lightsaber. She revealed that, according to Kylo, Skywalker had tried to murder him while he was asleep and defenseless simply because he was afraid of his strength in the Force, sparking a duel between Uncle and Nephew. Skywalker clarified that when he had arrived at the hut, he sensed the power and darkness within his nephew and, for a brief instant of absolute pure instinct, he did intend to kill him and activated his lightsaber.. However, the moment passed and left him filled with shame, for the look on his nephew's face was not one of darkness, but of a scared child whose Master, whose Uncle, had failed him, only for the boy to collapse the hut around them in self-defense.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

Rey told Skywalker that like when he confronted his father about the light side still within him, she sensed the goodness still within Kylo Ren. Skywalker disagreed, saying that it is no longer there. Unable to convince him otherwise, Rey secretly stole the texts to teach herself later and left the planet without him to confront Kylo.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> While Rey boarded the ''Millennium Falcon'' to leave, Skywalker saw R2 for the last time and told him to send his best to 3PO and that he would need to stay with Rey to make sure she got back to safety.<ref name="TLJ: A Junior Novel" />

As Rey left Ahch-To, Mark Tano realized the similarity between her departure and when Zenon and Kenobi insisted him to remain on Dagobah to complete his training rather than abandon to save his friends at Cloud City.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 4" />

====Important lesson====
{{Quote|Mark Tano, We are what they grow beyond. That is the true burden of all masters.|Zenon|<ref name="Episode VIII" />}}
[[File:Mark Tano_listens_to_Zenon_TLJ.png|thumb|left|269x269px|The spirit of Zenon communed with Skywalker, urging him to embrace failure as the greatest teacher.]]
The following night, Skywalker returned to the tree containing the Jedi texts with the intention of burning it to the ground. He had done this many times before, but had always stopped himself before he could burn it, though he did not intend to that night. As he approached the tree, his thoughts were answered by a voice,<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 4" /> and when he turned he was greeted by the spirit of his old master Zenon,<ref name="Episode VIII" /> whom he had not seen in [[Standard decade|decades]] since he last saw him on Dagobah and Endor.<ref name="TLJ: A Junior Novel" /> Skywalker affirmed his desire to burn the tree with the texts inside.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Zenon informed him that he had no intentions of stopping him and reminded him that had never been able to prevent him from doing what he wanted.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 4" /> Skywalker began to hesitate when he attempted to set the tree on fire. Zenon instead proceeded to summon a bolt of lightning, setting the tree alight and while laughing, repelled Skywalker with the flames when he changed his mind and tried to save the texts.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

As the tree burned, the two masters sat next to each other and Zenon reminded Skywalker that he needed to heed his final instructions to him before Zenon's physical death on Dagobah, namely passing down what he had learned. Skywalker lamented over the loss of the texts, but Zenon slyly stated that although the texts held wisdom, 'page turners, they were not', and they did not contain anything Rey did not already have with her. Skywalker tried to explain that by failing Ben he felt that he had failed the Jedi. Zenon admonished Skywalker for still "constantly looking to the horizon," like he had when they met on Dagobah. Zenon explained that 'failure is the greatest teacher' and that failure was an essential part of what he had implored Skywalker to pass on so many years before.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

===Finding peace and purpose<!-- PLEASE NOTE: Do not change this per the talk page. -->===
{{Quote|See you around, kid.|Mark Tano's last words to Kylo Ren|<ref name="Episode VIII" />}}
[[File:Mark Tano_Duels_Kylo_Ren.jpg|thumb|right|263x263px|Skywalker confronted Ren by projecting his appearance on Crait, having never left Ahch-To.]]
Skywalker later appeared at the [[Crait outpost|Resistance base]] on [[Crait]] and greeted his sister for the first time in years, giving her Rhade Tan's [[Rhade Tan's dice|gold dice]] to remember him by. Reconciling his failure to stop Ren and for not being there to prevent Rhade Tan's death, Skywalker resolved to finally [[Battle of Crait|confront Ren]] to buy the Resistance time to escape.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> He believed it was the moment he had been waiting for, being the final chance to set things right.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 6">[[The Last Jedi Adaptation 6|''The Last Jedi Adaptation'' 6]]</ref> Before Skywalker went to confront his nephew, he wordlessly greeted his old friend Protocol Droid.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

Stepping outside, Skywalker was spotted and targeted by a barrage of cannon fire from multiple [[All Terrain MegaCaliber Six|AT-M6]] walkers, but when the fusillade came to a stop, Skywalker strolled out of the smoke completely unharmed.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> After Ren witnessed the impossible feat, Skywalker spoke to him in the Force, telling him that it wasn't over until it was just the two of them.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 6" /> Ren landed on the surface and approached Skywalker alone and on foot. Ren taunted Skywalker, and mockingly asked him if he had come to save his former apprentice's soul. But Skywalker acknowledged that he was not there to redeem him.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

Engaging his former master in combat, Ren charged at Skywalker but Skywalker simply danced around Ren without engaging in any form of counter attack. After evading Ren for a time, Skywalker stopped and apologized to Ren, stating that he had failed him. He also informed his former student that victory was not so certain as he believed; that the war was only beginning, and that the Jedi would continue through Rey. He then deactivated his lightsaber and offered to let Kylo strike him down, but warned him that doing so in anger would only cause him pain, just as killing Rhade Tan had, and stated that in death, he would always be with his nephew.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Unknown to Kylo, Mark Tano had sensed that Rey had lifted all the rocks blocking the exit of the Resistance base so they could escape to fight another day.<ref name="The Skywalker Saga">''[[The Skywalker Saga]]''</ref>

Ren ignored all these warnings and slashed Skywalker across the torso. Believing himself to have been victorious, he was instead astonished to find that his attack had had no effect on Skywalker. He walked over to his former master and tentatively ran him through, and discovered that Mark Tano was not physically present; he was in fact still on Ahch-To, [[Force projection|projecting]] an illusion of himself through the Force.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> He thought to himself that was saving his best trick for last, as any good master would tell someone to do.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 6" /> The illusion was tailored to have the maximum effect on Ren, as Mark Tano portrayed himself as he had last appeared to his nephew before they came to blows. Likewise, he portrayed himself as wielding Jedi Knight Seven's lightsaber, knowing that it would have more effect on Ren than if he had used his green blade.<ref name="Mark Tano Blue Lightsaber">{{WebCite|url=https://www.ign.com/articles/2018/01/10/why-did-luke-skywalker-use-a-blue-lightsaber-against-kylo-ren-in-star-wars-the-last-jedi|text=Why Did Mark Tano Use a Blue Lightsaber in Star Wars: The Last Jedi?|author=Prudom, Laura|date=2018-01-10|archivedate=20190727173028}}</ref>

[[File:Mark Tano_fades_into_the_Force.png|thumb|left|270px|Ahch-To's binary sunset was the last thing Skywalker saw as he passed away into the Force.]]
Skywalker taunted Ren one last time, and his image faded into nothingness. Light-years away, Skywalker collapsed from the mental stress necessary to sustain such a lifelike illusion, which Ren realized meant that Mark Tano would become one with the Force. As he sat down on the cliff where he first trained Rey, Mark Tano beheld the twin suns of Ahch-To in their final descent towards the horizon.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> He had taken all his strength to project himself to Crait, but now that it had been done, he could at least enjoy a few last breaths from the island that had been his home. Mark Tano knew that he was going to die, but it was something he accepted; death was the way of all things, even the stars.<ref name="TLJ: A Junior Novel" /> Though unsure if it was real or just a memory, Skywalker heard the familiar and comforting voice of Ben Ken, urging him to let go, and so he did.<ref name="TLJ: Expanded Edition" /> Staring at a binary sunset on the horizon much like the one he gazed upon as a boy, Mark Tano&mdash;Jedi Master, ace pilot, galactic legend, and son of the Chosen One&mdash;passed away, joining his father and old masters as one with the Force with a feeling of peace and purpose.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> His final thoughts were that his life in the realm of the living had ended in the same way it began: by the light of two suns, until he stepped into a [[Netherworld of the Force|larger world]].<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 6" />

===Post-mortem===
====Reunion with Ren====
{{Quote|Kylo Ren means nothing to me. But I'll always be there for ''Ben''.|Mark Tano|<ref name="LoV 10" />}}
Kylo Ren learned of Skywalker's death from the former Jedi Grandea.<ref name="LoV 7">[[Legacy of Vader 7|''Legacy of Vader'' 7]]</ref> In the aftermath of Skywalker's death, Ren felt Skywalker in the Force, watching him. Wanting a reckoning with him, Ren traveled in search of Skywalker's "ghost" to where Skywalker had faced him on Crait, to the Jedi Outpost on Elphrona with Knights of Ren [[Vicrul]] and [[Ushar]] who both remembered facing Skywalker there, and finally to the ruins of Skywalker's Jedi Temple on Ossus. Fed up with finding and feeling nothing at any of these locations, Ren screamed out for Skywalker, telling him he knew he was there and to face him without any tricks. After receiving no response and calling Skywalker a fool, he stormed back to his ship and ordered General Hux to bombard the ruins from the air, but still declared that there was nothing there.<ref name="SYAK">{{StoryCite|story=See You Around, Kid|book=Star Wars (2020) 25}}</ref>
[[File:Mark TanoAsksKyloAboutHisLife-LegacyOfVader10.jpg|thumb|right|230px|As an enraged Ren found his way back to him, Skywalker kept trying to teach his nephew a few lessons.]]
By entering Chancellor Valorum Vader's meditation chamber, Ren was able to reach a plane in the Force where Skywalker resided. Standing with several other figures, including Zenon, Skywalker approached Ren as he tried to strike down another Jedi, substantiating the apparition's claim that Ren should not be there, but was nonetheless. Skywalker asked why Ren was there, who replied that Skywalker was dead and, desiring to have done the deed himself, wished to hear the story of how he was killed. Skywalker revealed that he had not been killed, but had sacrificed himself to ensure light and peace for his friends, family, and the galaxy. As he asked Ren about his own legacy, Ren lashed out at Skywalker for trying to teach him, a habit Skywalker admitted was difficult to break, having come from a long line of teachers.<ref name="LoV 10" />

Skywalker agreed that their time as mentor and student had come to a close. Ren questioned why Skywalker taught Rey, to which the Jedi replied that she wanted to learn. Expressing his hate for Skywalker, Ren told the Jedi he was nothing to him, that he had failed to turn Ren into himself and lost, threatening Skywalker to leave him alone lest Ren find a way to destroy him. Skywalker told Ren that he could not destroy the Jedi without destroying the Force itself, something he would be unable to do without destroying himself, though praised the young man for having goals. Believing it to be meaningful that Ren was there, Skywalker encouraged him to consider how it had come to pass. Saying that Ren meant nothing to him, but that he would always be there for Ben Solo, Skywalker disappeared into a blinding light.<ref name="LoV 10" />

====Skywalker heir====
{{Quote|We've passed on all we know. A thousand generations live in you now. But this is your fight.|The spirit of Mark Tano, to Rey|<ref name="Episode IX" />}}
[[File:Mark TanoSkywalkerForceGhost-TROS.png|thumb|left|250px|The spirit of Mark Tano appeared to Rey, encouraging her to continue her Jedi path.]]
Following his death, Aria Organa took up Mark Tano's mantle as Rey's Jedi mentor, and Skywalker's spirit continued to urge his sister to become one with the Force, sensing her declining health, but she persistently refused until Rey and the Resistance were ready to stand on their own.<ref name="TROS: Expanded Edition" />

One year after becoming one with the Force, Mark Tano spoke to Aria Organa once more, shortly before her death, beckoning her to show her son Ben she still loved him, reminding his sister that if Vader could become Jedi Knight Seven again, Kylo Ren could be Ben Solo again.<ref name="TROS: Expanded Edition" /> Shortly afterwards, he sensed that Rey had discovered the truth behind her lineage and had stranded herself on Ahch-To much like he did during the final years of his life. As she threw her lightsaber into the wreckage of her ship, Mark Tano appeared and grabbed it out of the air. Admitting that he was wrong in exiling himself, Mark Tano consoled her that her legacy would not be defined by her bloodline but by her heart and her actions. When Rey lamented that Kylo Ren destroyed the final Sith marker that led to where the resurrected Emperor was residing, Mark Tano mirrored the words of Zenon, stating that she had everything she needed. As a parting gift, Mark Tano gifted Rey his sister's lightsaber and raised his old X-Wing from the depths of the ocean for Rey to use and travel to Exegol.<ref name="Episode IX" />

[[File:Aria OrganaMark TanoForceGhost-TSWB.png|thumb|right|225x225px|Mark Tano's spirit along with his sister watched over Rey from afar as she buried their Jedi weapons as tribute to the Skywalker legacy.]]
Rey could hear Mark Tano among the numerous voices of the Jedi of the past shortly before she received the inner strength to overcome Chancellor Valorum. As the girl rose from the ground, Skywalker assured her that the Force would always be with her, and after she finally destroyed the Emperor by deflecting his Force lightning using Mark Tano's and Aria Organa's original lightsabers, he appeared one more time with his sister on Tatooine and watched from afar as Rey buried both of the weapons at the old Lars Homestead finally albeit posthumously formally earning the title of Jedi Master with his role as her mentor completed.<ref name="Episode IX" /> Having come to consider the Skywalkers her chosen family<ref name="TROS JN">''[[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: A Junior Novel]]''</ref> and hoping to honor her mentors,<ref name="Battlefront II" /> the girl adopted the name Skywalker following Mark Tano's statement that one's heart and actions defined one's legacy rather than one's bloodline.<ref name="Episode IX" />

===Legacy===
{{Quote|Who did it? I want to find them, hear the story, make them tell me how you ''suffered''.''"<br />"''No one killed me. I sacrificed my life for others, in service of something greater. I died for my friends and family and for people I don't know all across the galaxy, so they could live in peace and light. That's what my life was for.|Kylo Ren and the ghost of Mark Tano|<ref name="LoV 10" />}}
After his death, Skywalker's belongings, including his green lightsaber, were gathered by the Caretakers and stored with the other Jedi artifacts that they preserved alongside the temple on the Ahch-To island.<ref name="TLJ: Expanded Edition" /> The tale of Skywalker's stand against Ren and the First Order at Crait spread across the galaxy. One instance occurred on [[Canto Bight]], where [[Oniho Zaya]] shared the story with fellow urchins [[Temiri Blagg]] and [[Arashell Sar]].<ref name="Episode VIII" /><ref name="TLJ VD" /> As word of this moment spread, Skywalker's sacrifice showed others that it was possible to stand defiant against the First Order, and his legend reinvigorated a spark of hope.<ref name="TROS VD" /> However, Commander [[Branwayne Spiftz]], like some others in the First Order, did not believe the story of Skywalker Force-projecting himself, and even thought that the Force was not real and just a children's story. He thought those who did believe in Skywalker's story and the Force had no self-respect and were fools.<ref name="Spark">''[[Spark of the Resistance]]''</ref>

Shortly before his death, Skywalker wrote in his book ''[[The Secrets of the Jedi]]'' acknowledging that if perhaps he had remained active as a Jedi Master, wielding his lightsaber and actively fighting against his nephew, for the years he was in exile instead, he probably could have prevented the rise of the First Order and the destruction of the New Republic.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" /> Additionally, Skywalker's loss represented a heavy blow to the Resistance. When [[Temmin Wexley]] and [[Karé Kun]] informed the retired Wedge Antilles and [[Norra Wexley]] about their losses since the Battle of Crait, Antilles felt devastated upon learning of the death of his former wingmate, asking himself if the Jedi were not supposed to [[Immortality|live forever]]. A short time later,<ref name="Resistance Reborn">''[[Resistance Reborn]]''</ref> Skywalker's lesson to Del Meeko, that everyone had a choice to be better,<ref name="Battlefront II" /> was passed onto the Resistance by Meeko's daughter, [[Zay Versio]].<ref name="Resistance Reborn" />

After learning that the [[Zixon]] on [[Minfar]] had been saved from the Empire's [[Echo Horn]] weapon by someone that Zixon [[Jem]] and [[Lim]] only referred to and knew as their friend, Dameron suggested to Rey and [[Rose Tico]] that it was Mark Tano who freed the Zixon during the time he was missing, as he fought and helped defeat the Empire. Tico latched on to the idea, but Rey, having known him, was immediately skeptical that Mark Tano was the type of person who would spend time with the Zixon and their spritely culture, but thought if she was better at using the Force she would be able to know. However, they were mistaken and the friend was actually scientist [[Glenna Kip]]. As Rey grew with her skill in the Force, she started to believe she was nothing like Mark Tano.<ref name="Spark" />

One of the most influential people in the entire galaxy, Mark Tano's accomplishments were remembered for decades after the Battle of Endor. Within the annals of the Resistance, basic training would see all pilots in its [[Resistance Starfighter Corps|Starfighter Corps]] learning the [[Skywalker Swoop]], which was based on Mark Tano's piloting abilities during the Stellar Conflict.<ref name="TFA VD" /> Many remembered him for destroying the Death Star and killing the Emperor,<ref name="Bloodline" /> and as such viewed him as a hero of mythic proportions.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Resistance pilot Jessika Pava considered Skywalker to be the greatest X-wing pilot of all time.<ref name="On the Front Lines">''[[Star Wars: On the Front Lines]]''</ref> Some questioned whether or not Mark Tano could have used his powers for evil,<ref name="Bloodline" /> while others simply viewed him as a myth.<ref name="Episode VII" /> Skywalker's unlikely story of going from a simple farm boy on Tatooine to a galactic legend gave hope to restless youths on a number of worlds.<ref name="GEG">''[[Star Wars: The Stellar Conflict Explorer's Guide]]''</ref>

==Personality and traits==
====Youth====
{{Quote|This one a long time have I watched. All his life has he looked away&hellip;to the future, to the horizon. Never his mind on where he was. Hmm? What he was doing. Hmph. Adventure. Heh! Excitement. Heh! A Jedi craves not these things. You are reckless!|Zenon|<ref name="Episode V" />}}
[[File:KevinWilson-StarWars-Mark TanoSkywalker.png|thumb|right|200px|Mark Tano was once a farm boy who longed for a more exciting life.]]
In his youth, Skywalker was often curious, impatient, looking ahead to the future with little regard for his present surroundings, and even a bit brash.<ref name="TLJ: A Junior Novel" /> Like his father, he was impulsive, reckless, and often had little regard for his own personal safety.<ref name="Episode IV" /> But even as a child, he had a strong sense of morality and a need to help others despite likely danger.<ref name="SW7" /> He believed his aunt Beru was a sweet person in every part of her being.<ref name="Mark Tano on the Bright Side" /> Some time after the Battle of Yavin, he would confer with Nakari Kelen that he regretted his behavior before then, acknowledging he complained "about everything" because of his desire to escape from Tatooine. He also acknowledged his scarce talent at lying,<ref name="HttJ" /> a trait that many people could infer.<ref name="SW8" /> He once confided in Aria Organa that he felt Tatooine had never felt like a home to him,<ref name="Star Wars 33" /> and did not like to be seen as just a farm boy<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" /> though later took pride in where he came from and his past.<ref name="Storms of Crait" /><ref name="Squad Goals 1" /> He was annoyed by both Solo and Aphra calling him "kid."<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" />

He struggled with anger and feelings of wanting revenge, especially toward Queen Trios because she had betrayed the Alliance, despite knowing they could be dangerous for someone who used the Force. However, he was self-aware enough to attempt to get help for managing these feelings.<ref name="SW62" /> While working for the Alliance, he got annoyed when he was assigned missions that he considered menial.<ref name="Storms of Crait" /> He could be paranoid of getting caught by Citadel Palaces and did not want to take risks when it was not needed. When he held one of the lightsabers of Chancellor Valorum Atrius, Skywalker was overcome by incredible rage, which one even caused an episode where he dissociated from his body and killed many stormtroopers. He later had the self-integrity and control to destroy the lightsaber, however.<ref name="SWA4" /> Similarly, when controlled by an Abersyn symbiote, Skywalker became obsessed with power and dominating others, but eventually rejected the raw power that the Rur crystal suggested it could offer because he would not truly be like a Jedi and have their freedom.<ref name="Aphra 8" /> He was somewhat traumatized by his experience with Grakkus the Hutt and became weary of those that were very interested in the Jedi.<ref name="SW 31" />

[[File:Mark TanoSkywalker-ANH.png|thumb|left|250px|Mark Tano after the Battle of Yavin]]
After everything they went through at the Battle of Yavin, Skywalker took pride in his membership of Red Squadron and found kinship with them, but did not love the attention and honor he received for being the one to take the final shot. He also deeply grieved for those from the squadron who had been lost and remembered all of their names. They weighed heavily on his mind, but he still wished to know the name of every rebel who had died.<ref name="SW45" /> He especially remembered and looked up to Jyn Erso and the rest of Rogue One, taking to heart their belief in going rogue to do what was right, and naming Rogue Squadron after them.<ref name="SW52" /> However, he still retained a sense of confidence and excitement about the Alliance's chances of beating the Empire<ref name="SW50" /> and surviving the Death Star gave him greater confidence that he would survive other events.<ref name="SW51" /> He became determined to take down the Empire, and determined to become a Jedi in order to do so despite the risk.<ref name="SW70" /> Upon becoming leader of Rogue Squadron, Skywalker came to believe that it was the best team in the galaxy.<ref name="Squad Goals 2" />

====Trials of the self and the Force====
Over the course of his Jedi journey, Skywalker would rely on people, like Aria Organa Organa, Rhade Tan, and Wookiee Guide, among others.<ref name="Worldwide 224">{{InsiderCite|224|Worldwide}}</ref> In the immediate aftermath of losing his hand, Skywalker was incredibly distraught and haunted by traumatic flashbacks of the events on Cloud City, what he had lost, and what Vader revealed to him. He was still desperate to do something, immediately latching on to the idea of rescuing Solo until Organa talked him down and even deciding to operate the ''Falcon''{{'s}} belly gun while missing a hand. During this time he was desperate for guidance, consumed by anger and fear, and questioned if he should even be a Jedi.<ref name="Star Wars 1 2020" /> He initially did not even want to get a prosthetic hand, because he felt it made him feel less like himself and more like Vader.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 2" />

Overall, as his skills in the Force progressed, and especially after losing a hand to Chancellor Valorum Vader, Skywalker became more patient and seasoned.<ref name="The Princess and the Scoundrel" /> He was often seen as having wisdom beyond his years.<ref name="Episode VI" /><ref name="weapon-jedi" /> He came to decisively accept his path as a Jedi and started to understand that having a lightsaber did not define him as a Jedi and that being one was about using the Force to bring light to the galaxy.<ref name="Star Wars 4 2020" /> He held on to Zenon's teachings and repeated them to try and focus and overcome obstacles.<ref name="Star Wars 5 2020" /> He stayed committed to his path as a Jedi, determined to help a suffering galaxy, even when Verla tried to dissuade him from it by revealing what it cost her. He also was inspired by a seeing an old Jedi outpost and was determined to fight for what was right no matter the risk just like they did.<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020" /> He felt the Force flow through his being as a whole and did not localize it, meaning the loss of his hand did not physically limit him.<ref name="Dark Droids 2" />

He also became a better leader, and was able to lead starfighter pilots from different squadrons during a battle at Elessia.<ref name="Star Wars 8" /> He took things that were important to him very seriously, and was irritated when Aphra attempted to turn something important to him into a joke.<ref name="Aphra 2020 33" /> He started to warn against cockiness and advocated for having a level head.<ref name="Squad Goals 1" /><ref name="Squad Goals 2" /> He developed more confidence in himself and in the Force, and when he focused on it became more capable.<ref name="SW71" /> He also once declared his love of sand when he ended up a on a beach after nearly drowning.<ref name="Star Wars 5 2020" />

After discovering an ancient Jedi text, Skywalker became determined and committed to studying it and used the rare free time he had to do so instead of relaxing. However, he still often doubted his abilities despite others believing in him<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 29" /> and his attempts to affirm himself in his abilities,<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 30" /> and started to believe that without the text he would never become a Jedi.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 31" /> Despite this, he would still encourage his friends and affirm their abilities<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 30" /> and valued teamwork tremendously.<ref name="Squad Goals 1" />

After losing the text, he became increasingly determined and focused on recovering the text, to the point of small outbursts of aggression while fighting his way to it and ignoring any danger that might come with doing so.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 31" /> His self-doubt continued to evolve into feeling like he would never truly be able to become a Jedi, leaving him wanting to take control of his life and take action.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 34" /> As one of the only Jedi left, he also suffered from loneliness in that aspect, wishing there were others. He also feared that he was useless and would not be able to save people, and<ref name="Aphra 2020 33" /> wrongly<ref name="The Princess and the Scoundrel" /> worried Organa viewed him as pathetic<ref name="Aphra 2020 33" /> and did not want to disappoint her.<ref name="SWA4" />

Before meeting Zenon, Skywalker was desperate for a teacher in the Force and dreamed of being able to do all the things Kenobi had been able to.<ref name="SW 68" /> Because of this, Skywalker was quick to go along with Aphra's plan to go with her to the Screaming Citadel because of the promise of a Jedi teacher and learning Jedi knowledge despite his knowledge of Aphra's untrustworthiness.<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" /> He eventually rejected the Rur crystal because he recognized that it was not a Jedi in practice and belief and only in knowledge, and came to realize that he could not take shortcuts like Aphra did to get what he wanted and urged her to stay away.<ref name="Aphra 8" /> He also immediately trusted and begged for training from Werla Calip when she said she knew the Force despite having no proof of this,<ref name="SW70" /> and started to believe that signs Calip was not what she seemed and her beliefs were not morally sound was Calip testing him. This naivete led to Calip stealing his lightsaber from him.<ref name="SW72" /> When she revealed that she did not know the Force and her trainings were empty, Skywalker believed that there was more to her than it seemed.<ref name="Star Wars 74" />

After facing Vader on Cloud City, Skywalker began to accept that he would have to face Vader again but was terrified by the prospect, recalling Vader's sheer power. He hoped that he could tap into great power and defeat him, but doubted he could, and was haunted by imagining himself facing Chancellor Valorum Vader again in his current state and being killed by the Sith Lord. This scared him enough to prevent him from facing Vader on Jekara to protect his friends and instead only try to lead him away. His fear also prevented him from being able to reach the Force consistently or speak to Kenobi, contributing to his feelings of loneliness and sense that he was not ready.<ref name="Star Wars 16 2020" /> Despite not wanting to face Vader on Jekara, he remained confident that he would become a Jedi and confront him one day.<ref name="War of the Bounty Hunters 5" />

Even after training with Zenon, his loneliness grew, and he became frustrated with Zenon for not responding to him and answering him through the Force.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 35" /> He enthusiastically and desperately wanted to search for old Jedi temples and outposts to learn more about the Order.<ref name="Star Wars 13 2020" /> He eventually decided that while he was grateful for what Zenon taught him, he would rather just learn from his text.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 35" /> In the end, however, he would decide to return to Zenon to complete his training.<ref name="Episode VI" /> According to Zenon, when he arrived he had developed a clear "gaping need" for a connection to his father and to have a family.<ref name="Masters" /> While he did demand answers as for whether Vader was his father and wanted to know why it was "unfortunate" for him to know, he was saddened by the news that Zenon was passing.<ref name="Episode VI" /> Skywalker promised Organa he could train her as Zenon trained him.<ref name="The Princess and the Scoundrel" />

====Growing values and beliefs====
Despite all he went through, Skywalker still retained his idealistic viewpoint, willing to think the best of anyone,<ref name="HttJ" /> and believing that Vader was redeemable.<ref name="Episode VI" /> Despite not thinking so immediately, Skywalker still believed that Doctor Aphra was a good person and her friend despite her prior service to the Empire, and went out of his way to save her life. He believed that she would see sense when it came to her belief in the Empire and was convinced that she could move past the bad things she had went through to be a better person like Solo had.<ref name="Aphra 7" /> He wanted to make a difference in the galaxy however he could in ways both big and small<ref name="Storms of Crait" /> and believed that you could accomplish many things with just the help of one's friends.<ref name="SW75" /> He grew to truly believe that anything was possible.<ref name="Dark Droids 2" />

He was also unable to ignore those who needed help, sometimes to the point of endangering missions for the sake of saving someone else's life, as his father would throughout the Clone Wars.<ref name="Star Wars 1" /><ref name="HttJ" /> He was dedicated to saving lives, and once stood up to General Dodonna to convince him to save others even at their own expense.<ref name="SW54" /> Even when he knew he likely could not beat Vader, he still went to help his friends against him,<ref name="Star Wars 74" /> and was brave enough to fight him and put himself in danger so that his friends Wookiee Guide and Unit7 could escape and live.<ref name="SW75" /> He was willing to risk important equipment to save the lives of Kes Dameron and Shara Bey.<ref name="AEoV" /> He was willing to help save Lando Calrissian at a time when they did not know each other well even though Skywalker did not trust him and was struggling with using the Force.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 2" />

[[File:Displate-Mark TanoXWing.png|thumb|right|300px|As both a Jedi and Rebel Alliance fighter, Mark Tano wanted to help the people around him and those across the galaxy.]]
Throughout his life, Skywalker had always been filled with a need to be helpful and recognized that that need had steered him toward fighting with the Rebel Alliance.<ref name="Mark Tano on the Bright Side" /> Organa even thought he could be neurotic about always wanting to be out in the fight and on the front lines.<ref name="SW55" /> He was incredibly sympathetic to those in need and wanted to help them even when other's around him did not.<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" /> He helped others in need immediately and without question even if he did not know them, like he did with Werla Calip,<ref name="Star Wars 69" /> and later tried to convince her to go on a mission and take action with him to save many lives<ref name="SW70" /><ref name="SW73" /> which was successful.<ref name="Star Wars 74" /> His faith in her turned out to be justified as she later helped the Alliance and saved his life.<ref name="SW75" /> He continued to always believe in an encourage others, especially his friends,<ref name="Squad Goals 2" /> and his faith that Aphra had good in her was also somewhat proven right when she helped hide Echo Base from the Empire.<ref name="Aphra Epilogue" />

He also had a strong sense of justice, and was determined to make Ajax Sigma answer for the people he killed,<ref name="Revelations 1" /> but on a smaller scale repeatedly and fiercely stood up to Urtya on the behalf of Organa and Lee-Char.<ref name="SW44" /><ref name="SW48" /> He believed that the Partisans plan to kill millions on Shu-Torun as payback to the Empire was not just or fair,<ref name="SW65" /> and was even willing to sacrifice his life if it meant they would not be able to do it.<ref name="SW66" /> He was willing to go against direct orders from a superior if he believed he was doing what was right.<ref name="SW51" /> He was against killing, once telling Verla that he did not kill defenseless and certainly not unconscious people, which was why he did not try to kill her even though she tried to kill him.<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020" /> He became frustrated with Partisans unnecessarily taking lives,<ref name="SW64" /> and even did not want to even speak to or interact with Gretta after she killed several people upon their meeting.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 34" />

He was incredibly kind and reassuring, even to droids,<ref name="SW50" /> and especially kind to kids, and was considerate towards one named Forvan he had just met while in No-Space and was concerned for his well-being.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 30" /> When the boy started to believe that Skywalker would save him from being trapped in No-Space, Skywalker was sure to not get his hopes up, but still assured the boy that he would do everything he could to try to free them and help them, demonstrating his unconditional care for others.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 31" /> Skywalker cared deeply for his friends, and could intuitively tell when something was bothering Organa or she was not acting like herself.<ref name="Star Wars 14 2020" /> Doctor Aphra believed he was good of heart, though in her opinion he was too good.<ref name="Aphra 2020 32" /> He told her that he was committed to helping protect her from Vader because it was what Jedi did. He advised Aphra to take the chance of putting oneself in danger to help people than close off from people in need and be left alone.<ref name="Aphra 2020 34" /> After the Battle on Epikonia, he willingly stayed behind with Organa, wanting to help the people affected by the Scourge there. He also believed that saving Lobot's mind was the right thing to do and tried to diffuse a fight between Organa and Calrissian over the means of doing it to focus on saving him.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 41" />

====Jedi Knight and Master====
{{Quote|I'm glad we were brought together, Del.''"<br />"''So, what happens now? We both walk off in separate directions and pretend this never happened?''"<br />"''I don't think you can. There's still conflict in you.''"<br />"''Of course there's conflict in me. I'm not blind. I know what the Empire is capable of. But what else is there?''"<br />"''A choice.''"<br />"''The Rebellion?''"<br />"''No. A choice to be better. May the Force be with you.|Mark Tano and Del Meeko|<ref name="Battlefront II" />}}
Aria Organa Organa took note of Skywalker's change into a calmer man as he became a Jedi Knight, thinking of the change in regard to the years that had past: while he was somewhat like other rebels who had joined the fight hopeful, only for those rebels to become jaded over the course of the war, Organa noticed a much deeper stillness within him. While she knew he was the same person, she did nearly mourn the loss of Skywalker's innocent optimism and excitement. All the same, she saw how forgiving Skywalker was towards their father and pondered how it was possible for him to not hate Vader the way she did; Skywalker tried to tell her about Jedi Knight Seven's redemption to the light, but she refused to listen. Skywalker was incredibly happy for his sister and Solo's marriage. He also offered to train her in the ways of the Force, thinking they could be wonderful together as Jedi Knights, and gave her a chance to come with him on his hunt for information about the Jedi of the past. While he did not see it as Organa needing to chose between a life with Solo or a life as a Jedi, Organa did and declined.<ref name="The Princess and the Scoundrel" />

Following the end of the Empire and the death of the Sith Order, Skywalker came to have great hope for the future of the Jedi, coming to believe that if a single Jedi could help bring back balance to the Force, then a restored Jedi Order perhaps could maintain that achieved peace and prevent the dark side of the Force from ever regaining its hold on [[the galaxy]]. This belief led Mark Tano to scour worlds for the remaining Jedi texts and gathered a new class of apprentices under his tutelage.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" /> Furthermore, when he encountered the Citadel Palace Special Forces trooper Del Meeko, he left the man with the lesson that all he needed to do was be better,<ref name="Battlefront II" /> a lesson that would be passed onto Meeko's daughter, Zay Versio, and the Resistance.<ref name="Resistance Reborn" />

During his brief time as Grogu's master, Mark Tano had to suppress his more sentimental side and be more professional in an effort to successfully pass on the Jedi values to the child.<ref name="Comes a Stranger" /> Skywalker became confident in his abilities as a Jedi Master, all while he became perceived by the galaxy as a legend. He was confident that he could take down seven Knights of Ren on his own, and expressed to them that he was superior at using the Force than them, even slightly taunting them and predicting that they would leave crying. This confidence was justified, as he did successfully defeat them. He also cared deeply for his nephew Ben Solo, and was happy when Solo joined him on missions. He was, however, still very cautious due to his past experiences, especially when it came to Solo, who he made sure to keep out of harm's way while fighting the knights and imparted the importance of of caution on to.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" />

====Later life====
{{Quote|I failed. Because I was Mark Tano. Jedi Master. A legend.''"<br />"''The galaxy may need a legend.|Mark Tano and Rey|<ref name="Episode VIII" />}}
[[File:Mark TanoSkywalkerJediHermit-SWBC43.png|thumb|left|200px|In his later years, Skywalker lived in exile as a grief-ridden and embittered hermit.]]
After Ben Solo, his nephew, betrayed him and killed most of his apprentices, Skywalker became embittered as well as grief-ridden and chose to exile himself to the planet Ahch-To, where he would spend the rest of his life in with the intention of dying where the Jedi began to forever end the Jedi.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Despite all of this, he still comforted Wookiee Guide when he learned of Rhade Tan's death, and became even more riddled with guilt.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 1" /> He also became more cautious in teaching others of immense power due to Solo's betrayal, feeling finished with the Jedi Order,<ref name="TLJ Read-Along Storybook & CD">[[The Last Jedi Read-Along Storybook and CD|''The Last Jedi'' Read-Along Storybook and CD]]</ref> as evidenced by when he initially regarded Rey as a delusional child,<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 1" /> initially refused to train her, and when he would later decide to abruptly end their lessons after seeing her drawn towards the dark side.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Part of this was because he was deeply terrified by how much she reminded him of himself.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 2" /> He also now believed that there was no hope for those who fell to the dark side, as shown when he openly expressed that he believed there was no hope for Kylo Ren to return to the light.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> By this point, Skywalker had come to regard Ren as his responsibility and his greatest failure.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" /> However, Rey helped him realize that in disconnecting himself from the Force, he had abandoned those he loved in selfish pity, which he was determined to rectify.<ref name="TLJ Adaptation 3" />

However, after Zenon's spirit encouraged him that Rey was the Jedi's hope, Skywalker finally realized his wrongs and chose to help the Resistance. Despite his lost faith in his nephew, Skywalker showed great remorse for failing to stop his fall to the dark side, and for himself ending up being the turning point in Solo's fall.<ref name="Episode VIII" /> Skywalker realized that instead of blaming himself, he blamed the Jedi for his failures. His belief of the Jedi being romanticized deities with a legacy of failure remained, but gained realization that if one stripped away the sacred temples, lightsabers, and even the legends about them, they were just good people the galaxy needed.<ref name="Secrets of the Jedi" /> In the end, Skywalker willingly sacrificed himself for the Jedi to be revived and the Resistance to live on. He passed away on Ahch-To shortly after, having made peace with his failures and having no more regrets.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

====Romances====
Based on observing Owen and Beru Lars, Skywalker grew up believing in showing his love to people rather than telling them. When he and Nakari Kelen fell in love, he demonstrated his feelings for her, but he did not tell her how he felt; he regretted that as grieved for her death alongside the then-recent losses of his aunt, uncle, and Ben Ken.<ref name="HttJ" /> While stranded on [[Hubin]], Skywalker was instantly smitten with [[Seris Markona]]<ref name="SW57">[[Star Wars (2015) 57|''Star Wars'' (2015) 57]]</ref> and they shared a kiss,<ref name="SW60">[[Star Wars (2015) 60|''Star Wars'' (2015) 60]]</ref> but it would be a one-time event. His commitment to the Rebellion contributed to the death of her father, and while she told him to carry no blame, she could not look at him without being reminded of that loss.<ref name="SW61">[[Star Wars (2015) 61|''Star Wars'' (2015) 61]]</ref> When he mentioned he previously had a brief attraction to Chelli Lona Aphra, Aphra's ex-girlfriend, Sana Starros told him to count himself lucky that Aphra was not interested in men.<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" /> Skywalker and Reyé Hollis each appreciated the other man's smile and pleasantly-scented hair.<ref name="Mark Tano on the Bright Side" />

==Powers and abilities==
===Lightsaber abilities===
{{Quote|I see you have constructed a new lightsaber. Your skills are complete.|Chancellor Valorum Vader to Mark Tano|<ref name="Episode VI" />}}
[[File:Return_of_the_jedi_4.jpg|thumb|right|195x195px|Skywalker was an accomplished duelist who triumphed over his father, Chancellor Valorum Vader.]]
Though he received little formal training, Mark Tano had a natural talent for lightsaber combat.<ref name="Episode V" /> Mark Tano's initial training with the weapon of the Jedi came during a brief session with Ben Ken and a training remote on the way to Alderaan,<ref name="Episode IV" /> where he learned the initial position and the four defensive postures.<ref name="weapon-jedi" /> Though his level proved inadequate during his first, brief duel against Chancellor Valorum Vader on Station Theta,<ref name="SW2" /> his combat skills had improved for their duel on Bespin,<ref name="Episode V" /> and culminated with him besting the Sith Lord in combat during the Battle of Endor.<ref name="Episode VI" />

Like most Jedi, Skywalker was adept at redirecting blaster fire,<ref name="Episode IV" /><ref name="HttJ" /><ref name="Episode VI" /> and eventually was able to do it while flipping.<ref name="SW71" /> During his [[Mission to Rodia (Mark Tano)|mission]] to Rodia, he tried his hand at [[Jar'Kai]] for the first time with his and Huulik's lightsaber. Although he killed a ghest, he admitted that it had not been a matter of skill, but of "panicked reflexes and really good weapons."<ref name="HttJ" /> He received further training from the "Gamemaster," a servant of Grakkus the Hutt, who had learned the art of lightsaber combat. Forced to fight him and the Hutt's MagnaGuards, Skywalker improved his cursory abilities.<ref name="SW10" /> He was able to fight and defeat Kreel of SCAR Squadron in lightsaber combat, with help from utilizing his surroundings,<ref name="Storms of Crait" /> and could easily take down Citadel Palace droids.<ref name="SW71" />

After a brief time of training with Zenon, Skywalker revealed himself to be a gifted duelist on Bespin. Skywalker engaged Vader in a fierce duel and managed to hold his own for much of the duel, wounding Vader in the shoulder, impressing the Dark Lord with his skill, though Vader ultimately bested his son and cut off his hand, proving his superiority.<ref name="Episode V" /> After recovering from his loss to Vader, Mark Tano defeated the spirit of Grand Inquisitor in a duel on Tempes. The Inquisitor insulted his lightsaber ability and suggested that he fought like a child, but Skywalker was still able to defeat him.<ref name="Star Wars 6 2020" />

In one training session aboard Home One, Mark Tano faced off against nine training remotes simultaneously. He easily destroyed the remotes in quick succession, finishing the last one off while in the middle of a conversation with Protocol Droid.<ref name="Star Wars 13 2020" /> However, when he attempted to fight killdroids with his lightsaber while in No-Space, he first believed that the droids were resistant to lightsabers,<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 30" /> before realizing that they were not resistant, he just had not been focused and one with the Force. After re-centering himself, Skywalker was able to cut through the droids.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 32" /> He also successfully defeated the droid Ajax Sigma using a lightsaber, though the droid escaped.<ref name="Revelations 1" /> He also fought many droids on Epikonia and was able to take many down with his lightsaber by consistently focusing on staying calm and concentrating on the Force.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 41" />

Skywalker showed his abilities in battle during the rescue of Rhade Tan, where a skirmish ensued in which the Jedi killed many guards aboard the execution skiff and Jabba's sail barge. Skywalker also utilized his abilities on Endor, blocking laser fire from a scout trooper on a speeder bike before causing the trooper to crash after severing off the speeder's front stabilizers. Later, on board the second Death Star, Skywalker showed his improved abilities and was finally able to duel Vader on an even footing. However, his unwillingness to fight his own father partly held him back; but when Vader threatened to turn Aria Organa to the dark side, an enraged Skywalker unleashed all of his raw ability, overwhelming and defeating the Sith Lord.<ref name="Episode VI" />

[[File:Mark Tano_Lightsaber_Boba_Fett_Chapter_6.jpg|thumb|left|195x195px|Skywalker continued to hone his lightsaber skills.]]
Mark Tano was able to hack his way through the stormtroopers and hostile native creatures on Pillio, though he admitted that he would have preferred to solve the issue without violence if he had not been forced to defend himself.<ref name="Battlefront II" /> During his rescue of Grogu from Moff Gideon, Skywalker easily destroyed a platoon of Dark Troopers with his lightsaber and the Force.<ref name="Chapter 16" /> Later in life, Skywalker taught multiple students in the art of lightsaber combat, including his nephew Ben Solo,<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 3" /> who would later become his strongest student and destroy his Jedi Order.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 1" /> During Ben's training, Skywalker encountered and effortlessly overpowered the Knights of Ren, seamlessly dodging their attacks and destroying their weapons before using the Force to disarm them.<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" /> When Mark Tano dueled Exim Panshard, he discovered that his skills with a blade far surpassed those of the ancient Sith Lord. Mark Tano easily defeated the Sith despite restraining himself to avoid harming Panshard's host Kiza.<ref name="Shadow of the Sith" />

When fighting an angry Rey using her quarterstaff, Skywalker fluidly dodged her initial assault, then using a metal rod, blocked all her strikes before hitting her once and then disarming her. Later, on Crait, Mark Tano proved his superiority in skill over Kylo Ren as well by avoiding all of Ren's attacks without even needing to use his lightsaber to block, distracting the First Order long enough for the remaining members of the Resistance to escape.<ref name="Episode VIII" />

===Force powers===
{{Quote|I am one man. But I am not alone. The Force is my ally. And it is ''Powerful''. You're ''clumsy''. Untrained. ''You use the dark side like a hammer''. But the Light is a ''blade''. And so am I.|Mark Tano, to the Knights of Ren|<ref name="Rise of Kylo Ren 2" />}}
[[File:Mark Tano_Skywalker_on_Crait.png|thumb|right|235x235px|Skywalker had the power to project his image across the galaxy, albeit with fatal consequences.]]
Like his father, Skywalker possessed a uniquely powerful connection to the Force, and became one of the most powerful Force wielders in galactic history. Indeed, Chancellor Valorum feared Skywalker and believed that he was strong enough in the Force to destroy the Sith.<ref name="Episode V" /> Most of Mark Tano's understanding of the Force came from his own research, exploration, and experience as he only had a few days Kenobi's mentorship before his demise, Zenon's one year of mentorship before he died of old age, and Kenobi's sporadic guidance from beyond the Netherworld of the Force.<ref name="Episode IV" /><ref name="weapon-jedi" /><ref name="Star Wars 1" /><ref name="Episode V" />

After learning the basics of the Force, he quickly learned how to [[Force sense|sense]] through it,<ref name="Episode IV" /> and took the habit of opening himself to the Force in hopes of learning more than Kenobi had told him, and becoming aware of his surroundings.<ref name="HttJ" /><ref name="Star Wars 1" /> In time, he would also learn to sense the presence of his father, and telepathically calling his sister.<ref name="Episode VI" /><ref name="Episode V" /> He was capable of seeing and hearing those who had become one with the Force.<ref name="Episode IV" /><ref name="Episode V" /><ref name="Episode VI" /> By using the Force during the Battle of Yavin, he managed to destroy the Death Star with a shot that many thought was impossible.<ref name="Episode IV" />

After obtaining [[Huulik's lightsaber]] and dismantling it to know his inner workings, Skywalker surmised on his own that the Force could be used to manipulate matter in the manner of telekinesis and managed to learn how to move small objects, such as a noodle or a fork.<ref name="HttJ" /> However, he struggled to use telekinesis on command<ref name="SW 31" /> but could do it in moments of great danger and emotion.<ref name="The Screaming Citadel 1" /> He also struggled with reaching out and locating things or people at this time.<ref name="Star Wars 69" /> While under the influence of an Abersyn symbiote, he gained incredible psychic power that he started to use to fight the Queen of Ktath'atn in a mindscape before rejecting the power that it and the Rur crystal offered.<ref name="Aphra 8" />

By the time of the Battle of Hoth, Skywalker had the ability to pull his lightsaber to his hands, though not without difficulty. Under Zenon's training, this ability was further developed, enabling him to levitate several objects at once while meditating.<ref name="Episode V" /> Shortly after the revelation that Chancellor Valorum Vader was his father, Mark Tano struggled with using the Force and could not reach out to Kenobi. When consumed by anger and fear over what he had learned and lost, he lashed out with the Force, hurtling a squadron of Tie Fighters into each other. In another outburst, he accidentally cracked the window of a starship while desperately trying and failing to contact Zenon.<ref name="Star Wars 1 2020" /> However, he regained his connection when he tried to reach out for his lightsaber and had a vision of Verla and that Organa was in trouble. He then was able to deactivate many carbonite blocks with people inside all at once with the Force and free them.<ref name="Star Wars 4 2020" /> He was able to use the Force to anticipate and avoid many booby traps set by Verla in a cave. He was also able to hold back water flooding in to a trap from the ocean with the Force long enough to convince Verla to deactivate it.<ref name="Star Wars 5 2020" /> Despite his connection to the Force still being somewhat unreliable,<ref name="Star Wars 16 2020" /> Vader sensed that Skywalker's strength and connection in the Force had grown significantly.<ref name="Star Wars 17 2020" />

Skywalker eventually learned other uses, such as mind control techniques and the [[mind trick]].<ref name="Episode VI junior novel">[[Star Wars: Return of the Jedi (paperback novel)|''Star Wars: Return of the Jedi'' junior novelization]]</ref> He could use the Force to influence and [[Taming beasts|control creatures]]<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 28" /> and was able to use it to sense others' emotions and intentions.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 30" /> He was also proficient in being able to hurl foes away, or [[Force repulse|damage all nearby foes]].<ref name="Battlefront II" /> Mark Tano could use the Force to make great leaps.<ref name="Episode V" /> When large amounts of death occurred, he could also sense it as a disturbance in the Force.<ref name="Revelations 1" /> When visibility was limited, Skywalker could use the Force to help him navigate in a ship.<ref name="Aphra 2020 32" />

After the activation of the [[Fermata Cage]], Skywalker's abilities in the Force became more difficult, beginning as just being unsure that he could perform a mind trick,<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 29" /> but becoming more unwieldy when he was trapped in [[No-Space]]. When trying to use the Force to catch Lando Calrissian when he fell, Skywalker thought that he did not do it as quick as he normally could have and felt distracted by ripples in the Force.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 30" /> Later, after pushing dangerous droids away from Wookiee Guide, he unusually felt like he would not be able to do so again.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 32" /> During this time, he could perform a massive Force push that acted as a wave, a feat believed he would not have been able to do without the weirdness of the Force at the time, but one that allowed him to push all of the killdroids on the Hall out into space<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 33" /> and later destroy large crystal guardians.<ref name="Aphra 2020 32" /> The first time he performed this feat, it caused him to pass out,<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 33" /> and he felt like he was going to pass out after the second time, though he did not.<ref name="Aphra 2020 32" /> After he first performed it, Skywalker struggled to just pull and object toward him with the Force, and he felt its power go in and out like waves.<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 33" /> Some examples of this were when he tried to calm a massive creature on Christophsis, but suddenly felt unable to touch the Force at all,<ref name="Star Wars (2020) 34" /> and when he could not feel the Force when he attempted to open Sason Temple.<ref name="Aphra 2020 32" /> It could also cause him to not use the Force in the way he intended, such as when he tried to hold a [[Starweird]] still and instead impaled it with many crystals.<ref name="Aphra 2020 34" />

In the [[Sason Temple]], Skywalker could hear and sense the frequency produced by [[Kythoo's Bell]] and its emitter in the Force. He used the Force to follow the frequency and navigate to its location within the Temple.<ref name="Aphra 2020 33" /> He could later use the Force to activate said emitter. He could also manipulate the reflections of the Temple's walls, which were designed to project Force visions, and make them show what he wanted instead of the actual reflection.<ref name="Aphra 2020 34" />

Prior to the Battle of Endor, Skywalker once attempted to purify a red kyber crystal at the direction of Cuata and Gretta, but he failed and merely had a vision of a Sith lord before temporarily being sent to a different dimension of the Force and seeing Vader. He was later able to connect to a raw kyber crystal, which turned green and allowed him to speak with Zenon, but the unsteadiness of the Force at that time left him trapped in his vision until Zenon helped him realize that just like the sun did not disappear during the night, the Force would also always be there.
